org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchAssetUiBuilder.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import java.lang.reflect.ParameterizedType;
import java.lang.reflect.RecordComponent;
import java.lang.reflect.Type;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.math.BigInteger;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;

final class StitchAssetUiBuilder {
  private static final String TAB_OVERVIEW = "overview";
  private static final String TAB_SEMANTIC = "semantic";
  private static final int DEFAULT_FIELD_GRID_COLUMNS = 4;
  private static final StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation DEFAULT_NESTED_PRESENTATION =
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.TABS;
  private static final int DEFAULT_RESULT_COLUMN_LIMIT = 4;
  private static final List<String> ENVELOPE_ALWAYS_READ_ONLY_FIELDS =
      List.of(
          "envelope.uuid",
          "envelope.createdTimeUtc",
          "envelope.createdBy",
          "envelope.updatedTimeUtc",
          "envelope.updatedBy");
  private static final Map<String, List<String>> SOURCE_DEFAULT_RESULT_FIELDS =
      Map.ofEntries(
          Map.entry(
              StitchAssetsFeature.APPS,
              List.of("appType", "sessionType", "controlEnabled", "displayName")),
          Map.entry(
              StitchAssetsFeature.SERVICES,
              List.of("serviceType", "lifecycleStatus", "namespace", "resourceId")),
          Map.entry(
              StitchAssetsFeature.CONNECTIONS,
              List.of("connectionType", "mode", "providerId", "physical.uriOrEndpoint")),
          Map.entry(
              StitchAssetsFeature.INGESTION,
              List.of("schemaMode", "datasetId", "outputSchemaId", "input.type")),
          Map.entry(
              StitchAssetsFeature.DATASETS,
              List.of("type", "namespace", "accessMode", "binding.duckdb.relationName")),
          Map.entry(
              StitchAssetsFeature.STREAMS,
              List.of("transport", "serde", "namespace", "versionName")),
          Map.entry(
              StitchAssetsFeature.CONFIGS,
              List.of("configId", "domain", "schemaRef", "recordType")),
          Map.entry(
              StitchAssetsFeature.SCHEMAS,
              List.of("schemaType", "schemaUsage", "versionSemantic", "status")));
  private static final Map<String, List<String>> SOURCE_DEFAULT_SUMMARY_FIELDS =
      Map.ofEntries(
          Map.entry(
              StitchAssetsFeature.APPS, List.of("displayName", "appType", "sessionType")),
          Map.entry(
              StitchAssetsFeature.SERVICES, List.of("serviceType", "namespace", "lifecycleStatus")),
          Map.entry(
              StitchAssetsFeature.CONNECTIONS, List.of("connectionType", "mode", "providerId")),
          Map.entry(
              StitchAssetsFeature.INGESTION, List.of("datasetId", "outputSchemaId", "schemaMode")),
          Map.entry(
              StitchAssetsFeature.DATASETS, List.of("namespace", "accessMode", "type")),
          Map.entry(
              StitchAssetsFeature.STREAMS, List.of("namespace", "transport", "serde")),
          Map.entry(
              StitchAssetsFeature.CONFIGS, List.of("configId", "domain", "schemaRef")),
          Map.entry(
              StitchAssetsFeature.SCHEMAS, List.of("schemaType", "schemaUsage", "versionSemantic")));

  StitchAssetUiDescriptor buildDescriptor(
      StitchAssetSourceSpec source,
      List<String> summaryFields,
      EditorOverrides editorOverrides) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(source, "source");
    int fieldGridColumns = resolveFieldGridColumns(editorOverrides);
    StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation nestedPresentation =
        resolveNestedPresentation(editorOverrides);
    StitchAssetUiDescriptor baseDescriptor =
        baseDescriptor(source, summaryFields, fieldGridColumns, nestedPresentation);
    if (editorOverrides == null || editorOverrides.groups().isEmpty()) {
      return applyVisibilityOverrides(baseDescriptor, editorOverrides);
    }
    StitchAssetUiDescriptor overridden = applyGroupOverrides(baseDescriptor, editorOverrides);
    return applyVisibilityOverrides(overridden, editorOverrides);
  }

  StitchAssetResultsConfig buildResultsConfig(
      StitchAssetSourceSpec source,
      ResultsOverrides resultsOverrides,
      List<String> summaryFieldsHint) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(source, "source");
    StitchAssetUiDescriptor descriptor =
        baseDescriptor(
            source,
            summaryFieldsHint,
            DEFAULT_FIELD_GRID_COLUMNS,
            DEFAULT_NESTED_PRESENTATION);
    List<StitchAssetsColumn> defaultColumns = defaultResultColumns(source, descriptor);
    List<String> defaultSummary = descriptor.summaryFields();
    if (defaultSummary.isEmpty()) {
      defaultSummary = defaultSummaryFields(source, descriptor);
    }
    List<StitchAssetsColumn> mergedColumns =
        StitchAssetResultsConfig.mergeVisibleFields(
            defaultColumns,
            resultsOverrides == null ? null : resultsOverrides.additionalFields(),
            resultsOverrides == null ? null : resultsOverrides.visibleFieldsOverride());
    List<String> mergedSummary =
        resultsOverrides != null && resultsOverrides.summaryFieldsOverride() != null
            ? StitchAssetResultsConfig.normalizeFieldKeys(resultsOverrides.summaryFieldsOverride())
            : defaultSummary;

    StitchAssetResultsConfig.Builder builder =
        StitchAssetResultsConfig.builder()
            .withVisibleFields(mergedColumns)
            .withSummaryLabel("Summary")
            .withSummaryFields(mergedSummary);
    return builder.build();
  }

  private StitchAssetUiDescriptor baseDescriptor(
      StitchAssetSourceSpec source,
      List<String> summaryFields,
      int fieldGridColumns,
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation nestedPresentation) {
    Class<? extends Definition> definitionClass = source.definitionClass();
    if (!definitionClass.isRecord()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Definition class must be a record: " + definitionClass.getName());
    }

    List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field> overviewFields = new ArrayList<>();
    List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab> nestedTabs = new ArrayList<>();
    StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab semanticTab = null;

    Map<String, EnumController> enumControllers = enumControllers(definitionClass);
    for (RecordComponent component : definitionClass.getRecordComponents()) {
      String componentPath = component.getName();
      if ("semantic".equalsIgnoreCase(componentPath)) {
        StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field semantic =
            buildField(componentPath, component, false, true);
        semanticTab =
            new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab(
                TAB_SEMANTIC,
                "Semantic",
                List.of(
                    new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Group(
                        "semantic", "Semantic", List.of(semantic), null, null, null)),
                null,
                null);
        continue;
      }

      if ("envelope".equalsIgnoreCase(componentPath)) {
        overviewFields.add(buildField(componentPath, component, true, true));
        continue;
      }

      if (isStructuredRecord(component.getType())) {
        StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field = buildField(componentPath, component, false, true);
        StitchAssetUiDescriptor.VisibilityRule rule = findRule(componentPath, enumControllers);
        nestedTabs.add(
            new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab(
                componentPath,
                display(componentPath),
                List.of(
                    new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Group(
                        componentPath + "-group",
                        display(componentPath),
                        List.of(field),
                        null,
                        null,
                        null)),
                null,
                rule));
        continue;
      }

      overviewFields.add(buildField(componentPath, component, false, true));
    }

    List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab> tabs = new ArrayList<>();
    tabs.add(
        new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab(
            TAB_OVERVIEW,
            "Overview",
            List.of(
                new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Group(
                    "overview-core", "Overview", overviewFields, null, null, null)),
            null,
            null));
    tabs.addAll(nestedTabs);
    if (semanticTab != null) {
      tabs.add(semanticTab);
    }

    List<String> resolvedSummary = StitchAssetResultsConfig.normalizeFieldKeys(summaryFields);
    if (resolvedSummary.isEmpty()) {
      resolvedSummary = sourceSummaryDefaults(source.sourceId());
    }
    if (resolvedSummary.isEmpty()) {
      resolvedSummary = defaultSummaryFieldsFromTabs(tabs);
    }
    return new StitchAssetUiDescriptor(
        source.sourceId(),
        source.definitionClass(),
        source.definitionType(),
        resolvedSummary,
        fieldGridColumns,
        nestedPresentation,
        tabs);
  }

  private StitchAssetUiDescriptor applyGroupOverrides(
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor descriptor, EditorOverrides overrides) {
    Map<String, StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field> byPath = descriptor.fieldsByPath();
    List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab> tabs = new ArrayList<>();

    for (GroupOverride groupOverride : overrides.groups()) {
      if (groupOverride == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String groupId = normalizeId(groupOverride.groupLabel());
      List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field> resolvedFields = new ArrayList<>();
      for (String requested : groupOverride.fields()) {
        StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field resolved = resolveField(byPath, groupId, requested);
        if (resolved != null) {
          resolvedFields.add(resolved);
        }
      }
      if (resolvedFields.isEmpty()) {
        continue;
      }
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.VisibilityRule inherited = inheritedRule(descriptor.tabs(), groupId);
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation inheritedPresentation =
          inheritedPresentation(descriptor.tabs(), groupId);
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Group group =
          new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Group(
              groupId + "-override",
              groupOverride.groupLabel(),
              resolvedFields,
              groupOverride.fieldGridColumns(),
              groupOverride.nestedRecordPresentation(),
              null);
      tabs.add(
          new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab(
              groupId,
              groupOverride.groupLabel(),
              List.of(group),
              groupOverride.nestedRecordPresentation() == null
                      || groupOverride.nestedRecordPresentation()
                          == StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.USE_DEFAULT
                  ? inheritedPresentation
                  : groupOverride.nestedRecordPresentation(),
              inherited));
    }

    if (tabs.isEmpty()) {
      return descriptor;
    }
    List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Group> semanticGroups = semanticGroups(descriptor.tabs());
    if (!semanticGroups.isEmpty()) {
      tabs.add(
          new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab(
              TAB_SEMANTIC,
              "Semantic",
              semanticGroups,
              inheritedPresentation(descriptor.tabs(), TAB_SEMANTIC),
              inheritedRule(descriptor.tabs(), TAB_SEMANTIC)));
    }
    return new StitchAssetUiDescriptor(
        descriptor.sourceId(),
        descriptor.definitionClass(),
        descriptor.definitionType(),
        descriptor.summaryFields(),
        descriptor.fieldGridColumns(),
        descriptor.nestedRecordPresentation(),
        dedupeTabs(tabs));
  }

  private StitchAssetUiDescriptor applyVisibilityOverrides(
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor descriptor, EditorOverrides overrides) {
    if (overrides == null || overrides.visibilityRules().isEmpty()) {
      return descriptor;
    }
    Map<String, VisibilityOverride> byTarget = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (VisibilityOverride override : overrides.visibilityRules()) {
      if (override == null || override.targetGroup() == null || override.targetGroup().isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      byTarget.put(normalizeId(override.targetGroup()), override);
    }
    if (byTarget.isEmpty()) {
      return descriptor;
    }

    List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab> tabs = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab tab : descriptor.tabs()) {
      if (tab == null) {
        continue;
      }
      VisibilityOverride tabOverride = byTarget.get(normalizeId(tab.id()));
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.VisibilityRule tabRule =
          tabOverride == null
              ? tab.visibilityRule()
              : new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.VisibilityRule(
                  tabOverride.controllerField(), tabOverride.allowedValues());
      List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Group> groups = new ArrayList<>();
      for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Group group : tab.groups()) {
        if (group == null) {
          continue;
        }
        VisibilityOverride groupOverride = byTarget.get(normalizeId(group.id()));
        StitchAssetUiDescriptor.VisibilityRule groupRule =
            groupOverride == null
                ? group.visibilityRule()
                : new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.VisibilityRule(
                    groupOverride.controllerField(), groupOverride.allowedValues());
        groups.add(
            new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Group(
                group.id(),
                group.label(),
                group.fields(),
                group.fieldGridColumns(),
                group.nestedRecordPresentation(),
                groupRule));
      }
      tabs.add(
          new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab(
              tab.id(), tab.label(), groups, tab.presentation(), tabRule));
    }

    return new StitchAssetUiDescriptor(
        descriptor.sourceId(),
        descriptor.definitionClass(),
        descriptor.definitionType(),
        descriptor.summaryFields(),
        descriptor.fieldGridColumns(),
        descriptor.nestedRecordPresentation(),
        tabs);
  }

  private List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Group> semanticGroups(List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab> tabs) {
    for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab tab : tabs) {
      if (tab != null && TAB_SEMANTIC.equalsIgnoreCase(tab.id())) {
        return tab.groups();
      }
    }
    return List.of();
  }

  private StitchAssetUiDescriptor.VisibilityRule inheritedRule(
      List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab> tabs, String tabId) {
    for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab tab : tabs) {
      if (tab == null || tabId == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (normalizeId(tab.id()).equals(normalizeId(tabId))) {
        return tab.visibilityRule();
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation inheritedPresentation(
      List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab> tabs, String tabId) {
    for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab tab : tabs) {
      if (tab == null || tabId == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (normalizeId(tab.id()).equals(normalizeId(tabId))) {
        return tab.presentation();
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab> dedupeTabs(List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab> tabs) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab> byId = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab tab : tabs) {
      if (tab == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = normalizeId(tab.id());
      if (!byId.containsKey(key)) {
        byId.put(key, tab);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(byId.values());
  }

  private StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field resolveField(
      Map<String, StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field> byPath, String groupId, String requested) {
    if (requested == null || requested.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = requested.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field exact = byPath.get(normalized);
    if (exact != null && exact.kind() != StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.STRUCT) {
      return exact;
    }
    if (!normalized.contains(".") && !TAB_OVERVIEW.equals(groupId)) {
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field prefixed = byPath.get((groupId + "." + normalized).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
      if (prefixed != null && prefixed.kind() != StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.STRUCT) {
        return prefixed;
      }
    }
    List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field> matches = new ArrayList<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field> entry : byPath.entrySet()) {
      if (entry.getValue() == null || entry.getValue().kind() == StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.STRUCT) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = entry.getKey();
      if (key.equals(normalized) || key.endsWith("." + normalized)) {
        matches.add(entry.getValue());
      }
    }
    if (matches.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    if (matches.size() == 1) {
      return matches.get(0);
    }
    for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field candidate : matches) {
      if (candidate.path().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).startsWith(groupId + ".")) {
        return candidate;
      }
    }
    return matches.get(0);
  }

  private List<StitchAssetsColumn> defaultResultColumns(
      StitchAssetSourceSpec source, StitchAssetUiDescriptor descriptor) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, StitchAssetsColumn> columns = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String preferred : sourceResultDefaults(source.sourceId())) {
      StitchAssetsColumn column = resolveResultColumn(descriptor, preferred);
      if (column == null) {
        continue;
      }
      columns.putIfAbsent(column.key().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT), column);
      if (columns.size() >= DEFAULT_RESULT_COLUMN_LIMIT) {
        return List.copyOf(columns.values());
      }
    }

    for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field : descriptor.fieldsByPath().values()) {
      if (field == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String path = field.path();
      if (path.startsWith("envelope.") || path.startsWith("semantic.")) {
        continue;
      }
      if (field.kind() == StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.STRUCT
          || field.kind() == StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.LIST
          || field.kind() == StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.JSON) {
        continue;
      }
      columns.putIfAbsent(
          path.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT), new StitchAssetsColumn(path, displayResultLabel(field.label(), path)));
      if (columns.size() >= DEFAULT_RESULT_COLUMN_LIMIT) {
        break;
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(columns.values());
  }

  private List<String> defaultSummaryFields(
      StitchAssetSourceSpec source, StitchAssetUiDescriptor descriptor) {
    List<String> summary = sourceSummaryDefaults(source.sourceId());
    if (!summary.isEmpty()) {
      return summary;
    }
    return defaultSummaryFields(descriptor);
  }

  private List<String> defaultSummaryFields(StitchAssetUiDescriptor descriptor) {
    List<String> summary = defaultSummaryFieldsFromTabs(descriptor.tabs());
    if (!summary.isEmpty()) {
      return summary;
    }
    return List.of("type");
  }

  private StitchAssetsColumn resolveResultColumn(StitchAssetUiDescriptor descriptor, String key) {
    if (key == null || key.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = key.trim();
    StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field direct = descriptor.field(normalized);
    if (direct != null) {
      return new StitchAssetsColumn(direct.path(), displayResultLabel(direct.label(), direct.path()));
    }
    StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field envelopeAlias = descriptor.field("envelope." + normalized);
    if (envelopeAlias != null) {
      return new StitchAssetsColumn(normalized, displayResultLabel(envelopeAlias.label(), normalized));
    }
    return new StitchAssetsColumn(normalized, displayResultLabel(null, normalized));
  }

  private List<String> sourceResultDefaults(String sourceId) {
    String key = normalizeId(sourceId);
    List<String> defaults = SOURCE_DEFAULT_RESULT_FIELDS.get(key);
    return defaults == null ? List.of() : defaults;
  }

  private List<String> sourceSummaryDefaults(String sourceId) {
    String key = normalizeId(sourceId);
    List<String> defaults = SOURCE_DEFAULT_SUMMARY_FIELDS.get(key);
    return defaults == null ? List.of() : defaults;
  }

  private int resolveFieldGridColumns(EditorOverrides overrides) {
    if (overrides == null || overrides.fieldGridColumns() == null) {
      return DEFAULT_FIELD_GRID_COLUMNS;
    }
    return normalizeFieldGridColumns(overrides.fieldGridColumns());
  }

  private StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation resolveNestedPresentation(
      EditorOverrides overrides) {
    if (overrides == null
        || overrides.nestedRecordPresentation() == null
        || overrides.nestedRecordPresentation()
            == StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.USE_DEFAULT) {
      return DEFAULT_NESTED_PRESENTATION;
    }
    return overrides.nestedRecordPresentation();
  }

  private static int normalizeFieldGridColumns(int value) {
    return Math.max(1, Math.min(6, value));
  }

  private static String displayResultLabel(String explicitLabel, String key) {
    String normalized = explicitLabel == null ? "" : explicitLabel.trim();
    if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
      return normalized;
    }
    return display(key == null ? "" : key);
  }

  private List<String> defaultSummaryFieldsFromTabs(List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab> tabs) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> fields = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab tab : tabs) {
      if (tab == null || TAB_SEMANTIC.equalsIgnoreCase(tab.id())) {
        continue;
      }
      for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Group group : tab.groups()) {
        if (group == null) {
          continue;
        }
        for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field : group.fields()) {
          collectSummaryField(field, fields);
          if (fields.size() >= 3) {
            return List.copyOf(fields);
          }
        }
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(fields);
  }

  private void collectSummaryField(StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field, LinkedHashSet<String> target) {
    if (field == null || target.size() >= 3) {
      return;
    }
    if (field.kind() == StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.STRUCT) {
      if (field.children() != null) {
        for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field child : field.children()) {
          collectSummaryField(child, target);
          if (target.size() >= 3) {
            return;
          }
        }
      }
      return;
    }
    if (field.kind() == StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.LIST || field.kind() == StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.JSON) {
      return;
    }
    if (field.path().startsWith("envelope.") || field.path().startsWith("semantic.")) {
      return;
    }
    target.add(field.path());
  }

  private Map<String, EnumController> enumControllers(Class<?> recordType) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, EnumController> controllers = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (RecordComponent component : recordType.getRecordComponents()) {
      Class<?> type = component.getType();
      if (type == null || !type.isEnum()) {
        continue;
      }
      List<String> values = new ArrayList<>();
      for (Object constant : type.getEnumConstants()) {
        if (constant == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String name = String.valueOf(constant).trim();
        if (name.isBlank() || "UNKNOWN".equalsIgnoreCase(name)) {
          continue;
        }
        values.add(name);
      }
      if (!values.isEmpty()) {
        controllers.put(component.getName(), new EnumController(component.getName(), values));
      }
    }
    return Map.copyOf(controllers);
  }

  private StitchAssetUiDescriptor.VisibilityRule findRule(
      String nestedName, Map<String, EnumController> enumControllers) {
    if (nestedName == null || nestedName.isBlank() || enumControllers.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    EnumController best = null;
    List<String> bestMatches = List.of();
    for (EnumController controller : enumControllers.values()) {
      List<String> matches = matchesFor(controller.values(), nestedName);
      if (matches.isEmpty()) {
        continue;
      }
      if (best == null || matches.size() > bestMatches.size()) {
        best = controller;
        bestMatches = matches;
      }
    }
    if (best == null || bestMatches.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    return new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.VisibilityRule(best.path(), bestMatches);
  }

  private List<String> matchesFor(List<String> enumValues, String nestedName) {
    String nestedToken = normalizeToken(nestedName);
    if (nestedToken.isBlank()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> matches = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String value : enumValues) {
      String token = normalizeToken(value);
      if (token.isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      if (token.contains(nestedToken) || nestedToken.contains(token)) {
        matches.add(value);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(matches);
  }

  private StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field buildField(
      String path, RecordComponent component, boolean inEnvelope, boolean includeChildren) {
    Class<?> type = component.getType();
    Type genericType = component.getGenericType();
    boolean readOnly = ENVELOPE_ALWAYS_READ_ONLY_FIELDS.contains(path);

    if (isStructuredRecord(type)) {
      List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field> children = new ArrayList<>();
      if (includeChildren) {
        for (RecordComponent child : type.getRecordComponents()) {
          String childPath = path + "." + child.getName();
          children.add(buildField(childPath, child, inEnvelope, true));
        }
      }
      return new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field(
          path,
          display(component.getName()),
          StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.STRUCT,
          type,
          genericType,
          List.of(),
          readOnly,
          children,
          null);
    }

    if (isJsonType(type)) {
      return new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field(
          path,
          display(component.getName()),
          StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.JSON,
          type,
          genericType,
          List.of(),
          readOnly,
          List.of(),
          null);
    }

    if (Map.class.isAssignableFrom(type)) {
      return new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field(
          path,
          display(component.getName()),
          StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.JSON,
          type,
          genericType,
          List.of(),
          readOnly,
          List.of(),
          null);
    }

    if (isListType(type)) {
      Type elementType = resolveListElementType(genericType);
      Class<?> elementClass = toClass(elementType);
      List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field> children = new ArrayList<>();
      if (elementClass != null && isStructuredRecord(elementClass)) {
        for (RecordComponent child : elementClass.getRecordComponents()) {
          String childPath = path + "." + child.getName();
          children.add(buildField(childPath, child, false, true));
        }
      }
      return new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field(
          path,
          display(component.getName()),
          StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.LIST,
          type,
          genericType,
          enumValues(elementClass),
          readOnly,
          children,
          null);
    }

    if (type.isEnum()) {
      return new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field(
          path,
          display(component.getName()),
          StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.ENUM,
          type,
          genericType,
          enumValues(type),
          readOnly,
          List.of(),
          null);
    }

    StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind kind = scalarKind(type);
    return new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field(
        path,
        display(component.getName()),
        kind,
        type,
        genericType,
        List.of(),
        readOnly,
        List.of(),
        null);
  }

  private static boolean isStructuredRecord(Class<?> type) {
    return type != null && type.isRecord();
  }

  private static boolean isJsonType(Class<?> type) {
    return type != null && JsonNode.class.isAssignableFrom(type);
  }

  private static boolean isListType(Class<?> type) {
    return type != null && java.util.Collection.class.isAssignableFrom(type);
  }

  private static Type resolveListElementType(Type genericType) {
    if (!(genericType instanceof ParameterizedType parameterized)) {
      return Object.class;
    }
    Type[] args = parameterized.getActualTypeArguments();
    if (args == null || args.length == 0) {
      return Object.class;
    }
    return args[0];
  }

  private static Class<?> toClass(Type type) {
    if (type instanceof Class<?> direct) {
      return direct;
    }
    if (type instanceof ParameterizedType parameterized && parameterized.getRawType() instanceof Class<?> raw) {
      return raw;
    }
    return Object.class;
  }

  private static StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind scalarKind(Class<?> type) {
    if (type == null) {
      return StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.STRING;
    }
    if (type == Boolean.class || type == boolean.class) {
      return StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.BOOLEAN;
    }
    if (type == Integer.class || type == int.class || type == Short.class || type == short.class) {
      return StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.INTEGER;
    }
    if (type == Long.class || type == long.class || type == BigInteger.class) {
      return StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.LONG;
    }
    if (type == Double.class
        || type == double.class
        || type == Float.class
        || type == float.class
        || type == BigDecimal.class) {
      return StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.DOUBLE;
    }
    return StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.STRING;
  }

  private static List<String> enumValues(Class<?> type) {
    if (type == null || !type.isEnum()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return Arrays.stream(type.getEnumConstants())
        .filter(Objects::nonNull)
        .map(Object::toString)
        .map(String::trim)
        .filter(value -> !value.isBlank())
        .toList();
  }

  private static String display(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    String normalized = value.trim().replace('_', ' ');
    String withSpaces = normalized.replaceAll("([a-z])([A-Z])", "$1 $2");
    if (withSpaces.isEmpty()) {
      return normalized;
    }
    return withSpaces.substring(0, 1).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT) + withSpaces.substring(1);
  }

  private static String normalizeId(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return value.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).replace(' ', '-');
  }

  private static String normalizeToken(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    String normalized =
        value
            .replaceAll("([a-z])([A-Z])", "$1_$2")
            .replace('-', '_')
            .trim()
            .toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return normalized.replaceAll("[^a-z0-9]", "");
  }

  record ResultsOverrides(
      List<String> additionalFields,
      List<String> visibleFieldsOverride,
      List<String> summaryFieldsOverride) {}

  record EditorOverrides(
      List<GroupOverride> groups,
      List<VisibilityOverride> visibilityRules,
      Integer fieldGridColumns,
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation nestedRecordPresentation) {}

  record GroupOverride(
      String groupLabel,
      List<String> fields,
      Integer fieldGridColumns,
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation nestedRecordPresentation) {}

  record VisibilityOverride(String targetGroup, String controllerField, List<String> allowedValues) {}

  private record EnumController(String path, List<String> values) {}
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchAssetUiDescriptor.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import java.lang.reflect.Type;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;

public final class StitchAssetUiDescriptor {
  private final String sourceId;
  private final Class<? extends Definition> definitionClass;
  private final DefinitionType definitionType;
  private final List<String> summaryFields;
  private final int fieldGridColumns;
  private final NestedRecordPresentation nestedRecordPresentation;
  private final List<Tab> tabs;
  private final Map<String, Field> byPath;

  public StitchAssetUiDescriptor(
      String sourceId,
      Class<? extends Definition> definitionClass,
      DefinitionType definitionType,
      List<String> summaryFields,
      int fieldGridColumns,
      NestedRecordPresentation nestedRecordPresentation,
      List<Tab> tabs) {
    this.sourceId = require(sourceId, "sourceId");
    this.definitionClass = Objects.requireNonNull(definitionClass, "definitionClass");
    this.definitionType = Objects.requireNonNull(definitionType, "definitionType");
    this.summaryFields = normalizeKeys(summaryFields);
    this.fieldGridColumns = normalizeColumns(fieldGridColumns);
    this.nestedRecordPresentation =
        nestedRecordPresentation == null
            ? NestedRecordPresentation.TABS
            : nestedRecordPresentation;
    this.tabs = tabs == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(tabs);
    this.byPath = indexFields(this.tabs);
  }

  public String sourceId() {
    return sourceId;
  }

  public Class<? extends Definition> definitionClass() {
    return definitionClass;
  }

  public DefinitionType definitionType() {
    return definitionType;
  }

  public List<String> summaryFields() {
    return summaryFields;
  }

  public int fieldGridColumns() {
    return fieldGridColumns;
  }

  public NestedRecordPresentation nestedRecordPresentation() {
    return nestedRecordPresentation;
  }

  public List<Tab> tabs() {
    return tabs;
  }

  public Map<String, Field> fieldsByPath() {
    return byPath;
  }

  public Field field(String path) {
    if (path == null || path.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return byPath.get(path.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
  }

  public record Tab(
      String id,
      String label,
      List<Group> groups,
      NestedRecordPresentation presentation,
      VisibilityRule visibilityRule) {
    public Tab {
      id = require(id, "id");
      label = normalizeLabel(label, id);
      groups = groups == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(groups);
      presentation =
          presentation == null ? NestedRecordPresentation.USE_DEFAULT : presentation;
    }
  }

  public record Group(
      String id,
      String label,
      List<Field> fields,
      Integer fieldGridColumns,
      NestedRecordPresentation nestedRecordPresentation,
      VisibilityRule visibilityRule) {
    public Group {
      id = require(id, "id");
      label = normalizeLabel(label, id);
      fields = fields == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(fields);
      fieldGridColumns =
          fieldGridColumns == null ? null : Integer.valueOf(normalizeColumns(fieldGridColumns));
      nestedRecordPresentation =
          nestedRecordPresentation == null
              ? NestedRecordPresentation.USE_DEFAULT
              : nestedRecordPresentation;
    }
  }

  public record Field(
      String path,
      String label,
      Kind kind,
      Class<?> javaType,
      Type genericType,
      List<String> enumValues,
      boolean readOnly,
      List<Field> children,
      VisibilityRule visibilityRule) {
    public Field {
      path = require(path, "path");
      label = normalizeLabel(label, path);
      kind = kind == null ? Kind.STRING : kind;
      javaType = javaType == null ? String.class : javaType;
      enumValues = enumValues == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(enumValues);
      children = children == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(children);
    }
  }

  public enum Kind {
    STRING,
    INTEGER,
    LONG,
    DOUBLE,
    BOOLEAN,
    ENUM,
    LIST,
    STRUCT,
    JSON
  }

  public enum NestedRecordPresentation {
    USE_DEFAULT,
    TABS,
    STACKED_PANELS
  }

  public record VisibilityRule(String controllerPath, List<String> allowedValues) {
    public VisibilityRule {
      controllerPath = require(controllerPath, "controllerPath");
      allowedValues = normalizeKeys(allowedValues);
    }

    public boolean matches(String currentValue) {
      if (allowedValues.isEmpty()) {
        return true;
      }
      if (currentValue == null) {
        return false;
      }
      String normalized = currentValue.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
      for (String allowed : allowedValues) {
        if (allowed.equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
          return true;
        }
      }
      return false;
    }
  }

  private static Map<String, Field> indexFields(List<Tab> tabs) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, Field> indexed = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (tabs == null) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    for (Tab tab : tabs) {
      if (tab == null || tab.groups() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      for (Group group : tab.groups()) {
        if (group == null || group.fields() == null) {
          continue;
        }
        for (Field field : group.fields()) {
          indexField(indexed, field);
        }
      }
    }
    return Map.copyOf(indexed);
  }

  private static void indexField(Map<String, Field> target, Field field) {
    if (field == null || field.path() == null) {
      return;
    }
    target.putIfAbsent(field.path().trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT), field);
    if (field.children() == null || field.children().isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    for (Field child : field.children()) {
      indexField(target, child);
    }
  }

  private static List<String> normalizeKeys(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> normalized = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String value : values) {
      String candidate = optional(value);
      if (candidate != null) {
        normalized.add(candidate);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    String normalized = optional(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String normalizeLabel(String value, String fallback) {
    String resolved = optional(value);
    if (resolved != null) {
      return resolved;
    }
    String normalized =
        (fallback == null ? "" : fallback).replace('_', ' ').replace('-', ' ').replace('.', ' ').trim();
    if (normalized.isEmpty()) {
      return "";
    }
    return normalized.substring(0, 1).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT) + normalized.substring(1);
  }

  private static int normalizeColumns(int value) {
    return Math.max(1, Math.min(6, value));
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchSchemaPresentationSupport.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.util.Locale;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionSchema;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

final class StitchSchemaPresentationSupport {
  static final String CONFIG_SCHEMA_FORMAT = "FABRIC_SCHEMA_CONFIG";

  private StitchSchemaPresentationSupport() {}

  static DefinitionSchema schemaDefinition(StitchAssetsRow row) {
    return row != null && row.sourceObject() instanceof DefinitionSchema schema ? schema : null;
  }

  static SchemaSnapshot snapshot(StitchAssetsRow row) {
    DefinitionSchema schema = schemaDefinition(row);
    if (schema != null) {
      return snapshot(
          schema,
          row == null ? null : row.group(),
          row == null ? null : row.name(),
          row == null ? null : row.field("updated"));
    }
    return new SchemaSnapshot(
        Strings.trimToNull(row == null ? null : row.group()),
        Strings.trimToNull(row == null ? null : row.name()),
        Strings.trimToNull(row == null ? null : row.field("versionSemantic")),
        Strings.trimToNull(row == null ? null : row.field("schemaType")),
        Strings.trimToNull(row == null ? null : row.field("schemaUsage")),
        Strings.trimToNull(row == null ? null : row.field("status")),
        Strings.trimToNull(row == null ? null : row.field("format")),
        Strings.trimToNull(row == null ? null : row.field("artifactType")),
        null,
        Strings.trimToNull(row == null ? null : row.field("updated")),
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        0,
        0,
        0,
        0,
        0,
        false,
        DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode(),
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            Strings.trimToNull(row == null ? null : row.field("schema")),
            Strings.trimToNull(row == null ? null : row.field("doc")),
            ""));
  }

  static SchemaSnapshot snapshot(DefinitionSchema schema, String fallbackGroup, String fallbackName) {
    return snapshot(schema, fallbackGroup, fallbackName, null);
  }

  static SchemaSnapshot snapshot(
      DefinitionSchema schema, String fallbackGroup, String fallbackName, String fallbackUpdated) {
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = schema == null ? null : schema.envelope();
    String group =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            Strings.trimToNull(envelope == null ? null : envelope.group()),
            Strings.trimToNull(fallbackGroup));
    String name =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            Strings.trimToNull(envelope == null ? null : envelope.name()),
            Strings.trimToNull(fallbackName));
    String updated =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            Strings.trimToNull(envelope == null ? null : envelope.updatedTimeUtc()),
            Strings.trimToNull(fallbackUpdated));
    String created =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            Strings.trimToNull(schema == null ? null : schema.createdTimeUtc()),
            Strings.trimToNull(envelope == null ? null : envelope.createdTimeUtc()));

    JsonNode payload = schemaPayload(schema);
    String schemaText = Strings.trimToNull(schema == null ? null : schema.schema());
    String title =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            text(payload, "displayName"),
            text(payload, "title"));
    String description =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            Strings.trimToNull(schema == null ? null : schema.doc()),
            text(payload, "description"));
    int groupsCount = arrayCount(payload, "groups");
    int structsCount = arrayCount(payload, "structs");
    int fieldsCount = arrayCount(payload, "fields");
    if (fieldsCount <= 0) {
      fieldsCount = objectFieldCount(payload, "properties");
    }
    int requiredCount = Math.max(arrayCount(payload, "requiredKeys"), arrayCount(payload, "required"));
    int refsCount = schema == null || schema.refs() == null ? 0 : schema.refs().size();

    String schemaType = enumName(schema == null ? null : schema.schemaType());
    String format = Strings.trimToNull(schema == null ? null : schema.format());
    boolean configCompatible =
        "CONFIG".equalsIgnoreCase(schemaType)
            || CONFIG_SCHEMA_FORMAT.equalsIgnoreCase(format)
            || (groupsCount > 0 && fieldsCount > 0);

    return new SchemaSnapshot(
        group,
        name,
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            Strings.trimToNull(schema == null ? null : schema.versionSemantic()),
            schema == null || schema.versionNum() == null ? null : String.valueOf(schema.versionNum())),
        schemaType,
        enumName(schema == null ? null : schema.schemaUsage()),
        Strings.trimToNull(schema == null ? null : schema.status()),
        format,
        Strings.trimToNull(schema == null ? null : schema.artifactType()),
        enumName(schema == null ? null : schema.compatibility()),
        updated,
        created,
        Strings.trimToNull(schema == null ? null : schema.hash()),
        title,
        description,
        Math.max(0, groupsCount),
        Math.max(0, structsCount),
        Math.max(0, fieldsCount),
        Math.max(0, requiredCount),
        Math.max(0, refsCount),
        configCompatible,
        payload,
        schemaText == null ? "" : schemaText);
  }

  static JsonNode schemaPayload(DefinitionSchema schema) {
    String text = Strings.trimToNull(schema == null ? null : schema.schema());
    if (text != null) {
      try {
        JsonNode parsed = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().readTree(text);
        if (parsed != null) {
          return parsed;
        }
      } catch (Exception ignored) {
      }
    }
    ObjectNode fallback = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    fallback.put("schemaText", Strings.firstNonBlank(text, ""));
    return fallback;
  }

  static String schemaExportFilename(String group, String name) {
    return "schema-" + safeFileToken(group) + "-" + safeFileToken(name) + ".json";
  }

  static String compareLabel(SchemaSnapshot snapshot) {
    if (snapshot == null) {
      return "-";
    }
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(snapshot.group(), "-")
        + "/"
        + Strings.firstNonBlank(snapshot.name(), "-")
        + "  |  v"
        + Strings.firstNonBlank(snapshot.version(), "0")
        + "  |  "
        + Strings.firstNonBlank(snapshot.status(), "UNKNOWN");
  }

  private static String safeFileToken(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return "unknown";
    }
    String sanitized = normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).replaceAll("[^a-z0-9._-]+", "-");
    return sanitized.isBlank() ? "unknown" : sanitized;
  }

  private static String text(JsonNode root, String field) {
    if (root == null || field == null || field.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    JsonNode node = root.get(field);
    if (node == null || node.isNull()) {
      return null;
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(node.asText());
  }

  private static int arrayCount(JsonNode root, String field) {
    if (root == null || field == null || field.isBlank()) {
      return 0;
    }
    JsonNode node = root.get(field);
    return node != null && node.isArray() ? node.size() : 0;
  }

  private static int objectFieldCount(JsonNode root, String field) {
    if (root == null || field == null || field.isBlank()) {
      return 0;
    }
    JsonNode node = root.get(field);
    return node != null && node.isObject() ? node.size() : 0;
  }

  private static String enumName(Enum<?> value) {
    return value == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(value.name());
  }

  record SchemaSnapshot(
      String group,
      String name,
      String version,
      String schemaType,
      String schemaUsage,
      String status,
      String format,
      String artifactType,
      String compatibility,
      String updated,
      String created,
      String hash,
      String title,
      String description,
      int groupsCount,
      int structsCount,
      int fieldsCount,
      int requiredCount,
      int refsCount,
      boolean configCompatible,
      JsonNode payload,
      String sourceText) {}
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.audit;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.UI;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.ComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.formlayout.FormLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.radiobutton.RadioButtonGroup;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextArea;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeEnterEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeEnterObserver;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.NotFoundException;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.QueryParameters;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;

import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialogs;
