import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchPage;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchResultsView;

public class StitchAuditBrowserScreen extends StitchPage implements BeforeEnterObserver {
  public static final String QUERY_PARAM_GROUP = "group";
  public static final String QUERY_PARAM_SEARCH = "search";

  private enum QueryMode {
    FILTERS,
    ADVANCED_SQL
  }

  private final Stitch stitch;
  private final StitchAuditScreenConfig config;
  private final StitchAuditFeedAdapter adapter;
  private final StitchAuditFilterBar filterBar;
  private final StitchFiltersBar filtersBar = new StitchFiltersBar();
  private final StitchResultsView<StitchAuditRow> results = new StitchResultsView<>();

  private final RadioButtonGroup<QueryMode> modeToggle = new RadioButtonGroup<>();
  private final VerticalLayout advancedPanel = new VerticalLayout();
  private final FormLayout advancedFiltersGrid = new FormLayout();
  private final VerticalLayout advancedSqlPanel = new VerticalLayout();
  private final TextArea advancedSqlInput = new TextArea();
  private final Span advancedSqlHint = new Span();
  private final Span statusMessage = new Span();

  private QueryMode activeMode = QueryMode.FILTERS;
  private int pageIndex;
  private int pageSize;
  private long totalRows;
  private String sortBy;
  private boolean sortAscending;
  private boolean suppressModeReload;
  private boolean suppressPagingCallbacks;

  public StitchAuditBrowserScreen(
      Stitch stitch,
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext,
      StitchAuditScreenConfig config,
      StitchAuditProvider provider,
      String feedId) {
    super(
        Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config").pageTitle(),
        Strings.firstNonBlank(config.pageSubtitle(), ""));
    this.stitch = Objects.requireNonNull(stitch, "stitch");
    this.config = config;
    this.adapter = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider").requireAdapter(feedId);
    this.filterBar = new StitchAuditFilterBar(Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext"));

    StitchAuditFilterModel defaults = adapter.defaultFilters(config.defaultPageSize());
    this.pageIndex = defaults.pageIndex();
    this.pageSize = defaults.pageSize();
    this.sortBy = defaults.sortBy();
    this.sortAscending = defaults.sortAscending();

    setSizeFull();
    body().setSizeFull();

    configureResults();
    filterBar.configureQuickFilters(adapter.filterDefinitions());
    filterBar.clearValues(adapter.defaultFeedFilters());

    configureModeControls();
    configureGrid(results.grid());
    configureFiltersBar();
    configureAdvancedPanel();
    applyModeVisibility();

    modeToggle.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          QueryMode requested = event.getValue();
          activeMode =
              requested == QueryMode.ADVANCED_SQL && !adapter.supportsAdvancedSql()
                  ? QueryMode.FILTERS
                  : requested;
          applyModeVisibility();
          if (suppressModeReload) {
            return;
          }
          pageIndex = 0;
          loadCurrentModePage(true);
        });

    addToBody(filtersBar, advancedPanel, results);
  }

  @Override
  public void beforeEnter(BeforeEnterEvent event) {
    applyRelatedContext(event);
    results.setItems(List.of());
    results.setEmpty(true);
    results.setEmptyState("Ready to search", "Set filters and click APPLY to load audit rows.");
    statusMessage.setText("Set filters and click APPLY.");
    syncPagingState(0, 0, pageSize);
  }

  private void configureResults() {
    results.setWidthFull();
    results.setHeight(null);
    results.setPaginationEnabled(true);
    results.setPageSizeOptions(resolvePageSizeOptions(config.defaultPageSize(), config.maxPageSize()));
    results.setPageSize(pageSize);
    results.setResultCountVisible(false);
    results.toolbar().setVisible(false);
    results.setEmptyState("No audit rows", "No matching audit rows were found.");
    results.grid().getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Audit results grid");

    statusMessage.getElement().setAttribute("aria-live", "polite");
    statusMessage.addClassName("stitch-audit-status-message");
    results.setStatus(statusMessage);

    results
        .pagination()
        .onPrevious(
            () -> {
              if (pageIndex <= 0) {
                return;
              }
              pageIndex--;
              loadCurrentModePage(false);
            })
        .onNext(
            () -> {
              if (!canAdvancePage()) {
                return;
              }
              pageIndex++;
              loadCurrentModePage(false);
            })
        .onPageSizeChange(
            value -> {
              if (suppressPagingCallbacks) {
                return;
              }
              int requested = value == null ? config.defaultPageSize() : value;
              int bounded = Math.max(1, Math.min(requested, config.maxPageSize()));
              if (bounded == pageSize) {
                return;
              }
              pageSize = bounded;
              pageIndex = 0;
              loadCurrentModePage(true);
            });

    syncPagingState(0, 0, pageSize);
  }

  private void configureModeControls() {
    if (adapter.supportsAdvancedSql()) {
      modeToggle.setItems(QueryMode.FILTERS, QueryMode.ADVANCED_SQL);
    } else {
      modeToggle.setItems(QueryMode.FILTERS);
    }
    modeToggle.setItemLabelGenerator(
        mode -> mode == QueryMode.ADVANCED_SQL ? "Advanced SQL" : "Filters");
    modeToggle.setValue(QueryMode.FILTERS);
    modeToggle.setLabel("");
    modeToggle.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Audit query mode");
  }

  private void configureGrid(StitchGrid<StitchAuditRow> grid) {
    List<StitchAuditColumn> columns = adapter.columns();
    for (StitchAuditColumn column : columns) {
      if (column == null || column.key().isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      StitchGridColumn<StitchAuditRow> stitchColumn;
      if (column.kind() == StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TIMESTAMP) {
        stitchColumn =
            StitchGridColumn.<StitchAuditRow>timestamp(
                    column.label(),
                    row -> {
                      if (row == null) {
                        return null;
                      }
                      Object value = row.value(column.key());
                      if (value instanceof Instant instant) {
                        return instant;
                      }
                      return StitchAuditDirectFeedSupport.parseEpoch(
                              value == null ? null : String.valueOf(value))
                          .orElse(null);
                    })
                .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.TIMESTAMP)
                .key(column.key());
      } else {
        stitchColumn =
            StitchGridColumn.<StitchAuditRow>text(
                    column.label(), row -> row == null ? "" : row.text(column.key()))
                .key(column.key())
                .kind(
                    column.kind() == StitchAuditColumn.Kind.STATUS
                        ? StitchGridColumn.Kind.STATUS
                        : StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP);
      }
      grid.addColumn(stitchColumn);
    }

    StitchRowActions<StitchAuditRow> rowActions = new StitchRowActions<>();
    rowActions.addAction(
        StitchRowActions.Action.icon(VaadinIcon.INFO_CIRCLE_O, "Details", this::openDetails));
    rowActions.addAction(
        StitchRowActions.Action.icon(VaadinIcon.LINK, "Session", this::openSessionDetails)
            .enabledWhen(row -> row != null && Strings.isNotBlank(row.sessionId())));
    rowActions.addAction(
        StitchRowActions.Action.icon(VaadinIcon.SHARE, "Related", this::openRelatedContext)
            .enabledWhen(row -> adapter.relatedSessionContext(row).isPresent()));
    rowActions.addColumn(grid);
  }

  private void configureFiltersBar() {
    Button refresh = new Button("REFRESH", event -> reloadCurrentPage());
    StitchResultsToolbar.stylePrimaryAction(refresh);
    refresh.addClassName("stitch-refresh-action");
    refresh.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Refresh audit rows");
    refresh.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Refresh audit rows");

    filterBar.search().addClassName("stitch-audit-top-search");

    filtersBar.withGroupSelector(filterBar.groupFilter());
    for (Map.Entry<String, ComboBox<String>> entry : filterBar.topBarQuickFilterComponents()) {
      ComboBox<String> component = entry.getValue();
      component.addClassName("stitch-audit-top-quick-filter");
      filtersBar.withFilter(component);
    }
    filtersBar.withSearch(filterBar.search()).withRightAction(refresh);
  }

  private void configureAdvancedPanel() {
    advancedPanel.setWidthFull();
    advancedPanel.setPadding(false);
    advancedPanel.setSpacing(false);
    advancedPanel.getStyle().set("gap", "0.6rem");
    advancedPanel.addClassName("stitch-audit-advanced-panel");

    Span modeLabel = new Span("Mode");
    modeLabel.addClassName("stitch-audit-advanced-mode-label");

    HorizontalLayout modeRow = new HorizontalLayout(modeLabel, modeToggle);
    modeRow.setPadding(false);
    modeRow.setSpacing(true);
    modeRow.setWidthFull();
    modeRow.addClassName("stitch-audit-advanced-mode-row");

    filterBar.timeFromUtc().setLabel("");
    filterBar.timeToUtc().setLabel("");

    advancedFiltersGrid.setWidth("fit-content");
    advancedFiltersGrid.setMaxWidth("100%");
    advancedFiltersGrid.getStyle().set("--vaadin-form-layout-column-width", "10.5rem");
    advancedFiltersGrid.getStyle().set("justify-content", "flex-start");
    advancedFiltersGrid.setResponsiveSteps(
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("0", 1),
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("46rem", 2),
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("72rem", 3));
    advancedFiltersGrid.addClassName("stitch-audit-advanced-grid");

    Button previousDay = new Button("-1D", event -> shiftDateWindow(-1));
    Button nextDay = new Button("+1D", event -> shiftDateWindow(1));
    StitchResultsToolbar.styleSecondaryAction(previousDay);
    StitchResultsToolbar.styleSecondaryAction(nextDay);
    previousDay.addClassName("stitch-audit-time-shift-button");
    nextDay.addClassName("stitch-audit-time-shift-button");
    previousDay.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Move From/To back one day");
    previousDay.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Move From and To back one day");
    nextDay.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Move From/To forward one day");
    nextDay.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Move From and To forward one day");

    HorizontalLayout dayShiftActions = new HorizontalLayout(previousDay, nextDay);
    dayShiftActions.setPadding(false);
    dayShiftActions.setSpacing(false);
    dayShiftActions.getStyle().set("gap", "0.45rem");
    dayShiftActions.addClassName("stitch-audit-time-shift-actions");

    advancedFiltersGrid.addFormItem(filterBar.timeFromUtc(), "From (UTC)");
    advancedFiltersGrid.addFormItem(filterBar.timeToUtc(), "To (UTC)");
    advancedFiltersGrid.addFormItem(dayShiftActions, "Shift Day");

    for (Map.Entry<String, ComboBox<String>> entry : filterBar.advancedQuickFilterComponents()) {
      ComboBox<String> component = entry.getValue();
      component.setWidthFull();
      component.setLabel("");
      advancedFiltersGrid.addFormItem(component, filterBar.quickFilterLabel(entry.getKey()));
    }

    advancedSqlHint.setText(
        adapter.supportsAdvancedSql()
            ? adapter.advancedSqlHelpText()
            : "Advanced SQL is not supported for this audit feed.");
    advancedSqlHint.getElement().setAttribute("aria-live", "polite");
    advancedSqlHint.addClassName("stitch-audit-advanced-sql-hint");

    advancedSqlInput.setWidthFull();
    advancedSqlInput.setMinHeight("12rem");
    advancedSqlInput.setMaxLength(32_000);
    advancedSqlInput.setValue(
        adapter.supportsAdvancedSql() ? adapter.advancedSqlTemplate() : "select * from ${AUDIT} limit 100");
    advancedSqlInput.setAriaLabel("Advanced SQL query");
    advancedSqlInput.getElement().setAttribute("placeholder", "select * from ${AUDIT} limit 100");
    advancedSqlInput.addClassName("stitch-audit-advanced-sql-input");

    advancedSqlPanel.setWidthFull();
    advancedSqlPanel.setPadding(false);
    advancedSqlPanel.setSpacing(false);
    advancedSqlPanel.getStyle().set("gap", "0.45rem");
    advancedSqlPanel.addClassName("stitch-audit-advanced-sql-panel");
    advancedSqlPanel.add(advancedSqlHint, advancedSqlInput);

    filterBar.applyButton().addClickListener(event -> onApplyRequested());
    filterBar.clearButton().addClickListener(event -> onClearRequested());

    HorizontalLayout actions = new HorizontalLayout(filterBar.applyButton(), filterBar.clearButton());
    actions.setPadding(false);
    actions.setSpacing(true);
    actions.setWidthFull();
    actions.addClassName("stitch-audit-advanced-actions");

    advancedPanel.add(modeRow, advancedFiltersGrid, advancedSqlPanel, actions);
  }

  private void onApplyRequested() {
    pageIndex = 0;
    loadCurrentModePage(activeMode == QueryMode.FILTERS);
  }

  private void onClearRequested() {
    pageIndex = 0;
    if (activeMode == QueryMode.ADVANCED_SQL) {
      advancedSqlInput.setValue(adapter.advancedSqlTemplate());
      statusMessage.setText("");
      return;
    }
    filterBar.clearValues(adapter.defaultFeedFilters());
    loadCurrentModePage(true);
  }

  private void shiftDateWindow(int days) {
    filterBar.shiftTimeRangeDays(days);
    onApplyRequested();
  }

  private void applyModeVisibility() {
    boolean sqlMode = activeMode == QueryMode.ADVANCED_SQL;
    advancedFiltersGrid.setVisible(!sqlMode);
    advancedSqlPanel.setVisible(sqlMode);
    if (sqlMode && Strings.isBlank(statusMessage.getText())) {
      statusMessage.setText("Advanced SQL mode");
      return;
    }
    if (!sqlMode && "Advanced SQL mode".equals(statusMessage.getText())) {
      statusMessage.setText("");
    }
  }

  private void loadCurrentModePage(boolean refreshFilterOptions) {
    if (activeMode == QueryMode.ADVANCED_SQL) {
      loadAdvancedSqlPage();
    } else {
      loadFilterPage(refreshFilterOptions);
    }
  }

  private void loadFilterPage(boolean refreshFilterOptions) {
    try {
      StitchAuditFilterModel filter =
          filterBar.toFilterModel(pageIndex, pageSize, sortBy, sortAscending, adapter.defaultFeedFilters());
      applyPage(adapter.query(filter), refreshFilterOptions);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      failLoad(
          "Unable to load audit rows",
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(error.getMessage()), "Audit rows could not be loaded."));
    }
  }

  private void loadAdvancedSqlPage() {
    try {
      if (!adapter.supportsAdvancedSql()) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Advanced SQL is not supported for this audit feed.");
      }
      StitchAuditFilterModel contextFilter =
          filterBar.toFilterModel(pageIndex, pageSize, sortBy, sortAscending, adapter.defaultFeedFilters());
      applyPage(adapter.queryAdvancedSql(advancedSqlInput.getValue(), contextFilter), false);
      if (Strings.isBlank(statusMessage.getText())) {
        statusMessage.setText("Advanced SQL mode");
      }
    } catch (Exception error) {
      failLoad(
          "Unable to execute advanced SQL",
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(error.getMessage()), "Advanced SQL execution failed."));
    }
  }

  private void failLoad(String title, String message) {
    results.setItems(List.of());
    results.setEmpty(true);
    results.setEmptyState(title, message);
    statusMessage.setText("Load failed");
    syncPagingState(0, 0, pageSize);
  }

  private void applyPage(StitchAuditPage page, boolean refreshFilterOptions) {
    this.pageIndex = page.pageIndex();
    this.pageSize = page.pageSize();
    this.totalRows = page.totalRows();
    results.setItems(page.rows());
    results.setEmpty(page.rows().isEmpty());
    syncPagingState(totalRows, pageIndex, pageSize);
    if (refreshFilterOptions) {
      filterBar.applyQuickFilterOptions(page.filterOptions());
    }
    statusMessage.setText(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(page.message()), ""));
  }

  private void reloadCurrentPage() {
    loadCurrentModePage(activeMode == QueryMode.FILTERS);
  }

  private void syncPagingState(long totalRows, int pageIndex, int pageSize) {
    int safePageSize = Math.max(1, pageSize);
    int totalPages = totalRows == 0 ? 1 : (int) ((totalRows - 1L) / safePageSize) + 1;
    int safePageIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(pageIndex, totalPages - 1));

    suppressPagingCallbacks = true;
    try {
      if (results.pagination().pageSize() != safePageSize) {
        results.pagination().setPageSize(safePageSize);
      }
      results
          .pagination()
          .setPageState(
              safePageIndex,
              totalPages,
              (int) Math.min(Integer.MAX_VALUE, Math.max(0L, totalRows)));
    } finally {
      suppressPagingCallbacks = false;
    }
  }

  private boolean canAdvancePage() {
    if (totalRows <= 0) {
      return false;
    }
    int totalPages = (int) ((totalRows - 1L) / Math.max(1, pageSize)) + 1;
    return pageIndex + 1 < totalPages;
  }

  private void openDetails(StitchAuditRow row) {
    if (row == null) {
      return;
    }
    StitchAuditDetailsDialog dialog = new StitchAuditDetailsDialog(adapter.details(row));
    adapter
        .relatedSessionContext(row)
        .ifPresent(
            context ->
                dialog.addPrimaryAction(
                    context.label(),
                    () -> {
                      dialog.close();
                      navigateToRelated(context);
                    }));
    dialog.open();
  }

  private void openSessionDetails(StitchAuditRow row) {
    if (row == null || Strings.isBlank(row.sessionId())) {
      return;
    }
    adapter
        .sessionDetails(row)
        .ifPresentOrElse(
            details -> new StitchAuditDetailsDialog(details).open(),
            () ->
                StitchDialogs.openInfo(
                    "Session Not Available",
                    "No related session details were found for " + row.sessionId()));
  }

  private void openRelatedContext(StitchAuditRow row) {
    if (row == null) {
      return;
    }
    adapter
        .relatedSessionContext(row)
        .ifPresentOrElse(
            this::navigateToRelated,
            () ->
                StitchDialogs.openInfo(
                    "Related Context Not Available", "No related context could be resolved."));
  }

  private void applyRelatedContext(BeforeEnterEvent event) {
    String group = firstQueryParam(event, QUERY_PARAM_GROUP);
    String search = firstQueryParam(event, QUERY_PARAM_SEARCH);
    if (group == null && search == null) {
      return;
    }
    suppressModeReload = true;
    try {
      activeMode = QueryMode.FILTERS;
      modeToggle.setValue(QueryMode.FILTERS);
    } finally {
      suppressModeReload = false;
    }
    filterBar.clearValues(adapter.defaultFeedFilters());
    filterBar.setSelectedGroup(group);
    filterBar.setSearchText(search);
    pageIndex = 0;
  }

  private void navigateToRelated(StitchAuditRelatedContext context) {
    StitchAuditRelatedContext resolved = Objects.requireNonNull(context, "context");
    String targetRoute =
        stitch
            .features()
            .audit()
            .flatMap(feature -> feature.screen(resolved.targetFeedId()))
            .filter(StitchAuditScreenConfig::enabled)
            .map(StitchAuditScreenConfig::routePath)
            .orElse(null);
    if (Strings.isBlank(targetRoute)) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Related Context Not Available", "The related audit feed is unavailable.");
      return;
    }

    LinkedHashMap<String, String> params = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (Strings.isNotBlank(resolved.group())) {
      params.put(QUERY_PARAM_GROUP, resolved.group());
    }
    if (Strings.isNotBlank(resolved.searchText())) {
      params.put(QUERY_PARAM_SEARCH, resolved.searchText());
    }

    UI ui = UI.getCurrent();
    if (ui == null) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Navigation Unavailable", "Unable to open related context.");
      return;
    }
    if (params.isEmpty()) {
      ui.navigate(targetRoute);
    } else {
      ui.navigate(targetRoute, QueryParameters.simple(params));
    }
  }

  private static String firstQueryParam(BeforeEnterEvent event, String key) {
    if (event == null || Strings.isBlank(key)) {
      return null;
    }
    List<String> values = event.getLocation().getQueryParameters().getParameters().get(key);
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(values.getFirst());
  }

  private static int[] resolvePageSizeOptions(int defaultPageSize, int maxPageSize) {
    int safeDefault = Math.max(1, defaultPageSize);
    int safeMax = Math.max(safeDefault, maxPageSize);
    LinkedHashSet<Integer> requested = new LinkedHashSet<>(List.of(25, 50, 100, 200));
    requested.add(safeDefault);
    requested.add(safeMax);

    List<Integer> bounded = new ArrayList<>();
    for (Integer value : requested) {
      if (value == null || value <= 0 || value > safeMax) {
        continue;
      }
      bounded.add(value);
    }
    if (bounded.isEmpty()) {
      return new int[] {safeDefault};
    }
    bounded.sort(Integer::compareTo);
    int[] options = new int[bounded.size()];
    for (int i = 0; i < bounded.size(); i++) {
      options[i] = bounded.get(i);
    }
    return options;
  }

  protected static StitchAuditScreenConfig requireEnabledConfig(Stitch stitch, String feedId) {
    return Objects.requireNonNull(stitch, "stitch")
        .features()
        .audit()
        .flatMap(feature -> feature.screen(feedId))
        .filter(StitchAuditScreenConfig::enabled)
        .orElseThrow(NotFoundException::new);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/audit/StitchAuditColumn.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.audit;

public record StitchAuditColumn(String key, String label, Kind kind) {
  public enum Kind {
    TEXT,
    TIMESTAMP,
    STATUS
  }

  public StitchAuditColumn {
    key = key == null ? "" : key.trim();
    label = label == null || label.isBlank() ? key : label.trim();
    kind = kind == null ? Kind.TEXT : kind;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/audit/StitchAuditConfigsFeedAdapter.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.audit;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.RowResult;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetId;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

public class StitchAuditConfigsFeedAdapter extends StitchAuditDirectFeedSupport
    implements StitchAuditFeedAdapter {
  private static final List<ConfigSource> SOURCES =
      List.of(
          new ConfigSource("config_resolved", "RESOLVED"),
          new ConfigSource("config_subscribed", "SUBSCRIBED"),
          new ConfigSource("config_update_callback", "UPDATE_CALLBACK"),
          new ConfigSource("config_unsubscribed", "UNSUBSCRIBED"),
          new ConfigSource("config_generated", "GENERATED"));
  private static final List<StitchAuditColumn> COLUMNS =
      List.of(
          new StitchAuditColumn("eventTime", "Event Time", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TIMESTAMP),
          new StitchAuditColumn("eventType", "Event Type", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT),
          new StitchAuditColumn("group", "Group", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT),
          new StitchAuditColumn("configId", "Config ID", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT),
          new StitchAuditColumn("layerId", "Layer ID", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT),
          new StitchAuditColumn("user", "User", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT),
          new StitchAuditColumn("requestId", "Request ID", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT),
          new StitchAuditColumn("sessionId", "Session ID", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT));
  private static final List<StitchAuditFilterDefinition> QUICK_FILTERS =
      List.of(new StitchAuditFilterDefinition("eventType", "Event Type"));
  private static final Map<String, String> DEFAULT_FEED_FILTERS =
      defaultQuickFilters("eventType", FILTER_ALL);
  private static final StitchAuditFilterModel NO_FILTER =
      new StitchAuditFilterModel(null, null, null, null, Map.of(), 0, 25, null, false);

  public StitchAuditConfigsFeedAdapter(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    super(runtimeContext);
  }

  @Override
  public String feedId() {
    return StitchAuditFeature.CONFIGS;
  }

  @Override
  public List<StitchAuditColumn> columns() {
    return COLUMNS;
  }

  @Override
  public List<StitchAuditFilterDefinition> filterDefinitions() {
    return QUICK_FILTERS;
  }

  @Override
  public Map<String, String> defaultFeedFilters() {
    return DEFAULT_FEED_FILTERS;
  }

  @Override
  public StitchAuditFilterModel defaultFilters(int defaultPageSize) {
    return new StitchAuditFilterModel(
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        defaultFeedFilters(),
        0,
        Math.max(1, defaultPageSize),
        "event_time_utc",
        false);
  }

  @Override
  public StitchAuditPage queryAdvancedSql(String sql, StitchAuditFilterModel contextFilter) {
    StitchAuditFilterModel filter = Objects.requireNonNull(contextFilter, "contextFilter");
    String datasetGroup = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(filter.group()), sessionGroup);
    List<AdvancedSqlSource> sources = new ArrayList<>();
    List<String> notices = new ArrayList<>();
    for (ConfigSource source : SOURCES) {
      DatasetId datasetId = datasetId(datasetGroup, source.datasetName());
      if (!datasetExists(datasetId)) {
        notices.add(datasetUnavailableMessage(datasetId));
        continue;
      }
      sources.add(
          new AdvancedSqlSource(
              datasetId, rewriteDatasetToken(configsSql(source.eventType(), NO_FILTER), datasetId)));
    }
    return queryAdvancedSqlFromSources(
        sql,
        filter,
        sources,
        "event_time_utc",
        "payload",
        "session_id",
        "request_id",
        notices.isEmpty() ? "" : String.join(" | ", notices));
  }

  @Override
  public StitchAuditPage query(StitchAuditFilterModel filter) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(filter, "filter");
    String datasetGroup = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(filter.group()), sessionGroup);

    List<String> notices = new ArrayList<>();
    List<StitchAuditRow> rows = new ArrayList<>();

    String requestedEventType = Strings.trimToNull(filter.filterValue("eventType"));
    for (ConfigSource source : SOURCES) {
      if (requestedEventType != null
          && !FILTER_ALL.equalsIgnoreCase(requestedEventType)
          && !requestedEventType.equalsIgnoreCase(source.eventType())) {
        continue;
      }
      DatasetId datasetId = datasetId(datasetGroup, source.datasetName());
      if (!datasetExists(datasetId)) {
        notices.add(datasetUnavailableMessage(datasetId));
        continue;
      }
      rows.addAll(loadRows(datasetId, source.eventType(), filter));
    }

    rows.sort(comparator(filter));
    String message = notices.isEmpty() ? "" : String.join(" | ", notices);
    return buildPage(rows, filter, MAX_PAGE_SIZE, filterOptions(rows, "eventType"), message);
  }

  @Override
  public StitchAuditDetailsModel details(StitchAuditRow row) {
    if (row == null) {
      return new StitchAuditDetailsModel("Configs Audit Event", "", Map.of(), null);
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> summary = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    summary.put("eventTimeUtc", formatInstant(row.eventTimeUtc()));
    summary.put("eventType", row.text("eventType"));
    summary.put("group", row.text("group"));
    summary.put("configId", row.text("configId"));
    summary.put("layerId", row.text("layerId"));
    summary.put("user", row.text("user"));
    summary.put("requestId", row.text("requestId"));
    summary.put("sessionId", row.text("sessionId"));
    summary.put("callerApp", row.text("callerApp"));

    String subtitle =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            row.text("configId") + " / " + row.text("layerId"),
            row.text("configId"),
            "Configs event");

    return new StitchAuditDetailsModel(
        "Configs Audit Event",
        subtitle,
        summary,
        parsePayload(row.payload()).orElse(row.payload()));
  }

  @Override
  public Optional<StitchAuditDetailsModel> sessionDetails(StitchAuditRow row) {
    if (row == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return lookupSessionDetails(row.text("group"), row.sessionId(), "Configs");
  }

  private List<StitchAuditRow> loadRows(
      DatasetId datasetId, String eventType, StitchAuditFilterModel filter) {
    String sql = configsSql(eventType, filter);
    RowResult result = directQuery(datasetId, sql);
    if (result.rows() == null || result.rows().isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }

    Map<String, Integer> index = columnIndex(result.columns());
    List<StitchAuditRow> rows = new ArrayList<>(result.rows().size());
    int ordinal = 0;
    for (List<Object> values : result.rows()) {
      String eventTime = valueAt(values, index, "event_time_utc");
      Instant instant = parseEpoch(eventTime).orElse(null);
      String group = valueAt(values, index, "group");
      String configId = valueAt(values, index, "config_id");
      String layerId = valueAt(values, index, "layer_id");
      String subject = valueAt(values, index, "subject");
      String delegated = valueAt(values, index, "delegated_user");
      String requestId = valueAt(values, index, "request_id");
      String sessionId = valueAt(values, index, "session_id");
      String callerApp = valueAt(values, index, "caller_app_name");
      String payload = valueAt(values, index, "payload");

      LinkedHashMap<String, Object> mapped = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      mapped.put("eventTime", instant);
      mapped.put("eventType", eventType);
      mapped.put("group", group);
      mapped.put("configId", configId);
      mapped.put("layerId", layerId);
      mapped.put("user", Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(delegated), Strings.trimToNull(subject), ""));
      mapped.put("requestId", requestId);
      mapped.put("sessionId", sessionId);
      mapped.put("callerApp", callerApp);

      String id =
          datasetId.group()
              + "/"
              + datasetId.name()
              + "/"
              + Strings.trimToEmpty(eventTime)
              + "/"
              + ordinal++;
      rows.add(new StitchAuditRow(id, instant, payload, sessionId, mapped, Map.of("dataset", datasetId.toString())));
    }
    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  private String configsSql(String eventType, StitchAuditFilterModel filter) {
    String eventTimeExpr =
        "coalesce(json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.timeUtc'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.envelope.timeUtc'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.timeUtc'))";
    String groupExpr =
        "coalesce(json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.group'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.envelope.group'))";
    String configExpr =
        "coalesce(json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.configId'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.envelope.configId'))";
    String layerExpr =
        "coalesce(json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.layerId'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.envelope.layerId'))";
    String subjectExpr =
        "coalesce(json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.subject'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.envelope.subject'), json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.callerAppSubject'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.envelope.callerAppSubject'))";
    String delegatedExpr =
        "coalesce(json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.delegatedUser'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.envelope.delegatedUser'))";
    String requestExpr =
        "coalesce(json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.requestId'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.envelope.requestId'))";
    String sessionExpr =
        "coalesce(json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.sessionId'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.envelope.sessionId'))";
    String callerAppExpr =
        "coalesce(json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.callerAppName'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.envelope.callerAppName'))";
    String payloadExpr = "cast(payload_json as varchar)";

    StringBuilder sql = new StringBuilder("select ");
    sql.append(eventTimeExpr).append(" as \"event_time_utc\", ");
    sql.append(groupExpr).append(" as \"group\", ");
    sql.append(configExpr).append(" as \"config_id\", ");
    sql.append(layerExpr).append(" as \"layer_id\", ");
    sql.append(subjectExpr).append(" as \"subject\", ");
    sql.append(delegatedExpr).append(" as \"delegated_user\", ");
    sql.append(requestExpr).append(" as \"request_id\", ");
    sql.append(sessionExpr).append(" as \"session_id\", ");
    sql.append(callerAppExpr).append(" as \"caller_app_name\", ");
    sql.append(payloadExpr).append(" as \"payload\" ");
    sql.append("from ${DATASET}");

    List<String> predicates = new ArrayList<>();
    addExactPredicate(predicates, groupExpr, filter.group(), FILTER_ALL);

    addIsoInstantRangePredicates(predicates, eventTimeExpr, filter.timeFromUtc(), filter.timeToUtc());
    addContainsAnyPredicate(
        predicates,
        filter.searchText(),
        configExpr,
        layerExpr,
        subjectExpr,
        delegatedExpr,
        requestExpr,
        sessionExpr,
        payloadExpr);

    if (!predicates.isEmpty()) {
      sql.append(" where ").append(String.join(" and ", predicates));
    }
    return sql.toString();
  }

  private Comparator<StitchAuditRow> comparator(StitchAuditFilterModel filter) {
    String sortBy = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(filter.sortBy()), "event_time_utc");
    Comparator<StitchAuditRow> base;
    if ("eventType".equalsIgnoreCase(sortBy) || "event_type".equalsIgnoreCase(sortBy)) {
      base = Comparator.comparing(row -> normalize(row.text("eventType")));
    } else if ("group".equalsIgnoreCase(sortBy)) {
      base = Comparator.comparing(row -> normalize(row.text("group")));
    } else {
      base = Comparator.comparing(StitchAuditRow::eventTimeUtc, Comparator.nullsLast(Comparator.naturalOrder()));
    }
    Comparator<StitchAuditRow> comparator =
        base.thenComparing(row -> normalize(row.text("configId"))).thenComparing(row -> normalize(row.text("layerId")));
    return filter.sortAscending() ? comparator : comparator.reversed();
  }

  private record ConfigSource(String datasetName, String eventType) {}
}

import com.vaadin.flow.component.formlayout.FormLayout;

public class StitchAuditDetailsDialog extends StitchDialog {
  public StitchAuditDetailsDialog(StitchAuditDetailsModel model) {
    super(model == null ? "Audit Details" : model.title(), false);
    setWidth("820px");
    setMaxWidth("95vw");
    setTop("8vh");

    StitchAuditDetailsModel resolved =
        model == null ? new StitchAuditDetailsModel("Audit Details", "", Map.of(), null) : model;

    String subtitle = Strings.trimToNull(resolved.subtitle());
    if (subtitle != null) {
      Span subtitleSpan = new Span(subtitle);
      subtitleSpan.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Details context");
      addToBody(subtitleSpan);
    }

    FormLayout summary = new FormLayout();
    summary.setWidthFull();
    summary.setResponsiveSteps(
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("0", 1), new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("42em", 2));

    if (resolved.summaryFields() != null) {
      for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : resolved.summaryFields().entrySet()) {
        String key = Strings.firstNonBlank(entry.getKey(), "Field");
        String value = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue()), "-");
        Span label = new Span(key.toUpperCase(java.util.Locale.ROOT));
        Span fieldValue = new Span(value);
        fieldValue.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", key + " value");
        com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout cell =
            new com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout(label, fieldValue);
        cell.setPadding(false);
        cell.setSpacing(false);
        cell.getStyle().set("gap", "0.2rem");
        summary.add(cell);
      }
    }

    addToBody(summary);

    if (resolved.payloadJson() != null) {
      addPrimaryAction("RAW JSON", () -> new StitchJsonDialog("Audit Payload", resolved.payloadJson()).open());
    }
    addSecondaryAction("Close", this::close);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/audit/StitchAuditDirectFeedSupport.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.audit;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.time.LocalDateTime;
import java.time.ZoneOffset;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.TreeSet;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import java.util.regex.Matcher;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.UserContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.UserPrincipal;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.RowResult;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.TabularManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetId;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager.TabularManagerImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.StitchIdentityContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

abstract class StitchAuditDirectFeedSupport {
  private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(StitchAuditDirectFeedSupport.class);
  protected static final String FILTER_ALL = "All";
  protected static final int MAX_PAGE_SIZE = 200;
  private static final long DATASET_EXISTS_TTL_MS = 30_000L;
  private static final Pattern AUDIT_TOKEN_PATTERN = Pattern.compile("\\$\\{AUDIT\\}", Pattern.CASE_INSENSITIVE);
  private static final List<String> SQL_BLOCKED_TOKENS =
      List.of(
          "insert",
          "update",
          "delete",
          "merge",
          "alter",
          "drop",
          "create",
          "truncate",
          "grant",
          "revoke",
          "replace",
          "attach",
          "detach",
          "pragma",
          "vacuum",
          "call",
          "execute",
          "copy");
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER = new ObjectMapper();

  private final StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext;
  protected final SessionImpl session;
  protected final String sessionGroup;
  private final ConcurrentHashMap<String, DatasetPresence> presenceCache = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();

  protected StitchAuditDirectFeedSupport(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    this.runtimeContext = Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(current instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    this.session = resolved;
    this.sessionGroup =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            this.session.context() == null ? null : this.session.context().getGroup(), "platform");
  }

  protected DatasetId datasetId(String group, String name) {
    String resolvedGroup = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(group), sessionGroup);
    return DatasetId.parse("dataset:" + resolvedGroup + "/default/" + Objects.requireNonNull(name, "name"));
  }

  public boolean supportsAdvancedSql() {
    return true;
  }

  public String advancedSqlTemplate() {
    return "select * from ${AUDIT}\nlimit 100";
  }

  public String advancedSqlHelpText() {
    return "Advanced SQL is read-only. Use SELECT statements only and reference ${AUDIT}.";
  }

  protected static Map<String, String> defaultQuickFilters(String... keyValuePairs) {
    if (keyValuePairs == null || keyValuePairs.length == 0) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    if ((keyValuePairs.length % 2) != 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("defaultQuickFilters requires key/value pairs");
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (int i = 0; i < keyValuePairs.length; i += 2) {
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(keyValuePairs[i]);
      if (key == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(keyValuePairs[i + 1]);
      values.put(key, value == null ? FILTER_ALL : value);
    }
    return values.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(values);
  }

  protected static String datasetUnavailableMessage(DatasetId datasetId) {
    return "Dataset unavailable: "
        + datasetId.group()
        + "/"
        + datasetId.namespace()
        + "/"
        + datasetId.name();
  }

  protected RowResult directQuery(DatasetId datasetId, String sql) {
    return directQuery(List.of(datasetId), rewriteDatasetToken(sql, datasetId));
  }

  protected RowResult directQuery(List<DatasetId> datasetIds, String sql) {
    List<DatasetId> safeDatasetIds = datasetIds == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(datasetIds);
    String resolvedSql = Strings.requireNonBlank(sql, "sql");
    String subject = currentSubject();
    LOG.info(
        "[Stitch][Audit][SQL] execute subject={} datasets={} sql={}",
        subject,
        safeDatasetIds.stream().filter(Objects::nonNull).map(DatasetId::toString).toList(),
        resolvedSql);
    try {
      RowResult result =
          runAsSubject(
              subject,
              () -> {
                TabularManager directTabular = session.data().direct().tabular();
                if (directTabular instanceof TabularManagerImpl directManager) {
                  for (DatasetId datasetId : safeDatasetIds) {
                    if (datasetId != null) {
                      directManager.installDataset(datasetId.toString());
                    }
                  }
                }
                return session.data().direct().rows().querySql(resolvedSql);
              });
      int rowCount = result.rows() == null ? 0 : result.rows().size();
      int colCount = result.columns() == null ? 0 : result.columns().size();
      LOG.info("[Stitch][Audit][SQL] success rows={} columns={}", rowCount, colCount);
      return result;
    } catch (Exception error) {
      LOG.error(
          "[Stitch][Audit][SQL] failure subject={} message={} sql={}",
          subject,
          Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(error.getMessage()), error.getClass().getName()),
          resolvedSql,
          error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  protected boolean datasetExists(DatasetId datasetId) {
    String key = datasetId.toString().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    DatasetPresence cached = presenceCache.get(key);
    long now = System.currentTimeMillis();
    if (cached != null && cached.expiresAtMs() > now) {
      return cached.present();
    }

    boolean present;
    try {
      directQuery(datasetId, "select 1 from ${DATASET} limit 1");
      present = true;
    } catch (RuntimeException error) {
      present = !isDatasetMissingError(error);
      if (!present) {
        // optional archive dataset missing
      } else {
        throw error;
      }
    }
    presenceCache.put(key, new DatasetPresence(present, now + DATASET_EXISTS_TTL_MS));
    return present;
  }

  protected String currentSubject() {
    return StitchIdentityContext.resolveSubject(runtimeContext.settings().sso().fallbackSubject());
  }

  protected Optional<StitchAuditDetailsModel> lookupSessionDetails(
      String group, String sessionId, String titlePrefix) {
    String normalizedSession = Strings.trimToNull(sessionId);
    if (normalizedSession == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    DatasetId statusApp = datasetId(group, "status_app");
    if (!datasetExists(statusApp)) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }

    String sql =
        "select "
            + "coalesce(cast(\"group\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.group')) as \"group\", "
            + "coalesce(cast(\"name\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.name')) as \"name\", "
            + "coalesce(cast(\"instance\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.instance')) as \"instance\", "
            + "coalesce(cast(\"state\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.state')) as \"state\", "
            + "coalesce(cast(\"host\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.host')) as \"host\", "
            + "coalesce(cast(\"session_id\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.sessionId')) as \"session_id\", "
            + "coalesce(cast(\"runtime_type\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.runtimeType')) as \"runtime_type\", "
            + "coalesce(cast(\"session_key\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.sessionKey')) as \"session_key\", "
            + "coalesce(cast(\"last_heartbeat_epoch_ms\" as bigint), try_cast(json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.lastHeartbeatEpochMs') as bigint)) as \"heartbeat_epoch_ms\", "
            + "cast(payload_json as varchar) as \"payload\" "
            + "from ${DATASET} "
            + "where lower(coalesce(cast(\"session_id\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.sessionId'), '')) = '"
            + escapeSqlLiteral(normalizedSession.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))
            + "' "
            + "order by coalesce(cast(\"last_heartbeat_epoch_ms\" as bigint), try_cast(json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.lastHeartbeatEpochMs') as bigint), 0) desc "
            + "limit 1";

    RowResult result = directQuery(statusApp, sql);
    if (result.rows() == null || result.rows().isEmpty()) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }

    Map<String, Integer> index = columnIndex(result.columns());
    List<Object> values = result.rows().getFirst();
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> summary = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    summary.put("group", valueAt(values, index, "group"));
    summary.put("name", valueAt(values, index, "name"));
    summary.put("instance", valueAt(values, index, "instance"));
    summary.put("state", valueAt(values, index, "state"));
    summary.put("host", valueAt(values, index, "host"));
    summary.put("sessionId", valueAt(values, index, "session_id"));
    summary.put("runtimeType", valueAt(values, index, "runtime_type"));
    summary.put("sessionKey", valueAt(values, index, "session_key"));
    summary.put(
        "heartbeatUtc", formatInstant(parseEpoch(valueAt(values, index, "heartbeat_epoch_ms")).orElse(null)));

    String payload = valueAt(values, index, "payload");
    Object payloadJson = parsePayload(payload).orElse(payload);
    String prefix = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(titlePrefix), "Status");
    return Optional.of(
        new StitchAuditDetailsModel(
            prefix + " Session Details",
            "Session " + normalizedSession,
            summary,
            payloadJson));
  }

  protected static String rewriteDatasetToken(String sql, DatasetId datasetId) {
    String normalizedSql = Strings.requireNonBlank(sql, "sql");
    if (!normalizedSql.contains("${DATASET}")) {
      return normalizedSql;
    }
    String token = quote(datasetId.namespace()) + "." + quote(datasetId.name());
    return normalizedSql.replace("${DATASET}", token);
  }

  protected static String quote(String identifier) {
    return "\"" + identifier.replace("\"", "\"\"") + "\"";
  }

  protected static String escapeSqlLiteral(String value) {
    return value == null ? "" : value.replace("'", "''");
  }

  protected static void addExactPredicate(
      List<String> predicates, String expression, String expectedValue, String allValue) {
    String expected = Strings.trimToNull(expectedValue);
    if (expected == null) {
      return;
    }
    if (allValue != null && allValue.equalsIgnoreCase(expected)) {
      return;
    }
    predicates.add(
        "lower(coalesce(" + expression + ", '')) = '" + escapeSqlLiteral(expected.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)) + "'");
  }

  protected static void addIsoInstantRangePredicates(
      List<String> predicates, String expression, Instant from, Instant to) {
    if (from != null) {
      predicates.add("coalesce(" + expression + ", '') >= '" + escapeSqlLiteral(from.toString()) + "'");
    }
    if (to != null) {
      predicates.add("coalesce(" + expression + ", '') <= '" + escapeSqlLiteral(to.toString()) + "'");
    }
  }

  protected static void addEpochRangePredicates(
      List<String> predicates, String expression, Instant from, Instant to) {
    if (from != null) {
      predicates.add("coalesce(" + expression + ", 0) >= " + from.toEpochMilli());
    }
    if (to != null) {
      predicates.add("coalesce(" + expression + ", 0) <= " + to.toEpochMilli());
    }
  }

  protected static void addContainsAnyPredicate(
      List<String> predicates, String search, String... expressions) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(search);
    if (normalized == null || expressions == null || expressions.length == 0) {
      return;
    }
    String token = escapeSqlLiteral(normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
    List<String> clauses = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String expression : expressions) {
      String field = Strings.trimToNull(expression);
      if (field == null) {
        continue;
      }
      clauses.add("lower(coalesce(" + field + ", '')) like '%" + token + "%'");
    }
    if (!clauses.isEmpty()) {
      predicates.add("(" + String.join(" or ", clauses) + ")");
    }
  }

  protected static LinkedHashMap<String, List<String>> filterOptions(
      List<StitchAuditRow> rows, String... keys) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, List<String>> options = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (keys == null || keys.length == 0) {
      return options;
    }
    for (String key : keys) {
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(key);
      if (normalized == null) {
        continue;
      }
      options.put(normalized, distinctValues(rows, normalized));
    }
    return options;
  }

  protected static List<String> distinctValues(List<StitchAuditRow> rows, String key) {
    if (rows == null || rows.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of(FILTER_ALL);
    }
    Set<String> values = new TreeSet<>(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    values.add(FILTER_ALL);
    for (StitchAuditRow row : rows) {
      if (row == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(row.text(key));
      if (value != null) {
        values.add(value);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(values);
  }

  protected static StitchAuditPage buildPage(
      List<StitchAuditRow> rows,
      StitchAuditFilterModel filter,
      int maxPageSize,
      Map<String, List<String>> filterOptions,
      String message) {
    List<StitchAuditRow> safeRows = rows == null ? List.of() : rows;
    StitchAuditFilterModel safeFilter = Objects.requireNonNull(filter, "filter");
    long totalRows = safeRows.size();
    int pageSize = Math.max(1, Math.min(safeFilter.pageSize(), Math.max(1, maxPageSize)));
    int requestedPage = Math.max(0, safeFilter.pageIndex());
    int maxPage = totalRows == 0 ? 0 : (int) ((totalRows - 1L) / pageSize);
    int pageIndex = Math.min(requestedPage, maxPage);
    int from = Math.max(0, pageIndex * pageSize);
    int to = Math.min(safeRows.size(), from + pageSize);
    List<StitchAuditRow> pageRows = from >= to ? List.of() : List.copyOf(safeRows.subList(from, to));
    return new StitchAuditPage(pageRows, totalRows, pageIndex, pageSize, filterOptions, message);
  }

  protected StitchAuditPage queryAdvancedSql(
      String sql, StitchAuditFilterModel contextFilter, AdvancedSqlContext context) {
    AdvancedSqlContext resolvedContext = Objects.requireNonNull(context, "context");
    StitchAuditFilterModel resolvedFilter = Objects.requireNonNull(contextFilter, "contextFilter");
    if (resolvedContext.datasetIds().isEmpty()) {
      return StitchAuditPage.empty(
          resolvedFilter.pageIndex(),
          resolvedFilter.pageSize(),
          Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(resolvedContext.unavailableMessage()), "No audit dataset available."));
    }

    String normalizedSql = validateAndNormalizeAdvancedSql(sql);
    String expanded = expandAuditToken(normalizedSql, resolvedContext.baseSql());
    int pageSize = Math.max(1, Math.min(resolvedFilter.pageSize(), MAX_PAGE_SIZE));
    int pageIndex = Math.max(0, resolvedFilter.pageIndex());
    int offset = pageIndex * pageSize;

    RowResult fullResult = directQuery(resolvedContext.datasetIds(), expanded);
    List<StitchAuditRow> allRows = mapAdvancedSqlRows(fullResult, resolvedContext, 0);
    long totalRows = allRows.size();
    int from = Math.min(offset, allRows.size());
    int to = Math.min(allRows.size(), from + pageSize);
    List<StitchAuditRow> rows = from >= to ? List.of() : List.copyOf(allRows.subList(from, to));
    return new StitchAuditPage(
        rows,
        totalRows,
        pageIndex,
        pageSize,
        Map.of(),
        Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(resolvedContext.unavailableMessage()), ""));
  }

  protected StitchAuditPage queryAdvancedSqlFromSources(
      String sql,
      StitchAuditFilterModel contextFilter,
      List<AdvancedSqlSource> sources,
      String eventTimeColumn,
      String payloadColumn,
      String sessionIdColumn,
      String idColumn,
      String unavailableMessage) {
    List<AdvancedSqlSource> safeSources = sources == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(sources);
    List<DatasetId> datasetIds = new ArrayList<>(safeSources.size());
    List<String> sourceSql = new ArrayList<>(safeSources.size());
    for (AdvancedSqlSource source : safeSources) {
      if (source == null || source.datasetId() == null || Strings.trimToNull(source.sql()) == null) {
        continue;
      }
      datasetIds.add(source.datasetId());
      sourceSql.add(source.sql());
    }
    return queryAdvancedSql(
        sql,
        contextFilter,
        new AdvancedSqlContext(
            datasetIds,
            String.join(" union all ", sourceSql),
            eventTimeColumn,
            payloadColumn,
            sessionIdColumn,
            idColumn,
            unavailableMessage));
  }

  protected static String validateAndNormalizeAdvancedSql(String sql) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(sql);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Enter a SQL SELECT statement.");
    }
    if (normalized.endsWith(";")) {
      normalized = Strings.trimToNull(normalized.substring(0, normalized.length() - 1));
    }
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Enter a SQL SELECT statement.");
    }

    String lower = normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    if (!(lower.startsWith("select") || lower.startsWith("with"))) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Advanced SQL is read-only. Use SELECT statements only.");
    }
    if (normalized.contains(";")) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Only a single read-only SQL statement is allowed.");
    }
    if (!lower.contains("${audit}")) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("SQL must reference ${AUDIT} as the feed source.");
    }
    for (String token : SQL_BLOCKED_TOKENS) {
      if (lower.matches("(?s).*\\b" + Pattern.quote(token) + "\\b.*")) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Advanced SQL is read-only. Statement contains blocked keyword: " + token);
      }
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  protected static String expandAuditToken(String sql, String baseSql) {
    String resolvedSql = Strings.requireNonBlank(sql, "sql");
    String resolvedBase = Strings.requireNonBlank(baseSql, "baseSql");
    Matcher matcher = AUDIT_TOKEN_PATTERN.matcher(resolvedSql);
    if (!matcher.find()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("SQL must reference ${AUDIT} as the feed source.");
    }
    return matcher.replaceAll(Matcher.quoteReplacement("(" + resolvedBase + ")"));
  }

  private static List<StitchAuditRow> mapAdvancedSqlRows(
      RowResult result, AdvancedSqlContext context, int offset) {
    if (result == null || result.rows() == null || result.rows().isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> columns = result.columns() == null ? List.of() : result.columns();
    Map<String, Integer> index = columnIndex(columns);
    List<StitchAuditRow> rows = new ArrayList<>(result.rows().size());
    int ordinal = 0;
    for (List<Object> values : result.rows()) {
      LinkedHashMap<String, Object> mapped = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      for (int i = 0; i < columns.size() && i < values.size(); i++) {
        String key = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(columns.get(i)), "column" + i);
        mapped.put(key, values.get(i));
      }
      String eventTimeRaw = valueAt(values, index, context.eventTimeColumn());
      String payload = valueAt(values, index, context.payloadColumn());
      String sessionId = valueAt(values, index, context.sessionIdColumn());
      String baseId =
          Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(valueAt(values, index, context.idColumn())), String.valueOf(offset + ordinal));
      rows.add(
          new StitchAuditRow(
              "sql/" + baseId + "/" + ordinal,
              parseEpoch(eventTimeRaw).orElse(null),
              payload,
              sessionId,
              mapped,
              Map.of("mode", "advanced-sql")));
      ordinal++;
    }
    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  protected record AdvancedSqlContext(
      List<DatasetId> datasetIds,
      String baseSql,
      String eventTimeColumn,
      String payloadColumn,
      String sessionIdColumn,
      String idColumn,
      String unavailableMessage) {

    public AdvancedSqlContext {
      datasetIds = datasetIds == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(datasetIds);
      baseSql = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(baseSql), "select 1 where 1=0");
      eventTimeColumn = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(eventTimeColumn), "eventTime");
      payloadColumn = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(payloadColumn), "payload");
      sessionIdColumn = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(sessionIdColumn), "sessionId");
      idColumn = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(idColumn), "id");
      unavailableMessage = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(unavailableMessage), "");
    }
  }

  protected record AdvancedSqlSource(DatasetId datasetId, String sql) {
    public AdvancedSqlSource {
      sql = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(sql), "");
    }
  }

  protected static Map<String, Integer> columnIndex(List<String> columns) {
    if (columns == null || columns.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, Integer> index = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (int i = 0; i < columns.size(); i++) {
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(columns.get(i));
      if (key != null) {
        index.putIfAbsent(key.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT), i);
      }
    }
    return Map.copyOf(index);
  }

  protected static String valueAt(List<Object> values, Map<String, Integer> index, String column) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty() || index == null || index.isEmpty()) {
      return "";
    }
    Integer position = index.get(column.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
    if (position == null || position < 0 || position >= values.size()) {
      return "";
    }
    Object value = values.get(position);
    return value == null ? "" : String.valueOf(value);
  }

  protected static Optional<Instant> parseEpoch(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    try {
      return Optional.of(Instant.ofEpochMilli(Long.parseLong(normalized)));
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      try {
        return Optional.of(Instant.parse(normalized));
      } catch (Exception nested) {
        return Optional.empty();
      }
    }
  }

  protected static Optional<Object> parsePayload(String payload) {
    String raw = Strings.trimToNull(payload);
    if (raw == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    try {
      return Optional.of(MAPPER.readValue(raw, Object.class));
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return Optional.of(raw);
    }
  }

  protected static String normalize(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  protected static String formatInstant(Instant instant) {
    if (instant == null) {
      return "";
    }
    LocalDateTime utc = LocalDateTime.ofInstant(instant, ZoneOffset.UTC);
    return utc.toString() + " UTC";
  }

  protected static boolean isDatasetMissingError(Throwable error) {
    if (error == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String message = Strings.trimToNull(error.getMessage());
    if (message != null) {
      String lower = message.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
      if (lower.contains("unknown table token")) {
        return true;
      }
      if (lower.contains("table with name") && lower.contains("does not exist")) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return isDatasetMissingError(error.getCause());
  }

  private static <T> T runAsSubject(String subject, java.util.function.Supplier<T> callback) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(callback, "callback");
    String normalizedSubject = Strings.trimToNull(subject);
    if (normalizedSubject == null) {
      return callback.get();
    }
    UserPrincipal previous = UserContext.get().orElse(null);
    UserContext.set(new UserPrincipal(normalizedSubject, Map.of()));
    try {
      return callback.get();
    } finally {
      if (previous == null) {
        UserContext.clear();
      } else {
        UserContext.set(previous);
      }
    }
  }

  private record DatasetPresence(boolean present, long expiresAtMs) {}
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/audit/StitchAuditDiscoveryFeedAdapter.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.audit;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.RowResult;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetId;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

public class StitchAuditDiscoveryFeedAdapter extends StitchAuditDirectFeedSupport
    implements StitchAuditFeedAdapter {
  private static final List<StitchAuditColumn> COLUMNS =
      List.of(
          new StitchAuditColumn("updatedTime", "Updated", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TIMESTAMP),
          new StitchAuditColumn("group", "Group", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT),
          new StitchAuditColumn("type", "Type", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT),
          new StitchAuditColumn("name", "Name", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT),
          new StitchAuditColumn("uuid", "UUID", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT),
          new StitchAuditColumn("lifecycle", "Lifecycle", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.STATUS),
          new StitchAuditColumn("ampsCommand", "Command", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT));
  private static final List<StitchAuditFilterDefinition> QUICK_FILTERS =
      List.of(
          new StitchAuditFilterDefinition("type", "Type"),
          new StitchAuditFilterDefinition("lifecycle", "Lifecycle"),
          new StitchAuditFilterDefinition("ampsCommand", "Command"));
  private static final Map<String, String> DEFAULT_FEED_FILTERS =
      defaultQuickFilters("type", FILTER_ALL, "lifecycle", FILTER_ALL, "ampsCommand", FILTER_ALL);
  private static final StitchAuditFilterModel NO_FILTER =
      new StitchAuditFilterModel(null, null, null, null, Map.of(), 0, 25, null, false);

  public StitchAuditDiscoveryFeedAdapter(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    super(runtimeContext);
  }

  @Override
  public String feedId() {
    return StitchAuditFeature.DISCOVERY;
  }

  @Override
  public List<StitchAuditColumn> columns() {
    return COLUMNS;
  }

  @Override
  public List<StitchAuditFilterDefinition> filterDefinitions() {
    return QUICK_FILTERS;
  }

  @Override
  public Map<String, String> defaultFeedFilters() {
    return DEFAULT_FEED_FILTERS;
  }

  @Override
  public StitchAuditFilterModel defaultFilters(int defaultPageSize) {
    return new StitchAuditFilterModel(
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        defaultFeedFilters(),
        0,
        Math.max(1, defaultPageSize),
        "updated_time_utc",
        false);
  }

  @Override
  public StitchAuditPage queryAdvancedSql(String sql, StitchAuditFilterModel contextFilter) {
    StitchAuditFilterModel filter = Objects.requireNonNull(contextFilter, "contextFilter");
    DatasetId datasetId = datasetId(filter.group(), "discovery");
    if (!datasetExists(datasetId)) {
      return StitchAuditPage.empty(
          filter.pageIndex(), filter.pageSize(), datasetUnavailableMessage(datasetId));
    }
    return queryAdvancedSqlFromSources(
        sql,
        filter,
        List.of(
            new AdvancedSqlSource(
                datasetId, rewriteDatasetToken(discoverySql(NO_FILTER), datasetId))),
        "updated_time_utc",
        "payload",
        "session_id",
        "uuid",
        "");
  }

  @Override
  public StitchAuditPage query(StitchAuditFilterModel filter) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(filter, "filter");
    DatasetId datasetId = datasetId(filter.group(), "discovery");
    if (!datasetExists(datasetId)) {
      return StitchAuditPage.empty(filter.pageIndex(), filter.pageSize(), datasetUnavailableMessage(datasetId));
    }

    List<StitchAuditRow> rows = loadRows(datasetId, filter);
    rows.sort(comparator(filter));
    return buildPage(rows, filter, MAX_PAGE_SIZE, filterOptions(rows, "type", "lifecycle", "ampsCommand"), "");
  }

  @Override
  public StitchAuditDetailsModel details(StitchAuditRow row) {
    if (row == null) {
      return new StitchAuditDetailsModel("Discovery Audit Event", "", Map.of(), null);
    }

    LinkedHashMap<String, String> summary = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    summary.put("updatedTimeUtc", formatInstant(row.eventTimeUtc()));
    summary.put("group", row.text("group"));
    summary.put("type", row.text("type"));
    summary.put("name", row.text("name"));
    summary.put("uuid", row.text("uuid"));
    summary.put("sessionId", row.text("sessionId"));
    summary.put("enabled", row.text("enabled"));
    summary.put("lifecycle", row.text("lifecycle"));
    summary.put("createdTimeUtc", row.text("createdTime"));
    summary.put("ampsCommand", row.text("ampsCommand"));

    String subtitle =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            row.text("group") + " / " + row.text("type") + " / " + row.text("name"),
            row.text("group"),
            "Discovery event");

    return new StitchAuditDetailsModel(
        "Discovery Audit Event", subtitle, summary, parsePayload(row.payload()).orElse(row.payload()));
  }

  private List<StitchAuditRow> loadRows(DatasetId datasetId, StitchAuditFilterModel filter) {
    String sql = discoverySql(filter);
    RowResult result = directQuery(datasetId, sql);
    if (result.rows() == null || result.rows().isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }

    Map<String, Integer> index = columnIndex(result.columns());
    List<StitchAuditRow> rows = new ArrayList<>(result.rows().size());
    int ordinal = 0;
    for (List<Object> values : result.rows()) {
      String updated = valueAt(values, index, "updated_time_utc");
      Instant updatedTime = parseEpoch(updated).orElse(null);
      String group = valueAt(values, index, "group");
      String type = valueAt(values, index, "type");
      String name = valueAt(values, index, "name");
      String uuid = valueAt(values, index, "uuid");
      String sessionId = valueAt(values, index, "session_id");
      String enabled = valueAt(values, index, "enabled");
      String lifecycle = valueAt(values, index, "lifecycle_status");
      String created = valueAt(values, index, "created_time_utc");
      String command = valueAt(values, index, "amps_command");
      String payload = valueAt(values, index, "payload");

      LinkedHashMap<String, Object> mapped = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      mapped.put("updatedTime", updatedTime);
      mapped.put("group", group);
      mapped.put("type", type);
      mapped.put("name", name);
      mapped.put("uuid", uuid);
      mapped.put("sessionId", sessionId);
      mapped.put("enabled", enabled);
      mapped.put("lifecycle", lifecycle);
      mapped.put("createdTime", created);
      mapped.put("ampsCommand", command);

      String id =
          datasetId.group()
              + "/"
              + datasetId.name()
              + "/"
              + Strings.trimToEmpty(uuid)
              + "/"
              + Strings.trimToEmpty(updated)
              + "/"
              + ordinal++;
      rows.add(
          new StitchAuditRow(
              id, updatedTime, payload, sessionId, mapped, Map.of("dataset", datasetId.toString())));
    }
    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  private String discoverySql(StitchAuditFilterModel filter) {
    String groupExpr =
        "coalesce(cast(\"group\" as varchar), json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.group'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.group'))";
    String typeExpr =
        "coalesce(cast(\"type\" as varchar), json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.type'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.type'))";
    String nameExpr =
        "coalesce(cast(\"name\" as varchar), json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.name'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.name'))";
    String uuidExpr =
        "coalesce(cast(\"uuid\" as varchar), json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.uuid'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.uuid'))";
    String sessionExpr =
        "coalesce(cast(\"session_id\" as varchar), json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.sessionId'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.sessionId'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.envelope.sessionId'))";
    String enabledExpr =
        "coalesce(cast(\"enabled\" as varchar), json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.enabled'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.enabled'))";
    String lifecycleExpr =
        "coalesce(cast(\"lifecycle_status\" as varchar), json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.lifecycleStatus'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.lifecycleStatus'))";
    String createdExpr =
        "coalesce(cast(\"created_time_utc\" as varchar), json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.createdTimeUtc'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.createdTimeUtc'))";
    String updatedExpr =
        "coalesce(cast(\"updated_time_utc\" as varchar), json_extract_string(envelope_json, '$.updatedTimeUtc'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.updatedTimeUtc'))";
    String commandExpr =
        "case upper(coalesce(cast(\"operation\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.op'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.operation'), '')) when 'OOF' then 'DELETE' when 'SOW_DELETE' then 'DELETE' else upper(coalesce(cast(\"operation\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.op'), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.operation'), 'UPDATE')) end";
    String payloadExpr = "cast(payload_json as varchar)";

    StringBuilder sql = new StringBuilder("select ");
    sql.append(groupExpr).append(" as \"group\", ");
    sql.append(typeExpr).append(" as \"type\", ");
    sql.append(nameExpr).append(" as \"name\", ");
    sql.append(uuidExpr).append(" as \"uuid\", ");
    sql.append(sessionExpr).append(" as \"session_id\", ");
    sql.append(enabledExpr).append(" as \"enabled\", ");
    sql.append(lifecycleExpr).append(" as \"lifecycle_status\", ");
    sql.append(createdExpr).append(" as \"created_time_utc\", ");
    sql.append(updatedExpr).append(" as \"updated_time_utc\", ");
    sql.append(commandExpr).append(" as \"amps_command\", ");
    sql.append(payloadExpr).append(" as \"payload\" ");
    sql.append("from ${DATASET}");

    List<String> predicates = new ArrayList<>();
    addExactPredicate(predicates, groupExpr, filter.group(), FILTER_ALL);
    addExactPredicate(predicates, typeExpr, filter.filterValue("type"), FILTER_ALL);
    addExactPredicate(predicates, lifecycleExpr, filter.filterValue("lifecycle"), FILTER_ALL);
    addExactPredicate(predicates, commandExpr, filter.filterValue("ampsCommand"), FILTER_ALL);

    addIsoInstantRangePredicates(predicates, updatedExpr, filter.timeFromUtc(), filter.timeToUtc());
    addContainsAnyPredicate(predicates, filter.searchText(), nameExpr, uuidExpr, payloadExpr);

    if (!predicates.isEmpty()) {
      sql.append(" where ").append(String.join(" and ", predicates));
    }
    return sql.toString();
  }

  private Comparator<StitchAuditRow> comparator(StitchAuditFilterModel filter) {
    String sortBy = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(filter.sortBy()), "updated_time_utc");
    Comparator<StitchAuditRow> base;
    if ("group".equalsIgnoreCase(sortBy)) {
      base = Comparator.comparing(row -> normalize(row.text("group")));
    } else if ("type".equalsIgnoreCase(sortBy)) {
      base = Comparator.comparing(row -> normalize(row.text("type")));
    } else if ("lifecycle_status".equalsIgnoreCase(sortBy) || "lifecycle".equalsIgnoreCase(sortBy)) {
      base = Comparator.comparing(row -> normalize(row.text("lifecycle")));
    } else {
      base = Comparator.comparing(StitchAuditRow::eventTimeUtc, Comparator.nullsLast(Comparator.naturalOrder()));
    }
    Comparator<StitchAuditRow> comparator =
        base.thenComparing(row -> normalize(row.text("name"))).thenComparing(row -> normalize(row.text("uuid")));
    return filter.sortAscending() ? comparator : comparator.reversed();
  }
}

  @Override
  public StitchAuditDetailsModel details(StitchAuditRow row) {
    if (row == null) {
      return new StitchAuditDetailsModel("Entitlements Audit Event", "", Map.of(), null);
    }

    LinkedHashMap<String, String> summary = new LinkedHashMap<>();
