    summary.put("implementation", row.text("implementation"));
    summary.put("reason", row.text("reason"));

    String subtitle =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            row.text("decision") + " / " + row.text("action") + " / " + row.text("resource"),
            row.text("eventId"),
            "Entitlements event");

    return new StitchAuditDetailsModel("Entitlements Audit Event", subtitle, summary, null);
  }

  @Override
  public Optional<StitchAuditDetailsModel> sessionDetails(StitchAuditRow row) {
    if (row == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return lookupSessionDetails(row.text("sessionGroup"), row.sessionId(), "Entitlements");
  }

  private List<StitchAuditRow> loadRows(DatasetId datasetId, StitchAuditFilterModel filter) {
    String sql = entitlementsSql(filter);
    RowResult result = directQuery(datasetId, sql);
    if (result.rows() == null || result.rows().isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }

    Map<String, Integer> index = columnIndex(result.columns());
    List<StitchAuditRow> rows = new ArrayList<>(result.rows().size());
    int ordinal = 0;
    for (List<Object> values : result.rows()) {
      String eventId = valueAt(values, index, "event_id");
      String eventTime = valueAt(values, index, "event_time_utc");
      Instant eventInstant = parseEpoch(eventTime).orElse(null);
      String scopeType = valueAt(values, index, "scope_type");
      String action = valueAt(values, index, "action");
      String operation = valueAt(values, index, "operation");
      String resource = valueAt(values, index, "resource_id");
      String subject = valueAt(values, index, "subject");
      String delegatedSubject = valueAt(values, index, "delegated_subject");
      String decision = valueAt(values, index, "decision");
      String reason = valueAt(values, index, "reason");
      String sessionGroup = valueAt(values, index, "session_group");
      String sessionApp = valueAt(values, index, "session_app");
      String sessionInstance = valueAt(values, index, "session_instance");
      String sessionId = valueAt(values, index, "session_id");
      String transport = valueAt(values, index, "transport");
      String implementation = valueAt(values, index, "implementation");

      LinkedHashMap<String, Object> mapped = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      mapped.put("eventId", eventId);
      mapped.put("eventTime", eventInstant);
      mapped.put("scopeType", scopeType);
      mapped.put("action", action);
      mapped.put("operation", operation);
      mapped.put("resource", resource);
      mapped.put("subject", subject);
      mapped.put("delegatedSubject", delegatedSubject);
      mapped.put("decision", decision);
      mapped.put("reason", reason);
      mapped.put("sessionGroup", sessionGroup);
      mapped.put("sessionApp", sessionApp);
      mapped.put("sessionInstance", sessionInstance);
      mapped.put("sessionId", sessionId);
      mapped.put("transport", transport);
      mapped.put("implementation", implementation);

      String id =
          datasetId.group()
              + "/"
              + datasetId.name()
              + "/"
              + Strings.trimToEmpty(eventId)
              + "/"
              + Strings.trimToEmpty(eventTime)
              + "/"
              + ordinal++;
      rows.add(new StitchAuditRow(id, eventInstant, "", sessionId, mapped, Map.of("dataset", datasetId.toString())));
    }
    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  private String entitlementsSql(StitchAuditFilterModel filter) {
    String eventIdExpr = "cast(\"eventId\" as varchar)";
    String eventTimeExpr = "cast(\"eventTimeUtc\" as varchar)";
    String scopeExpr = "cast(\"scopeType\" as varchar)";
    String actionExpr = "cast(\"action\" as varchar)";
    String operationExpr = "cast(\"operation\" as varchar)";
    String resourceExpr = "cast(\"resourceId\" as varchar)";
    String subjectExpr = "cast(\"subject\" as varchar)";
    String delegatedExpr = "cast(\"delegatedSubject\" as varchar)";
    String decisionExpr = "case when coalesce(cast(\"allowed\" as boolean), false) then 'ALLOW' else 'DENY' end";
    String reasonExpr = "cast(\"reason\" as varchar)";
    String sessionGroupExpr = "cast(\"sessionGroup\" as varchar)";
    String sessionAppExpr = "cast(\"sessionApp\" as varchar)";
    String sessionInstanceExpr = "cast(\"sessionInstance\" as varchar)";
    String sessionIdExpr = "cast(\"sessionId\" as varchar)";
    String transportExpr = "cast(\"transport\" as varchar)";
    String implementationExpr = "cast(\"implementation\" as varchar)";

    StringBuilder sql = new StringBuilder("select ");
    sql.append(eventIdExpr).append(" as \"event_id\", ");
    sql.append(eventTimeExpr).append(" as \"event_time_utc\", ");
    sql.append(scopeExpr).append(" as \"scope_type\", ");
    sql.append(actionExpr).append(" as \"action\", ");
    sql.append(operationExpr).append(" as \"operation\", ");
    sql.append(resourceExpr).append(" as \"resource_id\", ");
    sql.append(subjectExpr).append(" as \"subject\", ");
    sql.append(delegatedExpr).append(" as \"delegated_subject\", ");
    sql.append(decisionExpr).append(" as \"decision\", ");
    sql.append(reasonExpr).append(" as \"reason\", ");
    sql.append(sessionGroupExpr).append(" as \"session_group\", ");
    sql.append(sessionAppExpr).append(" as \"session_app\", ");
    sql.append(sessionInstanceExpr).append(" as \"session_instance\", ");
    sql.append(sessionIdExpr).append(" as \"session_id\", ");
    sql.append(transportExpr).append(" as \"transport\", ");
    sql.append(implementationExpr).append(" as \"implementation\" ");
    sql.append("from ${DATASET}");

    List<String> predicates = new ArrayList<>();
    addExactPredicate(predicates, sessionGroupExpr, filter.group(), FILTER_ALL);
    addExactPredicate(predicates, scopeExpr, filter.filterValue("scopeType"), FILTER_ALL);
    addExactPredicate(predicates, actionExpr, filter.filterValue("action"), FILTER_ALL);
    addExactPredicate(predicates, decisionExpr, filter.filterValue("decision"), FILTER_ALL);

    addIsoInstantRangePredicates(predicates, eventTimeExpr, filter.timeFromUtc(), filter.timeToUtc());
    addContainsAnyPredicate(
        predicates,
        filter.searchText(),
        subjectExpr,
        delegatedExpr,
        resourceExpr,
        operationExpr,
        reasonExpr,
        sessionAppExpr,
        eventIdExpr);

    if (!predicates.isEmpty()) {
      sql.append(" where ").append(String.join(" and ", predicates));
    }
    return sql.toString();
  }

  private Comparator<StitchAuditRow> comparator(StitchAuditFilterModel filter) {
    String sortBy = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(filter.sortBy()), "eventTimeUtc");
    Comparator<StitchAuditRow> base;
    if ("decision".equalsIgnoreCase(sortBy)) {
      base = Comparator.comparing(row -> normalize(row.text("decision")));
    } else if ("action".equalsIgnoreCase(sortBy)) {
      base = Comparator.comparing(row -> normalize(row.text("action")));
    } else if ("scopeType".equalsIgnoreCase(sortBy) || "scope_type".equalsIgnoreCase(sortBy)) {
      base = Comparator.comparing(row -> normalize(row.text("scopeType")));
    } else {
      base = Comparator.comparing(StitchAuditRow::eventTimeUtc, Comparator.nullsLast(Comparator.naturalOrder()));
    }
    Comparator<StitchAuditRow> comparator =
        base.thenComparing(row -> normalize(row.text("eventId"))).thenComparing(row -> normalize(row.text("subject")));
    return filter.sortAscending() ? comparator : comparator.reversed();
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.audit;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.StitchFeatureSet;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu.StitchMenuEntry;

public final class StitchAuditFeature implements StitchFeatureSet {
  public static final String FEATURE_ID = "audit";
  public static final String STATUS = "status";
  public static final String CONFIGS = "configs";
  public static final String DISCOVERY = "discovery";
  public static final String ENTITLEMENTS = "entitlements";
  public static final String ENTRY_STATUS = "admin.audit.status";
  public static final String ENTRY_CONFIGS = "admin.audit.configs";
  public static final String ENTRY_DISCOVERY = "admin.audit.discovery";
  public static final String ENTRY_ENTITLEMENTS = "admin.audit.entitlements";

  private final String menuLabel;
  private final String auditLabel;
  private final int order;
  private final StitchAuditScreenConfig status;
  private final StitchAuditScreenConfig configs;
  private final StitchAuditScreenConfig discovery;
  private final StitchAuditScreenConfig entitlements;

  private StitchAuditFeature(Builder builder) {
    this.menuLabel = require(builder.menuLabel, "menuLabel");
    this.auditLabel = require(builder.auditLabel, "auditLabel");
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.status = builder.statusBuilder.build();
    this.configs = builder.configsBuilder.build();
    this.discovery = builder.discoveryBuilder.build();
    this.entitlements = builder.entitlementsBuilder.build();
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  @Override
  public String id() {
    return FEATURE_ID;
  }

  @Override
  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public StitchAuditScreenConfig status() {
    return status;
  }

  public StitchAuditScreenConfig configs() {
    return configs;
  }

  public StitchAuditScreenConfig discovery() {
    return discovery;
  }

  public StitchAuditScreenConfig entitlements() {
    return entitlements;
  }

  public Optional<StitchAuditScreenConfig> screen(String screenId) {
    if (screenId == null || screenId.isBlank()) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return switch (screenId.trim().toLowerCase(java.util.Locale.ROOT)) {
      case STATUS -> Optional.of(status);
      case CONFIGS -> Optional.of(configs);
      case DISCOVERY -> Optional.of(discovery);
      case ENTITLEMENTS -> Optional.of(entitlements);
      default -> Optional.empty();
    };
  }

  @Override
  public List<StitchMenuEntry> menuEntries() {
    List<StitchMenuEntry> entries = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
    addEntry(entries, status, ENTRY_STATUS);
    addEntry(entries, configs, ENTRY_CONFIGS);
    addEntry(entries, discovery, ENTRY_DISCOVERY);
    addEntry(entries, entitlements, ENTRY_ENTITLEMENTS);
    return List.copyOf(entries);
  }

  private static void addEntry(
      List<StitchMenuEntry> entries, StitchAuditScreenConfig config, String entryId) {
    if (config == null || !config.enabled()) {
      return;
    }
    entries.add(
        StitchMenuEntry.builder(entryId)
            .withLabel(config.label())
            .withRoutePath(config.routePath())
            .withOrder(config.order())
            .build());
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String menuLabel = "Admin";
    private String auditLabel = "Audit";
    private int order = 30;
    private final StitchAuditScreenConfig.Builder statusBuilder =
        StitchAuditScreenConfig.builder(STATUS);
    private final StitchAuditScreenConfig.Builder configsBuilder =
        StitchAuditScreenConfig.builder(CONFIGS)
            .withLabel("Configs")
            .withRoutePath("admin/audit/configs")
            .withPageTitle("Admin - Audit - Configs")
            .withPageSubtitle("Browse archived configs audit events.")
            .withOrder(20);
    private final StitchAuditScreenConfig.Builder discoveryBuilder =
        StitchAuditScreenConfig.builder(DISCOVERY)
            .withLabel("Discovery")
            .withRoutePath("admin/audit/discovery")
            .withPageTitle("Admin - Audit - Discovery")
            .withPageSubtitle("Browse archived discovery audit events.")
            .withOrder(30);
    private final StitchAuditScreenConfig.Builder entitlementsBuilder =
        StitchAuditScreenConfig.builder(ENTITLEMENTS)
            .withLabel("Entitlements")
            .withRoutePath("admin/audit/entitlements")
            .withPageTitle("Admin - Audit - Entitlements")
            .withPageSubtitle("Browse archived entitlements audit events.")
            .withOrder(40);

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withMenuLabel(String value) {
      this.menuLabel = require(value, "menuLabel");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withAuditLabel(String value) {
      this.auditLabel = require(value, "auditLabel");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder status(Consumer<StitchAuditScreenConfig.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(statusBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder configs(Consumer<StitchAuditScreenConfig.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(configsBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder discovery(Consumer<StitchAuditScreenConfig.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(discoveryBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder entitlements(Consumer<StitchAuditScreenConfig.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(entitlementsBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public StitchAuditFeature build() {
      return new StitchAuditFeature(this);
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/audit/StitchAuditFeedAdapter.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.audit;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public interface StitchAuditFeedAdapter {
  String feedId();

  List<StitchAuditColumn> columns();

  List<StitchAuditFilterDefinition> filterDefinitions();

  StitchAuditFilterModel defaultFilters(int defaultPageSize);

  StitchAuditPage query(StitchAuditFilterModel filter);

  default boolean supportsAdvancedSql() {
    return false;
  }

  default String advancedSqlTemplate() {
    return "select * from ${AUDIT} limit 100";
  }

  default String advancedSqlHelpText() {
    return "Advanced SQL is read-only. Use SELECT statements only and reference ${AUDIT}.";
  }

  default StitchAuditPage queryAdvancedSql(String sql, StitchAuditFilterModel contextFilter) {
    throw new IllegalArgumentException("Advanced SQL mode is not supported for feed: " + feedId());
  }

  StitchAuditDetailsModel details(StitchAuditRow row);

  default Optional<StitchAuditDetailsModel> sessionDetails(StitchAuditRow row) {
    return Optional.empty();
  }

  default Optional<Object> payloadJson(StitchAuditRow row) {
    if (row == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    String payload = row.payload();
    if (payload == null || payload.isBlank()) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return Optional.of(payload);
  }

  default Optional<StitchAuditRelatedContext> relatedSessionContext(StitchAuditRow row) {
    if (row == null || Strings.isBlank(row.sessionId())) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    String group =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(row.text("group")), Strings.trimToNull(row.text("sessionGroup")));
    return Optional.of(StitchAuditRelatedContext.relatedSession(group, row.sessionId()));
  }

  default Map<String, String> defaultFeedFilters() {
    return Map.of();
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/audit/StitchAuditFilterBar.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.audit;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.ComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.datetimepicker.DateTimePicker;
import java.time.Duration;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.time.LocalDateTime;
import java.time.ZoneOffset;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchGroupFilter;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchResultsSearch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchResultsToolbar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

public class StitchAuditFilterBar {
  private static final String FILTER_ALL = "All";
  private static final List<String> TOP_BAR_FILTER_PRIORITY = List.of("type", "state");

  private final StitchGroupFilter groupFilter;
  private final DateTimePicker timeFromUtc = new DateTimePicker();
  private final DateTimePicker timeToUtc = new DateTimePicker();
  private final StitchResultsSearch search =
      new StitchResultsSearch("Contains text...", "Search audit rows");
  private final Button apply = new Button("APPLY");
  private final Button clear = new Button("CLEAR");
  private final LinkedHashMap<String, ComboBox<String>> quickFilters = new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private final LinkedHashMap<String, String> quickFilterLabels = new LinkedHashMap<>();

  public StitchAuditFilterBar(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    this.groupFilter = new StitchGroupFilter(Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext"));
    this.groupFilter.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Filter audit rows by group");
    this.groupFilter.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Audit group filter");

    timeFromUtc.setStep(Duration.ofMinutes(1));
    timeFromUtc.getElement().setProperty("placeholder", "From UTC");
    timeFromUtc.setAriaLabel("From UTC time");
    timeFromUtc.getElement().setAttribute(
        "title", "Start of UTC time range used to filter audit rows");
    timeFromUtc.setWidth("10.75rem");
    timeFromUtc.addClassName("stitch-audit-time-field");

    timeToUtc.setStep(Duration.ofMinutes(1));
    timeToUtc.getElement().setProperty("placeholder", "To UTC");
    timeToUtc.setAriaLabel("To UTC time");
    timeToUtc.getElement().setAttribute(
        "title", "End of UTC time range used to filter audit rows");
    timeToUtc.setWidth("10.75rem");
    timeToUtc.addClassName("stitch-audit-time-field");

    resetTimeRangeDefaults();
    search.getElement().setAttribute(
        "title", "Search audit rows by matching text in key fields");
    search.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Audit text search filter");

    StitchResultsToolbar.stylePrimaryAction(apply);
    StitchResultsToolbar.styleSecondaryAction(clear);
    apply.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Apply audit filters");
    apply.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Apply audit filters");
    clear.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Clear audit filters");
    clear.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Clear audit filters");
  }

  public StitchGroupFilter groupFilter() {
    return groupFilter;
  }

  public DateTimePicker timeFromUtc() {
    return timeFromUtc;
  }

  public DateTimePicker timeToUtc() {
    return timeToUtc;
  }

  public StitchResultsSearch search() {
    return search;
  }

  public Button applyButton() {
    return apply;
  }

  public Button clearButton() {
    return clear;
  }

  public List<Map.Entry<String, ComboBox<String>>> quickFilterComponents() {
    return List.copyOf(quickFilters.entrySet());
  }

  public List<Map.Entry<String, ComboBox<String>>> topBarQuickFilterComponents() {
    List<Map.Entry<String, ComboBox<String>>> ordered = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String key : TOP_BAR_FILTER_PRIORITY) {
      ComboBox<String> combo = quickFilters.get(key);
      if (combo != null) {
        ordered.add(Map.entry(key, combo));
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(ordered);
  }

  public List<Map.Entry<String, ComboBox<String>>> advancedQuickFilterComponents() {
    if (quickFilters.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<Map.Entry<String, ComboBox<String>>> advanced = new ArrayList<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, ComboBox<String>> entry : quickFilters.entrySet()) {
      if (!TOP_BAR_FILTER_PRIORITY.contains(entry.getKey())) {
        advanced.add(entry);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(advanced);
  }

  public String quickFilterLabel(String key) {
    return quickFilterLabels.getOrDefault(key, key == null ? "" : key);
  }

  public void configureQuickFilters(List<StitchAuditFilterDefinition> definitions) {
    quickFilters.clear();
    quickFilterLabels.clear();
    if (definitions == null || definitions.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    for (StitchAuditFilterDefinition definition : definitions) {
      if (definition == null || definition.key().isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      ComboBox<String> combo = new ComboBox<>();
      combo.setWidth("10rem");
      combo.setAllowCustomValue(false);
      combo.setClearButtonVisible(false);
      combo.setItems(FILTER_ALL);
      combo.setValue(FILTER_ALL);
      combo.addClassName("stitch-audit-quick-filter");
      List<String> initialOptions = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
      initialOptions.add(FILTER_ALL);
      initialOptions.addAll(definition.options());
      combo.setItems(initialOptions);
      combo.setAriaLabel(definition.label().isBlank() ? definition.key() : definition.label());
      combo.getElement().setAttribute("title", Strings.firstNonBlank(definition.tooltip(), "Filter values"));
      quickFilters.put(definition.key(), combo);
      quickFilterLabels.put(definition.key(), definition.label());
    }
  }

  public void applyQuickFilterOptions(Map<String, List<String>> options) {
    if (quickFilters.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    for (Map.Entry<String, ComboBox<String>> entry : quickFilters.entrySet()) {
      String key = entry.getKey();
      ComboBox<String> combo = entry.getValue();
      String current = Strings.trimToNull(combo.getValue());
      List<String> values = options == null ? null : options.get(key);
      java.util.LinkedHashSet<String> normalized = new java.util.LinkedHashSet<>();
      normalized.add(FILTER_ALL);
      if (values != null) {
        for (String value : values) {
          String token = Strings.trimToNull(value);
          if (token != null) {
            normalized.add(token);
          }
        }
      }
      List<String> ordered = new java.util.ArrayList<>(normalized);
      ordered.sort((left, right) -> {
        if (FILTER_ALL.equalsIgnoreCase(left)) {
          return -1;
        }
        if (FILTER_ALL.equalsIgnoreCase(right)) {
          return 1;
        }
        return left.compareToIgnoreCase(right);
      });
      combo.setItems(ordered);
      String next = current != null && ordered.stream().anyMatch(current::equalsIgnoreCase) ? current : FILTER_ALL;
      combo.setValue(next);
    }
  }

  public void clearValues(Map<String, String> defaultFeedFilters) {
    groupFilter.refresh();
    resetTimeRangeDefaults();
    search.clear();

    for (Map.Entry<String, ComboBox<String>> entry : quickFilters.entrySet()) {
      String key = entry.getKey();
      ComboBox<String> combo = entry.getValue();
      String preferred =
          defaultFeedFilters == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(defaultFeedFilters.get(key));
      if (preferred != null) {
        List<String> items = combo.getListDataView().getItems().toList();
        String matched =
            items.stream().filter(value -> preferred.equalsIgnoreCase(value)).findFirst().orElse(FILTER_ALL);
        combo.setValue(matched);
      } else {
        combo.setValue(FILTER_ALL);
      }
    }
  }

  public void setSelectedGroup(String groupKey) {
    List<StitchGroupFilter.Option> options = groupFilter.getListDataView().getItems().toList();
    if (options.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    String requested = Strings.trimToNull(groupKey);
    if (requested == null) {
      groupFilter.setValue(options.getFirst());
      return;
    }
    StitchGroupFilter.Option matched =
        options.stream()
            .filter(option -> option != null && requested.equalsIgnoreCase(Strings.trimToEmpty(option.key())))
            .findFirst()
            .orElse(options.getFirst());
    groupFilter.setValue(matched);
  }

  public void setSearchText(String value) {
    search.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(value));
  }

  public void shiftTimeRangeDays(int days) {
    if (days == 0) {
      return;
    }
    LocalDateTime from = timeFromUtc.getValue();
    LocalDateTime to = timeToUtc.getValue();
    if (from == null || to == null) {
      resetTimeRangeDefaults();
      from = timeFromUtc.getValue();
      to = timeToUtc.getValue();
    }
    if (from != null) {
      timeFromUtc.setValue(from.plusDays(days));
    }
    if (to != null) {
      timeToUtc.setValue(to.plusDays(days));
    }
  }

  public StitchAuditFilterModel toFilterModel(
      int pageIndex,
      int pageSize,
      String sortBy,
      boolean sortAscending,
      Map<String, String> defaultFeedFilters) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> feedValues = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (defaultFeedFilters != null) {
      feedValues.putAll(defaultFeedFilters);
    }
    for (Map.Entry<String, ComboBox<String>> entry : quickFilters.entrySet()) {
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue().getValue());
      feedValues.put(entry.getKey(), value == null ? FILTER_ALL : value);
    }

    Instant fromUtc = toInstant(timeFromUtc.getValue());
    Instant toUtc = toInstant(timeToUtc.getValue());
    if (fromUtc != null && toUtc != null && fromUtc.isAfter(toUtc)) {
      Instant swap = fromUtc;
      fromUtc = toUtc;
      toUtc = swap;
    }

    return new StitchAuditFilterModel(
        selectedGroup(),
        fromUtc,
        toUtc,
        normalizedSearch(),
        feedValues,
        pageIndex,
        pageSize,
        sortBy,
        sortAscending);
  }

  private String selectedGroup() {
    StitchGroupFilter.Option option = groupFilter.getValue();
    if (option == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String key = Strings.trimToNull(option.key());
    if (key == null || "__all__".equalsIgnoreCase(key)) {
      return null;
    }
    return key;
  }

  private String normalizedSearch() {
    String query = Strings.trimToNull(search.normalizedQuery());
    return query == null ? null : query.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static Instant toInstant(LocalDateTime value) {
    return value == null ? null : value.toInstant(ZoneOffset.UTC);
  }

  private void resetTimeRangeDefaults() {
    timeFromUtc.clear();
    timeToUtc.clear();
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/audit/StitchAuditFilterDefinition.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.audit;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public record StitchAuditFilterDefinition(String key, String label, String tooltip, List<String> options) {
  public StitchAuditFilterDefinition(String key, String label) {
    this(key, label, null, List.of());
  }

  public StitchAuditFilterDefinition(String key, String label, String tooltip) {
    this(key, label, tooltip, List.of());
  }

  public StitchAuditFilterDefinition {
    key = Strings.trimToEmpty(key);
    label = Strings.trimToEmpty(label);
    tooltip = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(tooltip), defaultTooltip(label, key));
    options = normalizeOptions(options);
  }

  private static String defaultTooltip(String label, String key) {
    String resolved = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(label), Strings.trimToNull(key), "Filter");
    return "Filter by " + resolved;
  }

  private static List<String> normalizeOptions(List<String> options) {
    if (options == null || options.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> distinct = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String value : options) {
      String token = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      if (token != null) {
        distinct.add(token);
      }
    }
    return distinct.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(new ArrayList<>(distinct));
  }
}

import java.time.Instant;

public record StitchAuditFilterModel(
    String group,
    Instant timeFromUtc,
    Instant timeToUtc,
    String searchText,
    Map<String, String> feedFilters,
    int pageIndex,
    int pageSize,
    String sortBy,
    boolean sortAscending) {

  public StitchAuditFilterModel {
    feedFilters =
        feedFilters == null || feedFilters.isEmpty()
            ? Map.of()
            : Map.copyOf(new LinkedHashMap<>(feedFilters));
    pageIndex = Math.max(0, pageIndex);
    pageSize = Math.max(1, pageSize);
  }

  public StitchAuditFilterModel withPageIndex(int value) {
    return new StitchAuditFilterModel(
        group,
        timeFromUtc,
        timeToUtc,
        searchText,
        feedFilters,
        Math.max(0, value),
        pageSize,
        sortBy,
        sortAscending);
  }

  public StitchAuditFilterModel withPageSize(int value) {
    return new StitchAuditFilterModel(
        group,
        timeFromUtc,
        timeToUtc,
        searchText,
        feedFilters,
        0,
        Math.max(1, value),
        sortBy,
        sortAscending);
  }

  public String filterValue(String key) {
    if (key == null || key.isBlank() || feedFilters.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    return feedFilters.get(key);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/audit/StitchAuditProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.audit;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;

public class StitchAuditProvider {
  private final Map<String, StitchAuditFeedAdapter> adapters;

  public StitchAuditProvider(List<StitchAuditFeedAdapter> adapters) {
    List<StitchAuditFeedAdapter> safe = List.copyOf(Objects.requireNonNull(adapters, "adapters"));
    if (safe.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("At least one audit feed adapter is required");
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, StitchAuditFeedAdapter> indexed = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (StitchAuditFeedAdapter adapter : safe) {
      StitchAuditFeedAdapter resolved = Objects.requireNonNull(adapter, "adapter");
      String key = normalize(resolved.feedId());
      if (indexed.containsKey(key)) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("Duplicate audit feed adapter: " + key);
      }
      indexed.put(key, resolved);
    }
    this.adapters = Map.copyOf(indexed);
  }

  public StitchAuditFeedAdapter requireAdapter(String feedId) {
    String key = normalize(feedId);
    StitchAuditFeedAdapter adapter = adapters.get(key);
    if (adapter == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported audit feed: " + feedId);
    }
    return adapter;
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    return value == null ? "" : value.trim().toLowerCase(java.util.Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/audit/StitchAuditRow.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.audit;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;

public record StitchAuditRow(
    String id,
    Instant eventTimeUtc,
    String payload,
    String sessionId,
    Map<String, Object> values,
    Object sourceObject) {

  public StitchAuditRow {
    id = id == null ? "" : id.trim();
    values = values == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(new LinkedHashMap<>(values));
  }

  public Object value(String key) {
    if (key == null || key.isBlank() || values.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    Object direct = values.get(key);
    if (direct != null) {
      return direct;
    }
    String expected = normalizeKey(key);
    for (Map.Entry<String, Object> entry : values.entrySet()) {
      if (normalizeKey(entry.getKey()).equals(expected)) {
        return entry.getValue();
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  public String text(String key) {
    Object value = value(key);
    return value == null ? "" : String.valueOf(value);
  }

  private static String normalizeKey(String key) {
    if (key == null) {
      return "";
    }
    return key.replace("_", "").replace("-", "").trim().toLowerCase(java.util.Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.audit;

public final class StitchAuditScreenConfig {
  private final String id;
  private final String label;
  private final String routePath;
  private final String pageTitle;
  private final String pageSubtitle;
  private final int order;
  private final boolean enabled;
  private final int defaultPageSize;
  private final int maxPageSize;

  private StitchAuditScreenConfig(Builder builder) {
    this.id = require(builder.id, "id");
    this.label = require(builder.label, "label");
    this.routePath = require(builder.routePath, "routePath");
    this.pageTitle = require(builder.pageTitle, "pageTitle");
    this.pageSubtitle = optional(builder.pageSubtitle);
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.enabled = builder.enabled;
    this.defaultPageSize = Math.max(1, builder.defaultPageSize);
    this.maxPageSize = Math.max(this.defaultPageSize, builder.maxPageSize);
  }

  public static Builder builder(String id) {
    return new Builder(id);
  }

  public String id() {
    return id;
  }

  public String label() {
    return label;
  }

  public String routePath() {
    return routePath;
  }

  public String pageTitle() {
    return pageTitle;
  }

  public String pageSubtitle() {
    return pageSubtitle;
  }

  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public boolean enabled() {
    return enabled;
  }

  public int defaultPageSize() {
    return defaultPageSize;
  }

  public int maxPageSize() {
    return maxPageSize;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final String id;
    private String label;
    private String routePath;
    private String pageTitle;
    private String pageSubtitle;
    private int order;
    private boolean enabled = true;
    private int defaultPageSize = 25;
    private int maxPageSize = 200;

    private Builder(String id) {
      this.id = require(id, "id");
      this.label = "Status";
      this.routePath = "admin/audit/status";
      this.pageTitle = "Admin - Audit - Status";
      this.pageSubtitle = "Browse archived status audit events.";
      this.order = 10;
    }

    public Builder withLabel(String value) {
      this.label = require(value, "label");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRoutePath(String value) {
      this.routePath = require(value, "routePath");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageTitle(String value) {
      this.pageTitle = require(value, "pageTitle");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageSubtitle(String value) {
      this.pageSubtitle = optional(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.enabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withDefaultPageSize(int value) {
      this.defaultPageSize = Math.max(1, value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withMaxPageSize(int value) {
      this.maxPageSize = Math.max(1, value);
      return this;
    }

    public StitchAuditScreenConfig build() {
      return new StitchAuditScreenConfig(this);
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/audit/StitchAuditStatusFeedAdapter.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.audit;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.TreeSet;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStatusApp;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStatusService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.RowResult;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetId;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

public class StitchAuditStatusFeedAdapter extends StitchAuditDirectFeedSupport
    implements StitchAuditFeedAdapter {
  private static final List<StitchAuditColumn> COLUMNS =
      List.of(
          new StitchAuditColumn("heartbeatTime", "Heartbeat", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TIMESTAMP),
          new StitchAuditColumn("type", "Type", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT),
          new StitchAuditColumn("group", "Group", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT),
          new StitchAuditColumn("name", "Name", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT),
          new StitchAuditColumn("instance", "Instance", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT),
          new StitchAuditColumn("state", "State", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.STATUS),
          new StitchAuditColumn("host", "Host", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT),
          new StitchAuditColumn("sessionId", "Session ID", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT),
          new StitchAuditColumn("message", "Message", StitchAuditColumn.Kind.TEXT));
  private static final List<String> TYPE_OPTIONS =
      List.of(StatusType.APP.name(), StatusType.SERVICE.name());
  private static final List<String> STATE_OPTIONS = statusStateOptions();
  private static final List<StitchAuditFilterDefinition> QUICK_FILTERS =
      List.of(
          new StitchAuditFilterDefinition(
              "type",
              "Type",
              "Filter status rows by runtime type (APP or SERVICE).",
              TYPE_OPTIONS),
          new StitchAuditFilterDefinition(
              "state",
              "State",
              "Filter status rows by service/app runtime state.",
              STATE_OPTIONS));
  private static final Map<String, String> DEFAULT_FEED_FILTERS =
      defaultQuickFilters("type", FILTER_ALL, "state", FILTER_ALL);
  private static final StitchAuditFilterModel NO_FILTER =
      new StitchAuditFilterModel(null, null, null, null, Map.of(), 0, 25, null, false);
  private static final List<StatusDataset> DATASETS =
      List.of(new StatusDataset("status_app", "APP"), new StatusDataset("status_service", "SERVICE"));

  public StitchAuditStatusFeedAdapter(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    super(runtimeContext);
  }

  @Override
  public String feedId() {
    return StitchAuditFeature.STATUS;
  }

  @Override
  public List<StitchAuditColumn> columns() {
    return COLUMNS;
  }

  @Override
  public List<StitchAuditFilterDefinition> filterDefinitions() {
    return QUICK_FILTERS;
  }

  @Override
  public Map<String, String> defaultFeedFilters() {
    return DEFAULT_FEED_FILTERS;
  }

  @Override
  public StitchAuditFilterModel defaultFilters(int defaultPageSize) {
    return new StitchAuditFilterModel(
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        defaultFeedFilters(),
        0,
        Math.max(1, defaultPageSize),
        "heartbeat_epoch_ms",
        false);
  }

  @Override
  public StitchAuditPage queryAdvancedSql(String sql, StitchAuditFilterModel contextFilter) {
    StitchAuditFilterModel filter = Objects.requireNonNull(contextFilter, "contextFilter");
    String datasetGroup = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(filter.group()), sessionGroup);
    List<AdvancedSqlSource> sources = new ArrayList<>();
    List<String> notices = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StatusDataset source : DATASETS) {
      DatasetId datasetId = datasetId(datasetGroup, source.datasetName());
      if (!datasetExists(datasetId)) {
        notices.add(datasetUnavailableMessage(datasetId));
        continue;
      }
      sources.add(
          new AdvancedSqlSource(
              datasetId, rewriteDatasetToken(statusDatasetSql(source.fallbackType(), NO_FILTER), datasetId)));
    }
    return queryAdvancedSqlFromSources(
        sql,
        filter,
        sources,
        "heartbeat_epoch_ms",
        "payload",
        "session_id",
        "heartbeat_epoch_ms",
        notices.isEmpty() ? "" : String.join(" | ", notices));
  }

  @Override
  public StitchAuditPage query(StitchAuditFilterModel filter) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(filter, "filter");
    String datasetGroup = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(filter.group()), sessionGroup);
    List<StitchAuditRow> rows = new ArrayList<>();
    List<String> notices = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StatusDataset source : DATASETS) {
      DatasetId datasetId = datasetId(datasetGroup, source.datasetName());
      if (!datasetExists(datasetId)) {
        notices.add(datasetUnavailableMessage(datasetId));
        continue;
      }
      rows.addAll(loadRows(datasetId, source.fallbackType(), filter));
    }

    rows.sort(comparator(filter));
    String message = notices.isEmpty() ? "" : String.join(" | ", notices);
    return buildPage(rows, filter, MAX_PAGE_SIZE, statusFilterOptions(rows), message);
  }

  @Override
  public StitchAuditDetailsModel details(StitchAuditRow row) {
    if (row == null) {
      return new StitchAuditDetailsModel("Status Audit Event", "", Map.of(), null);
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> summary = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    summary.put("heartbeatUtc", formatInstant(row.eventTimeUtc()));
    summary.put("type", row.text("type"));
    summary.put("group", row.text("group"));
    summary.put("name", row.text("name"));
    summary.put("instance", row.text("instance"));
    summary.put("state", row.text("state"));
    summary.put("host", row.text("host"));
    summary.put("sessionId", row.text("sessionId"));
    summary.put("message", row.text("message"));
    String subtitle =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            row.text("group") + " / " + row.text("name"),
            row.text("group"),
            row.text("name"),
            "Status event");
    return new StitchAuditDetailsModel(
        "Status Audit Event", subtitle, summary, parsePayload(row.payload()).orElse(row.payload()));
  }

  @Override
  public Optional<StitchAuditDetailsModel> sessionDetails(StitchAuditRow row) {
    if (row == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return lookupSessionDetails(row.text("group"), row.sessionId(), "Status");
  }

  private List<StitchAuditRow> loadRows(
      DatasetId datasetId, String fallbackType, StitchAuditFilterModel filter) {
    RowResult result = directQuery(datasetId, statusDatasetSql(fallbackType, filter));
    if (result.rows() == null || result.rows().isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }

    Map<String, Integer> index = columnIndex(result.columns());
    List<StitchAuditRow> rows = new ArrayList<>(result.rows().size());
    int ordinal = 0;
    for (List<Object> values : result.rows()) {
      String heartbeatEpoch = valueAt(values, index, "heartbeat_epoch_ms");
      Instant heartbeat = parseEpoch(heartbeatEpoch).orElse(null);
      String sessionId = valueAt(values, index, "session_id");
      String payload = valueAt(values, index, "payload");

      LinkedHashMap<String, Object> mapped = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      mapped.put("heartbeatTime", heartbeat);
      mapped.put("type", valueAt(values, index, "type"));
      mapped.put("group", valueAt(values, index, "group"));
      mapped.put("name", valueAt(values, index, "name"));
      mapped.put("instance", valueAt(values, index, "instance"));
      mapped.put("state", valueAt(values, index, "state"));
      mapped.put("host", valueAt(values, index, "host"));
      mapped.put("sessionId", sessionId);
      mapped.put("message", valueAt(values, index, "message"));

      String id =
          datasetId.group()
              + "/"
              + datasetId.name()
              + "/"
              + Strings.trimToEmpty(heartbeatEpoch)
              + "/"
              + ordinal++;
      rows.add(new StitchAuditRow(id, heartbeat, payload, sessionId, mapped, Map.of("dataset", datasetId.toString())));
    }
    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  private String statusDatasetSql(String fallbackType, StitchAuditFilterModel filter) {
    String typeExpr =
        "coalesce(cast(\"type\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.type'), '"
            + escapeSqlLiteral(fallbackType)
            + "')";
    String groupExpr = "coalesce(cast(\"group\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.group'))";
    String nameExpr = "coalesce(cast(\"name\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.name'))";
    String instanceExpr =
        "coalesce(cast(\"instance\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.instance'))";
    String stateExpr = "coalesce(cast(\"state\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.state'))";
    String hostExpr = "coalesce(cast(\"host\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.host'))";
    String sessionExpr =
        "coalesce(cast(\"session_id\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.sessionId'))";
    String messageExpr =
        "coalesce(cast(\"message\" as varchar), json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.message'))";
    String heartbeatExpr =
        "coalesce(cast(\"last_heartbeat_epoch_ms\" as bigint), try_cast(json_extract_string(payload_json, '$.lastHeartbeatEpochMs') as bigint))";
    String payloadExpr = "cast(payload_json as varchar)";

    StringBuilder sql = new StringBuilder("select ");
    sql.append(typeExpr).append(" as \"type\", ");
    sql.append(groupExpr).append(" as \"group\", ");
    sql.append(nameExpr).append(" as \"name\", ");
    sql.append(instanceExpr).append(" as \"instance\", ");
    sql.append(stateExpr).append(" as \"state\", ");
    sql.append(hostExpr).append(" as \"host\", ");
    sql.append(sessionExpr).append(" as \"session_id\", ");
    sql.append(messageExpr).append(" as \"message\", ");
    sql.append(heartbeatExpr).append(" as \"heartbeat_epoch_ms\", ");
    sql.append(payloadExpr).append(" as \"payload\" ");
    sql.append("from ${DATASET}");

    List<String> predicates = new ArrayList<>();
    addExactPredicate(predicates, groupExpr, filter.group(), FILTER_ALL);
    addExactPredicate(predicates, typeExpr, filter.filterValue("type"), FILTER_ALL);
    addExactPredicate(predicates, stateExpr, filter.filterValue("state"), FILTER_ALL);
    addEpochRangePredicates(predicates, heartbeatExpr, filter.timeFromUtc(), filter.timeToUtc());
    addContainsAnyPredicate(
        predicates,
        filter.searchText(),
        nameExpr,
        instanceExpr,
        hostExpr,
        sessionExpr,
        messageExpr,
        payloadExpr);

    if (!predicates.isEmpty()) {
      sql.append(" where ").append(String.join(" and ", predicates));
    }
    return sql.toString();
  }

  private Comparator<StitchAuditRow> comparator(StitchAuditFilterModel filter) {
    String sortBy = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(filter.sortBy()), "heartbeat_epoch_ms");
    boolean ascending = filter.sortAscending();
    Comparator<StitchAuditRow> base;
    if ("type".equalsIgnoreCase(sortBy)) {
      base = Comparator.comparing(row -> normalize(row.text("type")));
    } else if ("state".equalsIgnoreCase(sortBy)) {
      base = Comparator.comparing(row -> normalize(row.text("state")));
    } else if ("group".equalsIgnoreCase(sortBy)) {
      base = Comparator.comparing(row -> normalize(row.text("group")));
    } else {
      base = Comparator.comparing(StitchAuditRow::eventTimeUtc, Comparator.nullsLast(Comparator.naturalOrder()));
    }
    Comparator<StitchAuditRow> comparator =
        base.thenComparing(row -> normalize(row.text("name"))).thenComparing(row -> normalize(row.text("instance")));
    return ascending ? comparator : comparator.reversed();
  }

  private static LinkedHashMap<String, List<String>> statusFilterOptions(List<StitchAuditRow> rows) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, List<String>> options = filterOptions(rows, "type", "state");
    options.put("type", mergeOptions(options.get("type"), TYPE_OPTIONS));
    options.put("state", mergeOptions(options.get("state"), STATE_OPTIONS));
    return options;
  }

  private static List<String> mergeOptions(List<String> discovered, List<String> defaults) {
    TreeSet<String> sorted = new TreeSet<>(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    if (defaults != null) {
      for (String value : defaults) {
        String token = Strings.trimToNull(value);
        if (token != null && !FILTER_ALL.equalsIgnoreCase(token)) {
          sorted.add(token);
        }
      }
    }
    if (discovered != null) {
      for (String value : discovered) {
        String token = Strings.trimToNull(value);
        if (token != null && !FILTER_ALL.equalsIgnoreCase(token)) {
          sorted.add(token);
        }
      }
    }
    List<String> values = new ArrayList<>(sorted.size() + 1);
    values.add(FILTER_ALL);
    values.addAll(sorted);
    return List.copyOf(values);
  }

  private static List<String> statusStateOptions() {
    LinkedHashSet<String> values = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (DefinitionStatusApp.State state : DefinitionStatusApp.State.values()) {
      values.add(state.name());
    }
    for (DefinitionStatusService.State state : DefinitionStatusService.State.values()) {
      values.add(state.name());
    }
    return List.copyOf(values);
  }

  private enum StatusType {
    APP,
    SERVICE
  }

  private record StatusDataset(String datasetName, String fallbackType) {}
}
