===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/catalog/StitchCatalogBrowserScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.catalog;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.ComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.MultiSelectComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.UI;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeEnterEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeEnterObserver;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.Location;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.NotFoundException;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.QueryParameters;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import elemental.json.Json;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.TreeSet;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.catalog.CatalogManager.CatalogDetails;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchFiltersBar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchResultsSearch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchResultsToolbar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialogs;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGridColumn;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchRowActions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout.StitchShellLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchTextSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchPage;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchResultsView;

@Route(value = "catalog", layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchCatalogBrowserScreen extends StitchPage implements BeforeEnterObserver {
  private static final String QUERY_ASSET_ID = "assetId";
  private static final String QUERY_MODE = "mode";
  private static final String QUERY_TARGET_LANE = "targetLane";

  private final StitchCatalogProvider provider;
  private final StitchFiltersBar filtersBar = new StitchFiltersBar();
  private final StitchResultsView<StitchCatalogRow> results = new StitchResultsView<>();
  private final StitchResultsSearch searchField =
      new StitchResultsSearch("Search catalog assets", "Catalog search input");
  private final ComboBox<String> groupFilter = new ComboBox<>();
  private final ComboBox<String> typeFilter = new ComboBox<>();
  private final MultiSelectComboBox<String> tagFilter = new MultiSelectComboBox<>();

  private final Button refreshAction;

  private List<StitchCatalogRow> currentRows = List.of();
  private boolean loadingFilterOptions;
  private boolean applyingQueryContext;
  private StitchCatalogDetailsDialog detailsDialog;
  private StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode pendingMode =
      StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode.RELATIONSHIPS;
  private String pendingTargetLane;

  public StitchCatalogBrowserScreen(Stitch stitch, StitchCatalogProvider provider) {
    this(requireConfig(stitch), provider);
  }

  StitchCatalogBrowserScreen(StitchCatalogScreenConfig config, StitchCatalogProvider provider) {
    super(
        Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config").pageTitle(),
        config.pageSubtitle() == null ? "" : config.pageSubtitle());
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");

    setSizeFull();
    body().setSizeFull();
    addClassName("stitch-catalog-screen");
    filtersBar.addClassName("stitch-catalog-filters");
    results.addClassName("stitch-catalog-results");

    configureToolbarFilters();
    configureResultsGrid();

    StitchSection resultsSection = new StitchSection("Catalog Results");
    resultsSection.setWidthFull();
    resultsSection.setHeight(null);
    resultsSection.body().setWidthFull();
    resultsSection.body().setHeight(null);
    resultsSection.addClassName("stitch-catalog-results-section");
    resultsSection.addToBody(results);

    refreshAction = new Button("REFRESH", event -> refreshRequested());
    StitchResultsToolbar.stylePrimaryAction(refreshAction);
    refreshAction.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Refresh catalog search");
    refreshAction.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Refresh catalog search");
    filtersBar.withRightAction(refreshAction);

    addToBody(filtersBar, resultsSection);

    loadFilterOptions();
    resetResultsForNoSearch();
  }

  @Override
  public void beforeEnter(BeforeEnterEvent event) {
    if (event == null) {
      return;
    }
    applyQueryContext(
        firstQueryParam(event, QUERY_ASSET_ID),
        StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode.fromToken(firstQueryParam(event, QUERY_MODE)),
        firstQueryParam(event, QUERY_TARGET_LANE));
  }

  private static StitchCatalogScreenConfig requireConfig(Stitch stitch) {
    return stitch
        .features()
        .catalog()
        .map(StitchCatalogFeature::screen)
        .filter(StitchCatalogScreenConfig::enabled)
        .orElseThrow(NotFoundException::new);
  }

  private void configureToolbarFilters() {
    results.setPaginationEnabled(true);
    results.setPageSizeOptions(25, 50, 100);
    results.setPageSize(25);
    results.setResultCountVisible(true);
    results.toolbar().setVisible(false);
    results.grid().getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Catalog results grid");

    configureSingleFilter(groupFilter, "Group", "11rem", "Catalog group filter");
    configureSingleFilter(typeFilter, "Type", "11rem", "Catalog type filter");

    tagFilter.setPlaceholder("Tags");
    tagFilter.setWidth("14rem");
    tagFilter.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Catalog tags filter");
    tagFilter.addValueChangeListener(event -> onFilterChanged());

    searchField.onQueryChange(query -> onFilterChanged());

    filtersBar
        .withGroupSelector(groupFilter)
        .withFilter(typeFilter)
        .withFilter(tagFilter)
        .withSearch(searchField);
  }

  private void configureSingleFilter(
      ComboBox<String> filter, String placeholder, String width, String ariaLabel) {
    filter.setPlaceholder(placeholder);
    filter.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    filter.setClearButtonVisible(true);
    filter.setWidth(width);
    filter.setMinWidth(width);
    filter.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabel);
    filter.addValueChangeListener(event -> onFilterChanged());
  }

  private void configureResultsGrid() {
    results
        .grid()
        .addColumn(
            StitchGridColumn.text("Group", StitchCatalogRow::group)
                .key("group")
                .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.GROUP));
    results
        .grid()
        .addColumn(
            StitchGridColumn.text("Name", StitchCatalogRow::name)
                .key("name")
                .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.NAME));
    results
        .grid()
        .addColumn(
            StitchGridColumn.text("Type", StitchCatalogRow::type)
                .key("type")
                .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));
    results
        .grid()
        .addColumn(
            StitchGridColumn.text("Namespace", StitchCatalogRow::namespace)
                .key("namespace")
                .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));
    results
        .grid()
        .addColumn(
            StitchGridColumn.text("Summary", StitchCatalogRow::summary)
                .key("summary")
                .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));

    StitchRowActions<StitchCatalogRow> rowActions = new StitchRowActions<>();
    rowActions.addAction(
        StitchRowActions.Action.icon(VaadinIcon.EXTERNAL_LINK, "OPEN", this::openRowDetails));
    rowActions.addColumn(results.grid());
  }

  private void refreshRequested() {
    loadFilterOptions();
    refreshSearchResults();
  }

  private void loadFilterOptions() {
    loadingFilterOptions = true;
    try {
      StitchCatalogProvider.StitchCatalogFilterOptions options = provider.filterOptions();
      syncFilterOptions(groupFilter, options.groups());
      syncFilterOptions(typeFilter, options.types());
      syncTagOptions(options.tags());
    } catch (Exception error) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to load catalog filters", rootMessage(error));
    } finally {
      loadingFilterOptions = false;
    }
  }

  private void syncFilterOptions(ComboBox<String> filter, List<String> options) {
    filter.setItems(options);
    if (filter.getValue() != null && !options.contains(filter.getValue())) {
      filter.clear();
    }
  }

  private void syncTagOptions(List<String> options) {
    Set<String> selected = new TreeSet<>(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    selected.addAll(tagFilter.getSelectedItems());
    selected.retainAll(options);
    tagFilter.setItems(options);
    tagFilter.select(selected);
  }

  private void onFilterChanged() {
    if (loadingFilterOptions) {
      return;
    }
    refreshSearchResults();
  }

  private void refreshSearchResults() {
    if (!hasActiveSearch()) {
      resetResultsForNoSearch();
      return;
    }
    try {
      StitchCatalogProvider.StitchCatalogPaging paging =
          new StitchCatalogProvider.StitchCatalogPaging(0, results.pagination().pageSize());
      StitchCatalogProvider.StitchCatalogPage page = provider.search(currentQuery(), paging);
      currentRows = page.rows();
      results.setEmptyState("No catalog rows", "No catalog assets matched the current search filters.");
      results.setItems(currentRows);
      results.setEmpty(currentRows.isEmpty());
      results.setResultCount(page.totalCount());
    } catch (Exception error) {
      currentRows = List.of();
      results.setItems(List.of());
      results.setEmpty(true);
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to search catalog", rootMessage(error));
    }
  }

  private void applyQueryContext(
      String assetId, StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode mode, String targetLane) {
    applyingQueryContext = true;
    try {
      pendingMode =
          mode == null ? StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode.RELATIONSHIPS : mode;
      pendingTargetLane = hasValue(targetLane) ? targetLane : null;

      if (!hasValue(assetId)) {
        if (detailsDialog != null && detailsDialog.isOpened()) {
          detailsDialog.applyImpactContext(pendingMode, pendingTargetLane);
        }
        return;
      }

      provider
          .loadDetails(assetId)
          .ifPresentOrElse(this::showDetailsDialog, this::closeDetailsDialog);
    } finally {
      applyingQueryContext = false;
      syncQueryContext();
    }
  }

  private StitchCatalogProvider.StitchCatalogQuery currentQuery() {
    return new StitchCatalogProvider.StitchCatalogQuery(
        searchField.getValue(),
        typeFilter.getValue(),
        groupFilter.getValue(),
        List.copyOf(tagFilter.getSelectedItems()),
        null);
  }

  private boolean hasActiveSearch() {
    return !searchField.normalizedQuery().isBlank()
        || hasValue(typeFilter.getValue())
        || hasValue(groupFilter.getValue())
        || !tagFilter.getSelectedItems().isEmpty();
  }

  private void resetResultsForNoSearch() {
    currentRows = List.of();
    results.setEmptyState(
        "No active search",
        "Enter search text or apply one or more filters to load catalog assets.");
    results.setItems(List.of());
    results.setEmpty(true);
    results.setResultCount(0);
  }

  private void openRowDetails(StitchCatalogRow row) {
    if (row == null || !hasValue(row.assetId())) {
      return;
    }
    provider
        .loadDetails(row.assetId())
        .ifPresentOrElse(
            this::showDetailsDialog,
            () -> StitchDialogs.openInfo("Catalog details unavailable", "Unable to load selected catalog asset."));
  }

  private void showDetailsDialog(CatalogDetails details) {
    if (details == null || details.summary() == null) {
      closeDetailsDialog();
      return;
    }
    if (detailsDialog != null && detailsDialog.isOpened()) {
      pendingMode = detailsDialog.mode();
      pendingTargetLane = detailsDialog.targetLane();
      detailsDialog.close();
      detailsDialog = null;
    }

    StitchCatalogDetailsDialog dialog =
        new StitchCatalogDetailsDialog(
            provider, details, pendingMode, pendingTargetLane, this::openRelatedAsset, this::syncQueryContext);
    dialog.addOpenedChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!event.isOpened()) {
            if (detailsDialog == dialog) {
              detailsDialog = null;
            }
            syncQueryContext();
          }
        });
    detailsDialog = dialog;
    dialog.open();
    syncQueryContext();
  }

  private void closeDetailsDialog() {
    StitchCatalogDetailsDialog current = detailsDialog;
    detailsDialog = null;
    if (current != null && current.isOpened()) {
      current.close();
    }
    syncQueryContext();
  }

  private void openRelatedAsset(String assetId) {
    String resolved = Strings.trimToNull(assetId);
    if (resolved == null) {
      return;
    }
    if (detailsDialog != null && detailsDialog.isOpened()) {
      pendingMode = detailsDialog.mode();
      pendingTargetLane = detailsDialog.targetLane();
    }

    searchField.setValue(resolved);
    StitchCatalogRow matched =
        currentRows.stream().filter(row -> resolved.equals(row.assetId())).findFirst().orElse(null);
    if (matched != null) {
      openRowDetails(matched);
      return;
    }
    provider
        .loadDetails(resolved)
        .ifPresentOrElse(
            this::showDetailsDialog,
            () ->
                StitchDialogs.openInfo(
                    "Relationship target not found",
                    "Unable to open related catalog asset " + resolved));
  }

  private void syncQueryContext() {
    if (applyingQueryContext) {
      return;
    }
    UI ui = UI.getCurrent();
    if (ui == null) {
      return;
    }

    StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode mode = pendingMode;
    String targetLane = pendingTargetLane;
    String assetId = null;

    if (detailsDialog != null && detailsDialog.isOpened()) {
      mode = detailsDialog.mode();
      targetLane = detailsDialog.targetLane();
      assetId = detailsDialog.selectedAssetId();
    }
    mode = mode == null ? StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode.RELATIONSHIPS : mode;

    LinkedHashMap<String, String> query = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (hasValue(assetId)) {
      query.put(QUERY_ASSET_ID, assetId);
    }
    query.put(QUERY_MODE, mode.name().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
    if (mode == StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode.PROMOTE && hasValue(targetLane)) {
      query.put(QUERY_TARGET_LANE, targetLane);
    }

    ui.getPage()
        .getHistory()
        .replaceState(
            Json.createObject(),
            new Location("catalog", QueryParameters.simple(Map.copyOf(query))));
  }

  private static String firstQueryParam(BeforeEnterEvent event, String key) {
    if (event == null || key == null || key.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    List<String> values = event.getLocation().getQueryParameters().getParameters().get(key);
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    return values.get(0);
  }

  private static boolean hasValue(String value) {
    return value != null && !value.isBlank();
  }

  private static String rootMessage(Throwable error) {
    return StitchTextSupport.rootMessage(error);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/catalog/StitchCatalogDetailsDialog.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.catalog;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification.Position;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextArea;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.catalog.CatalogManager.CatalogDetails;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.catalog.CatalogManager.CatalogSummary;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle.RelationshipType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchActionStyles;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchInspectorPreviewPanel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSummaryStrip;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchTabbedDetailsPanel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialogs;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchTextSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchDirtyStateSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchEditorModeController;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;

final class StitchCatalogDetailsDialog extends StitchDialog {
  private final StitchCatalogProvider provider;
  private final Consumer<String> onOpenAsset;
  private final Runnable onContextChanged;

  private final StitchInspectorPreviewPanel inspectorPanel =
      new StitchInspectorPreviewPanel("Catalog Inspector", "Catalog inspector preview");
  private final StitchCatalogSemanticEditorPanel semanticEditor = new StitchCatalogSemanticEditorPanel();
  private final StitchCatalogRelationshipPanel relationshipPanel = new StitchCatalogRelationshipPanel();
  private final StitchCatalogImpactPanel impactPanel = new StitchCatalogImpactPanel();
  private final StitchSummaryStrip inspectorSummary = new StitchSummaryStrip();
  private final StitchTabbedDetailsPanel inspectorTabs = new StitchTabbedDetailsPanel();
  private final TextArea inspectorJson = new TextArea("Catalog JSON");
  private final StitchEditorModeController semanticMode = new StitchEditorModeController();
  private final StitchDirtyStateSupport dirtyStateSupport = new StitchDirtyStateSupport();

  private final Button editAction = action("EDIT", "Edit semantic metadata for selected catalog asset", this::editRequested);
  private final Button saveAction = action("SAVE", "Save semantic metadata updates", this::saveRequestedFromAction);
  private final Button cancelAction = action("CANCEL", "Cancel semantic metadata editing", this::cancelRequested);

  private CatalogDetails selectedDetails;
  private StitchCatalogProvider.SemanticAssetLoadResult selectedSemantic;

  StitchCatalogDetailsDialog(
      StitchCatalogProvider provider,
      CatalogDetails details,
      StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode initialMode,
      String initialTargetLane,
      Consumer<String> onOpenAsset,
      Runnable onContextChanged) {
    super("Catalog Metadata");
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.onOpenAsset = Objects.requireNonNullElse(onOpenAsset, assetId -> {});
    this.onContextChanged = Objects.requireNonNullElse(onContextChanged, () -> {});

    addClassName("stitch-catalog-details-dialog");
    setWidth("min(1180px, 96vw)");
    setHeight("86vh");
    setMaxHeight("92vh");
    body().getStyle().set("max-height", "72vh");
    body().getStyle().set("overflow", "auto");
    body().getStyle().set("min-height", "0");

    inspectorPanel.previewField().setReadOnly(true);
    inspectorPanel.previewField().setMinHeight("16rem");
    inspectorPanel.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Catalog inspector");

    inspectorJson.setWidthFull();
    inspectorJson.setReadOnly(true);
    inspectorJson.setMinHeight("22rem");
    inspectorJson.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Catalog inspector JSON");

    semanticEditor.addClassName("stitch-catalog-semantic-editor");
    relationshipPanel.addClassName("stitch-catalog-relationships-panel");
    impactPanel.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-panel");
    inspectorTabs.addClassName("stitch-catalog-inspector-tabs");

    inspectorTabs
        .addTab("overview", "Overview", inspectorPanel)
        .addTab("semantics", "Semantics", semanticEditor)
        .addTab("relationships", "Relationships", relationshipPanel)
        .addTab("impact", "Impact", impactPanel)
        .addTab("json", "JSON", inspectorJson)
        .selectTab("overview")
        .onTabChanged(ignored -> refreshActions());
    inspectorTabs.getStyle().set("min-height", "0");
    inspectorTabs.getStyle().set("width", "100%");

    VerticalLayout content = new VerticalLayout(inspectorSummary, inspectorTabs);
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(true);
    content.setWidthFull();
    content.addClassName("stitch-catalog-details-content");
    content.getStyle().set("min-height", "0");
    addToBody(content);

    withJsonPayloadSupplier(() -> selectedDetails == null ? Map.of("asset", "") : selectedDetails);
    addSecondaryAction("CLOSE", this::closeRequested);
    footer().addComponentAtIndex(0, editAction);
    footer().addComponentAtIndex(1, saveAction);
    footer().addComponentAtIndex(2, cancelAction);

    semanticEditor.onChange(this::semanticChanged);
    relationshipPanel.onOpenAsset(this::openRelatedAssetRequested);
    impactPanel.onOpenAsset(this::openRelatedAssetRequested);
    impactPanel.onModeChanged(this::modeChangedRequested);
    impactPanel.setTargetLanes(provider.promotionLanes());

    applyImpactContext(initialMode, initialTargetLane);
    showDetails(details);
  }

  String selectedAssetId() {
    return selectedDetails == null || selectedDetails.summary() == null
        ? null
        : selectedDetails.summary().assetId();
  }

  StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode mode() {
    return impactPanel.mode();
  }

  String targetLane() {
    return impactPanel.targetLane();
  }

  void applyImpactContext(StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode mode, String targetLane) {
    impactPanel.setMode(mode);
    if (hasValue(targetLane)) {
      impactPanel.setTargetLane(targetLane);
    }
    refreshImpact();
    notifyContextChanged();
  }

  private void showDetails(CatalogDetails details) {
    CatalogSummary summary = details == null ? null : details.summary();
    if (summary == null) {
      close();
      return;
    }

    semanticMode.clear();
    selectedDetails = details;
    selectedSemantic = provider.loadSemanticForEditor(summary.assetId());

    LinkedHashMap<String, String> metadata = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    metadata.put("Title", summary.title());
    metadata.put("Owner", summary.ownerId());
    metadata.put("Tags", String.join(", ", summary.tags() == null ? List.of() : summary.tags()));
    metadata.put("Trust", trustScore(summary));
    metadata.put("Freshness", summary.freshnessCadence());
    metadata.put(
        "Semantic",
        summary.semanticCompletenessClass().name() + " (" + summary.semanticCompletenessScore() + "%)");
    metadata.put("Asset Id", Strings.firstNonBlank(summary.assetId(), "-"));

    inspectorPanel
        .setContext("Asset", summary.type().name() + " " + summary.group() + "/" + summary.name())
        .setMetadata(metadata)
        .setPreviewVisible(true)
        .setPreviewReadOnly(true)
        .setPreviewAriaLabel("Catalog preview for " + summary.assetId())
        .setPreviewValue(detailPreview(details));

    semanticEditor.setSemantic(selectedSemantic.semantic(), selectedSemantic.type(), selectedSemantic.editable());
    relationshipPanel.setRelationships(summary.assetId(), details.relationshipsByType());
    inspectorSummary.setItems(inspectorSummary(summary));
    inspectorJson.setValue(prettyJson(details));
    inspectorTabs.selectTab("overview");
    setDialogTitle("Catalog Metadata - " + Strings.firstNonBlank(summary.name(), summary.assetId()));

    refreshImpact();
    refreshActions();
    notifyContextChanged();
  }

  private void refreshImpact() {
    if (selectedDetails == null || selectedDetails.summary() == null) {
      impactPanel.clear("Select a catalog asset to load relationships and impact preview.");
      return;
    }
    try {
      StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphResult graph =
          provider.loadGraph(selectedDetails.summary().assetId(), impactPanel.request());
      impactPanel.setGraph(graph);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      impactPanel.clear("Unable to load graph/impact details: " + rootMessage(error));
    }
  }

  private void modeChangedRequested() {
    refreshImpact();
    notifyContextChanged();
  }

  private void openRelatedAssetRequested(String assetId) {
    String resolved = Strings.trimToNull(assetId);
    if (resolved == null) {
      return;
    }
    runWithUnsavedGuard(() -> onOpenAsset.accept(resolved));
  }

  private void editRequested() {
    if (selectedSemantic == null || !selectedSemantic.editable()) {
      return;
    }
    semanticMode.enterEditMode();
    semanticEditor.setEditable(true);
    inspectorTabs.selectTab("semantics");
    refreshActions();
  }

  private void saveRequestedFromAction() {
    saveRequested();
  }

  private boolean saveRequested() {
    if (!semanticMode.isEditMode() || selectedDetails == null || selectedDetails.summary() == null) {
      return false;
    }
    try {
      StitchCatalogProvider.SemanticUpdateResult result =
          provider.updateSemantic(selectedDetails.summary().assetId(), semanticEditor.semantic());
      if (!result.updated()) {
        StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to save semantic metadata", Strings.trimToEmpty(result.message()));
        return false;
      }
      semanticMode.clear();
      reloadSelectedDetails(result.resolvedAssetId());
      Notification.show("Semantic metadata saved", 1500, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      return true;
    } catch (Exception error) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to save semantic metadata", rootMessage(error));
      return false;
    }
  }

  private void cancelRequested() {
    if (!semanticMode.hasUnsavedChanges()) {
      discardSemanticChanges();
      return;
    }
    dirtyStateSupport.guard(this::saveRequested, this::discardSemanticChanges, () -> {});
  }

  private void semanticChanged() {
    if (!semanticMode.isEditMode()) {
      return;
    }
    semanticMode.markDirty();
    refreshActions();
  }

  private void discardSemanticChanges() {
    semanticMode.clear();
    reloadSelectedDetails(selectedAssetId());
  }

  private void reloadSelectedDetails(String assetId) {
    String resolved = Strings.trimToNull(assetId);
    if (resolved == null) {
      close();
      return;
    }
    provider.loadDetails(resolved).ifPresentOrElse(this::showDetails, this::close);
  }

  private void closeRequested() {
    runWithUnsavedGuard(this::close);
  }

  private void runWithUnsavedGuard(Runnable action) {
    if (!semanticMode.hasUnsavedChanges()) {
      action.run();
      return;
    }
    dirtyStateSupport.guard(
        () -> {
          if (saveRequested()) {
            action.run();
            return true;
          }
          return false;
        },
        () -> {
          discardSemanticChanges();
          action.run();
        },
        () -> {});
  }

  private void refreshActions() {
    boolean hasSelection = selectedDetails != null && selectedDetails.summary() != null;
    boolean editable = selectedSemantic != null && selectedSemantic.editable();
    boolean editMode = semanticMode.isEditMode();

    editAction.setVisible(hasSelection && editable && !editMode);
    editAction.setEnabled(hasSelection && editable && !editMode);
    saveAction.setVisible(hasSelection && editMode);
    saveAction.setEnabled(hasSelection && editMode);
    cancelAction.setVisible(hasSelection && editMode);
    cancelAction.setEnabled(hasSelection && editMode);

    impactPanel.setEnabled(!editMode);
    inspectorTabs.setEnabled(!editMode || inspectorTabs.isSelected("semantics"));
  }

  private void notifyContextChanged() {
    onContextChanged.run();
  }

  private static Button action(String text, String ariaLabel, Runnable action) {
    Button button = new Button(text, event -> action.run());
    button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    button.addClassName("stitch-dialog-action-button");
    button.addClassName("stitch-btn");
    StitchActionStyles.applyByLabel(button, text);
    button.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabel);
    button.getElement().setAttribute("title", ariaLabel);
    return button;
  }

  private static Map<String, String> inspectorSummary(CatalogSummary summary) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    values.put("Type", summary.type().name());
    values.put("Group", summary.group());
    values.put("Name", summary.name());
    values.put("Namespace", Strings.firstNonBlank(summary.namespace(), "-"));
    values.put("Owner", Strings.firstNonBlank(summary.ownerId(), "-"));
    values.put("Trust", summary.trustCertification().name());
    return values;
  }

  private static String trustScore(CatalogSummary summary) {
    return summary.trustCertification().name() + " / " + summary.trustQualityStatus().name();
  }

  private static String detailPreview(CatalogDetails details) {
    List<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
    lines.add("Usage Hints");
    List<String> questions = details.usage() == null ? List.of() : details.usage().exampleQuestions();
    List<String> hints = details.usage() == null ? List.of() : details.usage().usageHints();
    if (questions.isEmpty() && hints.isEmpty()) {
      lines.add("-");
    } else {
      questions.forEach(value -> lines.add("- " + value));
      hints.forEach(value -> lines.add("- " + value));
    }
    lines.add("");
    lines.add("Relationships");
    if (details.relationshipCounts().isEmpty()) {
      lines.add("-");
    } else {
      details.relationshipCounts().entrySet().stream()
          .sorted(Map.Entry.comparingByKey(Comparator.comparing(RelationshipType::name)))
          .forEach(entry -> lines.add("- " + entry.getKey().name() + ": " + entry.getValue()));
    }
    return String.join("\n", lines);
  }

  private static String prettyJson(Object payload) {
    try {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().writerWithDefaultPrettyPrinter().writeValueAsString(payload);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      return String.valueOf(payload);
    }
  }

  private static boolean hasValue(String value) {
    return value != null && !value.isBlank();
  }

  private static String rootMessage(Throwable error) {
    return StitchTextSupport.rootMessage(error);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/catalog/StitchCatalogFeature.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.catalog;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.StitchFeatureSet;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu.StitchMenuEntry;

public final class StitchCatalogFeature implements StitchFeatureSet {
  public static final String FEATURE_ID = "catalog";
  public static final String SCREEN = "catalog";
  public static final String ENTRY_BROWSER = "catalog.browser";

  private final String menuLabel;
  private final int order;
  private final StitchCatalogScreenConfig screen;

  private StitchCatalogFeature(Builder builder) {
    this.menuLabel = require(builder.menuLabel, "menuLabel");
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.screen = builder.screenBuilder.build();
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  @Override
  public String id() {
    return FEATURE_ID;
  }

  @Override
  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public StitchCatalogScreenConfig screen() {
    return screen;
  }

  @Override
  public List<StitchMenuEntry> menuEntries() {
    if (!screen.enabled()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    StitchMenuEntry catalogEntry =
        StitchMenuEntry.builder(ENTRY_BROWSER)
            .withLabel(screen.label())
            .withRoutePath(screen.routePath())
            .withOrder(order)
            .build();
    return List.of(catalogEntry);
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String menuLabel = "Catalog";
    private int order = 21;
    private final StitchCatalogScreenConfig.Builder screenBuilder =
        StitchCatalogScreenConfig.builder(SCREEN);

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withMenuLabel(String value) {
      this.menuLabel = require(value, "menuLabel");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder screen(Consumer<StitchCatalogScreenConfig.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(screenBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public StitchCatalogFeature build() {
      return new StitchCatalogFeature(this);
    }
  }
}

import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.checkbox.Checkbox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.ComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.details.Details;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.tabs.Tab;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle.DeleteOptions;

final class StitchCatalogImpactPanel extends VerticalLayout {
  private final Tab relationshipsTab = new Tab("RELATIONSHIPS");
  private final Tab deleteTab = new Tab("DELETE");
  private final Tab promoteTab = new Tab("PROMOTE");
  private final StitchTabs modeTabs = new StitchTabs(relationshipsTab, deleteTab, promoteTab);
  private final ComboBox<String> targetLane = new ComboBox<>("Target Lane");
  private final Checkbox deleteHistory = new Checkbox("Delete history");
  private final Checkbox deleteData = new Checkbox("Delete data");
  private final Checkbox forceDelete = new Checkbox("Force");
  private final Checkbox includeOptionalDependencies =
      new Checkbox("Include optional dependencies");
  private final Checkbox includeDocs = new Checkbox("Include docs");
  private final Checkbox rebindSharedAssets = new Checkbox("Rebind shared assets");
  private final Checkbox failIfMissingTargetDependencies =
      new Checkbox("Block if required target dependency is missing");
  private final VerticalLayout deleteOptions = new VerticalLayout();
  private final VerticalLayout promoteOptions = new VerticalLayout();
  private final StitchSummaryStrip impactSummary = new StitchSummaryStrip();
  private final Span summary = new Span("No impact context loaded.");
  private final VerticalLayout graphHost = new VerticalLayout();
  private final VerticalLayout warningsHost = new VerticalLayout();
  private boolean suppressEvents;

  private Consumer<String> onOpenAsset = assetId -> {};
  private Runnable onModeChanged = () -> {};

  StitchCatalogImpactPanel() {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(true);
    setWidthFull();
    addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact");
    getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Catalog graph and planner impact panel");

    modeTabs.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Catalog impact mode");
    modeTabs.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-tabs");
    modeTabs.addSelectedChangeListener(event -> modeChanged());

    configureTargetLane();
    configureDeleteOptions();
    configurePromoteOptions();

    summary.getElement().setAttribute("aria-live", "polite");
    summary.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Catalog impact summary");
    summary.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-summary-text");
    graphHost.setPadding(false);
    graphHost.setSpacing(true);
    graphHost.setWidthFull();
    graphHost.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-graph");
    graphHost.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Catalog graph view");

    warningsHost.setPadding(false);
    warningsHost.setSpacing(false);
    warningsHost.setWidthFull();
    warningsHost.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-planner");
    warningsHost.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Catalog planner warnings and execution order");

    add(modeTabs, targetLane, deleteOptions, promoteOptions, impactSummary, summary, graphHost, warningsHost);
    updateModeVisibility();
  }

  StitchCatalogImpactPanel onOpenAsset(Consumer<String> callback) {
    onOpenAsset = Objects.requireNonNullElse(callback, assetId -> {});
    return this;
  }

  StitchCatalogImpactPanel onModeChanged(Runnable callback) {
    onModeChanged = Objects.requireNonNullElse(callback, () -> {});
    return this;
  }

  void setTargetLanes(List<String> lanes) {
    suppressEvents = true;
    try {
      List<String> values = lanes == null ? List.of() : lanes;
      targetLane.setItems(values);
      if (targetLane.getValue() == null && !values.isEmpty()) {
        targetLane.setValue(values.get(0));
      }
    } finally {
      suppressEvents = false;
    }
  }

  void setTargetLane(String lane) {
    if (lane == null || lane.isBlank()) {
      return;
    }
    suppressEvents = true;
    try {
      targetLane.setValue(lane);
    } finally {
      suppressEvents = false;
    }
  }

  String targetLane() {
    String value = targetLane.getValue();
    return value == null || value.isBlank() ? "UAT" : value;
  }

  void setMode(StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode mode) {
    StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode resolved =
        mode == null ? StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode.RELATIONSHIPS : mode;
    suppressEvents = true;
    try {
      modeTabs.setSelectedTab(tabForMode(resolved));
      updateModeVisibility();
    } finally {
      suppressEvents = false;
    }
  }

  StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode mode() {
    return modeOf(modeTabs.getSelectedTab());
  }

  StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactRequest request() {
    return new StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactRequest(
        mode(), targetLane(), deleteOptions(), promotionOptions());
  }

  void clear(String message) {
    impactSummary.setItems(Map.of());
    summary.setText(message == null ? "" : message);
    graphHost.removeAll();
    warningsHost.removeAll();
  }

  void setGraph(StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphResult graph) {
    StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphResult result =
        graph == null
            ? StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphResult.empty("", mode(), targetLane())
            : graph;
    impactSummary.setItems(summaryItems(result));
    summary.setText(summaryText(result));
    renderGraph(result);
    renderPlannerDetails(result);
  }

  private void configureTargetLane() {
    targetLane.setAllowCustomValue(true);
    targetLane.setClearButtonVisible(false);
    targetLane.setWidthFull();
    targetLane.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Catalog promotion target lane");
    targetLane.addCustomValueSetListener(event -> targetLane.setValue(event.getDetail()));
    targetLane.addValueChangeListener(event -> modeChanged());
  }

  private void configureDeleteOptions() {
    deleteOptions.setPadding(false);
    deleteOptions.setSpacing(false);
    deleteOptions.setWidthFull();
    deleteOptions.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-options");
    deleteOptions.add(new Span("Delete Options"), deleteHistory, deleteData, forceDelete);
    deleteHistory.setValue(false);
    deleteData.setValue(false);
    forceDelete.setValue(false);
    deleteHistory.addValueChangeListener(event -> modeChanged());
    deleteData.addValueChangeListener(event -> modeChanged());
    forceDelete.addValueChangeListener(event -> modeChanged());
    deleteOptions.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Catalog delete impact options");
  }

  private void configurePromoteOptions() {
    promoteOptions.setPadding(false);
    promoteOptions.setSpacing(false);
    promoteOptions.setWidthFull();
    promoteOptions.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-options");
    promoteOptions.add(
        new Span("Promotion Options"),
        includeOptionalDependencies,
        includeDocs,
        rebindSharedAssets,
        failIfMissingTargetDependencies);
    includeOptionalDependencies.setValue(false);
    includeDocs.setValue(false);
    rebindSharedAssets.setValue(true);
    failIfMissingTargetDependencies.setValue(true);
    includeOptionalDependencies.addValueChangeListener(event -> modeChanged());
    includeDocs.addValueChangeListener(event -> modeChanged());
    rebindSharedAssets.addValueChangeListener(event -> modeChanged());
    failIfMissingTargetDependencies.addValueChangeListener(event -> modeChanged());
    promoteOptions.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Catalog promotion impact options");
  }

  private void modeChanged() {
    updateModeVisibility();
    if (!suppressEvents) {
      onModeChanged.run();
    }
  }

  private void updateModeVisibility() {
    boolean deleteMode = mode() == StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode.DELETE;
    boolean promoteMode = mode() == StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode.PROMOTE;
    deleteOptions.setVisible(deleteMode);
    promoteOptions.setVisible(promoteMode);
    targetLane.setVisible(promoteMode);
  }

  private DeleteOptions deleteOptions() {
    return new DeleteOptions(
        true,
        true,
        true,
        deleteHistory.getValue(),
        deleteData.getValue(),
        false,
        forceDelete.getValue(),
        true,
        List.of());
  }

  private PromotionOptions promotionOptions() {
    return new PromotionOptions(
        true,
        includeOptionalDependencies.getValue(),
        true,
        true,
        true,
        includeDocs.getValue(),
        rebindSharedAssets.getValue(),
        failIfMissingTargetDependencies.getValue(),
        true);
  }

  private void renderGraph(StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphResult result) {
    graphHost.removeAll();
    if (result.nodes().isEmpty()) {
      graphHost.add(new Span("No graph relationships are visible for the current selection."));
      return;
    }

    VerticalLayout nodeRows = new VerticalLayout();
    nodeRows.setPadding(false);
    nodeRows.setSpacing(false);
    nodeRows.setWidthFull();
    result.nodes().stream()
        .sorted(
            Comparator.comparingInt(StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphNode::hop)
                .thenComparing(
                    StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphNode::assetId, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
        .forEach(node -> nodeRows.add(nodeRow(node)));
    Details nodes = new Details("NODES (" + result.nodes().size() + ")", nodeRows);
    nodes.setOpened(true);
    nodes.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-group");
    nodes.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Catalog graph nodes");
    graphHost.add(nodes);

    VerticalLayout edgeRows = new VerticalLayout();
    edgeRows.setPadding(false);
    edgeRows.setSpacing(false);
    edgeRows.setWidthFull();
    result.edges().stream()
        .sorted(
            Comparator.comparing(
                    StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphEdge::relationshipType,
                    Comparator.comparing(RelationshipType::name))
                .thenComparing(
                    StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphEdge::fromAssetId,
                    String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
                .thenComparing(
                    StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphEdge::toAssetId,
                    String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
        .forEach(edge -> edgeRows.add(edgeRow(edge)));
    Details edges = new Details("EDGES (" + result.edges().size() + ")", edgeRows);
    edges.setOpened(true);
    edges.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-group");
    edges.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Catalog graph edges");
    graphHost.add(edges);
  }

  private void renderPlannerDetails(StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphResult result) {
    warningsHost.removeAll();
    warningsHost.add(linesDetails("Warnings", result.warnings(), false));
    warningsHost.add(linesDetails("Execution Order", result.executionOrder(), true));
  }

  private HorizontalLayout nodeRow(StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphNode node) {
    Span title = new Span(node.assetId());
    title.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-node-title");
    Span typeChip = new Span(node.type().name());
    typeChip.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-chip");
    Span stateChip = new Span(node.impactState().name());
    stateChip.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-chip");
    HorizontalLayout chips = new HorizontalLayout(typeChip, stateChip);
    chips.setPadding(false);
    chips.setSpacing(true);
    chips.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-chips");
    VerticalLayout text = new VerticalLayout(title, chips);
    text.setPadding(false);
    text.setSpacing(true);
    text.setWidthFull();
    if (!node.impactReason().isBlank()) {
      Span reason = new Span(node.impactReason());
      reason.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-reason");
      text.add(reason);
    }
    Button open = new Button("OPEN");
    open.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY_INLINE);
    open.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Open graph node asset " + node.assetId());
    open.setEnabled(node.assetId() != null && !node.assetId().isBlank());
    open.addClickListener(event -> onOpenAsset.accept(node.assetId()));
    HorizontalLayout row = new HorizontalLayout(text, open);
    row.setPadding(false);
    row.setSpacing(true);
    row.setWidthFull();
    row.setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.START);
    row.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-node-row");
    row.expand(text);
    return row;
  }

  private HorizontalLayout edgeRow(StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphEdge edge) {
    Span relation = new Span(edge.fromAssetId() + " -> " + edge.toAssetId());
    relation.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-edge-title");
    Span typeChip = new Span(edge.relationshipType().name());
    typeChip.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-chip");
    Span stateChip = new Span(edge.impactState().name());
    stateChip.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-chip");
    HorizontalLayout chips = new HorizontalLayout(typeChip, stateChip);
    chips.setPadding(false);
    chips.setSpacing(true);
    chips.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-chips");
    VerticalLayout text = new VerticalLayout(relation, chips);
    text.setPadding(false);
    text.setSpacing(true);
    text.setWidthFull();
    if (!edge.impactReason().isBlank()) {
      Span reason = new Span(edge.impactReason());
      reason.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-reason");
      text.add(reason);
    }
    HorizontalLayout row = new HorizontalLayout(text);
    row.setPadding(false);
    row.setSpacing(false);
    row.setWidthFull();
    row.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-edge-row");
    row.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Catalog graph edge " + edge.id());
    return row;
  }

  private static Details linesDetails(String title, List<String> values, boolean opened) {
    VerticalLayout body = new VerticalLayout();
    body.setPadding(false);
    body.setSpacing(false);
    body.setWidthFull();
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      body.add(new Span("-"));
    } else {
      values.forEach(
          value -> {
            Span line = new Span(value);
            line.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-line");
            body.add(line);
          });
    }
    Details details = new Details(title, body);
    details.setOpened(opened);
    details.addClassName("stitch-catalog-impact-group");
    return details;
  }

  private static Map<String, String> summaryItems(StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphResult result) {
    java.util.LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new java.util.LinkedHashMap<>();
    values.put("Mode", result.mode().name());
    values.put("Nodes", String.valueOf(result.nodes().size()));
    values.put("Edges", String.valueOf(result.edges().size()));
    if (result.mode() == StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode.PROMOTE) {
      values.put("Target", result.targetLane() == null || result.targetLane().isBlank() ? "-" : result.targetLane());
    }
    if (!result.impactSummary().isEmpty()) {
      String topState =
          result.impactSummary().entrySet().stream()
              .max(Map.Entry.comparingByValue())
              .map(entry -> entry.getKey().name() + " (" + entry.getValue() + ")")
              .orElse("-");
      values.put("Primary Impact", topState);
    }
    return values;
  }

  private String summaryText(StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphResult result) {
    StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder();
    builder
        .append("Mode: ")
        .append(result.mode().name())
        .append(" | Nodes: ")
        .append(result.nodes().size())
        .append(" | Edges: ")
        .append(result.edges().size());
    if (mode() == StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode.PROMOTE) {
      builder.append(" | Target Lane: ").append(result.targetLane());
    }
    if (!result.impactSummary().isEmpty()) {
      builder.append(" | States: ");
      String states =
          result.impactSummary().entrySet().stream()
              .sorted(
                  Map.Entry.comparingByKey(
                      Comparator.comparing(StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState::name)))
              .map(entry -> entry.getKey().name() + "=" + entry.getValue())
              .reduce((left, right) -> left + ", " + right)
              .orElse("");
      builder.append(states);
    }
    return builder.toString();
  }

  private Tab tabForMode(StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode mode) {
    return switch (mode == null ? StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode.RELATIONSHIPS : mode) {
      case DELETE -> deleteTab;
      case PROMOTE -> promoteTab;
      case RELATIONSHIPS -> relationshipsTab;
    };
  }

  private StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode modeOf(Tab tab) {
    if (tab == deleteTab) {
      return StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode.DELETE;
    }
    if (tab == promoteTab) {
      return StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode.PROMOTE;
    }
    return StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactMode.RELATIONSHIPS;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/catalog/StitchCatalogImpactSupport.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.catalog;

import java.util.EnumMap;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.HashSet;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Set;

final class StitchCatalogImpactSupport {
  private StitchCatalogImpactSupport() {}

  static Map<String, StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState> resolveAssetStates(
      List<StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphNode> nodes,
      List<StateRule> rules,
      StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState fallback) {
    Map<String, StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState> resolved = new HashMap<>();
    if (nodes == null || nodes.isEmpty()) {
      return resolved;
    }
    for (StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphNode node : nodes) {
      StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState state = fallback;
      for (StateRule rule : rules) {
        if (rule.assets().contains(node.assetId())) {
          state = rule.state();
          break;
        }
      }
      resolved.put(node.assetId(), state);
    }
    return resolved;
  }

  static List<StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphNode> applyNodeImpact(
      List<StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphNode> nodes,
      Map<String, StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState> statesByAssetId) {
    if (nodes == null || nodes.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return nodes.stream()
        .map(
            node -> {
              StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState state =
                  statesByAssetId.getOrDefault(node.assetId(), StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState.NONE);
              return node.withImpact(state, state.name(), impactReason(state));
            })
        .toList();
  }

  static List<StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphEdge> applyEdgeImpact(
      List<StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphEdge> edges,
      Map<String, StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState> statesByAssetId,
      Set<String> blockerPairs,
      List<StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState> precedence) {
    if (edges == null || edges.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return edges.stream()
        .map(
            edge -> {
              StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState from =
                  statesByAssetId.getOrDefault(edge.fromAssetId(), StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState.NONE);
              StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState to =
                  statesByAssetId.getOrDefault(edge.toAssetId(), StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState.NONE);
              StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState state =
                  blockerPairs.contains(pair(edge.fromAssetId(), edge.toAssetId()))
                      ? StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState.BLOCKS
                      : highestState(from, to, precedence);
              return edge.withImpact(state, impactReason(state));
            })
        .toList();
  }

  static Set<String> normalizeAssetSet(List<String> values, Set<String> graphAssets) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return new HashSet<>();
    }
    Set<String> normalized = new HashSet<>();
    for (String value : values) {
      if (hasValue(value) && graphAssets.contains(value)) {
        normalized.add(value);
      }
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  static Set<String> referencedAssets(List<String> lines, Set<String> graphAssets) {
    if (lines == null || lines.isEmpty() || graphAssets.isEmpty()) {
      return Set.of();
    }
    Set<String> resolved = new HashSet<>();
    for (String line : lines) {
      if (!hasValue(line)) {
        continue;
      }
      for (String assetId : graphAssets) {
        if (line.contains(assetId)) {
          resolved.add(assetId);
        }
      }
    }
    return resolved;
  }

  @SafeVarargs
  static List<String> mergeLines(List<String>... values) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> merged = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    if (values != null) {
      for (List<String> value : values) {
        if (value == null || value.isEmpty()) {
          continue;
        }
        for (String line : value) {
          if (hasValue(line)) {
            merged.add(line);
          }
        }
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(merged);
  }

  static Map<StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState, Integer> summarizeImpact(
      List<StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphNode> nodes) {
    EnumMap<StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState, Integer> summary =
        new EnumMap<>(StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState.class);
    if (nodes == null || nodes.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    for (StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogGraphNode node : nodes) {
      if (node == null) {
        continue;
      }
      summary.merge(node.impactState(), 1, Integer::sum);
    }
    return Map.copyOf(summary);
  }

  static String impactReason(StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState state) {
    return switch (state) {
      case BLOCKS -> "Blocked by planner.";
      case MANUAL -> "Manual planner action required.";
      case IMPACTED -> "Impacted by planner.";
      case DETACHED -> "Marked detached by planner.";
      case RETAINED -> "Marked retained by planner.";
      case REQUIRED -> "Required for promotion.";
      case REBIND -> "Rebind required in target lane.";
      case OPTIONAL -> "Optional for target lane.";
      case SKIPPED -> "Skipped by planner.";
      case SAFE, NONE -> "";
    };
  }

  static String pair(String left, String right) {
    return (left == null ? "" : left) + "|" + (right == null ? "" : right);
  }

  static StateRule stateRule(StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState state, Set<String> assets) {
    return new StateRule(state, assets);
  }

  private static StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState highestState(
      StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState first,
      StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState second,
      List<StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState> precedence) {
    for (StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState state : precedence) {
      if (state == first || state == second) {
        return state;
      }
    }
    return StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState.NONE;
  }

  private static boolean hasValue(String value) {
    return value != null && !value.isBlank();
  }

  record StateRule(StitchCatalogProvider.CatalogImpactState state, Set<String> assets) {}
}
