public final class StitchCatalogProvider {
  private final StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext;
  private final SessionImpl session;
  private final CatalogManager catalogManager;

  public StitchCatalogProvider(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    this.runtimeContext = Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(current instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    this.session = resolved;
    this.catalogManager = current.catalog();
    if (catalogManager == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("CatalogManager is not available");
    }
  }

  public StitchCatalogPage search(StitchCatalogQuery query, StitchCatalogPaging paging) {
    StitchCatalogQuery resolvedQuery =
        query == null ? new StitchCatalogQuery(null, null, null, List.of(), null) : query;
    StitchCatalogPaging resolvedPaging = paging == null ? new StitchCatalogPaging(0, 100) : paging;

    CatalogSearchQuery catalogQuery =
        new CatalogSearchQuery(
            resolvedQuery.text(),
            resolvedQuery.type(),
            null,
            resolvedQuery.tags(),
            resolvedQuery.owner(),
            null,
            null,
            Math.max(1, Math.min(CatalogSearchQuery.MAX_LIMIT, resolvedPaging.pageSize())),
            null);

    CatalogSearchResult result = catalogManager.search(catalogQuery, accessContext(null));
    List<StitchCatalogRow> rows =
        result.results().stream().map(this::toRow).filter(Objects::nonNull).toList();
    if (hasValue(resolvedQuery.group())) {
      rows = rows.stream().filter(row -> resolvedQuery.group().equals(row.group())).toList();
    }
    return new StitchCatalogPage(rows, rows.size());
  }

  public Optional<CatalogDetails> loadDetails(String assetId) {
    if (!hasValue(assetId)) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return catalogManager.getAsset(assetId, accessContext(assetId));
  }

  public SemanticAssetLoadResult loadSemanticForEditor(String assetId) {
    Optional<CatalogDetails> detailsOptional = loadDetails(assetId);
    if (detailsOptional.isEmpty()) {
      return SemanticAssetLoadResult.notFound(assetId);
    }
    CatalogDetails details = detailsOptional.get();
    CatalogSummary summary = details.summary();
    DefinitionType type = summary == null ? DefinitionType.UNKNOWN : summary.type();
    Semantic semantic = loadSemantic(details);
    return new SemanticAssetLoadResult(
        true,
        isEditableType(type),
        isEditableType(type)
            ? null
            : "Semantic edits are supported for DATASET, SERVICE, SCHEMA, CONFIG, INGEST, and STREAM assets.",
        summary == null ? assetId : summary.assetId(),
        type,
        semantic,
        details);
  }

  public SemanticUpdateResult updateSemantic(String assetId, Semantic semanticMetadata) {
    String resolvedAssetId = hasValue(assetId) ? assetId : null;
    if (resolvedAssetId == null) {
      return SemanticUpdateResult.failed("assetId is required");
    }

    CatalogDetails details =
        loadDetails(resolvedAssetId)
            .orElse(null);
    if (details == null || details.summary() == null) {
      return SemanticUpdateResult.failed("Asset not found or not visible: " + resolvedAssetId);
    }

    CatalogSummary summary = details.summary();
    if (!isEditableType(summary.type())) {
      return SemanticUpdateResult.failed(
          "Unsupported asset type for semantic edit: " + summary.type().name());
    }

    Definition definition = loadDefinition(summary).orElse(null);
    if (definition == null) {
      return SemanticUpdateResult.failed(
          "Definition not found for semantic edit: " + summary.assetId());
    }

    Semantic semantic = semanticMetadata == null ? emptySemantic() : semanticMetadata;
    requireCache().upsert(updatedDefinition(definition, semantic));

    CatalogDetails refreshed = loadDetails(summary.assetId()).orElse(details);
    String refreshedAssetId =
        refreshed.summary() == null ? summary.assetId() : refreshed.summary().assetId();
    return new SemanticUpdateResult(true, "Semantic metadata updated.", refreshedAssetId, refreshed);
  }

  public StitchCatalogFilterOptions filterOptions() {
    CatalogSearchQuery query =
        new CatalogSearchQuery(
            null, null, null, List.of(), null, null, null, CatalogSearchQuery.MAX_LIMIT, null);
    CatalogSearchResult searchResult = catalogManager.search(query, accessContext(null));
    CatalogSearchFacet facets = searchResult.facets();
    return new StitchCatalogFilterOptions(
        sortedValues(facets == null ? null : facets.typeCounts()),
        distinctGroups(),
        sortedValues(facets == null ? null : facets.tagCounts()),
        sortedValues(facets == null ? null : facets.ownerCounts()));
  }

  private StitchCatalogRow toRow(CatalogSummary summary) {
    if (summary == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return new StitchCatalogRow(
        summary.assetId(),
        summary.type().name(),
        summary.group(),
        summary.name(),
        summary.namespace(),
        summary.description(),
        summary.tags(),
        summary.ownerId(),
        summary.trustCertification().name() + " / " + summary.trustQualityStatus().name(),
        summary.freshnessCadence(),
        summary.description(),
        updatedTimeUtc(summary));
  }

  private List<String> distinctGroups() {
    DiscoveryCache cache = session.internal().discoveryCache();
    if (cache == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<Definition> definitions = cache.allDefinitions();
    if (definitions == null || definitions.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> groups = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (Definition definition : definitions) {
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope = definition == null ? null : definition.envelope();
      if (envelope != null && hasValue(envelope.group())) {
        groups.add(envelope.group());
      }
    }
    return groups.stream().sorted(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER).toList();
  }

  private String updatedTimeUtc(CatalogSummary summary) {
    return loadDefinition(summary).map(this::updated).orElse("");
  }

  private String updated(Definition definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.envelope() == null || definition.envelope().updatedTimeUtc() == null) {
      return "";
    }
    return definition.envelope().updatedTimeUtc();
  }

  private Semantic loadSemantic(CatalogDetails details) {
    CatalogSummary summary = details == null ? null : details.summary();
    if (summary == null) {
      return emptySemantic();
    }
    Semantic fromDefinition = loadDefinition(summary).map(this::semanticOf).orElse(null);
    if (fromDefinition != null) {
      return fromDefinition;
    }
    return semanticFromDetails(details);
  }

  private Optional<Definition> loadDefinition(CatalogSummary summary) {
    if (summary == null || summary.type() == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    DiscoveryCache cache = requireCache();
    return switch (summary.type()) {
      case APP ->
          cache.get(DefinitionApp.class, summary.group(), summary.name()).map(definition -> (Definition) definition);
      case SERVICE ->
          cache
              .get(DefinitionService.class, summary.group(), summary.name())
              .map(definition -> (Definition) definition);
      case CONNECTION ->
          cache
              .get(DefinitionConnection.class, summary.group(), summary.name())
              .map(definition -> (Definition) definition);
      case INGEST ->
          cache
              .get(DefinitionIngest.class, summary.group(), summary.name())
              .map(definition -> (Definition) definition);
      case DATASET ->
          cache
              .get(DefinitionDataset.class, summary.group(), summary.namespace() + "/" + summary.name())
              .map(definition -> (Definition) definition);
      case STREAM ->
          cache
              .get(DefinitionStream.class, summary.group(), summary.name())
              .map(definition -> (Definition) definition);
      case CONFIG, CONFIG_LAYER -> loadConfigDefinition(summary, cache).map(definition -> (Definition) definition);
      case SCHEMA ->
          cache
              .get(DefinitionSchema.class, summary.group(), summary.name())
              .map(definition -> (Definition) definition);
      default -> Optional.empty();
    };
  }

  private Optional<DefinitionConfig> loadConfigDefinition(
      CatalogSummary summary, DiscoveryCache cache) {
    if (!hasValue(summary.group())) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    if (summary.type() == DefinitionType.CONFIG_LAYER
        && hasValue(summary.namespace())) {
      Optional<DefinitionConfig> fromNamespace =
          cache.get(DefinitionConfig.class, summary.group(), "config__" + summary.namespace());
      if (fromNamespace.isPresent()) {
        return fromNamespace;
      }
      return cache.list(DefinitionConfig.class, summary.group()).stream()
          .filter(Objects::nonNull)
          .filter(definition -> summary.namespace().equals(definition.configId()))
          .findFirst();
    }
    if (hasValue(summary.name())) {
      Optional<DefinitionConfig> direct =
          cache.get(DefinitionConfig.class, summary.group(), summary.name());
      if (direct.isPresent()) {
        return direct;
      }
      return cache.list(DefinitionConfig.class, summary.group()).stream()
          .filter(Objects::nonNull)
          .filter(definition -> summary.name().equals(definition.configId()))
          .findFirst();
    }
    return Optional.empty();
  }

  private Semantic semanticOf(Definition definition) {
    return switch (definition) {
      case DefinitionDataset dataset -> dataset.semantic();
      case DefinitionService service -> service.semantic();
      case DefinitionSchema schema -> schema.semantic();
      case DefinitionConfig config -> config.semantic();
      case DefinitionIngest ingest -> ingest.semantic();
      case DefinitionStream stream -> stream.semantic();
      default -> null;
    };
  }

  private static Definition updatedDefinition(Definition definition, Semantic semantic) {
    return switch (definition) {
      case DefinitionDataset existing ->
          new DefinitionDataset(
              existing.envelope(),
              existing.type(),
              existing.namespace(),
              existing.binding(),
              existing.view(),
              existing.accessMode(),
              semantic,
              existing.entitlements());
      case DefinitionService existing ->
          new DefinitionService(
              existing.envelope(),
              existing.resourceId(),
              existing.namespace(),
              existing.connectionRefs(),
              existing.schemaRef(),
              existing.serviceType(),
              existing.amps(),
              existing.grpc(),
              existing.arrow(),
              existing.otel(),
              existing.tags(),
              semantic,
              existing.entitlements());
      case DefinitionSchema existing ->
          new DefinitionSchema(
              existing.envelope(),
              existing.versionSemantic(),
              existing.versionNum(),
              existing.artifactType(),
              existing.format(),
              existing.schema(),
              existing.status(),
              existing.compatibility(),
              existing.refs(),
              existing.tags(),
              existing.hash(),
              existing.createdTimeUtc(),
              existing.schemaUsage(),
              existing.schemaType(),
              existing.doc(),
              existing.usageGroup(),
              semantic);
      case DefinitionConfig existing ->
          new DefinitionConfig(
              existing.envelope(),
              existing.recordType(),
              existing.resourceId(),
              existing.id(),
              existing.domain(),
              existing.group(),
              existing.tags(),
              existing.configId(),
              existing.schemaRef(),
              semantic,
              existing.notifications(),
              existing.publish(),
              existing.extensions());
      case DefinitionIngest existing ->
          new DefinitionIngest(
              existing.envelope(),
              existing.datasetId(),
              existing.outputSchemaId(),
              existing.input(),
              existing.schemaMode(),
              semantic);
      case DefinitionStream existing ->
          new DefinitionStream(
              existing.envelope(),
              existing.versionNum(),
              existing.versionName(),
              existing.namespace(),
              existing.streamId(),
              existing.transport(),
              existing.address(),
              existing.schemaId(),
              existing.schemaKey(),
              existing.messageType(),
              existing.serde(),
              existing.compatibilityMode(),
              existing.resolutionPolicy(),
              existing.connectionRefs(),
              existing.dependencyRefs(),
              existing.schema(),
              semantic);
      default ->
          throw new IllegalStateException(
              "Unsupported definition type for semantic update: "
                  + definition.getClass().getSimpleName());
    };
  }

  private static Semantic semanticFromDetails(CatalogDetails details) {
    CatalogSummary summary = details == null ? null : details.summary();
    if (summary == null) {
      return emptySemantic();
    }
    return new Semantic(
        summary.title(),
        summary.description(),
        details.businessMeaning(),
        summary.domain(),
        summary.subdomain(),
        summary.tags(),
        details.aliases(),
        details.keywords(),
        details.ownership(),
        details.dataShape(),
        details.freshness(),
        details.trust(),
        details.usage(),
        details.toolHints(),
        relationshipHints(details.relationshipsByType()));
  }

  private static List<Semantic.RelationshipHint> relationshipHints(
      Map<RelationshipType, List<CatalogRelationshipView>> relationshipsByType) {
    if (relationshipsByType == null || relationshipsByType.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return relationshipsByType.entrySet().stream()
        .sorted(Map.Entry.comparingByKey(Comparator.comparing(RelationshipType::name)))
        .flatMap(
            entry ->
                (entry.getValue() == null ? List.<CatalogRelationshipView>of() : entry.getValue())
                    .stream()
                    .filter(Objects::nonNull)
                    .map(
                        relationship ->
                            new Semantic.RelationshipHint(
                                semanticRelationshipType(relationship.relationshipType()),
                                relationship.direction() == CatalogRelationshipDirection.OUTGOING
                                    ? relationship.toAssetId()
                                    : relationship.fromAssetId(),
                                relationship.notes(),
                                relationship.targetLocator())))
        .toList();
  }

  private static Semantic.RelationshipType semanticRelationshipType(RelationshipType relationshipType) {
    if (relationshipType == null) {
      return Semantic.RelationshipType.DEPENDS_ON;
    }
    return switch (relationshipType) {
      case DERIVED_FROM -> Semantic.RelationshipType.DERIVED_FROM;
      case JOINS_TO -> Semantic.RelationshipType.JOINS_TO;
      case CONSUMES -> Semantic.RelationshipType.CONSUMES;
      case PRODUCES -> Semantic.RelationshipType.PRODUCES;
      case DOCUMENTED_BY -> Semantic.RelationshipType.DOCUMENTED_BY;
      case GOVERNED_BY -> Semantic.RelationshipType.GOVERNED_BY;
      default -> Semantic.RelationshipType.DEPENDS_ON;
    };
  }

  public List<String> promotionLanes() {
    String env = session.context() == null ? null : session.context().getEnv();
    LinkedHashSet<String> lanes = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    if (hasValue(env)) {
      lanes.add(env.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT));
    }
    lanes.add("DEV");
    lanes.add("UAT");
        lanes.add("PROD");
    return List.copyOf(lanes);
  }

  public CatalogGraphResult loadGraph(String assetId, CatalogImpactRequest request) {
    CatalogImpactRequest resolved = request == null ? CatalogImpactRequest.defaults() : request;
    CatalogImpactMode mode =
        resolved.mode() == null ? CatalogImpactMode.RELATIONSHIPS : resolved.mode();
    String targetLane = resolved.targetLane() == null ? "" : resolved.targetLane();
    DeleteOptions deleteOptions =
        resolved.deleteOptions() == null ? DeleteOptions.defaults() : resolved.deleteOptions();
    PromotionOptions promotionOptions =
        resolved.promotionOptions() == null
            ? PromotionOptions.defaults()
            : resolved.promotionOptions();
    CatalogDetails details = loadDetails(assetId).orElse(null);
    CatalogSummary summary = details == null ? null : details.summary();
    if (summary == null) {
      return CatalogGraphResult.empty(assetId, mode, targetLane);
    }

    AssetLifecycleGraph lifecycleGraph = buildLifecycleGraph();
    String rootAssetId = resolveGraphRootAssetId(lifecycleGraph, summary);
    if (!hasValue(rootAssetId)) {
      return CatalogGraphResult.empty(summary.assetId(), mode, targetLane);
    }

    CatalogGraphResult base = buildGraph(lifecycleGraph, rootAssetId, 2, mode, targetLane);
    return switch (mode) {
      case DELETE -> applyDeleteImpact(base, planDelete(rootAssetId, deleteOptions));
      case PROMOTE ->
          applyPromotionImpact(
              base,
              planPromotion(
                  lifecycleGraph, rootAssetId, targetLane, promotionOptions));
      case RELATIONSHIPS ->
          withSummary(base, StitchCatalogImpactSupport.summarizeImpact(base.nodes()));
    };
  }

  private AssetLifecycleGraph buildLifecycleGraph() {
    List<Definition> definitions = requireCache().allDefinitions();
    return AssetLifecycleGraphBuilder.build(definitions == null ? List.of() : definitions);
  }

  private String resolveGraphRootAssetId(AssetLifecycleGraph graph, CatalogSummary summary) {
    if (summary == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String direct = graph.resolveAssetId(summary.assetId());
    if (hasValue(direct)) {
      return direct;
    }
    String group = summary.group();
    String name = summary.name();
    if (hasValue(group) && hasValue(name)) {
      String fromGroupName = graph.resolveAssetId(group + "/" + name);
      if (hasValue(fromGroupName)) {
        return fromGroupName;
      }
    }
    return graph.resolveAssetId(name);
  }

  private CatalogGraphResult buildGraph(
      AssetLifecycleGraph lifecycleGraph,
      String rootAssetId,
      int depth,
      CatalogImpactMode mode,
      String targetLane) {
    int maxDepth = Math.max(1, Math.min(depth, 2));
    ArrayDeque<String> queue = new ArrayDeque<>();
    Map<String, Integer> hopsByAssetId = new HashMap<>();
    Map<String, CatalogGraphNode> nodesByAssetId = new HashMap<>();
    Set<String> visited = new HashSet<>();
    Set<String> edgeIds = new HashSet<>();
    List<CatalogGraphEdge> edges = new ArrayList<>();

    queue.add(rootAssetId);
    hopsByAssetId.put(rootAssetId, 0);
    visited.add(rootAssetId);

    while (!queue.isEmpty()) {
      String currentAssetId = queue.removeFirst();
      int currentHop = hopsByAssetId.getOrDefault(currentAssetId, 0);
      nodesByAssetId.put(
          currentAssetId,
          nodeOf(lifecycleGraph.node(currentAssetId).orElse(null), currentAssetId, currentHop));
      if (currentHop >= maxDepth) {
        continue;
      }
      collectAdjacentEdges(
          lifecycleGraph,
          currentAssetId,
          currentHop,
          maxDepth,
          queue,
          hopsByAssetId,
          visited,
          edgeIds,
          edges);
    }

    List<CatalogGraphNode> nodes =
        nodesByAssetId.values().stream()
            .sorted(
                Comparator.comparingInt(CatalogGraphNode::hop)
                    .thenComparing(CatalogGraphNode::assetId, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
            .toList();
    List<CatalogGraphEdge> sortedEdges =
        edges.stream()
            .sorted(
                Comparator.comparing(CatalogGraphEdge::relationshipType)
                    .thenComparing(CatalogGraphEdge::fromAssetId, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
                    .thenComparing(CatalogGraphEdge::toAssetId, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
            .toList();
    return new CatalogGraphResult(
        rootAssetId,
        mode == null ? CatalogImpactMode.RELATIONSHIPS : mode,
        targetLane == null ? "" : targetLane,
        nodes,
        sortedEdges,
        Map.of(),
        List.of(),
        List.of());
  }

  private void collectAdjacentEdges(
      AssetLifecycleGraph lifecycleGraph,
      String currentAssetId,
      int currentHop,
      int maxDepth,
      ArrayDeque<String> queue,
      Map<String, Integer> hopsByAssetId,
      Set<String> visited,
      Set<String> edgeIds,
      List<CatalogGraphEdge> edges) {
    for (AssetLifecycleEdge edge : lifecycleGraph.outgoing(currentAssetId)) {
      appendGraphEdge(
          edge,
          currentHop,
          maxDepth,
          queue,
          hopsByAssetId,
          visited,
          edgeIds,
          edges,
          edge.toAssetId());
    }
    for (AssetLifecycleEdge edge : lifecycleGraph.incoming(currentAssetId)) {
      appendGraphEdge(
          edge,
          currentHop,
          maxDepth,
          queue,
          hopsByAssetId,
          visited,
          edgeIds,
          edges,
          edge.fromAssetId());
    }
  }

  private void appendGraphEdge(
      AssetLifecycleEdge edge,
      int currentHop,
      int maxDepth,
      ArrayDeque<String> queue,
      Map<String, Integer> hopsByAssetId,
      Set<String> visited,
      Set<String> edgeIds,
      List<CatalogGraphEdge> edges,
      String neighborAssetId) {
    if (edge == null || !hasValue(edge.fromAssetId()) || !hasValue(edge.toAssetId())) {
      return;
    }
    String edgeId = edgeId(edge.relationshipType(), edge.fromAssetId(), edge.toAssetId());
    if (edgeIds.add(edgeId)) {
      edges.add(
          new CatalogGraphEdge(
              edgeId,
              edge.relationshipType() == null ? RelationshipType.REFERENCES : edge.relationshipType(),
              edge.fromAssetId(),
              edge.toAssetId(),
              CatalogImpactState.NONE,
              ""));
    }
    int neighborHop = currentHop + 1;
    if (!hasValue(neighborAssetId) || neighborHop > maxDepth || visited.contains(neighborAssetId)) {
      return;
    }
    visited.add(neighborAssetId);
    hopsByAssetId.put(neighborAssetId, neighborHop);
    queue.addLast(neighborAssetId);
  }

  private CatalogGraphNode nodeOf(AssetLifecycleNode node, String assetId, int hop) {
    if (node == null) {
      return new CatalogGraphNode(
          assetId,
          assetId,
          DefinitionType.UNKNOWN,
          "",
          assetId,
          "",
          hop,
          CatalogImpactState.NONE,
          "",
          "");
    }
    String title = hasValue(node.name()) ? node.name() : node.assetId();
    return new CatalogGraphNode(
        node.assetId(),
        title,
        node.type(),
        node.group(),
        node.name(),
        node.namespace(),
        hop,
        CatalogImpactState.NONE,
        "",
          "");
  }

  private DeletePlan planDelete(String assetId, DeleteOptions options) {
    DeleteOptions resolved = options == null ? DeleteOptions.defaults() : options;
    DeleteManager manager = session.deletes();
    if (manager == null) {
      return new DeletePlan(
          assetId,
          resolved,
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          List.of("Delete planner is unavailable."),
          List.of(),
          List.of());
    }
    return manager.planDelete(assetId, resolved);
  }

  private PromotionPlan planPromotion(
      AssetLifecycleGraph lifecycleGraph, String assetId, String targetLane, PromotionOptions options) {
    PromotionOptions resolved = options == null ? PromotionOptions.defaults() : options;
    String lane = hasValue(targetLane) ? targetLane : "UAT";
    return PromotionPlanner.plan(lifecycleGraph, assetId, lane, null, resolved);
  }

  private CatalogGraphResult applyDeleteImpact(CatalogGraphResult base, DeletePlan plan) {
    Set<String> graphAssets =
        base.nodes().stream().map(CatalogGraphNode::assetId).collect(java.util.stream.Collectors.toSet());
    Set<String> impacted =
        StitchCatalogImpactSupport.normalizeAssetSet(
            plan == null ? null : plan.assetsToDelete(), graphAssets);
    Set<String> detached =
        StitchCatalogImpactSupport.normalizeAssetSet(
            plan == null ? null : plan.assetsToDetach(), graphAssets);
    Set<String> retained =
        StitchCatalogImpactSupport.normalizeAssetSet(
            plan == null ? null : plan.assetsRetained(), graphAssets);
    Set<String> manual =
        StitchCatalogImpactSupport.referencedAssets(
            StitchCatalogImpactSupport.mergeLines(
                plan == null ? null : plan.manualActions(),
                plan == null ? null : plan.storageToDelete(),
                plan == null ? null : plan.historyToDelete()),
            graphAssets);

    Set<String> blockedAssets = new HashSet<>();
    Set<String> blockerPairs = new HashSet<>();
    List<DeleteBlocker> blockerList = plan == null ? List.of() : plan.blockers();
    if (blockerList != null) {
      for (DeleteBlocker blocker : blockerList) {
        if (blocker == null) {
          continue;
        }
        if (graphAssets.contains(blocker.assetId())) {
          blockedAssets.add(blocker.assetId());
        }
        if (graphAssets.contains(blocker.blockedByAssetId())) {
          blockedAssets.add(blocker.blockedByAssetId());
        }
        blockerPairs.add(StitchCatalogImpactSupport.pair(blocker.assetId(), blocker.blockedByAssetId()));
        blockerPairs.add(StitchCatalogImpactSupport.pair(blocker.blockedByAssetId(), blocker.assetId()));
      }
    }

    List<StitchCatalogImpactSupport.StateRule> rules =
        List.of(
            StitchCatalogImpactSupport.stateRule(CatalogImpactState.BLOCKS, blockedAssets),
            StitchCatalogImpactSupport.stateRule(CatalogImpactState.MANUAL, manual),
            StitchCatalogImpactSupport.stateRule(CatalogImpactState.IMPACTED, impacted),
            StitchCatalogImpactSupport.stateRule(CatalogImpactState.DETACHED, detached),
            StitchCatalogImpactSupport.stateRule(CatalogImpactState.RETAINED, retained));
    Map<String, CatalogImpactState> stateByAsset =
        StitchCatalogImpactSupport.resolveAssetStates(base.nodes(), rules, CatalogImpactState.SAFE);
    List<CatalogGraphNode> nodes = StitchCatalogImpactSupport.applyNodeImpact(base.nodes(), stateByAsset);
    List<CatalogGraphEdge> edges =
        StitchCatalogImpactSupport.applyEdgeImpact(
            base.edges(),
            stateByAsset,
            blockerPairs,
            List.of(
                CatalogImpactState.BLOCKS,
                CatalogImpactState.MANUAL,
                CatalogImpactState.IMPACTED,
                CatalogImpactState.DETACHED,
                CatalogImpactState.RETAINED,
                CatalogImpactState.SAFE));
    return new CatalogGraphResult(
        base.rootAssetId(),
        CatalogImpactMode.DELETE,
        base.targetLane(),
        nodes,
        edges,
        StitchCatalogImpactSupport.summarizeImpact(nodes),
        plan == null
            ? List.of()
            : StitchCatalogImpactSupport.mergeLines(plan.warnings(), plan.manualActions()),
        plan == null ? List.of() : plan.executionOrder());
  }

  private CatalogGraphResult applyPromotionImpact(CatalogGraphResult base, PromotionPlan plan) {
    Set<String> graphAssets =
        base.nodes().stream().map(CatalogGraphNode::assetId).collect(java.util.stream.Collectors.toSet());
    Set<String> required =
        StitchCatalogImpactSupport.normalizeAssetSet(
            plan == null ? null : plan.assetsToPromote(), graphAssets);
    Set<String> rebind =
        StitchCatalogImpactSupport.normalizeAssetSet(
            plan == null ? null : plan.assetsToRebind(), graphAssets);
    Set<String> skipped =
        StitchCatalogImpactSupport.normalizeAssetSet(
            plan == null ? null : plan.assetsSkipped(), graphAssets);
    Set<String> optional =
        StitchCatalogImpactSupport.normalizeAssetSet(
            plan == null ? null : plan.sharedAssets(), graphAssets);
    optional.addAll(
        StitchCatalogImpactSupport.normalizeAssetSet(
            plan == null ? null : plan.missingTargetAssets(), graphAssets));

    Set<String> blockedAssets = new HashSet<>();
    Set<String> blockerPairs = new HashSet<>();
    List<PromotionBlocker> blockerList = plan == null ? List.of() : plan.blockers();
    if (blockerList != null) {
      for (PromotionBlocker blocker : blockerList) {
        if (blocker == null) {
          continue;
        }
        if (graphAssets.contains(blocker.assetId())) {
          blockedAssets.add(blocker.assetId());
        }
        if (graphAssets.contains(blocker.blockedByAssetId())) {
          blockedAssets.add(blocker.blockedByAssetId());
        }
        blockerPairs.add(StitchCatalogImpactSupport.pair(blocker.assetId(), blocker.blockedByAssetId()));
        blockerPairs.add(StitchCatalogImpactSupport.pair(blocker.blockedByAssetId(), blocker.assetId()));
      }
    }

    List<StitchCatalogImpactSupport.StateRule> rules =
        List.of(
            StitchCatalogImpactSupport.stateRule(CatalogImpactState.BLOCKS, blockedAssets),
            StitchCatalogImpactSupport.stateRule(CatalogImpactState.REBIND, rebind),
            StitchCatalogImpactSupport.stateRule(CatalogImpactState.REQUIRED, required),
            StitchCatalogImpactSupport.stateRule(CatalogImpactState.OPTIONAL, optional),
            StitchCatalogImpactSupport.stateRule(CatalogImpactState.SKIPPED, skipped));
    Map<String, CatalogImpactState> stateByAsset =
        StitchCatalogImpactSupport.resolveAssetStates(base.nodes(), rules, CatalogImpactState.SAFE);
    List<CatalogGraphNode> nodes = StitchCatalogImpactSupport.applyNodeImpact(base.nodes(), stateByAsset);
    List<CatalogGraphEdge> edges =
        StitchCatalogImpactSupport.applyEdgeImpact(
            base.edges(),
            stateByAsset,
            blockerPairs,
            List.of(
                CatalogImpactState.BLOCKS,
                CatalogImpactState.REBIND,
                CatalogImpactState.REQUIRED,
                CatalogImpactState.OPTIONAL,
                CatalogImpactState.SKIPPED,
                CatalogImpactState.SAFE));
    return new CatalogGraphResult(
        base.rootAssetId(),
        CatalogImpactMode.PROMOTE,
        plan == null ? base.targetLane() : plan.targetLane(),
        nodes,
        edges,
        StitchCatalogImpactSupport.summarizeImpact(nodes),
        plan == null
            ? List.of()
            : StitchCatalogImpactSupport.mergeLines(
                plan.warnings(), plan.missingTargetAssets(), plan.manualActions()),
        plan == null ? List.of() : plan.executionOrder());
  }

  private static CatalogGraphResult withSummary(
      CatalogGraphResult result, Map<CatalogImpactState, Integer> summary) {
    return new CatalogGraphResult(
        result.rootAssetId(),
        result.mode(),
        result.targetLane(),
        result.nodes(),
        result.edges(),
        summary,
        result.warnings(),
        result.executionOrder());
  }

  private static String edgeId(RelationshipType relationshipType, String fromAssetId, String toAssetId) {
    String type = relationshipType == null ? RelationshipType.REFERENCES.name() : relationshipType.name();
    return type + "|" + fromAssetId + "|" + toAssetId;
  }

  private static boolean isEditableType(DefinitionType type) {
    return type == DefinitionType.DATASET
        || type == DefinitionType.SERVICE
        || type == DefinitionType.SCHEMA
        || type == DefinitionType.CONFIG
        || type == DefinitionType.CONFIG_LAYER
        || type == DefinitionType.INGEST
        || type == DefinitionType.STREAM;
  }

  private DiscoveryCache requireCache() {
    DiscoveryCache cache = session.internal().discoveryCache();
    if (cache == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DiscoveryCache is not available");
    }
    return cache;
  }

  private CatalogAccessContext accessContext(String seedAssetId) {
    String subject = StitchIdentityContext.resolveSubject(runtimeContext.settings().sso().fallbackSubject());
    String lane = session.context() == null ? null : session.context().getEnv();
    if (lane != null) {
      lane = lane.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    }
    return new CatalogAccessContext(subject, null, lane, seedAssetId);
  }

  private static List<String> sortedValues(Map<String, Integer> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return values.keySet().stream()
        .filter(StitchCatalogProvider::hasValue)
        .sorted(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
        .toList();
  }

  private static boolean hasValue(String value) {
    return value != null && !value.isBlank();
  }

  private static Semantic emptySemantic() {
    return new Semantic(
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        List.of(),
        List.of(),
        List.of(),
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        List.of());
  }

  public record StitchCatalogQuery(
      String text, String type, String group, List<String> tags, String owner) {
    public StitchCatalogQuery {
      tags = tags == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(tags);
    }
  }

  public record StitchCatalogPaging(int page, int pageSize) {
    public StitchCatalogPaging {
      page = Math.max(0, page);
      pageSize = pageSize <= 0 ? 100 : pageSize;
    }
  }

  public record StitchCatalogPage(List<StitchCatalogRow> rows, int totalCount) {
    public StitchCatalogPage {
      rows = rows == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(rows);
      totalCount = Math.max(0, totalCount);
    }
  }

  public record StitchCatalogFilterOptions(
      List<String> types, List<String> groups, List<String> tags, List<String> owners) {
    public StitchCatalogFilterOptions {
      types = types == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(types);
      groups = groups == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(groups);
      tags = tags == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(tags);
      owners = owners == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(owners);
    }
  }

  public record SemanticAssetLoadResult(
      boolean found,
      boolean editable,
      String message,
      String resolvedAssetId,
      DefinitionType type,
      Semantic semantic,
      CatalogDetails details) {
    public static SemanticAssetLoadResult notFound(String assetId) {
      return new SemanticAssetLoadResult(
          false,
          false,
          "Asset not found or not visible: " + assetId,
          assetId,
          DefinitionType.UNKNOWN,
          emptySemantic(),
          null);
    }
  }

  public record SemanticUpdateResult(
      boolean updated, String message, String resolvedAssetId, CatalogDetails details) {
    public static SemanticUpdateResult failed(String message) {
      return new SemanticUpdateResult(false, message, null, null);
    }
  }

  public enum CatalogImpactMode {
    RELATIONSHIPS,
    DELETE,
    PROMOTE;

    public static CatalogImpactMode fromToken(String value) {
      if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
        return RELATIONSHIPS;
      }
      String normalized = value.trim().toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
      return switch (normalized) {
        case "DELETE" -> DELETE;
        case "PROMOTE" -> PROMOTE;
        default -> RELATIONSHIPS;
      };
    }
  }

  public enum CatalogImpactState {
    NONE,
    BLOCKS,
    IMPACTED,
    SAFE,
    MANUAL,
    REQUIRED,
    REBIND,
    OPTIONAL,
    SKIPPED,
    RETAINED,
    DETACHED
  }

  public record CatalogImpactRequest(
      CatalogImpactMode mode,
      String targetLane,
      DeleteOptions deleteOptions,
      PromotionOptions promotionOptions) {
    public static CatalogImpactRequest defaults() {
      return new CatalogImpactRequest(
          CatalogImpactMode.RELATIONSHIPS, "", DeleteOptions.defaults(), PromotionOptions.defaults());
    }
  }

  public record CatalogGraphNode(
      String assetId,
      String title,
      DefinitionType type,
      String group,
      String name,
      String namespace,
      int hop,
      CatalogImpactState impactState,
      String impactLabel,
      String impactReason) {
    public CatalogGraphNode withImpact(CatalogImpactState state, String label, String reason) {
      return new CatalogGraphNode(
          assetId,
          title,
          type,
          group,
          name,
          namespace,
          hop,
          state,
          label,
          reason);
    }
  }

  public record CatalogGraphEdge(
      String id,
      RelationshipType relationshipType,
      String fromAssetId,
      String toAssetId,
      CatalogImpactState impactState,
      String impactReason) {
    public CatalogGraphEdge withImpact(CatalogImpactState state, String reason) {
      return new CatalogGraphEdge(id, relationshipType, fromAssetId, toAssetId, state, reason);
    }
  }

  public record CatalogGraphResult(
      String rootAssetId,
      CatalogImpactMode mode,
      String targetLane,
      List<CatalogGraphNode> nodes,
      List<CatalogGraphEdge> edges,
      Map<CatalogImpactState, Integer> impactSummary,
      List<String> warnings,
      List<String> executionOrder) {
    public static CatalogGraphResult empty(
        String rootAssetId, CatalogImpactMode mode, String targetLane) {
      return new CatalogGraphResult(
          rootAssetId, mode, targetLane, List.of(), List.of(), Map.of(), List.of(), List.of());
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.catalog;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.details.Details;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.Alignment;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.catalog.CatalogManager.CatalogRelationshipDirection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.catalog.CatalogManager.CatalogRelationshipView;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle.RelationshipType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

final class StitchCatalogRelationshipPanel extends VerticalLayout {
  private Consumer<String> onOpenAsset = assetId -> {};

  StitchCatalogRelationshipPanel() {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(true);
    setWidthFull();
    addClassName("stitch-catalog-relationships");
    getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Catalog relationships grouped by type");
  }

  StitchCatalogRelationshipPanel onOpenAsset(Consumer<String> consumer) {
    onOpenAsset = Objects.requireNonNullElse(consumer, assetId -> {});
    return this;
  }

  void clear(String message) {
    removeAll();
    Span placeholder = new Span(Strings.trimToEmpty(message));
    placeholder.addClassName("stitch-catalog-relationships-empty");
    add(placeholder);
  }

  void setRelationships(
      String currentAssetId, Map<RelationshipType, List<CatalogRelationshipView>> relationshipsByType) {
    removeAll();
    if (relationshipsByType == null || relationshipsByType.isEmpty()) {
      clear("No visible relationships.");
      return;
    }

    relationshipsByType.entrySet().stream()
        .filter(entry -> entry.getKey() != null && entry.getValue() != null && !entry.getValue().isEmpty())
        .sorted(Map.Entry.comparingByKey(Comparator.comparing(RelationshipType::name)))
        .forEach(entry -> add(typeGroup(currentAssetId, entry.getKey(), entry.getValue())));

    if (getComponentCount() == 0) {
      clear("No visible relationships.");
    }
  }

  private Details typeGroup(
      String currentAssetId, RelationshipType type, List<CatalogRelationshipView> relationships) {
    VerticalLayout rows = new VerticalLayout();
    rows.setPadding(false);
    rows.setSpacing(false);
    rows.setWidthFull();

    relationships.stream()
        .filter(Objects::nonNull)
        .sorted(
            Comparator.comparing(
                    StitchCatalogRelationshipPanel::relatedAssetType, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
                .thenComparing(value -> relatedAssetId(currentAssetId, value), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
        .forEach(value -> rows.add(relationshipRow(currentAssetId, value)));

    Details details = new Details(type.name() + " (" + relationships.size() + ")", rows);
    details.setOpened(true);
    details.addClassName("stitch-catalog-relationship-group");
    details.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Relationship type " + type.name());
    return details;
  }

  private HorizontalLayout relationshipRow(String currentAssetId, CatalogRelationshipView relationship) {
    String relatedAssetId = relatedAssetId(currentAssetId, relationship);
    String relatedType = relatedAssetType(relationship);
    String relatedLabel = relatedIdentity(relationship, relatedAssetId);
    String direction =
        relationship.direction() == null
            ? CatalogRelationshipDirection.OUTGOING.name()
            : relationship.direction().name();
    String notes = Strings.trimToEmpty(relationship.notes());

    Span identity = new Span(relatedLabel);
    identity.addClassName("stitch-catalog-relationship-identity");
    Span assetId = new Span(Strings.firstNonBlank(relatedAssetId, "-"));
    assetId.addClassName("stitch-catalog-relationship-asset-id");

    Span directionChip = new Span(direction);
    directionChip.addClassName("stitch-catalog-relationship-chip");
    Span typeChip = new Span(relatedType);
    typeChip.addClassName("stitch-catalog-relationship-chip");
    HorizontalLayout chips = new HorizontalLayout(directionChip, typeChip);
    chips.setPadding(false);
    chips.setSpacing(true);
    chips.addClassName("stitch-catalog-relationship-chips");

    VerticalLayout text = new VerticalLayout(identity, assetId, chips);
    text.setPadding(false);
    text.setSpacing(true);
    text.setWidthFull();
    text.addClassName("stitch-catalog-relationship-text");

    if (!notes.isBlank()) {
      Span notesText = new Span(notes);
      notesText.addClassName("stitch-catalog-relationship-notes-text");
      Div notesBody = new Div(notesText);
      notesBody.addClassName("stitch-catalog-relationship-notes-body");
      Details notesDetails = new Details("Notes", notesBody);
      notesDetails.addClassName("stitch-catalog-relationship-notes");
      text.add(notesDetails);
    }

    Button open = new Button("OPEN");
    open.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY_INLINE);
    open.addClassName("stitch-catalog-relationship-open");
    open.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Open related catalog asset " + relatedAssetId);
    open.setEnabled(hasValue(relatedAssetId));
    open.addClickListener(event -> onOpenAsset.accept(relatedAssetId));

    HorizontalLayout row = new HorizontalLayout(text, open);
    row.setPadding(false);
    row.setSpacing(true);
    row.setWidthFull();
    row.setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.START);
    row.addClassName("stitch-catalog-relationship-row");
    return row;
  }

  private static String relatedAssetId(String currentAssetId, CatalogRelationshipView relationship) {
    String fromAssetId = Strings.trimToNull(relationship.fromAssetId());
    String toAssetId = Strings.trimToNull(relationship.toAssetId());
    String current = Strings.trimToNull(currentAssetId);
    if (current != null) {
      if (current.equals(fromAssetId) && toAssetId != null) {
        return toAssetId;
      }
      if (current.equals(toAssetId) && fromAssetId != null) {
        return fromAssetId;
      }
    }
    CatalogRelationshipDirection direction = relationship.direction();
    if (direction == CatalogRelationshipDirection.INCOMING && fromAssetId != null) {
      return fromAssetId;
    }
    return toAssetId == null ? fromAssetId : toAssetId;
  }

  private static String relatedAssetType(CatalogRelationshipView relationship) {
    return relationship.relatedAssetType() == null ? "-" : relationship.relatedAssetType().name();
  }

  private static String relatedIdentity(CatalogRelationshipView relationship, String relatedAssetId) {
    String group = Strings.trimToNull(relationship.relatedAssetGroup());
    String namespace = Strings.trimToNull(relationship.relatedAssetNamespace());
    String name = Strings.trimToNull(relationship.relatedAssetName());
    if (group == null || name == null) {
      return Strings.firstNonBlank(relatedAssetId, "-");
    }
    return namespace == null ? group + "/" + name : group + "/" + namespace + "/" + name;
  }

  private static boolean hasValue(String value) {
    return value != null && !value.isBlank();
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/catalog/StitchCatalogRow.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.catalog;

import java.util.List;

public record StitchCatalogRow(
    String assetId,
    String type,
    String group,
    String name,
    String namespace,
    String description,
    List<String> tags,
    String owner,
    String trustScore,
    String freshness,
    String summary,
    String updatedTimeUtc) {

  public StitchCatalogRow {
    assetId = value(assetId);
    type = value(type);
    group = value(group);
    name = value(name);
    namespace = value(namespace);
    description = value(description);
    tags = tags == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(tags);
    owner = value(owner);
    trustScore = value(trustScore);
    freshness = value(freshness);
    summary = value(summary);
    updatedTimeUtc = value(updatedTimeUtc);
  }

  private static String value(String value) {
    return value == null ? "" : value;
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/catalog/StitchCatalogScreenConfig.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.catalog;

public final class StitchCatalogScreenConfig {
  private final String id;
  private final String label;
  private final String routePath;
  private final String pageTitle;
  private final String pageSubtitle;
  private final int order;
  private final boolean enabled;

  private StitchCatalogScreenConfig(Builder builder) {
    this.id = require(builder.id, "id");
    this.label = require(builder.label, "label");
    this.routePath = require(builder.routePath, "routePath");
    this.pageTitle = require(builder.pageTitle, "pageTitle");
    this.pageSubtitle = optional(builder.pageSubtitle);
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.enabled = builder.enabled;
  }

  public static Builder builder(String id) {
    return new Builder(id);
  }

  public String id() {
    return id;
  }

  public String label() {
    return label;
  }

  public String routePath() {
    return routePath;
  }

  public String pageTitle() {
    return pageTitle;
  }

  public String pageSubtitle() {
    return pageSubtitle;
  }

  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public boolean enabled() {
    return enabled;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final String id;
    private String label;
    private String routePath;
    private String pageTitle;
    private String pageSubtitle;
    private int order;
    private boolean enabled = true;

    private Builder(String id) {
      this.id = require(id, "id");
      this.label = "Catalog";
      this.routePath = "catalog";
      this.pageTitle = "Catalog";
      this.pageSubtitle = "Search and inspect catalog semantic metadata.";
      this.order = 10;
    }

    public Builder withLabel(String value) {
      this.label = require(value, "label");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRoutePath(String value) {
      this.routePath = require(value, "routePath");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageTitle(String value) {
      this.pageTitle = require(value, "pageTitle");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageSubtitle(String value) {
      this.pageSubtitle = optional(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.enabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public StitchCatalogScreenConfig build() {
      return new StitchCatalogScreenConfig(this);
    }
  }
}

import com.vaadin.flow.component.HasValue;

final class StitchCatalogSemanticEditorPanel extends VerticalLayout {

  private final TextField ownerId = field("Owner");
  private final TextField stewardId = field("Steward");
  private final TextField teamId = field("Team");
  private final TextArea contacts = area("Contacts (comma or newline)", "4.5rem");

  private final ComboBox<Semantic.Certification> certification = combo("Certification", Semantic.Certification.values());
  private final ComboBox<Semantic.QualityStatus> qualityStatus = combo("Quality Status", Semantic.QualityStatus.values());
  private final TextField sourceOfTruth = field("Source of Truth");
  private final TextArea usageRestrictions = area("Usage Restrictions", "4.5rem");

  private final TextField updateCadence = field("Freshness Cadence");
  private final TextField freshnessSla = field("Freshness SLA");
  private final TextField latencyClass = field("Latency Class");

  private final TextArea usageHints = area("Usage Hints", "4.5rem");
  private final TextArea exampleQuestions = area("Example Questions", "4.5rem");

  private final ComboBox<Semantic.ActionClass> actionClass = combo("Action Class", Semantic.ActionClass.values());
  private final Checkbox readOnly = new Checkbox("Read-only");
  private final Checkbox idempotent = new Checkbox("Idempotent");

  private final ComboBox<Semantic.Type> dataShapeType = combo("Data Shape Type", Semantic.Type.values());
  private final TextField grain = field("Dataset Grain");

  private final VerticalLayout usageSection = section("Usage");
  private final VerticalLayout serviceSection = section("Service Tool Hints");
  private final VerticalLayout datasetSection = section("Dataset Shape");

  private final List<HasEnabled> editableInputs =
      List.of(
          title,
          description,
          businessMeaning,
          domain,
          subdomain,
          tags,
          aliases,
          keywords,
          ownerId,
          stewardId,
          teamId,
          contacts,
          certification,
          qualityStatus,
          sourceOfTruth,
          usageRestrictions,
          updateCadence,
          freshnessSla,
          latencyClass,
          usageHints,
          exampleQuestions,
          actionClass,
          readOnly,
          idempotent,
          dataShapeType,
          grain);

  private Runnable onChange = () -> {};
  private Semantic baseline = emptySemantic();
  private DefinitionType currentType = DefinitionType.UNKNOWN;
  private boolean typeEditable;
  private boolean suppressEvents;

  StitchCatalogSemanticEditorPanel() {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(true);
    setWidthFull();
    addClassName("stitch-catalog-semantic-fields");
    getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Catalog semantic metadata editor");
    status.addClassName("stitch-catalog-semantic-status");

    status.getElement().setAttribute("aria-live", "polite");

    usageSection.add(form(
        usageHints,
        2,
        exampleQuestions,
        2));
    serviceSection.add(form(actionClass, 1, readOnly, 1, idempotent, 1));
    datasetSection.add(form(dataShapeType, 1, grain, 1));

    add(
        status,
        h4("Core"),
        form(title, 1, domain, 1, description, 2, subdomain, 1, businessMeaning, 2, tags, 2, aliases, 2, keywords, 2),
        h4("Ownership"),
        form(ownerId, 1, stewardId, 1, teamId, 1, contacts, 2),
        h4("Trust"),
        form(certification, 1, qualityStatus, 1, sourceOfTruth, 1, usageRestrictions, 2),
        h4("Freshness"),
        form(updateCadence, 1, freshnessSla, 1, latencyClass, 1),
        usageSection,
        serviceSection,
        datasetSection);

    watchAll(
        title,
        description,
        businessMeaning,
        domain,
        subdomain,
        tags,
        aliases,
        keywords,
        ownerId,
        stewardId,
        teamId,
        contacts,

        qualityStatus,

        usageRestrictions,
        updateCadence,
        freshnessSla,
        latencyClass,
        usageHints,
        exampleQuestions,
        actionClass,
        readOnly,
        idempotent,
        dataShapeType,
        grain);
  }

  StitchCatalogSemanticEditorPanel onChange(Runnable callback) {
    onChange = Objects.requireNonNullElse(callback, () -> {});
    return this;
  }

  void setSemantic(Semantic semantic, DefinitionType type, boolean editableType) {
    suppressEvents = true;
    baseline = semantic == null ? emptySemantic() : semantic;
    currentType = type == null ? DefinitionType.UNKNOWN : type;
    typeEditable = editableType;

    title.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(baseline.title()));
    description.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(baseline.description()));
    businessMeaning.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(baseline.businessMeaning()));
    domain.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(baseline.domain()));
    subdomain.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(baseline.subdomain()));
    tags.setValue(joinList(baseline.tags()));
    aliases.setValue(joinList(baseline.aliases()));
    keywords.setValue(joinList(baseline.keywords()));

    Semantic.Ownership ownership = baseline.ownership();
    ownerId.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(ownership == null ? null : ownership.ownerId()));
    stewardId.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(ownership == null ? null : ownership.stewardId()));
    teamId.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(ownership == null ? null : ownership.teamId()));
    contacts.setValue(joinList(ownership == null ? List.of() : ownership.contactIds()));

    Semantic.Trust trust = baseline.trust();
    certification.setValue(trust == null ? Semantic.Certification.NONE : trust.certification());
    qualityStatus.setValue(trust == null ? Semantic.QualityStatus.UNKNOWN : trust.qualityStatus());
    sourceOfTruth.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(trust == null ? null : trust.sourceOfTruth()));
    usageRestrictions.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(trust == null ? null : trust.usageRestrictions()));

    Semantic.Freshness freshness = baseline.freshness();
    updateCadence.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(freshness == null ? null : freshness.updateCadence()));
    freshnessSla.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(freshness == null ? null : freshness.freshnessSla()));
    latencyClass.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(freshness == null ? null : freshness.latencyClass()));

    Semantic.Usage usage = baseline.usage();
    usageHints.setValue(joinList(usage == null ? List.of() : usage.usageHints()));
    exampleQuestions.setValue(joinList(usage == null ? List.of() : usage.exampleQuestions()));

    Semantic.ToolHints toolHints = baseline.toolHints();
    actionClass.setValue(toolHints == null ? Semantic.ActionClass.READ : toolHints.actionClass());
    readOnly.setValue(toolHints != null && Boolean.TRUE.equals(toolHints.readOnly()));
    idempotent.setValue(toolHints != null && Boolean.TRUE.equals(toolHints.idempotent()));

    Semantic.DataShape shape = baseline.dataShape();
    dataShapeType.setValue(shape == null ? Semantic.Type.DOCUMENT : shape.type());
    grain.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(shape == null ? null : shape.grain()));

    usageSection.setVisible(currentType != DefinitionType.CONFIG && currentType != DefinitionType.CONFIG_LAYER);
    serviceSection.setVisible(currentType == DefinitionType.SERVICE);
    datasetSection.setVisible(currentType == DefinitionType.DATASET);
    setEditable(false);
    suppressEvents = false;
  }

  void setEditable(boolean editable) {
    boolean enabled = editable && typeEditable;
    for (HasEnabled input : editableInputs) {
      input.setEnabled(enabled);
    }
    status.setText(
        !typeEditable
            ? "Semantic metadata is read-only for this asset type."
            : (enabled
                ? "Editing semantic metadata."
                : "Click EDIT to modify semantic metadata."));
  }

  Semantic semantic() {
    Semantic base = baseline == null ? emptySemantic() : baseline;
    Semantic.Usage baseUsage = base.usage();
    Semantic.ToolHints baseToolHints = base.toolHints();
    Semantic.DataShape baseShape = base.dataShape();

    Semantic.Usage usage =
        new Semantic.Usage(
            parseList(exampleQuestions.getValue()),
            baseUsage == null ? List.of() : baseUsage.exampleQueries(),
            parseList(usageHints.getValue()),
            baseUsage == null ? List.of() : baseUsage.knownPitfalls());

    Semantic.ToolHints toolHints =
        new Semantic.ToolHints(
            actionClass.getValue(),
            readOnly.getValue(),
            idempotent.getValue(),
            baseToolHints == null ? null : baseToolHints.safeDefaultLimit(),
            baseToolHints == null ? null : baseToolHints.safeDefaultTimeout(),
            baseToolHints == null ? null : baseToolHints.riskClass());

    Semantic.DataShape dataShape =
        new Semantic.DataShape(
            dataShapeType.getValue(),
            Strings.trimToNull(grain.getValue()),
            baseShape == null ? List.of() : baseShape.keyFields(),
            baseShape == null ? List.of() : baseShape.timeFields(),
            baseShape == null ? List.of() : baseShape.measureFields(),
            baseShape == null ? List.of() : baseShape.dimensionFields(),
            baseShape == null ? List.of() : baseShape.fieldRoles());

    return new Semantic(
        Strings.trimToNull(title.getValue()),
        Strings.trimToNull(description.getValue()),
        Strings.trimToNull(businessMeaning.getValue()),
        Strings.trimToNull(domain.getValue()),
        Strings.trimToNull(subdomain.getValue()),
        parseList(tags.getValue()),
        parseList(aliases.getValue()),
        parseList(keywords.getValue()),
        new Semantic.Ownership(
            Strings.trimToNull(ownerId.getValue()),
            Strings.trimToNull(stewardId.getValue()),
            Strings.trimToNull(teamId.getValue()),
            parseList(contacts.getValue())),
        currentType == DefinitionType.DATASET ? dataShape : base.dataShape(),
        new Semantic.Freshness(
            Strings.trimToNull(updateCadence.getValue()),
            Strings.trimToNull(freshnessSla.getValue()),
            Strings.trimToNull(latencyClass.getValue())),
        new Semantic.Trust(
            certification.getValue(),
            qualityStatus.getValue(),
            Strings.trimToNull(sourceOfTruth.getValue()),
            Strings.trimToNull(usageRestrictions.getValue())),
        currentType == DefinitionType.CONFIG || currentType == DefinitionType.CONFIG_LAYER
            ? base.usage()
            : usage,
        currentType == DefinitionType.SERVICE ? toolHints : base.toolHints(),
        base.relationshipHints());
  }

  @SafeVarargs
  private final void watchAll(HasValue<?, ?>... fields) {
    for (HasValue<?, ?> field : fields) {
      watch(field);
    }
  }

  @SuppressWarnings({"rawtypes", "unchecked"})
  private void watch(HasValue<?, ?> field) {
    HasValue rawField = field;
    rawField.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!suppressEvents && event.isFromClient()) {
            onChange.run();
          }
        });
  }

  private static TextField field(String label) {
    TextField value = new TextField(label);
    value.setWidthFull();
    return value;
  }

  private static TextArea area(String label, String minHeight) {
    TextArea value = new TextArea(label);
    value.setWidthFull();
    value.setMinHeight(minHeight);
    return value;
  }

  @SafeVarargs
  private static <T extends Enum<T>> ComboBox<T> combo(String label, T... values) {
    ComboBox<T> combo = new ComboBox<>(label);
    combo.setItems(values);
    combo.setWidthFull();
    return combo;
  }

  private static H4 h4(String title) {
    H4 heading = new H4(title);
    heading.addClassName("stitch-catalog-semantic-heading");
    heading.getStyle().set("margin", "0.2rem 0");
    return heading;
  }

  private static VerticalLayout section(String title) {
    VerticalLayout section = new VerticalLayout(h4(title));
    section.setPadding(false);
    section.setSpacing(false);
    section.setWidthFull();
    section.addClassName("stitch-catalog-semantic-section");
    return section;
  }

  private static FormLayout form(Object... valuesAndSpans) {
    FormLayout form = new FormLayout();
    form.setWidthFull();
    form.setResponsiveSteps(
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("0", 1), new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("44em", 2));
    for (int i = 0; i < valuesAndSpans.length; i += 2) {
      com.vaadin.flow.component.Component field = (com.vaadin.flow.component.Component) valuesAndSpans[i];
      int span = (Integer) valuesAndSpans[i + 1];
      form.add(field);
      if (span > 1) {
        form.setColspan(field, span);
      }
    }
    return form;
  }

  private static String joinList(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return "";
    }
    return values.stream()
        .map(Strings::trimToNull)
        .filter(Objects::nonNull)
        .distinct()
        .reduce((left, right) -> left + "\n" + right)
        .orElse("");
  }

  private static List<String> parseList(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> values = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String token : normalized.replace('\r', '\n').split("[,\n]")) {
      String cleaned = Strings.trimToNull(token);
      if (cleaned != null) {
        values.add(cleaned);
      }
    }
    return values.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(values);
  }

  private static Semantic emptySemantic() {
    return new Semantic(
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        List.of(),
        List.of(),
        List.of(),
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        List.of());
  }
}
