package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.configs;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.ComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification.Position;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchJsonDiffDialog;

/** Configs compare orchestration using shared Stitch JSON diff dialog. */
public final class StitchConfigCompareDialog {
  private StitchConfigCompareDialog() {}

  public static StitchJsonDiffDialog compareToLive(
      String context,
      String selectedLabel,
      JsonNode selectedPayload,
      String liveLabel,
      JsonNode livePayload) {
    String title =
        Strings.trimToNull(context) == null ? "Compare To Live" : "Compare To Live - " + context.trim();
    return new StitchJsonDiffDialog(
        title,
        Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(liveLabel), "Live"),
        livePayload,
        Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(selectedLabel), "Selected Layer"),
        selectedPayload);
  }

  public static StitchDialog compareToLayer(
      String context,
      String selectedLabel,
      JsonNode selectedPayload,
      List<CompareTarget> candidates) {
    List<CompareTarget> options = candidates == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(candidates);
    if (options.isEmpty()) {
      return new StitchJsonDiffDialog(
          "Compare Layers",
          "Selected Layer",
          selectedPayload,
          "Other Layer",
          DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode());
    }
    if (options.size() == 1) {
      CompareTarget only = options.get(0);
      return new StitchJsonDiffDialog(
          "Compare Layers",
          Strings.firstNonBlank(only.label(), only.id()),
          only.payload(),
          Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(selectedLabel), "Selected Layer"),
          selectedPayload);
    }

    StitchDialog picker = new StitchDialog("Choose Layer To Compare");
    picker.withJsonPayloadSupplier(
        () ->
            java.util.Map.of(
                "context", Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(context), ""),
                "candidateCount", options.size()));

    VerticalLayout body = new VerticalLayout();
    body.setPadding(false);
    body.setSpacing(true);
    body.setWidthFull();

    String normalizedContext = Strings.trimToNull(context);
    if (normalizedContext != null) {
      body.add(new Span(normalizedContext));
    }

    ComboBox<CompareTarget> selector = new ComboBox<>("Compare Selected Layer To");
    selector.setItems(options);
    selector.setItemLabelGenerator(item -> item == null ? "" : Strings.firstNonBlank(item.label(), item.id()));
    selector.setWidthFull();
    selector.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    selector.setAriaLabel("Choose a config layer to compare against the selected layer");
    selector.setValue(options.get(0));
    body.add(selector);

    picker.addToBody(body);
    picker.addPrimaryAction(
        "OPEN",
        () -> {
          CompareTarget target = selector.getValue();
          if (target == null) {
            Notification.show("Choose a layer to compare.", 1400, Position.BOTTOM_START);
            return;
          }
          new StitchJsonDiffDialog(
                  "Compare Layers",
                  Strings.firstNonBlank(target.label(), target.id()),
                  target.payload(),
                  Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(selectedLabel), "Selected Layer"),
                  selectedPayload)
              .open();
          picker.close();
        });
    picker.addSecondaryAction("Close", picker::close);
    return picker;
  }

  public record CompareTarget(String id, String label, JsonNode payload) {}
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/configs/StitchConfigDagDialog.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.configs;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.checkbox.Checkbox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.Grid;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.GridVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Pre;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import java.util.ArrayDeque;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.HashSet;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Queue;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchEmptyState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSummaryStrip;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchTabbedDetailsPanel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialog;

/** Read-only DAG dialog for Configs layer trees. */
public final class StitchConfigDagDialog extends StitchDialog {
  private final StitchConfigsProvider provider;
  private final Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> layersByPath;
  private final String selectedLayerId;
  private final Checkbox selectedPathOnly = new Checkbox("Selected Path Only");
  private final StitchSummaryStrip summaryStrip = new StitchSummaryStrip();
  private final Div graphHost = new Div();
  private final Div graphCanvas = new Div();
  private final Grid<StitchConfigsProvider.DagNode> nodesGrid = new Grid<>(StitchConfigsProvider.DagNode.class, false);
  private final Grid<StitchConfigsProvider.DagEdge> edgesGrid = new Grid<>(StitchConfigsProvider.DagEdge.class, false);
  private final Pre adjacency = new Pre();

  public StitchConfigDagDialog(
      String title,
      StitchConfigsProvider provider,
      Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> layersByPath,
      String selectedLayerId) {
    super(title == null || title.isBlank() ? "Config DAG" : title.trim(), false);
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.layersByPath = layersByPath == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(layersByPath);
    this.selectedLayerId = Strings.trimToNull(selectedLayerId);

    setWidth("1120px");
    setMaxWidth("98vw");
    setTop("6vh");

    selectedPathOnly.setValue(false);
    selectedPathOnly.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Show selected path only");
    selectedPathOnly.addValueChangeListener(event -> refresh());

    HorizontalLayout controls = new HorizontalLayout(selectedPathOnly);
    controls.setPadding(false);
    controls.setSpacing(true);
    controls.setWidthFull();

    configureNodesGrid();
    configureEdgesGrid();
    configureGraphHost();

    StitchTabbedDetailsPanel tabs = new StitchTabbedDetailsPanel();
    tabs.addTab("graph", "Graph", graphHost)
        .addTab("nodes", "Nodes", nodesGrid)
        .addTab("edges", "Edges", edgesGrid)
        .addTab("adjacency", "Adjacency", adjacency)
        .selectTab("graph");

    VerticalLayout bodyContent = new VerticalLayout(summaryStrip, controls, tabs);
    bodyContent.setPadding(false);
    bodyContent.setSpacing(true);
    bodyContent.setWidthFull();
    bodyContent.setSizeFull();

    addToBody(bodyContent);
    addSecondaryAction("Close", this::close);
    refresh();
  }

  private void refresh() {
    StitchConfigsProvider.DagModel model =
        provider.buildDagModel(layersByPath, selectedLayerId, selectedPathOnly.getValue());
    renderGraph(model);
    nodesGrid.setItems(model.nodes());
    edgesGrid.setItems(model.edges());
    adjacency.setText(adjacencyText(model));
    adjacency.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Config DAG adjacency list");

    LinkedHashMap<String, String> summary = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    summary.put("Nodes", String.valueOf(model.nodes().size()));
    summary.put("Edges", String.valueOf(model.edges().size()));
    summary.put("Selected", Strings.firstNonBlank(selectedLayerId, "-"));
    summary.put("Path Nodes", String.valueOf(model.selectedPath().size()));
    summaryStrip.setItems(summary);
  }

  private void configureGraphHost() {
    graphHost.addClassName("stitch-config-dag-graph-host");
    graphHost.setWidthFull();
    graphHost.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Config DAG graph");
    graphCanvas.addClassName("stitch-config-dag-graph-canvas");
    graphHost.add(graphCanvas);
  }

  private void configureNodesGrid() {
    nodesGrid.setWidthFull();
    nodesGrid.setHeight("22rem");
    nodesGrid.addThemeVariants(GridVariant.LUMO_COMPACT, GridVariant.LUMO_ROW_STRIPES);
    nodesGrid.addColumn(StitchConfigsProvider.DagNode::id).setHeader("Layer ID").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    nodesGrid.addColumn(StitchConfigsProvider.DagNode::label).setHeader("Label").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(1);
    nodesGrid.addColumn(node -> node.kind().name()).setHeader("Kind").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    nodesGrid
        .addColumn(node -> Strings.firstNonBlank(node.parentId(), "(root)"))
        .setHeader("Parent")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setFlexGrow(0);
    nodesGrid.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Config layer DAG nodes");
  }

  private void configureEdgesGrid() {
    edgesGrid.setWidthFull();
    edgesGrid.setHeight("22rem");
    edgesGrid.addThemeVariants(GridVariant.LUMO_COMPACT, GridVariant.LUMO_ROW_STRIPES);
    edgesGrid.addColumn(StitchConfigsProvider.DagEdge::fromId).setHeader("Parent").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(1);
    edgesGrid.addColumn(StitchConfigsProvider.DagEdge::toId).setHeader("Child").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(1);
    edgesGrid.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Config layer DAG edges");
  }

  private void renderGraph(StitchConfigsProvider.DagModel model) {
    graphHost.removeAll();
    graphCanvas.removeAll();
    if (model == null || model.nodes().isEmpty()) {
      graphHost.add(
          new StitchEmptyState("No DAG graph available", "No nodes are available for this config."));
      return;
    }

    Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.DagNode> nodesById = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (StitchConfigsProvider.DagNode node : model.nodes()) {
      if (node == null || Strings.trimToNull(node.id()) == null) {
        continue;
      }
      nodesById.put(node.id(), node);
    }
    if (nodesById.isEmpty()) {
      graphHost.add(new StitchEmptyState("No DAG graph available", "No nodes are available for this config."));
      return;
    }

    Map<String, List<String>> childrenByParent = new HashMap<>();
    Map<String, Integer> inDegree = new HashMap<>();
    for (String nodeId : nodesById.keySet()) {
      childrenByParent.put(nodeId, new ArrayList<>());
      inDegree.put(nodeId, 0);
    }
    for (StitchConfigsProvider.DagEdge edge : model.edges()) {
      if (edge == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String from = Strings.trimToNull(edge.fromId());
      String to = Strings.trimToNull(edge.toId());
      if (from == null || to == null || !nodesById.containsKey(from) || !nodesById.containsKey(to)) {
        continue;
      }
      childrenByParent.computeIfAbsent(from, ignored -> new ArrayList<>()).add(to);
      inDegree.compute(to, (ignored, value) -> value == null ? 1 : value + 1);
    }

    List<String> roots = new ArrayList<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, Integer> entry : inDegree.entrySet()) {
      if (entry.getValue() == 0) {
        roots.add(entry.getKey());
      }
    }
    if (roots.isEmpty()) {
      roots.addAll(nodesById.keySet());
    }

    Map<String, Integer> depthById = new HashMap<>();
    Queue<String> queue = new ArrayDeque<>();
    Set<String> visited = new HashSet<>();
    for (String root : roots) {
      depthById.put(root, 0);
      queue.add(root);
      visited.add(root);
    }
    while (!queue.isEmpty()) {
      String current = queue.remove();
      int currentDepth = depthById.getOrDefault(current, 0);
      for (String child : childrenByParent.getOrDefault(current, List.of())) {
        int nextDepth = currentDepth + 1;
        Integer existing = depthById.get(child);
        if (existing == null || nextDepth > existing) {
          depthById.put(child, nextDepth);
        }
        if (visited.add(child)) {
          queue.add(child);
        }
      }
    }
    int maxDepth = depthById.values().stream().mapToInt(Integer::intValue).max().orElse(0);
    for (String nodeId : nodesById.keySet()) {
      if (!depthById.containsKey(nodeId)) {
        maxDepth++;
        depthById.put(nodeId, maxDepth);
      }
    }

    Map<Integer, List<StitchConfigsProvider.DagNode>> byDepth = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (StitchConfigsProvider.DagNode node : nodesById.values()) {
      int depth = depthById.getOrDefault(node.id(), 0);
      byDepth.computeIfAbsent(depth, ignored -> new ArrayList<>()).add(node);
    }
    for (List<StitchConfigsProvider.DagNode> levelNodes : byDepth.values()) {
      levelNodes.sort(
          java.util.Comparator.comparing(
              dagNode -> Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(dagNode.label()), dagNode.id()),
              String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER));
    }

    final int nodeWidth = 172;
    final int nodeHeight = 46;
    final int columnGap = 214;
    final int rowGap = 82;
    final int padX = 34;
    final int padY = 30;
    int maxRows = byDepth.values().stream().mapToInt(List::size).max().orElse(1);
    int canvasWidth = padX * 2 + (maxDepth * columnGap) + nodeWidth;
    int canvasHeight = padY * 2 + ((Math.max(1, maxRows) - 1) * rowGap) + nodeHeight;
    graphCanvas.getStyle().set("width", canvasWidth + "px");
    graphCanvas.getStyle().set("height", canvasHeight + "px");
    graphCanvas.getElement().setAttribute("data-base-width", String.valueOf(canvasWidth));
    graphCanvas.getElement().setAttribute("data-base-height", String.valueOf(canvasHeight));

    Map<String, DagNodePosition> positions = new HashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<Integer, List<StitchConfigsProvider.DagNode>> entry : byDepth.entrySet()) {
      int depth = entry.getKey();
      List<StitchConfigsProvider.DagNode> levelNodes = entry.getValue();
      int levelHeight = ((Math.max(1, levelNodes.size()) - 1) * rowGap) + nodeHeight;
      int startY = padY + Math.max(0, ((canvasHeight - (padY * 2)) - levelHeight) / 2);
      for (int index = 0; index < levelNodes.size(); index++) {
        StitchConfigsProvider.DagNode node = levelNodes.get(index);
        int left = padX + (depth * columnGap);
        int top = startY + (index * rowGap);
        positions.put(node.id(), new DagNodePosition(left, top));
      }
    }

    Set<String> selectedPath = new LinkedHashSet<>(model.selectedPath());
    for (StitchConfigsProvider.DagEdge edge : model.edges()) {
      if (edge == null) {
        continue;
      }
      DagNodePosition from = positions.get(edge.fromId());
      DagNodePosition to = positions.get(edge.toId());
      if (from == null || to == null) {
        continue;
      }
      Div line = new Div();
      line.addClassName("stitch-config-dag-edge-line");
      if (selectedPath.contains(edge.fromId()) && selectedPath.contains(edge.toId())) {
        line.addClassName("stitch-config-dag-edge-line-selected");
      }
      double startX = from.left() + nodeWidth;
      double startY = from.top() + (nodeHeight / 2.0d);
      double endX = to.left();
      double endY = to.top() + (nodeHeight / 2.0d);
      double dx = endX - startX;
      double dy = endY - startY;
      double length = Math.hypot(dx, dy);
      double angle = Math.toDegrees(Math.atan2(dy, dx));
      line.getStyle().set("left", startX + "px");
      line.getStyle().set("top", startY + "px");
      line.getStyle().set("width", Math.max(1.0d, length) + "px");
      line.getStyle().set("transform", "rotate(" + angle + "deg)");
      graphCanvas.add(line);
    }

    for (StitchConfigsProvider.DagNode node : model.nodes()) {
      DagNodePosition position = positions.get(node.id());
      if (position == null) {
        continue;
      }
      Div nodeChip = new Div();
      nodeChip.addClassName("stitch-config-dag-node");
      nodeChip.addClassName("stitch-config-dag-node--" + node.kind().name().toLowerCase(java.util.Locale.ROOT));
      if (selectedPath.contains(node.id())) {
        nodeChip.addClassName("stitch-config-dag-node--selected-path");
      }
      nodeChip.getStyle().set("left", position.left() + "px");
      nodeChip.getStyle().set("top", position.top() + "px");

      Span label = new Span(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(node.label()), node.id()));
      label.addClassName("stitch-config-dag-node-label");
      Span id = new Span(node.id());
      id.addClassName("stitch-config-dag-node-id");
      nodeChip.add(label, id);
      nodeChip.getElement().setAttribute("title", node.id() + " (" + node.kind().name() + ")");
      graphCanvas.add(nodeChip);
    }

    graphHost.add(graphCanvas);
    applyGraphViewportFit();
  }

  private void applyGraphViewportFit() {
    graphHost
        .getElement()
        .executeJs(
            """
            const host = this;
            const canvas = $0;
            if (!host || !canvas) {
              return;
            }
            const baseWidth = Number.parseFloat(canvas.getAttribute('data-base-width')) || canvas.offsetWidth || 1;
            const baseHeight = Number.parseFloat(canvas.getAttribute('data-base-height')) || canvas.offsetHeight || 1;
            const minScale = 0.62;
            const fitPadding = 28;
            const applyFit = () => {
              const availableWidth = Math.max(120, host.clientWidth - (fitPadding * 2));
              const availableHeight = Math.max(120, host.clientHeight - (fitPadding * 2));
              let scale = Math.min(availableWidth / baseWidth, availableHeight / baseHeight);
              if (!Number.isFinite(scale) || scale <= 0) {
                scale = 1;
              }
              scale = Math.max(minScale, Math.min(1, scale));
              canvas.style.transformOrigin = 'top left';
              canvas.style.transform = `scale(${scale})`;
              const scaledWidth = baseWidth * scale;
              const scaledHeight = baseHeight * scale;
              host.scrollLeft = Math.max(0, Math.round((baseWidth - scaledWidth) / 2));
              host.scrollTop = Math.max(0, Math.round((baseHeight - scaledHeight) / 2));
            };
            requestAnimationFrame(() => requestAnimationFrame(applyFit));
            """,
            graphCanvas.getElement());
  }

  private static String adjacencyText(StitchConfigsProvider.DagModel model) {
    if (model == null || model.edges().isEmpty()) {
      return "No DAG edges available.";
    }
    StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder();
    for (StitchConfigsProvider.DagEdge edge : model.edges()) {
      if (edge == null) {
        continue;
      }
      builder
          .append(Strings.firstNonBlank(edge.fromId(), "-"))
          .append(" -> ")
          .append(Strings.firstNonBlank(edge.toId(), "-"))
          .append(System.lineSeparator());
    }
    return builder.length() == 0 ? "No DAG edges available." : builder.toString();
  }

  private record DagNodePosition(int left, int top) {}
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/configs/StitchConfigJsonModesDialog.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.configs;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.ComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification.Position;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.Alignment;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextArea;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextField;
import com.vaadin.flow.server.StreamResource;
import java.io.ByteArrayInputStream;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.stream.Collectors;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;

/** Read-only JSON modes dialog for Configs view parity. */
public final class StitchConfigJsonModesDialog extends StitchDialog {
  private final StitchConfigsProvider provider;
  private final String group;
  private final String configName;
  private final StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord selectedLayer;
  private final StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView selectedLayerView;
  private final Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> layersByPath;
  private ConfigManager.ConfigCodegen lastCodegen;

  public StitchConfigJsonModesDialog(
      StitchConfigsProvider provider,
      String group,
      String configName,
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord selectedLayer,
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView selectedLayerView,
      Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> layersByPath) {
    super(dialogTitle(selectedLayer, configName), false);
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.group = Strings.trimToNull(group);
    this.configName = Strings.trimToNull(configName);
    this.selectedLayer = selectedLayer;
    this.selectedLayerView = selectedLayerView;
    this.layersByPath = layersByPath == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(layersByPath);
    setWidth("1180px");
    setMaxWidth("98vw");
    setTop("5vh");

    StitchTabbedDetailsPanel tabs = new StitchTabbedDetailsPanel();
    if (selectedLayer != null && selectedLayerView != null) {
      tabs.addTab("json", "JSON", buildJsonTab())
          .addTab("flat", "FLAT", buildFlatTab())
          .addTab("template", "TEMPLATE", buildTemplateTab());
    }
    tabs.addTab("code", "CODE", buildCodeTab()).addTab("schema", "SCHEMA", buildSchemaTab());
    tabs.selectTab(selectedLayer == null ? "code" : "json");
    tabs.onTabChanged(this::ensureAllowedTab);
    addToBody(tabs);
    addSecondaryAction("Close", this::close);
  }

  private void ensureAllowedTab(String key) {
    if (selectedLayer != null && selectedLayerView != null) {
      return;
    }
    if ("code".equalsIgnoreCase(key) || "schema".equalsIgnoreCase(key)) {
      return;
    }
    Notification.show("Select a layer to access JSON, FLAT, and TEMPLATE views.", 1800, Position.BOTTOM_START);
  }

  private VerticalLayout buildJsonTab() {
    TextArea declared = readOnlyArea("Declared JSON", "Declared layer JSON payload");
    declared.setValue(prettyJson(selectedLayerView.declaredPayload()));
    TextArea resolved = readOnlyArea("Resolved JSON", "Resolved layer JSON payload");
    resolved.setValue(prettyJson(selectedLayerView.resolvedPayload()));
    return buildSplitTab(declared, resolved);
  }

  private VerticalLayout buildFlatTab() {
    TextArea declaredFlat = readOnlyArea("Declared Flat", "Flattened declared payload lines");
    declaredFlat.setValue(flatten(selectedLayerView.declaredPayload()));
    TextArea fullFlat = readOnlyArea("Full Flat", "Flattened resolved payload lines");
    fullFlat.setValue(flatten(selectedLayerView.resolvedPayload()));
    return buildSplitTab(declaredFlat, fullFlat);
  }

  private VerticalLayout buildTemplateTab() {
    TextArea template = new TextArea("Template");
    template.setWidthFull();
    template.setMinHeight("18rem");
    template.setValue("{{group}}/{{config}}/{{layer}}\nStatus={{status}}\nPayload={{json}}");
    template.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Template input");
    template.addClassName("stitch-config-json-panel");

    TextArea rendered = readOnlyArea("Rendered", "Rendered template output");
    rendered.addClassName("stitch-config-json-panel");
    Button convert = new Button("CONVERT");
    convert.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL, ButtonVariant.LUMO_PRIMARY);
    convert.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Convert template using selected layer values");
    convert.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          Map<String, String> values = flattenMap(selectedLayerView.resolvedPayload());
          values.put("group", Strings.firstNonBlank(selectedLayer.group(), ""));
          values.put("config", Strings.firstNonBlank(selectedLayer.configName(), ""));
          values.put("layer", Strings.firstNonBlank(selectedLayer.layerId(), ""));
          values.put("json", prettyJson(selectedLayerView.resolvedPayload()));
          rendered.setValue(renderTemplate(template.getValue(), values));
        });

    HorizontalLayout actions = new HorizontalLayout(convert);
    actions.setPadding(false);
    actions.setSpacing(true);
    actions.setWidthFull();
    actions.setJustifyContentMode(com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.JustifyContentMode.END);

    HorizontalLayout split = new HorizontalLayout(template, rendered);
    split.setPadding(false);
    split.setSpacing(true);
    split.setWidthFull();
    split.setAlignItems(Alignment.STRETCH);
    split.addClassName("stitch-config-json-split");
    split.setFlexGrow(1, template, rendered);

    VerticalLayout content = new VerticalLayout(actions, split);
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(true);
    content.setWidthFull();
    content.setFlexGrow(1, split);
    return content;
  }

  private VerticalLayout buildCodeTab() {
    ComboBox<ConfigManager.Language> language = new ComboBox<>("Language");
    language.setItems(ConfigManager.Language.values());
    language.setItemLabelGenerator(Enum::name);
    language.setValue(ConfigManager.Language.JAVA);
    language.setWidth("14rem");
    language.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Code generation language");

    TextField packageOrModule = new TextField("Package / Module");
    packageOrModule.setValue(defaultPackageBase());
    packageOrModule.setWidth("20rem");
    packageOrModule.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Code generation package or module");

    TextArea generated = readOnlyArea("Generated Code", "Generated code preview");

    Button generate = new Button("GENERATE");
    generate.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL, ButtonVariant.LUMO_PRIMARY);
    generate.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Generate config code");

    Button download = new Button("DOWNLOAD");
    download.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    download.setEnabled(false);
    download.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Download generated config code zip");

    generate.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          try {
            lastCodegen =
                provider.generateCode(
                    group,
                    configName,
                    selectedLayer == null ? null : selectedLayer.layerId(),
                    language.getValue(),
                    packageOrModule.getValue());
            String preview =
                lastCodegen.autogenCode().isEmpty()
                    ? "(Generated zip has no text entries)"
                    : String.join(
                        System.lineSeparator() + System.lineSeparator() + "-----" + System.lineSeparator(),
                        lastCodegen.autogenCode());
            generated.setValue(preview);
            download.setEnabled(lastCodegen.zipBytes().length > 0);
          } catch (Exception error) {
            Notification.show("Code generation failed: " + rootMessage(error), 3000, Position.BOTTOM_START);
          }
        });

    download.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          if (lastCodegen == null || lastCodegen.zipBytes().length == 0) {
            Notification.show("Generate code first.", 1400, Position.BOTTOM_START);
            return;
          }
          String filename = Strings.firstNonBlank(lastCodegen.filename(), "config-codegen.zip");
          StreamResource resource =
              new StreamResource(filename, () -> new ByteArrayInputStream(lastCodegen.zipBytes()));
          String uri =
              event.getSource()
                  .getUI()
                  .map(
                      ui ->
                          ui.getSession()
                              .getResourceRegistry()
                              .registerResource(resource)
                              .getResourceUri()
                              .toString())
                  .orElse(null);
          if (uri == null) {
            Notification.show("Unable to prepare download.", 1800, Position.BOTTOM_START);
            return;
          }
          event.getSource().getUI().ifPresent(ui -> ui.getPage().open(uri));
        });

    HorizontalLayout controls = new HorizontalLayout(language, packageOrModule, generate, download);
    controls.setPadding(false);
    controls.setSpacing(true);
    controls.setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.END);

    Div hint = new Div();
    hint.setText("Generate and download read-only config code bundle.");
    hint.getElement().setAttribute("aria-live", "polite");

    VerticalLayout content = new VerticalLayout(controls, hint, generated);
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(true);
    content.setWidthFull();
    return content;
  }

  private VerticalLayout buildSchemaTab() {
    JsonNode schema =
        selectedLayer != null
            ? selectedLayerView.schemaDocument()
            : provider.resolveSchemaDocument(group, configName, layersByPath);
    TextArea schemaArea = readOnlyArea("Schema", "Resolved schema JSON");
    schemaArea.setValue(prettyJson(schema));
    VerticalLayout content = new VerticalLayout(schemaArea);
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(true);
    content.setWidthFull();
    return content;
  }

  private static String dialogTitle(
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord selectedLayer, String configName) {
    if (selectedLayer == null) {
      return Strings.firstNonBlank(configName, "Selection");
    }
    String path =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            Strings.trimToNull(selectedLayer.path()), Strings.trimToNull(selectedLayer.layerId()));
    if (path == null) {
      return Strings.firstNonBlank(configName, "Selection");
    }
    return path.replace("/", " / ");
  }

  private String defaultPackageBase() {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(configName);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return "config";
    }
    return normalized.toLowerCase().replace('-', '_').replace(' ', '_');
  }

  private static TextArea readOnlyArea(String label, String ariaLabel) {
    TextArea area = new TextArea(label);
    area.setWidthFull();
    area.setMinHeight("18rem");
    area.setReadOnly(true);
    area.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", Strings.firstNonBlank(ariaLabel, label));
    return area;
  }

  private static VerticalLayout buildSplitTab(TextArea left, TextArea right) {
    left.addClassName("stitch-config-json-panel");
    right.addClassName("stitch-config-json-panel");

    HorizontalLayout split = new HorizontalLayout(left, right);
    split.setPadding(false);
    split.setSpacing(true);
    split.setWidthFull();
    split.setAlignItems(Alignment.STRETCH);
    split.addClassName("stitch-config-json-split");
    split.setFlexGrow(1, left, right);

    VerticalLayout content = new VerticalLayout(split);
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(false);
    content.setWidthFull();
    content.setFlexGrow(1, split);
    return content;
  }

  private static String prettyJson(JsonNode value) {
    JsonNode safe = value == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : value;
    try {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().writerWithDefaultPrettyPrinter().writeValueAsString(safe);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      return safe.toString();
    }
  }

  private static String flatten(JsonNode node) {
    Map<String, String> flat = flattenMap(node);
    if (flat.isEmpty()) {
      return "(empty)";
    }
    return flat.entrySet().stream()
        .map(entry -> entry.getKey() + "=" + entry.getValue())
        .collect(Collectors.joining(System.lineSeparator()));
  }

  private static Map<String, String> flattenMap(JsonNode node) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> result = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    flattenNode("", node, result);
    return result;
  }

  private static void flattenNode(String prefix, JsonNode node, Map<String, String> result) {
    if (node == null || node.isNull()) {
      if (!prefix.isBlank()) {
        result.put(prefix, "null");
      }
      return;
    }
    if (node.isObject()) {
      node.fieldNames()
          .forEachRemaining(
              field -> flattenNode(joinPath(prefix, field), node.get(field), result));
      return;
    }
    if (node.isArray()) {
      for (int index = 0; index < node.size(); index++) {
        flattenNode(joinPath(prefix, "[" + index + "]"), node.get(index), result);
      }
      return;
    }
    if (!prefix.isBlank()) {
      result.put(prefix, node.asText());
    }
  }

  private static String joinPath(String left, String right) {
    if (Strings.trimToNull(left) == null) {
      return right;
    }
    if (right.startsWith("[")) {
      return left + right;
    }
    return left + "." + right;
  }

  private static String renderTemplate(String template, Map<String, String> values) {
    String output = Strings.trimToEmpty(template);
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return output;
    }
    for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : values.entrySet()) {
      output =
          output.replace(
              "{{" + entry.getKey() + "}}",
              Strings.firstNonBlank(entry.getValue(), ""));
    }
    return output;
  }

  private static String rootMessage(Throwable error) {
    Throwable cursor = error;
    while (cursor != null && cursor.getCause() != null && cursor.getCause() != cursor) {
      cursor = cursor.getCause();
    }
    return cursor == null ? "Unknown error" : Strings.firstNonBlank(cursor.getMessage(), cursor.getClass().getSimpleName());
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/configs/StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.configs;

import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.CanonicalIds;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfig;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfigLayer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport {
  private static final Pattern LAYER_ID_PATTERN = Pattern.compile("[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+");

  private StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport() {}

  public static String configNameFromDefinition(DefinitionConfig definition) {
    if (definition == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return trimToNull(Strings.requireNonBlank(definition.configId(), "definition.configId"));
  }

  public static LayerIdentity layerIdentity(DefinitionConfigLayer layer) {
    if (layer == null) {
      return new LayerIdentity(null, null, null);
    }
    Objects.requireNonNull(layer.envelope(), "layer.envelope");
    CanonicalIds.ParsedId parsed =
        CanonicalIds.parse(Strings.requireNonBlank(layer.resourceId(), "layer.resourceId"));
    if (!"config".equals(parsed.type())) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Config layer resource id must have type config: " + layer.resourceId());
    }
    String group = trimToNull(Strings.requireNonBlank(layer.envelope().group(), "layer.envelope.group"));
    String configName = trimToNull(Strings.requireNonBlank(parsed.namespace(), "layer.resourceId.namespace"));
    String layerId = trimToNull(Strings.requireNonBlank(parsed.name(), "layer.resourceId.name"));
    return new LayerIdentity(group, configName, layerId);
  }

  public static String parentLayerId(DefinitionConfigLayer layer) {
    String parentId = trimToNull(layer == null ? null : layer.parentId());
    if (parentId == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (!parentId.startsWith("config:")) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Config parent id must use canonical config resource id: " + parentId);
    }
    CanonicalIds.ParsedId parsed = CanonicalIds.parse(parentId);
    if (!"config".equals(parsed.type())) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Config parent id must have type config: " + parentId);
    }
    return trimToNull(Strings.requireNonBlank(parsed.name(), "parentId.name"));
  }

  public static DefinitionConfigLayer findLayer(
      DiscoveryCache cache, String group, String configName, String layerId) {
    for (DefinitionConfigLayer layer : cache.list(DefinitionConfigLayer.class, group)) {
      LayerIdentity identity = layerIdentity(layer);
      if (!Objects.equals(configName, identity.configName()) || !Objects.equals(layerId, identity.layerId())) {
        continue;
      }
      return layer;
    }
    return null;
  }

  public static String normalizeLayerId(String value, String fieldName) {
    String normalized = trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    if (!LAYER_ID_PATTERN.matcher(normalized).matches()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(fieldName + " must match [a-zA-Z0-9._-]+");
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  public static String canonicalLayerResourceId(String group, String configName, String layerId) {
    return "config:" + group + "/" + configName + "/" + layerId;
  }

  public static String canonicalParentLayerId(String group, String configName, String parentLayerId) {
    String parent = trimToNull(parentLayerId);
    return parent == null ? null : canonicalLayerResourceId(group, configName, parent);
  }

  public static String configLayerDefinitionName(String configName, String layerId) {
    return configName + "__" + layerId;
  }

  public static String configLayerDisplayName(String configName, String layerId) {
    return configName + " / " + layerId;
  }

  public static String trimToNull(String value) {
    return Strings.trimToNull(value);
  }

  public record LayerIdentity(String group, String configName, String layerId) {}
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.configs;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;

/** Shared config-layer inspector composition for metadata + payload preview. */
public final class StitchConfigLayerInspector {

  private Map<String, String> validationErrorsByPath = Map.of();

  public StitchConfigLayerInspector(
      StitchInspectorPreviewPanel panel,
      boolean editable,
      BooleanSupplier editModeSupplier,
      Runnable markDirty) {
    this.panel = Objects.requireNonNull(panel, "panel");
    this.editable = editable;
    this.editModeSupplier = editModeSupplier == null ? () -> false : editModeSupplier;
    this.markDirty = markDirty == null ? () -> {} : markDirty;

  public Component renderLineage(
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView view,
      Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> layersByPath,
      Consumer<String> onLayerSelected) {
    if (view == null || view.layer() == null) {
      return new org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchEmptyState(
          "No layer selected", "Select a config layer to view lineage.");
    }
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord selected = view.layer();
    String selectedLayerId = Strings.trimToNull(selected.layerId());
    LinkedHashMap<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> byLayerId = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (layersByPath != null && !layersByPath.isEmpty()) {
      for (StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record : layersByPath.values()) {
        if (record == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String layerId = Strings.trimToNull(record.layerId());
        if (layerId != null && !byLayerId.containsKey(layerId)) {
          byLayerId.put(layerId, record);
        }
      }
    }

    List<String> lineageLayerIds = new ArrayList<>();
    if (view.lineageLayers() != null) {
      view.lineageLayers().stream()
          .map(Strings::trimToNull)
          .filter(Objects::nonNull)
          .forEach(lineageLayerIds::add);
    }
    if (selectedLayerId != null && !lineageLayerIds.contains(selectedLayerId)) {
      lineageLayerIds.add(selectedLayerId);
    }
    if (lineageLayerIds.isEmpty()) {
      return new org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchEmptyState(
          "No lineage available", "Lineage is unavailable for the selected layer.");
    }

    StitchSection section = new StitchSection("Lineage");
    section.addClassName("stitch-config-lineage-section");

    Span progression = new Span(lineageProgression(lineageLayerIds));
    progression.addClassName("stitch-config-lineage-progress");

    VerticalLayout rows = new VerticalLayout();
    rows.setPadding(false);
    rows.setSpacing(true);
    rows.setWidthFull();
    rows.addClassName("stitch-config-lineage-rows");

    for (int index = 0; index < lineageLayerIds.size(); index++) {
      String layerId = lineageLayerIds.get(index);
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record = byLayerId.get(layerId);
      String nodeId =
          Strings.trimToNull(
              record == null ? null : Strings.firstNonBlank(record.path(), record.layerId()));
      boolean selectedRow =
          selectedLayerId != null && selectedLayerId.equalsIgnoreCase(Strings.firstNonBlank(layerId, ""));

      Button row = new Button();
      row.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL, ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY);
      row.addClassName("stitch-config-lineage-row");
      row.addClassName(selectedRow ? "stitch-config-lineage-row--selected" : "stitch-config-lineage-row--parent");
      row.setWidthFull();
      row.setEnabled(nodeId != null && onLayerSelected != null);
      row.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Select lineage layer " + Strings.firstNonBlank(layerId, "-"));

      Span indexBadge = new Span(String.valueOf(index + 1));
      indexBadge.addClassName("stitch-config-lineage-index");

      Span layerBadge = new Span(Strings.firstNonBlank(layerId, "-").toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT));
      layerBadge.addClassName("stitch-config-layer-pill");
      if (selectedRow) {
        layerBadge.addClassName("stitch-config-layer-pill--selected");
      } else if ("base".equalsIgnoreCase(layerId)) {
        layerBadge.addClassName("stitch-config-layer-pill--base");
      } else {
        layerBadge.addClassName("stitch-config-layer-pill--inherited");
      }

      Span configPath =
          new Span(
              "config:"
                  + Strings.firstNonBlank(
                      Strings.trimToNull(record == null ? null : record.group()),
                      Strings.trimToNull(selected.group()),
                      "-")
                  + "/"
                  + Strings.firstNonBlank(
                      Strings.trimToNull(record == null ? null : record.configName()),
                      Strings.trimToNull(selected.configName()),
                      "-")
                  + "/"
                  + Strings.firstNonBlank(layerId, "-"));
      configPath.addClassName("stitch-config-lineage-path");

      HorizontalLayout rowContent = new HorizontalLayout(indexBadge, layerBadge, configPath);
      rowContent.setPadding(false);
      rowContent.setSpacing(true);
      rowContent.setWidthFull();
      rowContent.setAlignItems(com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.Alignment.CENTER);
      row.getElement().appendChild(rowContent.getElement());
      if (nodeId != null && onLayerSelected != null) {
        row.addClickListener(event -> onLayerSelected.accept(nodeId));
      }
      rows.add(row);
    }

    section.addToBody(progression, rows);
    return section;
  }

  public Component render(
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView view,
      boolean editMode,
      boolean lineageVisible,

    return render(view, editMode, lineageVisible, true, previewValue);
  }

  public Component render(
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView view,
      boolean editMode,
      boolean lineageVisible,
      boolean showInheritedValues,
      String previewValue) {
    return render(
        view,
        editMode,
        lineageVisible,
        showInheritedValues,

  public Component render(
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView view,
      boolean editMode,
      boolean lineageVisible,
      boolean showInheritedValues,
      String previewValue,
      Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> layersByPath) {
    if (view == null || view.layer() == null) {
      return render(
          new StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord(
              null,
              null,
              null,
              null,
              null,
              null,
              null,
              null,
              null,
              DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode(),
              List.of(),
              null),
          editMode,
          previewValue,
          Map.of());
    }
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record = view.layer();
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> parityMetadata = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    parityMetadata.put("Resolved At", Strings.firstNonBlank(view.resolvedAtUtc(), "-"));
    parityMetadata.put("Lineage", Strings.firstNonBlank(view.lineageSummary(), "-"));
    parityMetadata.put(
        "Impact",
        view.impactTotalLeaves() <= 0
            ? "-"
            : (view.impactAffectedLeaves() + "/" + view.impactTotalLeaves()));
    parityMetadata.put("Pending", Strings.firstNonBlank(view.pendingSummary(), "None"));
    parityMetadata.put(
        "Source Keys",
        view.sourceByPath() == null ? "0" : String.valueOf(view.sourceByPath().size()));

    panel.setContext("Layer", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.layerId(), "-"));
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> allMetadata = metadata(record);
    allMetadata.putAll(parityMetadata);
    panel.setMetadata(allMetadata);
    panel.setPreviewVisible(true);
    panel.setPreviewReadOnly(!(editable && editMode));
    panel.setPreviewAriaLabel(
        (editable && editMode ? "Editable" : "Read-only")
            + " declared payload for layer "
            + Strings.firstNonBlank(record.layerId(), "-"));
    setPreviewValue(previewValue);

    Component overridesView =
        buildFieldEditor(
            view,
            editMode,
            previewValue,
            showInheritedValues,
            layersByPath);
    VerticalLayout content = new VerticalLayout(overridesView);
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(false);
    content.setWidthFull();
    content.addClassName("stitch-config-layer-inspector-content");
    return content;
  }

  public Component render(
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record,
      boolean editMode,
      String previewValue,
      Map<String, String> additionalMetadata) {
    panel.setContext("Layer", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.layerId(), "-"));
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> fields = metadata(record);
    if (additionalMetadata != null && !additionalMetadata.isEmpty()) {
      fields.putAll(additionalMetadata);
    }
    panel.setMetadata(fields);
    panel.setPreviewVisible(true);
    panel.setPreviewReadOnly(!(editable && editMode));
    panel.setPreviewAriaLabel(
        (editable && editMode ? "Editable" : "Read-only")
            + " declared payload for layer "
            + Strings.firstNonBlank(record.layerId(), "-"));
    setPreviewValue(previewValue);

    LinkedHashMap<String, String> combined = metadata(record);
    if (additionalMetadata != null && !additionalMetadata.isEmpty()) {
      combined.putAll(additionalMetadata);
    }

    StitchSummaryStrip summaryStrip = new StitchSummaryStrip();
    summaryStrip.setItems(summaryItems(record));

    StitchTabbedDetailsPanel tabs = new StitchTabbedDetailsPanel();
    tabs.addTab("overview", "Overview", buildForm(selectOverview(combined)))
        .addTab("runtime", "Effective / Runtime", buildForm(selectRuntime(combined)))
        .addTab("declared", "Declared", buildDeclaredPreview(previewValue))
        .addTab("json", "JSON", panel)
        .selectTab("overview");

    VerticalLayout content = new VerticalLayout(summaryStrip, tabs);
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(true);
    content.setWidthFull();
    return content;
  }

  public List<Component> readOnlyActions(
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record, Runnable onCloseSelection) {
    return readOnlyActions(record, onCloseSelection, List.of());
  }

  public List<Component> readOnlyActions(
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record,
      Runnable onCloseSelection,
      List<Component> leadingActions) {
    List<Component> actions = new ArrayList<>();
    if (leadingActions != null) {
      for (Component action : leadingActions) {
        if (action != null) {
          actions.add(action);
        }
      }
    }
    if (record == null) {
      actions.add(panel.createCloseAction(onCloseSelection, "Close layer inspector"));
      return List.copyOf(actions);
    }
    Button json =
        panel.createJsonAction(
            () -> openJsonDialog(record), "Open selected layer payload as JSON");
    Button copy =
        panel.createCopyAction(
            "Copied layer JSON", "Nothing to copy", "Copy selected layer payload");
    copy.setEnabled(Strings.isNotBlank(panel.previewField().getValue()));
    Button close = panel.createCloseAction(onCloseSelection, "Close layer inspector");
    actions.add(json);
    actions.add(copy);
    actions.add(close);
    return List.copyOf(actions);
  }

  public JsonNode parseEditorDeclaredJson() throws Exception {
    return parseDeclaredJson(panel.previewField().getValue());
  }

  public JsonNode parseAndValidateEditorDeclaredJson(StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView view)
      throws Exception {
    JsonNode parsed = parseDeclaredJson(panel.previewField().getValue());
    if (!(parsed instanceof ObjectNode declaredObject)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Declared payload must be a JSON object.");
    }
    ValidationResult validation = validateDraft(declaredObject, view);
    if (!validation.isValid()) {
      validationErrorsByPath = validation.errorsByPath();
      String first =
          validation
              .errorsByPath()
              .entrySet()
              .stream()
              .findFirst()
              .map(entry -> entry.getKey() + ": " + entry.getValue())
              .orElse("Validation failed.");
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          first
              + (validation.errorsByPath().size() > 1
                  ? " (and " + (validation.errorsByPath().size() - 1) + " more)"
                  : ""));
    }
    validationErrorsByPath = Map.of();
    return declaredObject;
  }

  public void clearValidationErrors() {
    validationErrorsByPath = Map.of();
  }

  public String previewValue() {
    return panel.previewField().getValue();
  }

  public void setPreviewValue(String value) {
    suppressPreviewEvents = true;
    panel.setPreviewValue(value);
    suppressPreviewEvents = false;
  }

  public String prettyJson(JsonNode value) {
    JsonNode normalized = value == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : value;
    try {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().writerWithDefaultPrettyPrinter().writeValueAsString(normalized);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      return normalized.toString();
    }
  }

  private void configurePreviewField() {
    panel.previewField().setMinHeight("24rem");
    panel.previewField().setReadOnly(!editable);
    panel
        .previewField()
        .addValueChangeListener(
            event -> {
              if (!suppressPreviewEvents
                  && editable
                  && editModeSupplier.getAsBoolean()
                  && event.isFromClient()) {
                markDirty.run();
              }
            });
  }

  private LinkedHashMap<String, String> metadata(StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> metadata = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    metadata.put("Group", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.group(), "-"));
    metadata.put("Name", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.configName(), "-"));
    metadata.put("Layer", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.layerId(), "-"));
    metadata.put("Parent Layer", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.parentLayerId(), "(root)"));
    metadata.put("Short Name", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.shortName(), "-"));
    metadata.put("Schema Key", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.schemaKey(), "-"));
    metadata.put("Config Version", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.configVersionId(), "-"));
    metadata.put("Effective Config", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.effectiveConfigId(), "-"));
    metadata.put("Scheduled Entries", String.valueOf(record.effective().size()));
    metadata.put("Pending State", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.pendingStateLabel(), "-"));
    metadata.put("Pending Mode", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.pendingModeLabel(), "-"));
    metadata.put("Pending Effective", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.pendingEffectiveAtUtc(), "-"));
    metadata.put("Pending Expires", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.pendingExpiresAtUtc(), "-"));
    metadata.put("Future Effective", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.firstFutureEffectiveAtUtc(), "-"));
    metadata.put("Path", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.path(), "-"));
    return metadata;
  }

  private static Map<String, String> summaryItems(StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> summary = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    summary.put("Group", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.group(), "-"));
    summary.put("Config", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.configName(), "-"));
    summary.put("Layer", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.layerId(), "-"));
    return summary;
  }

  private static Map<String, String> summaryItems(
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView view) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> summary = new LinkedHashMap<>(summaryItems(record));
    summary.put(
        "Impact",
        view.impactTotalLeaves() <= 0
            ? "-"
            : (view.impactAffectedLeaves() + "/" + view.impactTotalLeaves()));
    summary.put("Pending", Strings.firstNonBlank(view.pendingSummary(), "None"));
    return summary;
  }

  private static FormLayout buildForm(Map<String, String> values) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> safe = new LinkedHashMap<>(values);
    if (safe.isEmpty()) {
      safe.put("Details", "-");
    }
    return StitchDetailsDialogSupport.buildForm(List.copyOf(safe.keySet()), safe, Map.of());
  }

  private static Component buildDeclaredPreview(String previewValue) {
    TextArea text = new TextArea("Declared");
    text.setWidthFull();
    text.setMinHeight("20rem");
    text.setReadOnly(true);
    text.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(previewValue));
    text.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Declared layer payload preview");
    return text;
  }

  private String buildPrettyJson(JsonNode value) {
    return prettyJsonStatic(value);
  }

  private Component buildJsonPreview(JsonNode value, String ariaLabel) {
    TextArea text = new TextArea("Resolved");
    text.setWidthFull();
    text.setMinHeight("20rem");
    text.setReadOnly(true);
    text.setValue(buildPrettyJson(value));
    text.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", Strings.firstNonBlank(ariaLabel, "JSON preview"));
    return text;
  }

  private static Component buildSourcePreview(Map<String, String> sources) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (sources != null && !sources.isEmpty()) {
      sources.entrySet().stream()
          .filter(entry -> Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey()) != null)
          .sorted(Comparator.comparing(Map.Entry::getKey, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
          .forEach(
              entry ->
                  values.put(
                      Strings.firstNonBlank(entry.getKey(), "-"),
                      Strings.firstNonBlank(entry.getValue(), "-")));
    }
    if (values.isEmpty()) {
      values.put("Source Attribution", "Unavailable");
    }
    return buildForm(values);
  }

  private Component buildFieldEditor(
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView view,
      boolean editMode,
      String previewValue,
      boolean showInheritedValues,
      Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> layersByPath) {
    ObjectNode originalDeclared = objectNode(view == null ? null : view.declaredPayload());
    ObjectNode draftDeclared = parseDraftDeclared(previewValue, originalDeclared);
    JsonNode resolvedPayload =
        view == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : view.resolvedPayload();
    Map<String, String> sources = view == null ? Map.of() : view.sourceByPath();
    JsonNode schemaDocument =
        view == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : view.schemaDocument();
    String selectedLayerId =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            view == null || view.layer() == null ? null : view.layer().layerId(),
            "Selected layer");
    ImpactContext impactContext = buildImpactContext(layersByPath, selectedLayerId);

    Grid<LayerFieldRow> grid = new Grid<>(LayerFieldRow.class, false);
    grid.addClassName("stitch-config-field-grid");
    grid.addClassName("stitch-results-grid");
    grid.setWidthFull();
    grid.setHeight("24rem");
    grid.addThemeVariants(GridVariant.LUMO_COMPACT);
    grid.setClassNameGenerator(
        row -> {
          List<String> classes = new ArrayList<>();
          if (row.inherited()) {
            classes.add("stitch-config-field-row-inherited");
          }
          if (row.selectedLayer()) {
            classes.add("stitch-config-field-row-selected");
          }
          if (row.modified()) {
            classes.add("stitch-config-field-row-modified");
          }
          if (row.cleared()) {
            classes.add("stitch-config-field-row-cleared");
          }
          if (Strings.trimToNull(row.validationError()) != null) {
            classes.add("stitch-config-field-row-invalid");
          }
          return String.join(" ", classes);
        });

    Div emptyState = new Div();
    emptyState.addClassName("stitch-config-overrides-empty");

    Runnable[] refreshRef = new Runnable[1];
    refreshRef[0] = () -> {
      List<LayerFieldRow> rows =
          buildFieldRows(
              resolvedPayload,
              draftDeclared,
              originalDeclared,
              sources,
              schemaDocument,
              selectedLayerId,
              showInheritedValues,
              impactContext);
      grid.setItems(rows);
      boolean noRows = rows.isEmpty();
      grid.setVisible(!noRows);
      emptyState.setVisible(noRows);
      emptyState.setText(
          showInheritedValues
              ? "No values are available for this layer."
              : "No values are defined directly at this layer.");
    };

    grid.addColumn(LayerFieldRow::path).setHeader("Name").setFlexGrow(1).setAutoWidth(true);
    grid.addComponentColumn(this::typePill).setHeader("Type").setFlexGrow(0).setAutoWidth(true);
    grid.addComponentColumn(row -> valueEditor(row, editMode, draftDeclared, refreshRef[0]))
        .setHeader("Value")
        .setFlexGrow(1)
        .setAutoWidth(true);
    Column<LayerFieldRow> layerColumn =
        grid.addComponentColumn(this::layerPill)
            .setHeader("Layer")
            .setFlexGrow(0)
            .setAutoWidth(true);
    layerColumn.setVisible(showInheritedValues);
    grid.addComponentColumn(this::impactCell).setHeader("Impact").setFlexGrow(0).setAutoWidth(true);
    if (editMode && editable) {
      grid.addComponentColumn(row -> clearOverrideButton(row, editMode, draftDeclared, refreshRef[0]))
          .setHeader("Clear")
          .setFlexGrow(0)
          .setAutoWidth(true);
    }
    grid.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Config field editor");

    refreshRef[0].run();

    VerticalLayout content = new VerticalLayout(emptyState, grid);
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(true);
    content.setWidthFull();
    content.addClassName("stitch-config-overrides-panel");
    return content;
  }

  private List<LayerFieldRow> buildFieldRows(
      JsonNode resolvedPayload,
      ObjectNode draftDeclared,
      ObjectNode originalDeclared,
      Map<String, String> sources,
      JsonNode schemaDocument,
      String selectedLayerId,
      boolean includeInherited,
      ImpactContext impactContext) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, JsonNode> resolved = flattenLeaves(resolvedPayload);
    LinkedHashMap<String, JsonNode> draft = flattenLeaves(draftDeclared);
    LinkedHashMap<String, LayerFieldRow> rows = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    Set<String> selectedLayerDeclaredKeys = flattenDeclaredPaths(draftDeclared);
    Map<ImpactLookupKey, ImpactCell> impactCache = new HashMap<>();
    Map<String, String> validationErrors = validationErrorsByPath;

    if (includeInherited) {
      for (Map.Entry<String, JsonNode> entry : resolved.entrySet()) {
        String path = entry.getKey();
        JsonNode resolvedValue = entry.getValue();
        JsonNode declaredValue = valueAtPath(draftDeclared, path);
        JsonNode originalValue = valueAtPath(originalDeclared, path);
        boolean overridden = declaredValue != null;
        boolean cleared = !overridden && originalValue != null;
        JsonNode displayValue = overridden ? declaredValue : resolvedValue;
        List<String> enumValues = enumValues(schemaDocument, path);
        boolean modified =
            overridden
                ? !jsonEquivalent(declaredValue, originalValue)
                : cleared;
        String sourceLayer =
            overridden ? selectedLayerId : Strings.trimToNull(sources == null ? null : sources.get(path));
        if (!overridden && sourceLayer == null) {
          sourceLayer =
              effectiveSourceLayerId(path, Strings.trimToNull(selectedLayerId), impactContext, selectedLayerDeclaredKeys);
        }
        String sourceLayerLabel = Strings.firstNonBlank(sourceLayer, "Inherited");
        ImpactCell impact =
            impactForPath(
                path,
                sourceLayer,
                impactContext,
                selectedLayerDeclaredKeys,
                impactCache);
        rows.put(
            path,
            new LayerFieldRow(
                path,
                detectType(displayValue, enumValues, schemaDocument, path),
                sourceLayerLabel,
                displayValue,
                overridden,
                !overridden,
                overridden,
                modified,
                cleared,
                !path.contains("["),
                enumValues,
                validationErrors.get(path),
                impact));
      }
    }

    for (Map.Entry<String, JsonNode> entry : draft.entrySet()) {
      if (rows.containsKey(entry.getKey())) {
        continue;
      }
      String path = entry.getKey();
      JsonNode value = entry.getValue();
      JsonNode originalValue = valueAtPath(originalDeclared, path);
      List<String> enumValues = enumValues(schemaDocument, path);
      ImpactCell impact =
          impactForPath(
              path,
              selectedLayerId,
              impactContext,
              selectedLayerDeclaredKeys,
              impactCache);
      rows.put(
          path,
          new LayerFieldRow(
              path,
              detectType(value, enumValues, schemaDocument, path),
              selectedLayerId,
              value,
              true,
              false,
              true,
              !jsonEquivalent(value, originalValue),
              false,
              !path.contains("["),
              enumValues,
              validationErrors.get(path),
              impact));
    }

    List<LayerFieldRow> ordered = new ArrayList<>(rows.values());
    ordered.sort(
        Comparator.comparing(LayerFieldRow::selectedLayer)
            .reversed()
            .thenComparing(LayerFieldRow::path, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER));
    return List.copyOf(ordered);
  }

  private Component impactCell(LayerFieldRow row) {
    ImpactCell impact = row == null ? null : row.impact();
    Span count = new Span(impact == null ? "-" : impact.label());
    count.addClassName("stitch-config-impact-count");
    if (impact != null && impact.total() > 0) {
      count.getStyle().set("color", impactHeatColor(impact.affected(), impact.total()));
      String sourceLayer = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(impact.sourceLayer()), "selected layer");
      count
          .getElement()
          .setProperty(
              "title",
              impact.affected()
                  + " of "
                  + impact.total()
                  + " leaf layers impacted by value from "
                  + sourceLayer);
    } else {
      count.getStyle().set("color", "#98a6b5");
      count.getElement().setProperty("title", "Impact unavailable");
    }
    return count;
  }

  private Component typePill(LayerFieldRow row) {
    String type =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(row == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(row.type()), "STRING")
            .toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    Span pill = new Span(type);
    pill.addClassName("stitch-config-type-pill");
    switch (type) {
      case "BOOLEAN" -> pill.addClassName("stitch-config-type-pill--boolean");
      case "INTEGER", "LONG", "DOUBLE", "DECIMAL" ->
          pill.addClassName("stitch-config-type-pill--number");
      case "ENUM" -> pill.addClassName("stitch-config-type-pill--enum");
      case "JSON" -> pill.addClassName("stitch-config-type-pill--json");
      default -> pill.addClassName("stitch-config-type-pill--string");
    }
    return pill;
  }

  private Component layerPill(LayerFieldRow row) {
    String sourceLayer =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(row == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(row.sourceLayer()), "-");
    Span pill = new Span(sourceLayer);
    pill.addClassName("stitch-config-layer-pill");
    if (row != null && row.selectedLayer()) {
      pill.addClassName("stitch-config-layer-pill--selected");
    } else {
      pill.addClassName("stitch-config-layer-pill--inherited");
    }
    if ("base".equalsIgnoreCase(sourceLayer)) {
      pill.addClassName("stitch-config-layer-pill--base");
    }
    return pill;
  }

  private Component valueEditor(
      LayerFieldRow row, boolean editMode, ObjectNode draftDeclared, Runnable refresh) {
    String validationError = Strings.trimToNull(row.validationError());
    if (!editMode || !editable || !row.editable()) {
      Span value = new Span(jsonValueToString(row.value()));
      value.addClassName("stitch-config-field-value");
      if (row.inherited()) {
        value.addClassName("stitch-config-field-value--inherited");
      }
      if (validationError != null) {
        value.addClassName("stitch-config-field-value--invalid");
      }
      value.getElement().setAttribute("title", jsonValueToString(row.value()));
      value.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Read-only value for " + row.path());
      return value;
    }

    switch (row.type()) {
      case "BOOLEAN":
        Checkbox toggle = new Checkbox();
        toggle.addClassName("stitch-boolean-toggle");
        toggle.addClassName("stitch-config-field-editor");
        toggle.setValue(row.value() != null && row.value().asBoolean(false));
        toggle.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Boolean value for " + row.path());
        if (validationError != null) {
          toggle.getElement().setAttribute("title", validationError);
        } else {
          toggle.getElement().removeAttribute("title");
        }
        toggle.addValueChangeListener(
            event -> {
              if (!event.isFromClient()) {
                return;
              }
              updateDraftValue(draftDeclared, row.path(), BooleanNode.valueOf(event.getValue()));
              syncPreviewFromDraft(draftDeclared);
              markDirty.run();
              refresh.run();
            });
        return toggle;
      case "INTEGER":
        IntegerField integerField = new IntegerField();
        integerField.setWidthFull();
        integerField.setValue(row.value() != null && row.value().isNumber() ? row.value().asInt() : null);
        integerField.addClassName("stitch-config-field-editor");
        integerField.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Integer value for " + row.path());
        integerField.setInvalid(validationError != null);
        integerField.setErrorMessage(validationError);
        java.util.function.Consumer<Integer> applyIntegerValue =
            value -> {
              if (value == null) {
                clearDraftValue(draftDeclared, row.path());
              } else {
                updateDraftValue(draftDeclared, row.path(), IntNode.valueOf(value));
              }
              syncPreviewFromDraft(draftDeclared);
              markDirty.run();
              refresh.run();
            };
        integerField.addValueChangeListener(
            event -> {
              if (!event.isFromClient()) {
                return;
              }
              applyIntegerValue.accept(event.getValue());
            });
        return numericStepper(
            integerField,
            row.path(),
            () -> {
              int current =
                  integerField.getValue() != null
                      ? integerField.getValue()
                      : (row.value() != null && row.value().isNumber() ? row.value().asInt() : 0);
              int next = current - 1;
              integerField.setValue(next);
              applyIntegerValue.accept(next);
            },
            () -> {
              int current =
                  integerField.getValue() != null
                      ? integerField.getValue()
                      : (row.value() != null && row.value().isNumber() ? row.value().asInt() : 0);
              int next = current + 1;
              integerField.setValue(next);
              applyIntegerValue.accept(next);
            });
      case "LONG":
        TextField longField = new TextField();
        longField.setWidthFull();
        longField.setValue(row.value() != null && row.value().isNumber() ? row.value().asText() : "");
        longField.addClassName("stitch-config-field-editor");
        longField.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Long value for " + row.path());
        longField.setInvalid(validationError != null);
        longField.setErrorMessage(validationError);
        java.util.function.Consumer<Long> applyLongValue =
            value -> {
              if (value == null) {
                clearDraftValue(draftDeclared, row.path());
              } else {
                updateDraftValue(draftDeclared, row.path(), LongNode.valueOf(value));
              }
              syncPreviewFromDraft(draftDeclared);
              markDirty.run();
              refresh.run();
            };
        longField.addValueChangeListener(
            event -> {
              if (!event.isFromClient()) {
                return;
              }
              String raw = Strings.trimToNull(event.getValue());
              if (raw == null) {
                longField.setInvalid(false);
                longField.setErrorMessage(null);
                applyLongValue.accept(null);
              } else {
                try {
                  long parsed = Long.parseLong(raw);
                  longField.setInvalid(false);
                  longField.setErrorMessage(null);
                  applyLongValue.accept(parsed);
                } catch (NumberFormatException ex) {
                  longField.setInvalid(true);
                  longField.setErrorMessage("Enter a valid long value.");
                  return;
                }
              }
            });
        return numericStepper(
            longField,
            row.path(),
            () -> {
              Long current = parseLongValue(longField.getValue());
              if (current == null) {
                current = row.value() != null && row.value().isNumber() ? row.value().asLong() : 0L;
              }
              long next = current - 1L;
              longField.setInvalid(false);
              longField.setErrorMessage(null);
              longField.setValue(Long.toString(next));
              applyLongValue.accept(next);
            },
            () -> {
              Long current = parseLongValue(longField.getValue());
              if (current == null) {
                current = row.value() != null && row.value().isNumber() ? row.value().asLong() : 0L;
              }
              long next = current + 1L;
              longField.setInvalid(false);
              longField.setErrorMessage(null);
              longField.setValue(Long.toString(next));
              applyLongValue.accept(next);
            });
      case "DOUBLE":
      case "DECIMAL":
        NumberField numberField = new NumberField();
        numberField.setWidthFull();
        numberField.setValue(row.value() != null && row.value().isNumber() ? row.value().asDouble() : null);
        numberField.addClassName("stitch-config-field-editor");
        numberField.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Numeric value for " + row.path());
        numberField.setInvalid(validationError != null);
        numberField.setErrorMessage(validationError);
        java.util.function.Consumer<BigDecimal> applyDecimalValue =
            value -> {
              if (value == null) {
                clearDraftValue(draftDeclared, row.path());
              } else {
                updateDraftValue(draftDeclared, row.path(), DoubleNode.valueOf(value.doubleValue()));
              }
              syncPreviewFromDraft(draftDeclared);
              markDirty.run();
              refresh.run();
            };
        numberField.addValueChangeListener(
            event -> {
              if (!event.isFromClient()) {
                return;
              }
              applyDecimalValue.accept(toBigDecimal(event.getValue()));
            });
        BigDecimal step = decimalStepForType(row.type());
        return numericStepper(
            numberField,
            row.path(),
            () -> {
              BigDecimal current =
                  firstNonNull(
                      toBigDecimal(numberField.getValue()),
                      toBigDecimal(row.value()),
                      BigDecimal.ZERO);
              BigDecimal next = normalizedDecimal(current.subtract(step));
              numberField.setValue(next.doubleValue());
              applyDecimalValue.accept(next);
            },
            () -> {
              BigDecimal current =
                  firstNonNull(
                      toBigDecimal(numberField.getValue()),
                      toBigDecimal(row.value()),
                      BigDecimal.ZERO);
              BigDecimal next = normalizedDecimal(current.add(step));
              numberField.setValue(next.doubleValue());
              applyDecimalValue.accept(next);
            });
      case "ENUM":
        ComboBox<String> enumField = new ComboBox<>();
        enumField.setWidthFull();
        List<String> options =
            row.enumValues().isEmpty()
                ? List.of(jsonValueToString(row.value()))
                : row.enumValues();
        enumField.setItems(options);
        enumField.setValue(jsonValueToString(row.value()));
        enumField.setAllowCustomValue(false);
        enumField.addClassName("stitch-config-field-editor");
        enumField.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Enum value for " + row.path());
        enumField.setInvalid(validationError != null);
        enumField.setErrorMessage(validationError);
        enumField.addValueChangeListener(
            event -> {
              if (!event.isFromClient()) {
                return;
              }
              updateDraftValue(draftDeclared, row.path(), TextNode.valueOf(Strings.trimToEmpty(event.getValue())));
              syncPreviewFromDraft(draftDeclared);
              markDirty.run();
              refresh.run();
            });
        return enumField;
      default:
        TextField textField = new TextField();
        textField.setWidthFull();
        textField.setValue(jsonValueToString(row.value()));
        textField.addClassName("stitch-config-field-editor");
        textField.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Text value for " + row.path());
        textField.setInvalid(validationError != null);
        textField.setErrorMessage(validationError);
        textField.addValueChangeListener(
            event -> {
              if (!event.isFromClient()) {
                return;
              }
              updateDraftValue(draftDeclared, row.path(), TextNode.valueOf(Strings.trimToEmpty(event.getValue())));
              syncPreviewFromDraft(draftDeclared);
              markDirty.run();
              refresh.run();
            });
        return textField;
    }
  }

  private Component numericStepper(
      Component field, String path, Runnable decrement, Runnable increment) {
    Button minus = new Button("-");
    minus.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL, ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY);
    minus.addClassName("stitch-config-stepper-button");
    minus.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Decrease value for " + path);
    minus.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Decrease");
    minus.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          if (decrement != null) {
            decrement.run();
          }
        });

    Button plus = new Button("+");
