    plus.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL, ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY);
    plus.addClassName("stitch-config-stepper-button");
    plus.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Increase value for " + path);
    plus.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Increase");
    plus.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          if (increment != null) {
            increment.run();
          }
        });

    HorizontalLayout layout = new HorizontalLayout(minus, field, plus);
    layout.setPadding(false);
    layout.setSpacing(true);
    layout.setWidthFull();
    layout.setAlignItems(com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.Alignment.CENTER);
    layout.addClassName("stitch-config-stepper");
    layout.expand(field);
    return layout;
  }

  private static Long parseLongValue(String raw) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(raw);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return Long.parseLong(normalized);
    } catch (NumberFormatException ignored) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private static BigDecimal decimalStepForType(String type) {
    String normalized = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(type), "DOUBLE").toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    if ("INTEGER".equals(normalized) || "LONG".equals(normalized)) {
      return BigDecimal.ONE;
    }
    return new BigDecimal("0.1");
  }

  private static BigDecimal toBigDecimal(Double value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return BigDecimal.valueOf(value);
  }

  private static BigDecimal toBigDecimal(JsonNode value) {
    if (value == null || !value.isNumber()) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return new BigDecimal(value.asText());
    } catch (NumberFormatException ignored) {
      return BigDecimal.valueOf(value.asDouble());
    }
  }

  @SafeVarargs
  private static <T> T firstNonNull(T... values) {
    if (values == null || values.length == 0) {
      return null;
    }
    for (T value : values) {
      if (value != null) {
        return value;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static BigDecimal normalizedDecimal(BigDecimal value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    BigDecimal normalized = value.stripTrailingZeros();
    if (normalized.scale() < 0) {
      normalized = normalized.setScale(0, RoundingMode.UNNECESSARY);
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private Component clearOverrideButton(
      LayerFieldRow row, boolean editMode, ObjectNode draftDeclared, Runnable refresh) {
    Button clear = new Button("Clear");
    clear.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    clear.addClassName("stitch-config-clear-override");
    clear.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Clear override for " + row.path());
    clear.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Clear override");
    clear.setEnabled(editMode && editable && row.overridden() && row.editable());
    clear.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          clearDraftValue(draftDeclared, row.path());
          syncPreviewFromDraft(draftDeclared);
          markDirty.run();
          refresh.run();
        });
    return clear;
  }

  private void syncPreviewFromDraft(ObjectNode draftDeclared) {
    setPreviewValue(prettyJson(draftDeclared));
  }

  private static ObjectNode parseDraftDeclared(String previewValue, ObjectNode fallback) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(previewValue);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return fallback.deepCopy();
    }
    try {
      JsonNode parsed = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().readTree(normalized);
      if (parsed instanceof ObjectNode objectNode) {
        return objectNode.deepCopy();
      }
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
    }
    return fallback.deepCopy();
  }

  private static ObjectNode objectNode(JsonNode value) {
    if (value instanceof ObjectNode object) {
      return object.deepCopy();
    }
    return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
  }

  private static LinkedHashMap<String, JsonNode> flattenLeaves(JsonNode payload) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, JsonNode> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    flatten("", payload, values);
    return values;
  }

  private static void flatten(String prefix, JsonNode value, Map<String, JsonNode> output) {
    if (value == null || value.isNull()) {
      if (!prefix.isBlank()) {
        output.put(prefix, value);
      }
      return;
    }
    if (value.isObject()) {
      value.fieldNames()
          .forEachRemaining(
              field -> flatten(join(prefix, field), value.get(field), output));
      return;
    }
    if (value.isArray()) {
      for (int index = 0; index < value.size(); index++) {
        flatten(join(prefix, "[" + index + "]"), value.get(index), output);
      }
      return;
    }
    if (!prefix.isBlank()) {
      output.put(prefix, value);
    }
  }

  private static String join(String left, String right) {
    if (left == null || left.isBlank()) {
      return right;
    }
    if (right.startsWith("[")) {
      return left + right;
    }
    return left + "." + right;
  }

  private static JsonNode valueAtPath(JsonNode object, String path) {
    if (!(object instanceof ObjectNode) || Strings.trimToNull(path) == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String[] segments = path.split("\\.");
    JsonNode cursor = object;
    for (String segment : segments) {
      if (cursor == null || !cursor.isObject()) {
        return null;
      }
      if (segment.contains("[")) {
        return null;
      }
      cursor = cursor.get(segment);
    }
    return cursor == null || cursor.isNull() ? null : cursor;
  }

  private static void updateDraftValue(ObjectNode root, String path, JsonNode value) {
    if (root == null || Strings.trimToNull(path) == null || path.contains("[")) {
      return;
    }
    String[] segments = path.split("\\.");
    ObjectNode cursor = root;
    for (int i = 0; i < segments.length - 1; i++) {
      String segment = segments[i];
      JsonNode next = cursor.get(segment);
      ObjectNode child;
      if (next instanceof ObjectNode objectNode) {
        child = objectNode;
      } else {
        child = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
        cursor.set(segment, child);
      }
      cursor = child;
    }
    cursor.set(segments[segments.length - 1], value == null ? TextNode.valueOf("") : value);
  }

  private static void clearDraftValue(ObjectNode root, String path) {
    if (root == null || Strings.trimToNull(path) == null || path.contains("[")) {
      return;
    }
    String[] segments = path.split("\\.");
    ObjectNode cursor = root;
    for (int i = 0; i < segments.length - 1; i++) {
      JsonNode next = cursor.get(segments[i]);
      if (!(next instanceof ObjectNode child)) {
        return;
      }
      cursor = child;
    }
    cursor.remove(segments[segments.length - 1]);
  }

  private static boolean jsonEquivalent(JsonNode left, JsonNode right) {
    if (left == right) {
      return true;
    }
    if (left == null || right == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return left.equals(right);
  }

  private static String detectType(
      JsonNode value, List<String> enumValues, JsonNode schemaDocument, String path) {
    if (enumValues != null && !enumValues.isEmpty()) {
      return "ENUM";
    }
    JsonNode schemaNode = schemaAtPath(schemaDocument, path);
    String schemaType = Strings.trimToNull(schemaNode == null ? null : schemaNode.path("type").asText(null));
    String schemaFormat =
        Strings.trimToNull(schemaNode == null ? null : schemaNode.path("format").asText(null));
    if (schemaType != null) {
      if ("boolean".equalsIgnoreCase(schemaType)) {
        return "BOOLEAN";
      }
      if ("integer".equalsIgnoreCase(schemaType)) {
        if (schemaFormat != null
            && ("int64".equalsIgnoreCase(schemaFormat) || "long".equalsIgnoreCase(schemaFormat))) {
          return "LONG";
        }
        return "INTEGER";
      }
      if ("number".equalsIgnoreCase(schemaType)) {
        if (schemaFormat != null
            && ("decimal".equalsIgnoreCase(schemaFormat)
                || "bigdecimal".equalsIgnoreCase(schemaFormat))) {
          return "DECIMAL";
        }
        return "DOUBLE";
      }
      if ("array".equalsIgnoreCase(schemaType) || "object".equalsIgnoreCase(schemaType)) {
        return "JSON";
      }
      if ("string".equalsIgnoreCase(schemaType)) {
        return "STRING";
      }
    }
    if (value == null || value.isNull()) {
      return "STRING";
    }
    if (value.isBoolean()) {
      return "BOOLEAN";
    }
    if (value.isIntegralNumber()) {
      return "INTEGER";
    }
    if (value.isFloatingPointNumber()) {
      return "DOUBLE";
    }
    if (value.isContainerNode()) {
      return "JSON";
    }
    return "STRING";
  }

  private static String jsonValueToString(JsonNode value) {
    if (value == null || value.isNull()) {
      return "";
    }
    if (value.isTextual()) {
      return value.asText();
    }
    return value.toString();
  }

  private static List<String> enumValues(JsonNode schemaDocument, String path) {
    JsonNode schemaNode = schemaAtPath(schemaDocument, path);
    if (schemaNode == null || !schemaNode.isObject()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    JsonNode enumNode = schemaNode.path("enum");
    if (!enumNode.isArray() || enumNode.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> values = new ArrayList<>();
    for (JsonNode entry : enumNode) {
      values.add(entry == null ? "" : entry.asText());
    }
    return List.copyOf(values);
  }

  private static Set<String> flattenDeclaredPaths(JsonNode payload) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> keys = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    if (payload == null) {
      return keys;
    }
    flattenLeaves(payload).keySet().stream()
        .map(Strings::trimToNull)
        .filter(Objects::nonNull)
        .forEach(keys::add);
    return Set.copyOf(keys);
  }

  private static JsonNode schemaAtPath(JsonNode schemaDocument, String path) {
    if (schemaDocument == null || !schemaDocument.isObject() || Strings.trimToNull(path) == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String[] segments = path.split("\\.");
    JsonNode cursor = schemaDocument;
    for (String segment : segments) {
      if (segment.contains("[") || cursor == null) {
        return null;
      }
      cursor = cursor.path("properties").path(segment);
      if (cursor.isMissingNode()) {
        return null;
      }
    }
    return cursor;
  }

  private static ValidationResult validateDraft(
      ObjectNode declaredPayload, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView view) {
    if (declaredPayload == null || view == null) {
      return ValidationResult.success();
    }
    JsonNode schemaDocument = view.schemaDocument();
    if (schemaDocument == null || !schemaDocument.isObject()) {
      return ValidationResult.success();
    }

    LinkedHashMap<String, String> errors = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    LinkedHashMap<String, JsonNode> declaredLeaves = flattenLeaves(declaredPayload);
    for (Map.Entry<String, JsonNode> entry : declaredLeaves.entrySet()) {
      String path = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
      if (path == null) {
        continue;
      }
      JsonNode schemaNode = schemaAtPath(schemaDocument, path);
      if (schemaNode == null || !schemaNode.isObject()) {
        continue;
      }
      String error = validateValueAgainstSchema(entry.getValue(), schemaNode);
      if (error != null) {
        errors.put(path, error);
      }
    }

    ObjectNode effectivePayload = mergeResolvedWithDeclared(view.resolvedPayload(), declaredPayload);
    validateRequired(schemaDocument, effectivePayload, "", errors);
    if (errors.isEmpty()) {
      return ValidationResult.success();
    }
    return ValidationResult.invalid(errors);
  }

  private static String validateValueAgainstSchema(JsonNode value, JsonNode schemaNode) {
    if (schemaNode == null || !schemaNode.isObject()) {
      return null;
    }
    JsonNode enumNode = schemaNode.path("enum");
    if (enumNode.isArray() && !enumNode.isEmpty()) {
      String candidate = jsonValueToString(value);
      for (JsonNode allowed : enumNode) {
        if (Objects.equals(candidate, jsonValueToString(allowed))) {
          return null;
        }
      }
      return "Value must be one of the defined enum options.";
    }

    String type = Strings.trimToNull(schemaNode.path("type").asText(null));
    if (type == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return switch (type.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)) {
      case "boolean" -> value != null && value.isBoolean() ? null : "Expected boolean value.";
      case "integer" ->
          value != null && value.isIntegralNumber() ? null : "Expected integer value.";
      case "number" -> value != null && value.isNumber() ? null : "Expected numeric value.";
      case "string" -> value != null && value.isTextual() ? null : "Expected text value.";
      case "object" -> value != null && value.isObject() ? null : "Expected object value.";
      case "array" -> value != null && value.isArray() ? null : "Expected array value.";
      default -> null;
    };
  }

  private static ObjectNode mergeResolvedWithDeclared(JsonNode resolvedPayload, ObjectNode declaredPayload) {
    ObjectNode merged = objectNode(resolvedPayload);
    mergeObject(merged, declaredPayload);
    return merged;
  }

  private static void mergeObject(ObjectNode target, JsonNode source) {
    if (target == null || source == null || !source.isObject()) {
      return;
    }
    source
        .fields()
        .forEachRemaining(
            entry -> {
              String key = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
              if (key == null) {
                return;
              }
              JsonNode sourceValue = entry.getValue();
              JsonNode targetValue = target.get(key);
              if (sourceValue != null
                  && sourceValue.isObject()
                  && targetValue != null
                  && targetValue.isObject()) {
                mergeObject((ObjectNode) targetValue, sourceValue);
                return;
              }
              target.set(key, sourceValue == null ? NullNode.instance : sourceValue.deepCopy());
            });
  }

  private static void validateRequired(
      JsonNode schemaNode, JsonNode valueNode, String pathPrefix, Map<String, String> errors) {
    if (schemaNode == null || !schemaNode.isObject()) {
      return;
    }
    JsonNode requiredNode = schemaNode.path("required");
    if (requiredNode.isArray()) {
      for (JsonNode requiredField : requiredNode) {
        String field = Strings.trimToNull(requiredField == null ? null : requiredField.asText(null));
        if (field == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String path = pathPrefix.isBlank() ? field : pathPrefix + "." + field;
        JsonNode child =
            valueNode != null && valueNode.isObject() ? valueNode.get(field) : null;
        if (child == null || child.isNull()) {
          errors.putIfAbsent(path, "Required value is missing.");
        }
      }
    }

    JsonNode propertiesNode = schemaNode.path("properties");
    if (!propertiesNode.isObject()) {
      return;
    }
    propertiesNode
        .fields()
        .forEachRemaining(
            entry -> {
              String childKey = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
              if (childKey == null) {
                return;
              }
              JsonNode nextValue =
                  valueNode != null && valueNode.isObject() ? valueNode.get(childKey) : null;
              String childPath = pathPrefix.isBlank() ? childKey : pathPrefix + "." + childKey;
              validateRequired(entry.getValue(), nextValue, childPath, errors);
            });
  }

  private static ImpactContext buildImpactContext(
      Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> layersByPath, String selectedLayerId) {
    String normalizedSelectedLayerId = Strings.trimToNull(selectedLayerId);
    if (layersByPath == null || layersByPath.isEmpty()) {
      return ImpactContext.empty(normalizedSelectedLayerId);
    }
    Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> byLayerId = indexByLayerId(layersByPath);
    if (byLayerId.isEmpty()) {
      return ImpactContext.empty(normalizedSelectedLayerId);
    }

    LinkedHashMap<String, String> parentByLayerId = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    LinkedHashMap<String, Set<String>> declaredPathsByLayerId = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    LinkedHashMap<String, List<String>> childrenByLayerId = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String layerId : byLayerId.keySet()) {
      childrenByLayerId.put(layerId, new ArrayList<>());
    }
    for (StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord layer : byLayerId.values()) {
      String layerId = Strings.trimToNull(layer.layerId());
      if (layerId == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String parentId = Strings.trimToNull(layer.parentLayerId());
      parentByLayerId.put(layerId, parentId);
      declaredPathsByLayerId.put(layerId, flattenDeclaredPaths(layer.declared()));
      if (parentId != null && childrenByLayerId.containsKey(parentId)) {
        childrenByLayerId.get(parentId).add(layerId);
      }
    }

    List<String> leafLayerIds = new ArrayList<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, List<String>> entry : childrenByLayerId.entrySet()) {
      List<String> children = entry.getValue();
      if (children == null || children.isEmpty()) {
        leafLayerIds.add(entry.getKey());
      }
    }
    return new ImpactContext(
        normalizedSelectedLayerId,
        Collections.unmodifiableMap(new LinkedHashMap<>(parentByLayerId)),
        Map.copyOf(declaredPathsByLayerId),
        List.copyOf(leafLayerIds),
        leafLayerIds.size());
  }

  private static ImpactCell impactForPath(
      String path,
      String sourceLayerId,
      ImpactContext context,
      Set<String> selectedLayerDeclaredPaths,
      Map<ImpactLookupKey, ImpactCell> cache) {
    String normalizedPath = Strings.trimToNull(path);
    String normalizedLayer = Strings.trimToNull(sourceLayerId);
    if (normalizedPath == null
        || normalizedLayer == null
        || context == null
        || context.totalLeafLayers() <= 0
        || context.leafLayerIds().isEmpty()) {
      return ImpactCell.unavailable();
    }
    ImpactLookupKey cacheKey = new ImpactLookupKey(normalizedPath, normalizedLayer);
    ImpactCell cached = cache.get(cacheKey);
    if (cached != null) {
      return cached;
    }
    int affected = 0;
    for (String leafLayerId : context.leafLayerIds()) {
      String effectiveSource =
          effectiveSourceLayerId(
              normalizedPath, leafLayerId, context, selectedLayerDeclaredPaths);
      if (Objects.equals(normalizedLayer, effectiveSource)) {
        affected++;
      }
    }
    ImpactCell computed = new ImpactCell(affected + "/" + context.totalLeafLayers(), affected, context.totalLeafLayers(), normalizedLayer);
    cache.put(cacheKey, computed);
    return computed;
  }

  private static String effectiveSourceLayerId(
      String key,
      String leafLayerId,
      ImpactContext context,
      Set<String> selectedLayerDeclaredPaths) {
    if (Strings.trimToNull(key) == null || Strings.trimToNull(leafLayerId) == null || context == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String current = Strings.trimToNull(leafLayerId);
    while (current != null) {
      Set<String> declaredPaths =
          Objects.equals(current, context.selectedLayerId())
              ? selectedLayerDeclaredPaths
              : context.declaredPathsByLayerId().getOrDefault(current, Set.of());
      if (declaredPaths.contains(key)) {
        return current;
      }
      current = context.parentByLayerId().get(current);
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> indexByLayerId(
      Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> layersByPath) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> byLayerId = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (layersByPath == null || layersByPath.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    for (StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord layer : layersByPath.values()) {
      if (layer == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String layerId = Strings.trimToNull(layer.layerId());
      if (layerId == null || byLayerId.containsKey(layerId)) {
        continue;
      }
      byLayerId.put(layerId, layer);
    }
    return Map.copyOf(byLayerId);
  }

  private static String impactHeatColor(int affected, int total) {
    if (total <= 0) {
      return "#98a6b5";
    }
    double ratio = Math.max(0.0, Math.min(1.0, (double) affected / (double) total));
    double hue = 120.0 * (1.0 - ratio);
    return String.format("hsl(%.1f, 72%%, 58%%)", hue);
  }

  private record LayerFieldRow(
      String path,
      String type,
      String sourceLayer,
      JsonNode value,
      boolean selectedLayer,
      boolean inherited,
      boolean overridden,
      boolean modified,
      boolean cleared,
      boolean editable,
      List<String> enumValues,
      String validationError,
      ImpactCell impact) {}

  private record ImpactLookupKey(String path, String sourceLayerId) {}

  private record ImpactContext(
      String selectedLayerId,
      Map<String, String> parentByLayerId,
      Map<String, Set<String>> declaredPathsByLayerId,
      List<String> leafLayerIds,
      int totalLeafLayers) {
    static ImpactContext empty(String selectedLayerId) {
      return new ImpactContext(selectedLayerId, Map.of(), Map.of(), List.of(), 0);
    }
  }

  private record ImpactCell(String label, int affected, int total, String sourceLayer) {
    static ImpactCell unavailable() {
      return new ImpactCell("-", 0, 0, null);
    }
  }

  private record ValidationResult(Map<String, String> errorsByPath) {
    static ValidationResult success() {
      return new ValidationResult(Map.of());
    }

    static ValidationResult invalid(Map<String, String> errorsByPath) {
      return new ValidationResult(errorsByPath == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(errorsByPath));
    }

    boolean isValid() {
      return errorsByPath == null || errorsByPath.isEmpty();
    }
  }

  private static Map<String, String> selectOverview(Map<String, String> all) {
    return selectByLabels(
        all,
        List.of(
            "Group",
            "Name",
            "Layer",
            "Parent Layer",
            "Short Name",
            "Schema Key",
            "Mode",
            "State",
            "Path",
            "Pending",
            "Pending State",
            "Pending Mode",
            "Pending Effective",
            "Pending Expires",
            "Future Effective"));
  }

  private static Map<String, String> selectRuntime(Map<String, String> all) {
    return selectByLabels(
        all,
        List.of(
            "Config Version",
            "Effective Config",
            "Scheduled Entries",
            "Effective",
            "Updated",
            "Updated By",
            "Release",
            "Target Release",
            "Resolved At",
            "Lineage",
            "Impact",
            "Source Keys"));
  }

  private static Map<String, String> selectByLabels(Map<String, String> all, List<String> labels) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> selected = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (all == null || all.isEmpty()) {
      return selected;
    }
    for (String label : labels) {
      if (all.containsKey(label)) {
        selected.put(label, all.get(label));
      }
    }
    return selected;
  }

  private static JsonNode parseDeclaredJson(String value) throws Exception {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Declared payload is required.");
    }
    JsonNode parsed = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().readTree(normalized);
    if (parsed == null || !parsed.isObject()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Declared payload must be a JSON object.");
    }
    return parsed;
  }

  private static String prettyJsonStatic(JsonNode value) {
    JsonNode normalized = value == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : value;
    try {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().writerWithDefaultPrettyPrinter().writeValueAsString(normalized);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      return normalized.toString();
    }
  }

  private static void openJsonDialog(StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record) {
    new StitchJsonDialog(
            "Raw JSON - " + Strings.firstNonBlank(record.layerId(), "layer"),
            record.declared())
        .open();
  }

  private static String lineageProgression(List<String> lineageLayers) {
    if (lineageLayers == null || lineageLayers.isEmpty()) {
      return "LINEAGE";
    }
    return lineageLayers.stream()
        .map(layer -> Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(layer), "-"))
        .map(value -> value.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT))
        .collect(java.util.stream.Collectors.joining(" -> "));
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/configs/StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.configs;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.workflow.ConfigAdminService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfigChange;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfigLayer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.StitchIdentityContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

/** Configs approvals queue + actions provider, separated from core view/edit provider. */
public final class StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider {
  private final SessionImpl session;
  private final StitchConfigsProvider configsProvider;

  public StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext, StitchConfigsProvider configsProvider) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    this.configsProvider = Objects.requireNonNull(configsProvider, "configsProvider");
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(current instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    this.session = resolved;
  }

  public List<String> listGroups() {
    return configsProvider.listGroups();
  }

  public List<ApprovalRecord> listApprovalQueue(String group) {
    String normalizedGroup = trimToNull(group);
    DiscoveryCache cache = requireCache();
    List<DefinitionConfigChange> changes =
        normalizedGroup == null
            ? cache.list(DefinitionConfigChange.class)
            : cache.list(DefinitionConfigChange.class, normalizedGroup);
    if (changes.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return changes.stream()
        .map(this::toApprovalRecord)
        .filter(Objects::nonNull)
        .sorted(
            Comparator.comparing(
                    ApprovalRecord::updatedTimeUtc,
                    Comparator.nullsLast(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
                .reversed()
                .thenComparing(
                    value -> Strings.firstNonBlank(value.group(), ""),
                    String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
                .thenComparing(
                    value -> Strings.firstNonBlank(value.configName(), ""),
                    String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
                .thenComparing(
                    value -> Strings.firstNonBlank(value.layerId(), ""),
                    String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
        .toList();
  }

  public ApprovalDetails loadApprovalDetails(ApprovalRecord record) {
    ApprovalRecord required = Objects.requireNonNull(record, "record");
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord layer = resolveLayer(required);
    StitchConfigsProvider.ComparePayload live = configsProvider.resolveLivePayload(layer);
    return new ApprovalDetails(required, layer, live);
  }

  public List<StitchConfigCompareDialog.CompareTarget> compareTargets(ApprovalRecord record) {
    ApprovalRecord required = Objects.requireNonNull(record, "record");
    StitchConfigsProvider.TreeModel tree =
        configsProvider.loadLayers(required.group(), required.configName());
    if (tree.layersByPath().isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return tree.layersByPath().values().stream()
        .filter(Objects::nonNull)
        .filter(candidate -> !Objects.equals(candidate.layerId(), required.layerId()))
        .sorted(
            Comparator.comparing(
                candidate ->
                    Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(candidate.path()), candidate.layerId()),
                String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
        .map(
            candidate ->
                new StitchConfigCompareDialog.CompareTarget(
                    Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(candidate.path()), candidate.layerId()),
                    Strings.firstNonBlank(candidate.shortName(), candidate.layerId()),
                    candidate.declared()))
        .toList();
  }

  public void approve(ApprovalRecord record, String comment) {
    ApprovalRecord required = Objects.requireNonNull(record, "record");
    workflow()
        .approve(
            required.group(),
            required.configName(),
            required.layerId(),
            Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(comment), "STITCH APPROVE"),
            StitchIdentityContext.currentSubject());
  }

  public void reject(ApprovalRecord record, String comment) {
    ApprovalRecord required = Objects.requireNonNull(record, "record");
    workflow()
        .reject(
            required.group(),
            required.configName(),
            required.layerId(),
            Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(comment), "STITCH REJECT"),
            StitchIdentityContext.currentSubject());
  }

  public void publishEmergency(ApprovalRecord record, String comment) {
    ApprovalRecord required = Objects.requireNonNull(record, "record");
    workflow()
        .publish(
            required.group(),
            required.configName(),
            required.layerId(),
            DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeMode.IMMEDIATE,
            null,
            null,
            Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(comment), "STITCH NUCLEAR PUBLISH"),
            StitchIdentityContext.currentSubject());
  }

  private ApprovalRecord toApprovalRecord(DefinitionConfigChange change) {
    if (change == null) {
      return null;
    }
    DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeEntry entry = firstChangeEntry(change.changes());
    DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState state = entry == null ? change.state() : entry.state();
    if (!pendingApprovalState(state)) {
      return null;
    }
    String group =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            trimToNull(change.group()),
            trimToNull(change.envelope() == null ? null : change.envelope().group()));
    String configName = trimToNull(change.configId());
    String layerId = trimToNull(change.layerId());
    if (group == null || configName == null || layerId == null) {
      return null;
    }

    DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeMode mode = entry == null ? change.mode() : entry.mode();
    JsonNode proposed = entry == null ? change.draftDeclared() : entry.draftDeclared();
    String effectiveAtUtc = entry == null ? change.effectiveAtUtc() : entry.effectiveAtUtc();
    String expiresAtUtc = entry == null ? change.expiresAtUtc() : entry.expiresAtUtc();
    String proposedBy =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            entry == null ? null : trimToNull(entry.createdBySubject()),
            trimToNull(change.createdBySubject()));
    String updatedBy =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            entry == null ? null : trimToNull(entry.updatedBySubject()),
            trimToNull(change.updatedBySubject()),
            proposedBy);
    String updatedTimeUtc =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            entry == null ? null : trimToNull(entry.updatedTimeUtc()),
            trimToNull(change.updatedTimeUtc()),
            entry == null ? null : trimToNull(entry.createdTimeUtc()),
            trimToNull(change.createdTimeUtc()));
    String changeId =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            entry == null ? null : trimToNull(entry.changeId()),
            trimToNull(change.envelope() == null ? null : change.envelope().uuid()),
            configName + "/" + layerId);
    return new ApprovalRecord(
        group,
        configName,
        layerId,
        changeId,
        state,
        mode == null ? DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeMode.IMMEDIATE : mode,
        trimToNull(effectiveAtUtc),
        trimToNull(expiresAtUtc),
        proposedBy,
        updatedBy,
        updatedTimeUtc,
        trimToNull(entry == null ? change.rationale() : entry.rationale()),
        safePayload(proposed));
  }

  private StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord resolveLayer(ApprovalRecord approval) {
    StitchConfigsProvider.TreeModel tree =
        configsProvider.loadLayers(approval.group(), approval.configName());
    for (StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord candidate : tree.layersByPath().values()) {
      if (candidate != null && Objects.equals(approval.layerId(), candidate.layerId())) {
        return candidate;
      }
    }
    return new StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord(
        approval.group(),
        approval.configName(),
        approval.layerId(),
        null,
        approval.layerId(),
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        approval.proposedPayload(),
        List.of(),
        null,
        approval.layerId());
  }

  private ConfigAdminService.Workflow workflow() {
    return session.internal().configAdminService().workflow();
  }

  private DiscoveryCache requireCache() {
    DiscoveryCache cache = session.internal().discoveryCache();
    if (cache == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DiscoveryCache is not available");
    }
    return cache;
  }

  private static DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeEntry firstChangeEntry(
      List<DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeEntry> entries) {
    if (entries == null || entries.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    for (DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeEntry entry : entries) {
      if (entry != null) {
        return entry;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static boolean pendingApprovalState(DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState state) {
    if (state == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return switch (state) {
      case PROPOSED, APPROVED, DRAFT -> true;
      default -> false;
    };
  }

  private static JsonNode safePayload(JsonNode value) {
    return value == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : value.deepCopy();
  }

  private static Instant parseUtc(String value) {
    String normalized = trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return Instant.parse(normalized);
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    return Strings.trimToNull(value);
  }

  private static String displayUtcOrDash(String value) {
    String normalized = trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return "-";
    }
    Instant parsed = parseUtc(normalized);
    return parsed == null ? normalized : parsed.toString();
  }

  public record ApprovalRecord(
      String group,
      String configName,
      String layerId,
      String changeId,
      DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState state,
      DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeMode mode,
      String effectiveAtUtc,
      String expiresAtUtc,
      String proposedBySubject,
      String updatedBySubject,
      String updatedTimeUtc,
      String rationale,
      JsonNode proposedPayload) {
    public ApprovalRecord {
      group = trimToNull(group);
      configName = trimToNull(configName);
      layerId = trimToNull(layerId);
      changeId = trimToNull(changeId);
      effectiveAtUtc = trimToNull(effectiveAtUtc);
      expiresAtUtc = trimToNull(expiresAtUtc);
      proposedBySubject = trimToNull(proposedBySubject);
      updatedBySubject = trimToNull(updatedBySubject);
      updatedTimeUtc = trimToNull(updatedTimeUtc);
      rationale = trimToNull(rationale);
      state = state == null ? DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState.UNKNOWN : state;
      mode = mode == null ? DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeMode.IMMEDIATE : mode;
      proposedPayload = safePayload(proposedPayload);
    }

    public String key() {
      return Strings.firstNonBlank(changeId, group + "/" + configName + "/" + layerId);
    }

    public boolean canApprove() {
      return state == DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState.PROPOSED
          || state == DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState.DRAFT;
    }

    public boolean canReject() {
      return state == DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState.PROPOSED
          || state == DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState.APPROVED
          || state == DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState.DRAFT;
    }

    public boolean canPublishEmergency() {
      return state == DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState.APPROVED
          || state == DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState.PROPOSED
          || state == DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState.DRAFT;
    }

    public String stateLabel() {
      return state == null ? "UNKNOWN" : state.name();
    }

    public String modeLabel() {
      if (mode == null) {
        return "IMMEDIATE";
      }
      return switch (mode) {
        case IMMEDIATE -> "Immediate";
        case SCHEDULED -> "Scheduled";
        default -> "Unknown";
      };
    }

    public String proposedByLabel() {
      return Strings.firstNonBlank(proposedBySubject, updatedBySubject, "-");
    }

    public String effectiveLabel() {
      return displayUtcOrDash(effectiveAtUtc);
    }

    public String expiresLabel() {
      return displayUtcOrDash(expiresAtUtc);
    }

    public String updatedLabel() {
      return displayUtcOrDash(updatedTimeUtc);
    }

    public String compareContext() {
      return "Group: "
          + Strings.firstNonBlank(group, "-")
          + " | Name: "
          + Strings.firstNonBlank(configName, "-")
          + " | Layer: "
          + Strings.firstNonBlank(layerId, "-");
    }

    public Map<String, String> workflowMetadata() {
      LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      values.put("Workflow State", stateLabel());
      values.put("Submission Mode", modeLabel());
      values.put("Effective", effectiveLabel());
      values.put("Expires", expiresLabel());
      values.put("Proposed By", proposedByLabel());
      values.put("Updated", updatedLabel());
      values.put("Change Id", Strings.firstNonBlank(changeId, "-"));
      values.put("Rationale", Strings.firstNonBlank(rationale, "-"));
      return values;
    }
  }

  public record ApprovalDetails(
      ApprovalRecord submission,
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord layer,
      StitchConfigsProvider.ComparePayload livePayload) {}
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/configs/StitchConfigScheduleControls.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.configs;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.checkbox.Checkbox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.datepicker.DatePicker;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.timepicker.TimePicker;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.time.LocalDate;
import java.time.LocalDateTime;
import java.time.LocalTime;
import java.time.ZoneOffset;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** Shared submission controls for Configs workflows. */
public final class StitchConfigScheduleControls extends VerticalLayout {
  private final Checkbox approvalRequired = new Checkbox("Approval required");
  private final Checkbox scheduleEnabled = new Checkbox("Schedule");
  private final Checkbox effectiveEnabled = new Checkbox("Effective");
  private final DatePicker effectiveDate = new DatePicker("Effective Date (UTC)");
  private final TimePicker effectiveTime = new TimePicker("Effective Time (UTC)");
  private final Checkbox expiryEnabled = new Checkbox("Expiry");
  private final DatePicker expiryDate = new DatePicker("Expiry Date (UTC)");
  private final TimePicker expiryTime = new TimePicker("Expiry Time (UTC)");
  private final HorizontalLayout effectiveRow = new HorizontalLayout();
  private final HorizontalLayout expiryRow = new HorizontalLayout();

  public StitchConfigScheduleControls() {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(true);
    setWidthFull();
    addClassName("stitch-config-submit-options");

    approvalRequired.setValue(true);
    approvalRequired.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Approval required");

    scheduleEnabled.setValue(false);
    scheduleEnabled.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Enable scheduling");

    effectiveEnabled.setValue(true);
    effectiveEnabled.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Enable effective time");

    effectiveDate.setWidthFull();
    effectiveDate.setClearButtonVisible(false);
    effectiveDate.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Effective date in UTC");

    effectiveTime.setWidth("11rem");
    effectiveTime.setStep(java.time.Duration.ofMinutes(1));
    effectiveTime.setClearButtonVisible(false);
    effectiveTime.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Effective time in UTC");

    expiryEnabled.setValue(false);
    expiryEnabled.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Enable expiry time");

    expiryDate.setWidthFull();
    expiryDate.setClearButtonVisible(false);
    expiryDate.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Expiry date in UTC");

    expiryTime.setWidth("11rem");
    expiryTime.setStep(java.time.Duration.ofMinutes(1));
    expiryTime.setClearButtonVisible(false);
    expiryTime.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Expiry time in UTC");

    effectiveRow.setPadding(false);
    effectiveRow.setSpacing(true);
    effectiveRow.setWidthFull();
    effectiveRow.addClassName("stitch-config-submit-time-row");
    effectiveRow.add(effectiveDate, effectiveTime);
    effectiveRow.setFlexGrow(1, effectiveDate);

    expiryRow.setPadding(false);
    expiryRow.setSpacing(true);
    expiryRow.setWidthFull();
    expiryRow.addClassName("stitch-config-submit-time-row");
    expiryRow.add(expiryDate, expiryTime);
    expiryRow.setFlexGrow(1, expiryDate);

    scheduleEnabled.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(event.getValue())) {
            ensureEffectiveDefaults();
          }
          refreshVisibility();
        });
    effectiveEnabled.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(event.getValue())) {
            ensureEffectiveDefaults();
          }
          refreshVisibility();
        });
    expiryEnabled.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(event.getValue())) {
            ensureExpiryDefaults();
          }
          refreshVisibility();
        });

    add(
        approvalRequired,
        scheduleEnabled,
        effectiveEnabled,
        effectiveRow,
        expiryEnabled,
        expiryRow);
    setSubmissionOptions(null);
  }

  public void setSubmissionOptions(StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions options) {
    StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions value =
        options == null ? StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions.immediate() : options;
    approvalRequired.setValue(value.approvalRequired());
    boolean scheduled = value.mode() == StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionMode.SCHEDULED;
    scheduleEnabled.setValue(scheduled);
    effectiveEnabled.setValue(true);
    setEffectiveDateTime(defaultEffectiveDateTime(value.effectiveAtUtc()));
    setExpiryDateTime(defaultExpiryDateTime(value.expiresAtUtc()));
    expiryEnabled.setValue(value.expiresAtUtc() != null);
    refreshVisibility();
  }

  public StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions submissionOptions(String note) {
    boolean scheduled = Boolean.TRUE.equals(scheduleEnabled.getValue());
    StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionMode mode =
        scheduled
            ? StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionMode.SCHEDULED
            : StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionMode.IMMEDIATE;
    Instant effective =
        scheduled && Boolean.TRUE.equals(effectiveEnabled.getValue())
            ? toInstant(effectiveDate.getValue(), effectiveTime.getValue())
            : null;
    Instant expires =
        scheduled && Boolean.TRUE.equals(expiryEnabled.getValue())
            ? toInstant(expiryDate.getValue(), expiryTime.getValue())
            : null;
    return new StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions(
        mode,
        effective,
        expires,
        Strings.trimToNull(note),
        Boolean.TRUE.equals(approvalRequired.getValue()));
  }

  public List<String> validationErrors() {
    List<String> errors = new ArrayList<>();
    if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(scheduleEnabled.getValue())) {
      if (!Boolean.TRUE.equals(effectiveEnabled.getValue())) {
        errors.add("Effective time must be enabled for scheduled submissions.");
      }
      LocalDateTime effective =
          Boolean.TRUE.equals(effectiveEnabled.getValue())
              ? toLocalDateTime(effectiveDate.getValue(), effectiveTime.getValue())
              : null;
      if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(effectiveEnabled.getValue()) && effective == null) {
        errors.add("Effective date and time are required.");
      }
      if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(expiryEnabled.getValue())) {
        LocalDateTime expires = toLocalDateTime(expiryDate.getValue(), expiryTime.getValue());
        if (expires == null) {
          errors.add("Expiry date and time are required when expiry is enabled.");
        } else if (effective != null && !expires.isAfter(effective)) {
          errors.add("Expiry time must be after effective time.");
        }
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(errors);
  }

  private void refreshVisibility() {
    boolean scheduled = Boolean.TRUE.equals(scheduleEnabled.getValue());
    effectiveEnabled.setVisible(scheduled);
    effectiveRow.setVisible(scheduled);
    boolean effectiveActive = scheduled && Boolean.TRUE.equals(effectiveEnabled.getValue());
    effectiveDate.setEnabled(effectiveActive);
    effectiveTime.setEnabled(effectiveActive);

    expiryEnabled.setVisible(scheduled);
    expiryRow.setVisible(scheduled);
    boolean expiryActive = scheduled && Boolean.TRUE.equals(expiryEnabled.getValue());
    expiryDate.setEnabled(expiryActive);
    expiryTime.setEnabled(expiryActive);
  }

  private void ensureEffectiveDefaults() {
    if (effectiveDate.getValue() == null) {
      effectiveDate.setValue(todayUtc());
    }
    if (effectiveTime.getValue() == null) {
      effectiveTime.setValue(LocalTime.MIDNIGHT);
    }
  }

  private void ensureExpiryDefaults() {
    if (expiryDate.getValue() == null) {
      expiryDate.setValue(todayUtc().plusDays(1));
    }
    if (expiryTime.getValue() == null) {
      expiryTime.setValue(LocalTime.MIDNIGHT);
    }
  }

  private void setEffectiveDateTime(LocalDateTime value) {
    LocalDateTime normalized = value == null ? defaultEffectiveDateTime(null) : value;
    effectiveDate.setValue(normalized.toLocalDate());
    effectiveTime.setValue(normalized.toLocalTime());
  }

  private void setExpiryDateTime(LocalDateTime value) {
    LocalDateTime normalized = value == null ? defaultExpiryDateTime(null) : value;
    expiryDate.setValue(normalized.toLocalDate());
    expiryTime.setValue(normalized.toLocalTime());
  }

  private static LocalDateTime defaultEffectiveDateTime(Instant configured) {
    if (configured != null) {
      return LocalDateTime.ofInstant(configured, ZoneOffset.UTC);
    }
    return LocalDateTime.of(todayUtc(), LocalTime.MIDNIGHT);
  }

  private static LocalDateTime defaultExpiryDateTime(Instant configured) {
    if (configured != null) {
      return LocalDateTime.ofInstant(configured, ZoneOffset.UTC);
    }
    return LocalDateTime.of(todayUtc().plusDays(1), LocalTime.MIDNIGHT);
  }

  private static LocalDate todayUtc() {
    return LocalDate.now(ZoneOffset.UTC);
  }

  private static LocalDateTime toLocalDateTime(LocalDate date, LocalTime time) {
    if (date == null || time == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return LocalDateTime.of(date, time);
  }

  private static Instant toInstant(LocalDate date, LocalTime time) {
    LocalDateTime value = toLocalDateTime(date, time);
    return value == null ? null : value.toInstant(ZoneOffset.UTC);
  }
}
