    historyModeColumn =
        grid
            .addComponentColumn(value -> statusBadge(value == null ? null : value.modeLabel()))
            .setHeader("Mode")
            .setWidth("9rem")
            .setFlexGrow(0)
            .setResizable(true);
    historyEffectiveColumn =
        grid
            .addColumn(value -> value == null ? "-" : value.effectiveLabel())
            .setHeader("Effective")
            .setWidth("13rem")
            .setFlexGrow(0)
            .setResizable(true);
    historyUpdatedByColumn =
        grid
            .addColumn(value -> value == null ? "-" : value.updatedByLabel())
            .setHeader("Updated By")
            .setWidth("12rem")
            .setFlexGrow(0)
            .setResizable(true);
    historyUpdatedColumn =
        grid
            .addColumn(value -> value == null ? "-" : value.updatedLabel())
            .setHeader("Updated")
            .setWidth("13rem")
            .setFlexGrow(0)
            .setResizable(true);
    historyKeysColumn =
        grid
            .addColumn(value -> value == null ? 0 : value.keysCount())
            .setHeader("Keys")
            .setWidth("7rem")
            .setFlexGrow(0)
            .setResizable(true);

    StitchRowActions<StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackRecord> rowActions = new StitchRowActions<>();
    rowActions.addAction(
        StitchRowActions.Action.icon(VaadinIcon.EXTERNAL_LINK, "OPEN", this::openHistoryDialog));
    rowActions.addColumn(grid).setFrozenToEnd(true);
    grid.addItemDoubleClickListener(event -> openHistoryDialog(event.getItem()));

    historyPanel.setDetailTitle("Release Details");
    historyPanel.setDetailContent(NO_HISTORY_SELECTED);
    historyPanel.setDetailActions();

    historyRoot.add(historyPanel);
  }

  private void configureEmergencyTab() {
    emergencyRoot.setWidthFull();
    emergencyRoot.setHeight(null);
    emergencyRoot.setPadding(false);
    emergencyRoot.setSpacing(false);
    emergencyRoot.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-tab");
    emergencyRoot.getStyle().set("min-width", "0");

    emergencyPanel.setWidthFull();
    emergencyPanel.setHeight(null);
    emergencyPanel.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-panel");
    emergencyPanel.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-panel--table-only");
    emergencyPanel.split().setSplitterPosition(100);
    emergencyPanel.setQueueTitle("Emergency Publish Queue");
    emergencyPanel.setQueueEmptyState(
        "No emergency candidates",
        "No pending workflow submissions are available for emergency publish.");

    Grid<StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalRecord> grid = emergencyPanel.queueView().grid();
    grid.addThemeVariants(GridVariant.LUMO_ROW_STRIPES);
    grid.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-grid");
    grid.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-emergency-grid");
    grid
        .addColumn(value -> Strings.firstNonBlank(value == null ? null : value.layerId(), "-"))
        .setHeader("Layer")
        .setWidth("10rem")
        .setFlexGrow(0)
        .setResizable(true);
    grid
        .addComponentColumn(value -> statusBadge(value == null ? null : value.stateLabel()))
        .setHeader("Status")
        .setWidth("9rem")
        .setFlexGrow(0)
        .setResizable(true);
    grid
        .addComponentColumn(value -> statusBadge(value == null ? null : value.modeLabel()))
        .setHeader("Mode")
        .setWidth("9rem")
        .setFlexGrow(0)
        .setResizable(true);
    grid
        .addColumn(value -> value == null ? "-" : value.effectiveLabel())
        .setHeader("Effective")
        .setWidth("14rem")
        .setFlexGrow(0)
        .setResizable(true);
    grid
        .addColumn(value -> value == null ? "-" : value.proposedByLabel())
        .setHeader("Submitted By")
        .setWidth("12rem")
        .setFlexGrow(0)
        .setResizable(true);
    grid
        .addColumn(value -> value == null ? "-" : value.updatedLabel())
        .setHeader("Updated")
        .setWidth("14rem")
        .setFlexGrow(0)
        .setResizable(true);

    StitchRowActions<StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalRecord> rowActions = new StitchRowActions<>();
    rowActions.addAction(
        StitchRowActions.Action.icon(VaadinIcon.EXTERNAL_LINK, "OPEN", this::openEmergencyDialog));
    rowActions.addColumn(grid).setFrozenToEnd(true);
    grid.addItemDoubleClickListener(event -> openEmergencyDialog(event.getItem()));

    emergencyRoot.add(emergencyPanel);
  }

  private void addTab(String label, ControlTab key) {
    Tab tab = new Tab(label);
    tab.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", label + " tab");
    tabKeys.put(tab, key);
    tabs.add(tab);
  }
  private void activateTab(ControlTab tab, boolean refresh) {
    activeTab = tab == null ? ControlTab.PENDING : tab;
    if (refresh) {
      refreshActiveTab(true);
    }
    syncHistoryPresentation();
    Component root = tabRoot(activeTab);
    contentHost.removeAll();
    contentHost.add(root);
    selectTab(activeTab);
    syncFiltersBar();
  }

  private void syncFiltersBar() {
    filtersBar.clear();
    filtersBar.withGroupSelector(historySelectionBar);
    refreshButton
        .getElement()
        .setAttribute(
            "title",
            "Refresh " + Strings.firstNonBlank(activeTabLabel(activeTab), "control").toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
    filtersBar.withRightAction(refreshButton);
  }

  private static String activeTabLabel(ControlTab tab) {
    return switch (tab) {
      case HISTORY -> "History";
      case ROLLBACK -> "Rollback";
      case EMERGENCY -> "Emergency";
      case PENDING -> "Pending";
    };
  }

  private void syncHistoryPresentation() {
    boolean rollback = activeTab == ControlTab.ROLLBACK;
    historyPanel.setQueueTitle(rollback ? "Rollback Candidates" : "Release Timeline");
    historyPanel.setDetailTitle(rollback ? "Rollback Candidate" : "Release Details");
    if (historyRollbackOptionColumn != null) {
      historyRollbackOptionColumn.setVisible(rollback);
    }
    if (historyReleaseColumn != null) {
      historyReleaseColumn.setVisible(!rollback);
    }
    if (historyModeColumn != null) {
      historyModeColumn.setVisible(!rollback);
    }
    if (historyEffectiveColumn != null) {
      historyEffectiveColumn.setVisible(!rollback);
    }
    if (historyUpdatedByColumn != null) {
      historyUpdatedByColumn.setVisible(true);
    }
    if (historyUpdatedColumn != null) {
      historyUpdatedColumn.setVisible(true);
    }
    if (historyKeysColumn != null) {
      historyKeysColumn.setHeader(rollback ? "Fields" : "Keys");
      historyKeysColumn.setVisible(true);
    }
    if (rollback) {
      historyPanel.setQueueEmptyState(
          "No rollback targets available",
          "No rollback candidates were found for the selected config layer.");
    } else {
      historyPanel.setQueueEmptyState(
          "No history found", "No release history entries were found for the selected layer.");
    }
  }

  private void selectTab(ControlTab target) {
    Tab selected = null;
    for (Map.Entry<Tab, ControlTab> entry : tabKeys.entrySet()) {
      if (entry.getValue() == target) {
        selected = entry.getKey();
        break;
      }
    }
    if (selected == null) {
      return;
    }
    suppressTabEvents = true;
    tabs.setSelectedTab(selected);
    suppressTabEvents = false;
  }

  private Component tabRoot(ControlTab tab) {
    return switch (tab) {
      case HISTORY, ROLLBACK -> historyRoot;
      case EMERGENCY -> emergencyRoot;
      case PENDING -> pendingRoot;
    };
  }

  private void refreshActiveTab(boolean preserveSelection) {
    if (activeTab == ControlTab.PENDING || activeTab == ControlTab.EMERGENCY) {
      refreshPending(preserveSelection);
      return;
    }
    refreshHistory(preserveSelection);
  }

  private void refreshPending(boolean preserveSelection) {
    String group = Strings.trimToNull(historySelection.group());
    String name = Strings.trimToNull(historySelection.name());
    if (group == null || name == null) {
      pendingItems = List.of();
      selectedPendingKey = null;
      pendingPanel.setQueueEmptyState(
          "Select Group and Name",
          "Choose both Group and Name to load pending workflow items.");
      pendingPanel.setItems(List.of());
      pendingPanel.clearSelection();
      emergencyPanel.setQueueEmptyState(
          "Select Group and Name",
          "Choose both Group and Name to load emergency candidates.");
      emergencyPanel.setItems(List.of());
      emergencyPanel.clearSelection();
      return;
    }
    try {
      List<StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalRecord> queue = approvalsProvider.listApprovalQueue(group);
      pendingItems =
          queue.stream()
              .filter(value -> Objects.equals(value == null ? null : value.configName(), name))
              .toList();
      pendingPanel.setQueueEmptyState(
          "No pending actions", "No config submissions are currently waiting for review.");
      pendingPanel.setItems(pendingItems);
      emergencyPanel.setQueueEmptyState(
          "No emergency candidates",
          "No pending workflow submissions are available for emergency publish.");
      emergencyPanel.setItems(pendingItems);
      selectedPendingKey = null;
      pendingPanel.clearSelection();
      pendingPanel.setDetailTitle("Pending Review Details");
      pendingPanel.setDetailContent(NO_PENDING_SELECTED);
      pendingPanel.setDetailActions();
    } catch (Exception error) {
      pendingItems = List.of();
      selectedPendingKey = null;
      pendingPanel.setItems(List.of());
      pendingPanel.clearSelection();
      emergencyPanel.setItems(List.of());
      emergencyPanel.clearSelection();
      pendingPanel.setDetailTitle("Pending Review Details");
      pendingPanel.setDetailContent(NO_PENDING_SELECTED);
      pendingPanel.setDetailActions();
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to load pending queue", rootMessage(error));
    }
  }

  private void onPendingSelected(StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalRecord selected) {
    if (selected == null) {
      selectedPendingKey = null;
      pendingPanel.setDetailTitle("Pending Review Details");
      pendingPanel.setDetailContent(NO_PENDING_SELECTED);
      pendingPanel.setDetailActions();
      return;
    }
    selectedPendingKey = selected.key();
    try {
      StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalDetails details = approvalsProvider.loadApprovalDetails(selected);
      pendingPanel.setDetailTitle(
          "Review - "
              + Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.configName(), "-")
              + " / "
              + Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.layerId(), "-"));
      pendingPanel.setDetailContent(buildPendingDetail(details));
      pendingPanel.setDetailActions(buildPendingActions(details).toArray(Component[]::new));
    } catch (Exception error) {
      pendingPanel.setDetailContent(
          new StitchEmptyState(
              "Unable to load pending details", Strings.firstNonBlank(rootMessage(error), "Unknown error")));
      pendingPanel.setDetailActions();
    }
  }

  private void openPendingDialog(StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalRecord selected) {
    if (selected == null) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalDetails details = approvalsProvider.loadApprovalDetails(selected);
      StitchDialog dialog =
          workflowDialog(
              "Pending Review - "
                  + Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.configName(), "-")
                  + " / "
                  + Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.layerId(), "-"));
      dialog.withJsonPayloadSupplier(() -> details.submission());
      dialog.addToBody(buildPendingDetail(details));
      attachDialogActions(dialog, buildPendingActions(details));
      dialog.open();
    } catch (Exception error) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to load pending details", rootMessage(error));
    }
  }

  private void openHistoryDialog(StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackRecord selected) {
    if (selected == null) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackDetails details = rollbacksProvider.loadDetails(selected);
      String titlePrefix = activeTab == ControlTab.ROLLBACK ? "Rollback Candidate - " : "History Entry - ";
      StitchDialog dialog =
          workflowDialog(
              titlePrefix
                  + Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.configName(), "-")
                  + " / "
                  + Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.layerId(), "-"));
      dialog.withJsonPayloadSupplier(() -> details.record().metadata());
      dialog.addToBody(buildHistoryDetail(details));
      attachDialogActions(dialog, buildHistoryActions(details));
      dialog.open();
    } catch (Exception error) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to load release details", rootMessage(error));
    }
  }

  private void openEmergencyDialog(StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalRecord selected) {
    if (selected == null) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalDetails details = approvalsProvider.loadApprovalDetails(selected);
      StitchDialog dialog =
          workflowDialog(
              "Emergency Publish - "
                  + Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.configName(), "-")
                  + " / "
                  + Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.layerId(), "-"));
      dialog.withJsonPayloadSupplier(() -> details.submission());

      Span warning =
          detailNote(
              "Emergency publish applies this pending payload immediately and bypasses scheduled rollout windows.");
      warning.getStyle().set("font-weight", "600");

      TextArea reason = new TextArea("Incident Reason");
      reason.setWidthFull();
      reason.setMaxLength(512);
      reason.setPlaceholder("Incident note (required)");
      reason.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Emergency publish reason");

      dialog.addToBody(warning, summaryStrip(pendingSummary(selected)), reason, buildPendingDetail(details));
      dialog.addPrimaryAction(
          "PUBLISH NOW",
          () -> {
            String reasonValue = Strings.trimToNull(reason.getValue());
            if (reasonValue == null) {
              Notification.show("Emergency reason is required.", 1600, Position.BOTTOM_START);
              return;
            }
            try {
              approvalsProvider.publishEmergency(selected, reasonValue);
              dialog.close();
              Notification.show("Emergency publish submitted", 1800, Position.BOTTOM_START);
              refreshPending(true);
              refreshHistory(true);
            } catch (Exception error) {
              StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to execute emergency publish", rootMessage(error));
            }
          });
      dialog.open();
    } catch (Exception error) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to load emergency target", rootMessage(error));
    }
  }
  private Component buildPendingDetail(StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalDetails details) {
    StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalRecord selected = details.submission();
    JsonNode currentDeclared =
        details.layer() == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : details.layer().declared();
    List<ConfigJsonDiff.DiffRow> changeRows = ConfigJsonDiff.diff(currentDeclared, selected.proposedPayload());
    VerticalLayout content = detailLayout();
    content.add(summaryStrip(pendingSummary(selected)));

    Span summarySentence =
        detailNote(
            pendingSummarySentence(
                selected,
                changeRows.size(),
                details.layer() == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(details.layer().shortName())));
    content.add(summarySentence);
    if (Strings.trimToNull(selected.rationale()) != null) {
      content.add(detailNote("Submission note: " + selected.rationale()));
    }
    content.add(
        changeSummarySection(
            "Proposed Changes",
            "Review each staged field-level change before approving or rejecting.",
            changeRows,
            80));

    Details payload =
        disclosure(
            "Raw proposed payload JSON",
            jsonViewer(
                "Proposed payload JSON",
                prettyJson(selected.proposedPayload()),
                "Pending proposed payload JSON"));
    Details technical = disclosure("Technical workflow metadata", metadataForm(selected.workflowMetadata()));
    content.add(payload, technical);
    return content;
  }

  private List<Component> buildPendingActions(StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalDetails details) {
    StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalRecord selected = details.submission();
    List<Component> actions = new ArrayList<>();

    Button approve = actionButton("APPROVE", "Approve selected pending submission");
    StitchActionStyles.applyPrimary(approve);
    approve.setEnabled(selected.canApprove());
    approve.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          try {
            approvalsProvider.approve(selected, "STITCH APPROVE");
            Notification.show("Approved pending submission", 1400, Position.BOTTOM_START);
            refreshPending(true);
            refreshHistory(true);
          } catch (Exception error) {
            StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to approve", rootMessage(error));
          }
        });
    actions.add(approve);

    Button reject = actionButton("REJECT", "Reject selected pending submission");
    StitchActionStyles.applyDanger(reject);
    reject.setEnabled(selected.canReject());
    reject.addClickListener(event -> openRejectDialog(selected));
    actions.add(reject);

    Button compareLive = actionButton("COMPARE LIVE", "Compare pending payload to live");
    StitchActionStyles.applySecondary(compareLive);
    compareLive.addClickListener(
        event ->
            StitchConfigCompareDialog.compareToLive(
                    selected.compareContext(),
                    "Pending",
                    selected.proposedPayload(),
                    details.livePayload().label(),
                    details.livePayload().payload())
                .open());
    actions.add(compareLive);

    Button compareLayer = actionButton("COMPARE LAYER", "Compare pending payload to another layer");
    StitchActionStyles.applySecondary(compareLayer);
    compareLayer.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          List<StitchConfigCompareDialog.CompareTarget> candidates = approvalsProvider.compareTargets(selected);
          if (candidates.isEmpty()) {
            Notification.show("No other layers available for comparison.", 1400, Position.BOTTOM_START);
            return;
          }
          StitchConfigCompareDialog.compareToLayer(
                  selected.compareContext(), "Pending", selected.proposedPayload(), candidates)
              .open();
        });
    actions.add(compareLayer);

    return List.copyOf(actions);
  }

  private void openRejectDialog(StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalRecord selected) {
    if (selected == null) {
      return;
    }
    StitchDialog dialog = new StitchDialog("Reject Submission");
    dialog.setWidth("620px");
    dialog.setMaxWidth("95vw");
    dialog.setTop("12vh");
    TextArea reason = new TextArea("Reason");
    reason.setWidthFull();
    reason.setMaxLength(512);
    reason.setPlaceholder("Provide rejection reason");
    reason.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Rejection reason");
    dialog.addToBody(
        new Span(
            "Reject "
                + Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.configName(), "-")
                + " / "
                + Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.layerId(), "-")),
        reason);
    dialog.addPrimaryAction(
        "REJECT",
        () -> {
          String reasonText = Strings.trimToNull(reason.getValue());
          if (reasonText == null) {
            Notification.show("Rejection reason is required.", 1600, Position.BOTTOM_START);
            return;
          }
          try {
            approvalsProvider.reject(selected, reasonText);
            dialog.close();
            Notification.show("Rejected pending submission", 1400, Position.BOTTOM_START);
            refreshPending(true);
            refreshHistory(true);
          } catch (Exception error) {
            StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to reject", rootMessage(error));
          }
        });
    dialog.addSecondaryAction("Cancel", dialog::close);
    dialog.open();
  }

  private void onHistorySelectionChanged(StitchConfigSelectionBar.SelectionChange selection) {
    historySelection = new StitchConfigSelectionBar.Selection(selection.group(), selection.name());
    StitchConfigSelectionContext.remember(historySelection.group(), historySelection.name());
    refreshPending(selection.preserveTreeSelection());
    refreshHistory(selection.preserveTreeSelection());
  }

  private void loadHistoryLayerOptions(boolean preserveSelection) {
    List<StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.LayerOption> options =
        rollbacksProvider.listLayerOptions(historySelection.group(), historySelection.name());
    StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.LayerOption current = historyLayerSelector.getValue();
    StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.LayerOption next =
        preserveSelection
            ? options.stream()
                .filter(
                    value ->
                        current != null
                            && Objects.equals(value.layer().layerId(), current.layer().layerId()))
                .findFirst()
                .orElse(null)
            : null;
    if (next == null && !options.isEmpty()) {
      next = options.get(0);
    }
    suppressLayerEvents = true;
    historyLayerSelector.setItems(options);
    if (next != null) {
      historyLayerSelector.setValue(next);
    } else {
      historyLayerSelector.clear();
    }
    historyLayerSelector.setEnabled(!options.isEmpty());
    suppressLayerEvents = false;
  }

  private void clearHistoryLayerOptions() {
    suppressLayerEvents = true;
    historyLayerSelector.clear();
    historyLayerSelector.setItems(List.of());
    historyLayerSelector.setEnabled(false);
    suppressLayerEvents = false;
  }
  private void refreshHistory(boolean preserveSelection) {
    if (historySelection.group() == null || historySelection.name() == null) {
      clearHistory(NO_CONFIG_SELECTED);
      return;
    }
    try {
      List<StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.LayerOption> layers =
          rollbacksProvider.listLayerOptions(historySelection.group(), historySelection.name());
      List<StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackRecord> rows = new ArrayList<>();
      for (StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.LayerOption option : layers) {
        if (option == null || option.layer() == null) {
          continue;
        }
        rows.addAll(
            rollbacksProvider.listRollbackHistory(
                historySelection.group(),
                historySelection.name(),
                option.layer().layerId(),
                50));
      }
      rows =
          rows.stream()
              .filter(Objects::nonNull)
              .sorted(
                  Comparator.comparing(
                          StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackRecord::updatedTimeUtc,
                          Comparator.nullsLast(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
                      .reversed()
                      .thenComparing(
                          value -> Strings.firstNonBlank(value.layerId(), ""),
                          String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
                      .thenComparing(
                          value -> Strings.firstNonBlank(value.targetConfigId(), ""),
                          String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
              .toList();
      historyPanel.setItems(rows);
      selectedHistoryKey = null;
      historyPanel.clearSelection();
      historyPanel.setDetailTitle(activeTab == ControlTab.ROLLBACK ? "Rollback Candidate" : "Release Details");
      historyPanel.setDetailContent(NO_HISTORY_SELECTED);
      historyPanel.setDetailActions();
    } catch (Exception error) {
      clearHistory(
          new StitchEmptyState(
              "Unable to load release history", Strings.firstNonBlank(rootMessage(error), "Unknown error")));
    }
  }

  private void clearHistory(Component detailContent) {
    selectedHistoryKey = null;
    historyPanel.setItems(List.of());
    historyPanel.clearSelection();
    historyPanel.setDetailTitle(activeTab == ControlTab.ROLLBACK ? "Rollback Candidate" : "Release Details");
    historyPanel.setDetailContent(detailContent == null ? NO_HISTORY_SELECTED : detailContent);
    historyPanel.setDetailActions();
  }

  private void onHistorySelected(StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackRecord selected) {
    if (selected == null) {
      selectedHistoryKey = null;
      historyPanel.setDetailTitle(activeTab == ControlTab.ROLLBACK ? "Rollback Candidate" : "Release Details");
      historyPanel.setDetailContent(NO_HISTORY_SELECTED);
      historyPanel.setDetailActions();
      return;
    }
    selectedHistoryKey = selected.key();
    try {
      StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackDetails details = rollbacksProvider.loadDetails(selected);
      historyPanel.setDetailTitle(
          (activeTab == ControlTab.ROLLBACK ? "Rollback - " : "Release - ")
              + Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.targetConfigId(), selected.releaseLabel(), "-"));
      historyPanel.setDetailContent(buildHistoryDetail(details));
      historyPanel.setDetailActions(buildHistoryActions(details).toArray(Component[]::new));
    } catch (Exception error) {
      historyPanel.setDetailContent(
          new StitchEmptyState(
              "Unable to load release details", Strings.firstNonBlank(rootMessage(error), "Unknown error")));
      historyPanel.setDetailActions();
    }
  }

  private Component buildHistoryDetail(StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackDetails details) {
    return activeTab == ControlTab.ROLLBACK ? buildRollbackDetail(details) : buildReleaseDetail(details);
  }

  private Component buildReleaseDetail(StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackDetails details) {
    StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackRecord record = details.record();
    List<ConfigJsonDiff.DiffRow> diffRows =
        ConfigJsonDiff.diff(details.currentPayload(), details.snapshotPayload());
    VerticalLayout content = detailLayout();
    content.add(summaryStrip(historySummary(record)));
    content.add(
        detailNote(
            "Release "
                + Strings.firstNonBlank(record.targetConfigId(), "-")
                + " was applied by "
                + record.updatedByLabel()
                + " on "
                + record.updatedLabel()
                + "."));
    content.add(
        detailNote(
            "Compared with current declared values, this release has "
                + diffRows.size()
                + " changed field"
                + (diffRows.size() == 1 ? "" : "s")
                + "."));
    content.add(
        changeSummarySection(
            "Release Delta",
            "Field-level difference between current declared payload and this release snapshot.",
            diffRows,
            60));

    Details comparison =
        disclosure(
            "Raw snapshot vs current payload",
            jsonSideBySide(
                "Current Declared",
                prettyJson(details.currentPayload()),
                "Release Snapshot",
                prettyJson(details.snapshotPayload())));
    Details technical = disclosure("Technical release metadata", metadataForm(record.metadata()));
    content.add(comparison, technical);
    return content;
  }

  private Component buildRollbackDetail(StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackDetails details) {
    StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackRecord record = details.record();
    List<ConfigJsonDiff.DiffRow> diffRows =
        ConfigJsonDiff.diff(details.currentPayload(), details.snapshotPayload());
    VerticalLayout content = detailLayout();
    content.add(summaryStrip(simplifiedRollbackMetadata(record)));
    content.add(
        detailNote(
            "This rollback restores "
                + Strings.firstNonBlank(record.configName(), "-")
                + " / "
                + Strings.firstNonBlank(record.layerId(), "-")
                + " to the release from "
                + record.updatedLabel()
                + " by "
                + record.updatedByLabel()
                + "."));
    content.add(
        detailNote(
            "Impact summary: "
                + diffRows.size()
                + " field"
                + (diffRows.size() == 1 ? "" : "s")
                + " will revert. Key paths: "
                + summarizePaths(diffRows, 8)));
    content.add(
        changeSummarySection(
            "Rollback Change Preview",
            "Review the exact fields that will change if rollback executes now.",
            diffRows,
            70));

    Details preview =
        disclosure(
            "Raw rollback payload preview",
            jsonSideBySide(
                "Current Declared",
                prettyJson(details.currentPayload()),
                "Rollback Target",
                prettyJson(details.snapshotPayload())));
    Details technical = disclosure("Technical rollback details", metadataForm(record.metadata()));
    content.add(preview, technical);
    return content;
  }

  private List<Component> buildHistoryActions(StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackDetails details) {
    StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackRecord selected = details.record();
    List<Component> actions = new ArrayList<>();

    if (activeTab == ControlTab.ROLLBACK) {
      Button rollback = actionButton("ROLLBACK", "Rollback selected release now");
      StitchActionStyles.applyDanger(rollback);
      rollback.setEnabled(selected.canRollback());
      rollback.addClickListener(event -> openRollbackDialog(details));
      actions.add(rollback);
    }

    Button compareCurrent =
        actionButton("COMPARE CURRENT", "Compare selected release snapshot to current declared payload");
    StitchActionStyles.applySecondary(compareCurrent);
    compareCurrent.addClickListener(
        event ->
            new StitchJsonDiffDialog(
                    "Compare To Current - " + selected.compareContext(),
                    "Current Declared",
                    details.currentPayload(),
                    "Release " + selected.releaseLabel(),
                    details.snapshotPayload())
                .open());
    actions.add(compareCurrent);

    Button compareLive = actionButton("COMPARE LIVE", "Compare selected release to live payload");
    StitchActionStyles.applySecondary(compareLive);
    compareLive.addClickListener(
        event ->
            StitchConfigCompareDialog.compareToLive(
                    selected.compareContext(),
                    "Release " + selected.releaseLabel(),
                    details.snapshotPayload(),
                    details.livePayload().label(),
                    details.livePayload().payload())
                .open());
    actions.add(compareLive);

    return List.copyOf(actions);
  }

  private void attachDialogActions(StitchDialog dialog, List<Component> actions) {
    if (dialog == null || actions == null || actions.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    HorizontalLayout footer = dialog.footer();
    int closeIndex = Math.max(0, footer.getComponentCount() - 1);
    for (Component action : actions) {
      if (action != null) {
        footer.addComponentAtIndex(closeIndex, action);
        closeIndex++;
      }
    }
  }

  private StitchDialog workflowDialog(String title) {
    StitchDialog dialog = new StitchDialog(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(title), "Workflow Detail"));
    dialog.setWidth("1120px");
    dialog.setMaxWidth("96vw");
    dialog.setTop("6vh");
    dialog.body().getStyle().set("max-height", "74vh");
    dialog.body().getStyle().set("overflow", "auto");
    return dialog;
  }

  private StitchStatusBadge statusBadge(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(value), "UNKNOWN").toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    StitchStatusBadge.Tone tone =
        switch (normalized) {
          case "APPROVED", "ACTIVE" -> StitchStatusBadge.Tone.SUCCESS;
          case "REJECTED", "EMERGENCY", "FAILED" -> StitchStatusBadge.Tone.ERROR;
          case "ROLLBACK", "ROLLED_BACK" -> StitchStatusBadge.Tone.WARNING;
          case "PROPOSED", "SCHEDULED", "DRAFT", "IMMEDIATE" -> StitchStatusBadge.Tone.INFO;
          default -> StitchStatusBadge.Tone.NEUTRAL;
        };
    return new StitchStatusBadge(normalized, tone);
  }

  private Map<String, String> pendingSummary(StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalRecord record) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    values.put("Group", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.group(), "-"));
    values.put("Config", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.configName(), "-"));
    values.put("Layer", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.layerId(), "-"));
    values.put("Status", record.stateLabel());
    values.put("Mode", record.modeLabel());
    values.put("Effective", record.effectiveLabel());
    values.put("Expires", record.expiresLabel());
    values.put("Submitted By", record.proposedByLabel());
    values.put("Last Updated", record.updatedLabel());
    return values;
  }

  private Map<String, String> historySummary(StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackRecord record) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    values.put("Group", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.group(), "-"));
    values.put("Config", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.configName(), "-"));
    values.put("Layer", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.layerId(), "-"));
    values.put("Release Id", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.targetConfigId(), "-"));
    values.put("Action", "Release snapshot");
    values.put("Mode", record.modeLabel());
    values.put("Effective", record.effectiveLabel());
    values.put("Updated By", record.updatedByLabel());
    values.put("Updated At", record.updatedLabel());
    values.put("Outcome", "Applied");
    return values;
  }
  private Map<String, String> simplifiedRollbackMetadata(
      StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackRecord record) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    values.put("Group", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.group(), "-"));
    values.put("Config", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.configName(), "-"));
    values.put("Layer", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.layerId(), "-"));
    values.put("Rollback To", Strings.firstNonBlank(record.targetConfigId(), "-"));
    values.put("Version Timestamp", record.updatedLabel());
    values.put("Version Owner", record.updatedByLabel());
    values.put("Effective", record.effectiveLabel());
    values.put("Fields To Revert", String.valueOf(record.keysCount()));
    return values;
  }

  private void openRollbackDialog(StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackDetails details) {
    StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackRecord selected = details.record();
    if (selected == null || !selected.canRollback()) {
      return;
    }
    List<ConfigJsonDiff.DiffRow> diffRows =
        ConfigJsonDiff.diff(details.currentPayload(), details.snapshotPayload());
    StitchDialog dialog = new StitchDialog("Confirm Rollback");
    dialog.setWidth("760px");
    dialog.setMaxWidth("96vw");
    dialog.setTop("10vh");

    Span question =
        new Span(
            "Roll back "
                + Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.configName(), "-")
                + " / "
                + Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.layerId(), "-")
                + " to the version from "
                + selected.updatedLabel()
                + "?");
    Span summary =
        new Span(
            "Target: "
                + Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.targetConfigId(), "-")
                + " | Changed fields: "
                + diffRows.size());

    Component changePreview =
        changeSummarySection(
            "Rollback Diff Preview",
            "These field-level values will change if you continue.",
            diffRows,
            50);

    Details preview =
        disclosure(
            "Changed paths summary",
            detailNote(
                summarizePaths(diffRows, 10)));
    Details technical = disclosure("Technical rollback details", metadataForm(selected.metadata()));

    TextArea reason = new TextArea("Reason");
    reason.setWidthFull();
    reason.setMaxLength(512);
    reason.setPlaceholder("Optional rollback reason");
    reason.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Rollback reason");

    dialog.addToBody(question, summary, changePreview, preview, technical, reason);
    dialog.addPrimaryAction(
        "ROLLBACK",
        () -> {
          try {
            rollbacksProvider.rollback(selected, Strings.trimToNull(reason.getValue()));
            dialog.close();
            Notification.show(
                "Rolled back to " + Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.targetConfigId(), "-"),
                1800,
                Position.BOTTOM_START);
            refreshHistory(true);
          } catch (Exception error) {
            StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to rollback release", rootMessage(error));
          }
        });
    dialog.addSecondaryAction("Cancel", dialog::close);
    dialog.open();
  }

  private String rollbackOptionLabel(StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackRecord record) {
    if (record == null) {
      return "-";
    }
    return "Return to version from "
        + record.updatedLabel()
        + " by "
        + record.updatedByLabel()
        + " ("
        + record.keysCount()
        + " field"
        + (record.keysCount() == 1 ? "" : "s")
        + ")";
  }

  private void syncEmergencyTargets() {
    StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalRecord current = emergencyTarget.getValue();
    String currentKey = current == null ? null : current.key();
    emergencyTarget.setItems(pendingItems);
    StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalRecord next =
        currentKey == null
            ? null
            : pendingItems.stream()
                .filter(value -> Objects.equals(value.key(), currentKey))
                .findFirst()
                .orElse(null);
    if (next != null) {
      emergencyTarget.setValue(next);
    } else {
      emergencyTarget.clear();
    }
    updateEmergencyActionState();
  }

  private void updateEmergencyActionState() {
    StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalRecord selected = emergencyTarget.getValue();
    boolean enabled = selected != null && selected.canPublishEmergency();
    emergencyPublishButton.setEnabled(enabled);
    refreshEmergencySummary(selected);
  }

  private void refreshEmergencySummary(StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalRecord selected) {
    if (selected == null) {
      emergencySummary.setItems(Map.of("Target", "No pending target selected."));
      setEmergencyTechnicalContent(
          detailNote("Select a pending target to inspect technical workflow details."));
      return;
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    values.put("Group", Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.group(), "-"));
    values.put("Config", Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.configName(), "-"));
    values.put("Layer", Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.layerId(), "-"));
    values.put("Status", selected.stateLabel());
    values.put("Effective", selected.effectiveLabel());
    values.put("Submitted By", selected.proposedByLabel());
    emergencySummary.setItems(values);
    setEmergencyTechnicalContent(metadataForm(selected.workflowMetadata()));
  }

  private void setEmergencyTechnicalContent(Component content) {
    emergencyTechnicalDetails.removeAll();
    emergencyTechnicalDetails.add(content == null ? detailNote("-") : content);
  }

  private void openEmergencyConfirm() {
    StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalRecord selected = emergencyTarget.getValue();
    if (selected == null || !selected.canPublishEmergency()) {
      Notification.show("Select a pending target first.", 1400, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      return;
    }
    String reasonValue = Strings.trimToNull(emergencyReason.getValue());
    if (reasonValue == null) {
      Notification.show("Emergency reason is required.", 1600, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      return;
    }
    StitchDialog dialog = new StitchDialog("Emergency Publish Confirmation");
    dialog.setWidth("760px");
    dialog.setMaxWidth("96vw");
    dialog.setTop("10vh");
    Span warning =
        new Span(
            "This action immediately publishes the selected pending config change and bypasses standard rollout timing.");
    warning.getStyle().set("font-weight", "600");
    Span target =
        new Span(
            "Target: "
                + Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.configName(), "-")
                + " / "
                + Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.layerId(), "-")
                + " ["
                + selected.stateLabel()
                + "]");
    Span note =
        new Span(
            "Reason: "
                + reasonValue);
    dialog.addToBody(warning, target, note);
    dialog.addPrimaryAction(
        "PUBLISH NOW",
        () -> {
          try {
            approvalsProvider.publishEmergency(selected, reasonValue);
            dialog.close();
            Notification.show("Emergency publish submitted", 1800, Position.BOTTOM_START);
            refreshPending(true);
          } catch (Exception error) {
            StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to execute emergency publish", rootMessage(error));
          }
        });
    dialog.addSecondaryAction("Cancel", dialog::close);
    dialog.open();
  }

  private void rerenderSelectedHistory() {
    StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.RollbackRecord selected = historyPanel.selectedItem();
    if (selected != null) {
      onHistorySelected(selected);
    }
  }

  private VerticalLayout detailLayout() {
    VerticalLayout layout = new VerticalLayout();
    layout.setPadding(false);
    layout.setSpacing(true);
    layout.setWidthFull();
    layout.getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    layout.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-detail");
    return layout;
  }

  private StitchSummaryStrip summaryStrip(Map<String, String> values) {
    StitchSummaryStrip strip = new StitchSummaryStrip();
    strip.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-summary");
    strip.setItems(values);
    return strip;
  }

  private Span detailNote(String value) {
    Span note = new Span(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(value), "-"));
    note.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-note");
    return note;
  }

  private Component changeSummarySection(
      String title, String subtitle, List<ConfigJsonDiff.DiffRow> rows, int maxRows) {
    VerticalLayout section = new VerticalLayout();
    section.setPadding(false);
    section.setSpacing(true);
    section.setWidthFull();
    section.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-change-section");

    Span heading = new Span(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(title), "Change Summary"));
    heading.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-change-title");
    section.add(heading);

    String subtitleText = Strings.trimToNull(subtitle);
    if (subtitleText != null) {
      Span subtitleLine = new Span(subtitleText);
      subtitleLine.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-note");
      section.add(subtitleLine);
    }

    List<ConfigJsonDiff.DiffRow> safeRows =
        rows == null ? List.of() : rows.stream().filter(Objects::nonNull).toList();
    int total = safeRows.size();
    int boundedMax = Math.max(1, maxRows);
    List<ChangeSummaryRow> limitedRows =
        safeRows.stream().limit(boundedMax).map(this::toChangeSummaryRow).toList();
    section.add(detailNote(changeCountLabel(total)));
    if (limitedRows.isEmpty()) {
      return section;
    }

    Grid<ChangeSummaryRow> grid = new Grid<>(ChangeSummaryRow.class, false);
    grid.addThemeVariants(GridVariant.LUMO_COMPACT, GridVariant.LUMO_ROW_STRIPES);
    grid.addClassName("stitch-results-grid");
    grid.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-change-grid");
    grid.setWidthFull();
    if (limitedRows.size() <= 8) {
      grid.setAllRowsVisible(true);
    } else {
      grid.setHeight("16rem");
    }
    grid.addColumn(ChangeSummaryRow::path).setHeader("Path").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(1);
    grid.addComponentColumn(row -> changeBadge(row.changeType()))
        .setHeader("Change")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setFlexGrow(0);
    grid.addComponentColumn(row -> diffValueCell(row.currentValue()))
        .setHeader("Current")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setFlexGrow(1);
    grid.addComponentColumn(row -> diffValueCell(row.newValue()))
        .setHeader("New")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setFlexGrow(1);
    grid.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Config change summary");
    grid.setItems(limitedRows);
    section.add(grid);

    if (total > boundedMax) {
      section.add(
          detailNote(
              "Showing first "
                  + boundedMax
                  + " changed rows out of "
                  + total
                  + ". Use compare actions for full detail."));
    }
    return section;
  }

  private ChangeSummaryRow toChangeSummaryRow(ConfigJsonDiff.DiffRow row) {
    return new ChangeSummaryRow(
        Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(row.path()), "<root>"),
        Strings.firstNonBlank(row.change() == null ? null : row.change().name(), "MODIFIED"),
        renderDiffValue(row.oldValue()),
        renderDiffValue(row.newValue()));
  }

  private Component diffValueCell(String value) {
    String text = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(value), "-");
    Span cell = new Span(text);
    cell.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-diff-value");
    cell.getElement().setProperty("title", text);
    return cell;
  }

  private Component changeBadge(String changeType) {
    String normalized = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(changeType), "MODIFIED");
    Span badge = new Span(normalized);
    badge.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-change-pill");
    badge.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-change-pill--" + normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
    return badge;
  }

  private static String renderDiffValue(JsonNode value) {
    if (value == null || value.isMissingNode()) {
      return "-";
    }
    return truncate(ConfigJsonDiff.formatJsonScalar(value), 220);
  }

  private static String truncate(String value, int maxLength) {
    String normalized = Strings.firstNonBlank(value, "-");
    int boundedMax = Math.max(8, maxLength);
    if (normalized.length() <= boundedMax) {
      return normalized;
    }
    return normalized.substring(0, boundedMax - 3) + "...";
  }

  private static String changeCountLabel(int changedRows) {
    if (changedRows <= 0) {
      return "No field-level changes detected.";
    }
    return changedRows + " field-level change" + (changedRows == 1 ? "" : "s") + ".";
  }

  private static String pendingSummarySentence(
      StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.ApprovalRecord selected, int changedRows, String layerLabel) {
    String actor = Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.proposedByLabel(), "A submitter");
    String targetLayer = Strings.firstNonBlank(layerLabel, selected.layerId(), "layer");
    String timing =
        "-".equals(selected.effectiveLabel())
            ? "effective immediately"
            : "scheduled for " + selected.effectiveLabel();
    return actor
        + " submitted "
        + changedRows
        + " field-level change"
        + (changedRows == 1 ? "" : "s")
        + " for "
        + Strings.firstNonBlank(selected.configName(), "-")
        + " / "
        + targetLayer
        + "; current state is "
        + selected.stateLabel()
        + " and the change is "
        + timing
        + ".";
  }

  private Details disclosure(String label, Component content) {
    Details details = new Details(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(label), "Details"), content);
    details.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-disclosure");
    details.setOpened(false);
    return details;
  }

  private Component metadataForm(Map<String, String> values) {
    Map<String, String> safe = values == null ? Map.of() : values;
    List<String> ordered = safe.keySet().stream().toList();
    FormLayout form = StitchDetailsDialogSupport.buildForm(ordered, safe, Map.of());
    form.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-metadata");
    return form;
  }

  private Component jsonSideBySide(
      String leftLabel, String leftJson, String rightLabel, String rightJson) {
    Component left = jsonViewer(leftLabel, leftJson, leftLabel + " JSON");
    Component right = jsonViewer(rightLabel, rightJson, rightLabel + " JSON");
    HorizontalLayout split = new HorizontalLayout(left, right);
    split.setPadding(false);
    split.setSpacing(true);
    split.setWidthFull();
    split.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-json-split");
    split.setFlexGrow(1, left);
    split.setFlexGrow(1, right);
    return split;
  }

  private TextArea jsonViewer(String label, String json, String ariaLabel) {
    TextArea text = new TextArea(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(label), "JSON"));
    text.setWidthFull();
    text.setReadOnly(true);
    text.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(json));
    text.setMinHeight("18rem");
    text.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-json");
    text.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(ariaLabel), "JSON"));
    return text;
  }

  private static String prettyJson(JsonNode value) {
    JsonNode normalized = value == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : value;
    try {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().writerWithDefaultPrettyPrinter().writeValueAsString(normalized);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      return normalized.toString();
    }
  }

  private static Button actionButton(String label, String ariaLabel) {
    Button button = new Button(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(label), "ACTION"));
    button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    button.addClassName("stitch-configs-control-action");
    StitchActionStyles.applyByLabel(button, button.getText());
    button
        .getElement()
        .setAttribute(
            "aria-label", Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(ariaLabel), button.getText()));
    return button;
  }

  private static String summarizePaths(List<ConfigJsonDiff.DiffRow> rows, int max) {
    if (rows == null || rows.isEmpty()) {
      return "<none>";
    }
    List<String> paths =
        rows.stream()
            .filter(Objects::nonNull)
            .map(ConfigJsonDiff.DiffRow::path)
            .map(Strings::trimToNull)
            .filter(Objects::nonNull)
            .distinct()
            .toList();
    if (paths.isEmpty()) {
      return "<none>";
    }
    int take = Math.min(Math.max(1, max), paths.size());
    String head = String.join(", ", paths.subList(0, take));
    int extra = paths.size() - take;
    return extra > 0 ? head + " (+" + extra + " more)" : head;
  }

  protected static String rootMessage(Throwable error) {
    return StitchTextSupport.rootMessage(error);
  }

  private record ChangeSummaryRow(String path, String changeType, String currentValue, String newValue) {}
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/configs/StitchConfigsControlView.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.configs;

import com.vaadin.flow.router.NotFoundException;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout.StitchShellLayout;

@Route(value = "configs/control", layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchConfigsControlView extends StitchConfigsControlScreen {
  public StitchConfigsControlView(
      Stitch stitch,
      StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider approvalsProvider,
      StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider rollbacksProvider) {
    super(requireConfig(stitch), approvalsProvider, rollbacksProvider, ControlTab.PENDING);
  }

  private static StitchConfigsScreenConfig requireConfig(Stitch stitch) {
    return stitch
        .features()
        .configs()
        .map(StitchConfigsFeature::control)
        .filter(StitchConfigsScreenConfig::enabled)
        .orElseThrow(NotFoundException::new);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/configs/StitchConfigSelectionBar.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.configs;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.ComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.Alignment;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Function;
import java.util.function.Supplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchGroupSelectionContext;

/** Shared Group -> Name selector bar for Configs screens. */
public final class StitchConfigSelectionBar extends HorizontalLayout {
  private final ComboBox<String> groupSelector = new ComboBox<>("Group");
  private final ComboBox<String> nameSelector = new ComboBox<>("Name");
  private final Supplier<List<String>> groupsLoader;
  private final Function<String, List<String>> namesLoader;

  private SelectionRequestHandler requestHandler = (current, requested, apply, revert) -> apply.run();
  private SelectionChangeListener selectionListener = selection -> {};

  private String selectedGroup;
  private String selectedName;
  private boolean suppressGroupEvents;
  private boolean suppressNameEvents;
  private boolean flatTopBarMode;

  public StitchConfigSelectionBar(
      Supplier<List<String>> groupsLoader, Function<String, List<String>> namesLoader) {
    this.groupsLoader = Objects.requireNonNull(groupsLoader, "groupsLoader");
    this.namesLoader = Objects.requireNonNull(namesLoader, "namesLoader");

    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(true);
    setWidthFull();
    setWrap(true);
    setAlignItems(Alignment.END);
    addClassName("stitch-config-selection-bar");

    configureSelectors();
    add(groupSelector, nameSelector);
  }

  public StitchConfigSelectionBar setSelectionRequestHandler(SelectionRequestHandler handler) {
    this.requestHandler =
        handler == null ? (current, requested, apply, revert) -> apply.run() : handler;
    return this;
  }

  public StitchConfigSelectionBar setSelectionChangeListener(SelectionChangeListener listener) {
    this.selectionListener = listener == null ? selection -> {} : listener;
    return this;
  }

  public String selectedGroup() {
    return selectedGroup;
  }

  public String selectedName() {
    return selectedName;
  }

  public StitchConfigSelectionBar setFlatTopBarMode(boolean flatMode) {
    this.flatTopBarMode = flatMode;
    if (flatMode) {
      addClassName("stitch-config-selection-bar--flat");
      groupSelector.setLabel("");
      nameSelector.setLabel("");
      groupSelector.setPlaceholder("All");
      nameSelector.setPlaceholder("All configs");
      setAlignItems(Alignment.CENTER);
    } else {
      removeClassName("stitch-config-selection-bar--flat");
      groupSelector.setLabel("Group");
      nameSelector.setLabel("Name");
      groupSelector.setPlaceholder("Select group");
      nameSelector.setPlaceholder("Select config name");
      setAlignItems(Alignment.END);
    }
    return this;
  }

  public SelectionChange reload(boolean preserveSelection) {
    String preferredGroup = preserveSelection ? selectedGroup : StitchGroupSelectionContext.current();
    String preferredName = preserveSelection ? selectedName : null;
    return reloadWithSelection(preferredGroup, preferredName, preserveSelection);
  }

  public SelectionChange reloadWithSelection(
      String preferredGroup, String preferredName, boolean preserveTreeSelection) {
    List<String> groups = normalize(groupsLoader.get());
    groupSelector.setItems(groups);
    if (groups.isEmpty()) {
      selectedGroup = null;
      setGroupValue(null);
      loadNameOptions(false);
      return notifySelectionChanged(preserveTreeSelection);
    }

    String nextGroup = resolveMatchingOption(groups, preferredGroup);
    if (nextGroup == null && preferredGroup == null) {
      nextGroup = groups.get(0);
    }
    if (nextGroup == null) {
      nextGroup = groups.get(0);
    }
    selectedGroup = nextGroup;
    setGroupValue(nextGroup);
    loadNameOptionsForSelection(preferredName);
    return notifySelectionChanged(preserveTreeSelection);
  }

  private void configureSelectors() {
    groupSelector.setLabel("Group");
    groupSelector.setWidthFull();
    groupSelector.setPlaceholder("Select group");
    groupSelector.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    groupSelector.setClearButtonVisible(false);
    groupSelector.addClassName("stitch-config-selection-group");
    groupSelector.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Config group selector");
    groupSelector.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!suppressGroupEvents) {
            requestGroupChange(event.getValue());
          }
        });

    nameSelector.setLabel("Name");
    nameSelector.setWidthFull();
    nameSelector.setPlaceholder("Select config name");
    nameSelector.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    nameSelector.setClearButtonVisible(false);
    nameSelector.addClassName("stitch-config-selection-name");
    nameSelector.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Config name selector");
    nameSelector.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!suppressNameEvents) {
            requestNameChange(event.getValue());
          }
        });
    setFlexGrow(1, groupSelector);
    setFlexGrow(1, nameSelector);
  }

  private void loadNameOptions(boolean preserveSelection) {
    if (selectedGroup == null) {
      nameSelector.setItems(List.of());
      selectedName = null;
      setNameValue(null);
      return;
    }
    List<String> names = normalize(namesLoader.apply(selectedGroup));
    nameSelector.setItems(names);
    String nextName = preserveSelection ? resolveMatchingOption(names, selectedName) : null;
    if (nextName == null
        && preserveSelection
        && Strings.trimToNull(selectedName) != null
        && !names.isEmpty()) {
      nextName = names.get(0);
    }
    selectedName = nextName;
    setNameValue(nextName);
  }

  private void loadNameOptionsForSelection(String preferredName) {
    if (selectedGroup == null) {
      nameSelector.setItems(List.of());
      selectedName = null;
      setNameValue(null);
      return;
    }
    List<String> names = normalize(namesLoader.apply(selectedGroup));
    nameSelector.setItems(names);
    selectedName = resolveMatchingOption(names, preferredName);
    setNameValue(selectedName);
  }

  private void requestGroupChange(String requestedGroup) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(requestedGroup);
    if (Objects.equals(selectedGroup, normalized)) {
      return;
    }
    Selection current = new Selection(selectedGroup, selectedName);
    Selection requested = new Selection(normalized, null);
    requestHandler.onSelectionRequested(
        current,
        requested,
        () -> {
          selectedGroup = normalized;
          setGroupValue(normalized);
          selectedName = null;
          setNameValue(null);
          loadNameOptions(false);
          notifySelectionChanged(false);
        },
        () -> setGroupValue(selectedGroup));
  }

  private void requestNameChange(String requestedName) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(requestedName);
    if (Objects.equals(selectedName, normalized)) {
      return;
    }
    Selection current = new Selection(selectedGroup, selectedName);
    Selection requested = new Selection(selectedGroup, normalized);
    requestHandler.onSelectionRequested(
        current,
        requested,
        () -> {
          selectedName = normalized;
          setNameValue(normalized);
          notifySelectionChanged(false);
        },
        () -> setNameValue(selectedName));
  }

  private SelectionChange notifySelectionChanged(boolean preserveTreeSelection) {
    SelectionChange change = new SelectionChange(selectedGroup, selectedName, preserveTreeSelection);
    selectionListener.onSelectionChanged(change);
    return change;
  }

  private void setGroupValue(String value) {
    suppressGroupEvents = true;
    if (value == null) {
      groupSelector.clear();
    } else {
      groupSelector.setValue(value);
    }
    suppressGroupEvents = false;
  }

  private void setNameValue(String value) {
    suppressNameEvents = true;
    if (value == null) {
      nameSelector.clear();
    } else {
      nameSelector.setValue(value);
    }
    suppressNameEvents = false;
  }

  private static List<String> normalize(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return values.stream().map(Strings::trimToNull).filter(Objects::nonNull).distinct().toList();
  }

  private static String resolveMatchingOption(List<String> options, String currentValue) {
    if (options == null || options.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalizedCurrent = Strings.trimToNull(currentValue);
    if (normalizedCurrent == null) {
      return null;
    }
    for (String option : options) {
      if (Objects.equals(option, normalizedCurrent)) {
        return option;
      }
    }
    for (String option : options) {
      if (option != null && option.equalsIgnoreCase(normalizedCurrent)) {
        return option;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  public record Selection(String group, String name) {}

  public record SelectionChange(String group, String name, boolean preserveTreeSelection) {}

  @FunctionalInterface
  public interface SelectionRequestHandler {
    void onSelectionRequested(Selection current, Selection requested, Runnable apply, Runnable revert);
  }

  @FunctionalInterface
  public interface SelectionChangeListener {
    void onSelectionChanged(SelectionChange selection);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/configs/StitchConfigSelectionContext.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.configs;

import com.vaadin.flow.server.VaadinSession;
import java.io.Serializable;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchGroupSelectionContext;

/** Lightweight per-session cache for last selected Configs group/name context. */
final class StitchConfigSelectionContext {
  private static final String ATTRIBUTE_KEY = StitchConfigSelectionContext.class.getName() + ".selection";

  private StitchConfigSelectionContext() {}

  static void remember(String group, String name) {
    VaadinSession session = VaadinSession.getCurrent();
    if (session == null) {
      return;
    }
    String normalizedGroup = Strings.trimToNull(group);
    String normalizedName = Strings.trimToNull(name);
    StitchGroupSelectionContext.remember(normalizedGroup);
    if (normalizedGroup == null && normalizedName == null) {
      session.setAttribute(ATTRIBUTE_KEY, null);
      return;
    }
    session.setAttribute(ATTRIBUTE_KEY, new Selection(normalizedGroup, normalizedName));
  }

  static Selection current() {
    VaadinSession session = VaadinSession.getCurrent();
    if (session == null) {
      return null;
    }
    Object value = session.getAttribute(ATTRIBUTE_KEY);
    return value instanceof Selection selection ? selection : null;
  }

  record Selection(String group, String name) implements Serializable {
    Selection {
      group = Strings.trimToNull(group);
      name = Strings.trimToNull(name);
    }
  }
}

  }

    return FEATURE_ID;
  }

  @Override
  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public StitchConfigsScreenConfig view() {
    return view;
  }

  public StitchConfigsScreenConfig edit() {
    return edit;
  }

  public StitchConfigsScreenConfig approvals() {
    return approvals;
  }

  public StitchConfigsScreenConfig control() {
    return control;
  }

  public StitchConfigsScreenConfig rollbacks() {
    return rollbacks;
  }

  public StitchConfigsScreenConfig schemas() {
    return schemas;
  }

  public StitchConfigsScreenConfig watcher() {
    return watcher;
  }

  public Optional<StitchConfigsScreenConfig> screen(String screenId) {
    if (screenId == null || screenId.isBlank()) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    String normalized = screenId.trim();
    if (VIEW.equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
      return Optional.of(view);
    }
    if (EDIT.equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
      return Optional.of(edit);
    }
    if (CONTROL.equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
      return Optional.of(control);
    }
    if (APPROVALS.equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
      return Optional.of(approvals);
    }
    if (ROLLBACKS.equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
      return Optional.of(rollbacks);
    }
    if (SCHEMAS.equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
      return Optional.of(schemas);
    }
    if (WATCHER.equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
      return Optional.of(watcher);
    }
    return Optional.empty();
  }

  @Override
  public List<StitchMenuEntry> menuEntries() {
    List<StitchMenuEntry> entries = new ArrayList<>();
    addEntry(entries, view, ENTRY_VIEW);
    addEntry(entries, edit, ENTRY_EDIT);
    addEntry(entries, control, ENTRY_CONTROL);
    addEntry(entries, approvals, ENTRY_APPROVALS);
    addEntry(entries, rollbacks, ENTRY_ROLLBACKS);
    addEntry(entries, schemas, ENTRY_SCHEMAS);
    addEntry(entries, watcher, ENTRY_WATCHER);
    return List.copyOf(entries);
  }

  private static void addEntry(
      List<StitchMenuEntry> entries, StitchConfigsScreenConfig screen, String entryId) {
    if (screen == null || !screen.enabled()) {
      return;
    }
    entries.add(
        StitchMenuEntry.builder(entryId)
            .withLabel(screen.label())
            .withRoutePath(screen.routePath())
            .withOrder(screen.order())
            .build());
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String menuLabel = "Configs";
    private int order = 45;

        StitchConfigsScreenConfig.builder(VIEW);

        StitchConfigsScreenConfig.builder(EDIT);

        StitchConfigsScreenConfig.builder(CONTROL);
    private final StitchConfigsScreenConfig.Builder approvalsBuilder =
        StitchConfigsScreenConfig.builder(APPROVALS);
    private final StitchConfigsScreenConfig.Builder rollbacksBuilder =
        StitchConfigsScreenConfig.builder(ROLLBACKS);
    private final StitchConfigsScreenConfig.Builder schemasBuilder =
        StitchConfigsScreenConfig.builder(SCHEMAS);
    private final StitchConfigsScreenConfig.Builder watcherBuilder =
        StitchConfigsScreenConfig.builder(WATCHER);

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withMenuLabel(String value) {
      this.menuLabel = require(value, "menuLabel");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder view(Consumer<StitchConfigsScreenConfig.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(viewBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder edit(Consumer<StitchConfigsScreenConfig.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(editBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder control(Consumer<StitchConfigsScreenConfig.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(controlBuilder);

  }
