===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/configs/StitchConfigsProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.configs;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.HashSet;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.UUID;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.manager.ConfigManagerImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.model.ConfigResolved;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.workflow.ConfigAdminService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfig;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfigChange;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfigLayer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionSchema;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.StitchGroupAccess;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.StitchIdentityContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter;

public final class StitchConfigsProvider {
  private static final String BASE_LAYER_ID = "base";
  private final SessionImpl session;
  private final StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext;
  private final StitchGroupAccess groupAccess;
  private final StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter keyAdapter = new StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter();

  public StitchConfigsProvider(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    this.runtimeContext = runtimeContext;
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(current instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    this.session = resolved;
    this.groupAccess = new StitchGroupAccess(current);
  }

  public List<String> listGroups() {
    DiscoveryCache cache = requireCache();
    LinkedHashSet<String> availableGroups = new LinkedHashSet<>();

    for (DefinitionConfig definition : cache.list(DefinitionConfig.class)) {
      if (definition == null || definition.envelope() == null) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("config.envelope is required");
      }
      String group = Strings.requireNonBlank(definition.envelope().group(), "config.envelope.group");
      availableGroups.add(group);
    }
    for (DefinitionConfigLayer definition : cache.list(DefinitionConfigLayer.class)) {
      if (definition == null) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("config.layer definition is required");
      }
      String group =
          Strings.requireNonBlank(
              StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.layerIdentity(definition).group(),
              "config.layer.group");
      availableGroups.add(group);
    }
    List<String> discovered = availableGroups.stream().sorted(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER).toList();
    if (discovered.isEmpty()) {
      StitchGroupAccess.GroupScope scope = currentGroupScope();
      if (scope == null) {
        return List.of();
      }
      List<String> fromScope = normalizeGroups(scope.visibleGroups());
      return fromScope.isEmpty() ? List.of() : fromScope;
    }

    StitchGroupAccess.GroupScope scope = currentGroupScope();
    if (scope == null) {
      return discovered;
    }
    List<String> scoped = normalizeGroups(scope.visibleGroups());
    if (!scoped.isEmpty()) {
      if (scope.admin()) {
        return scoped;
      }
      return scoped;
    }

    if (scope.visibleGroups().isEmpty()
        && scope.configuredGroups().isEmpty()
        && scope.subjectGroups().isEmpty()) {
      return discovered;
    }

    if (scope.visibleGroups().isEmpty()) {
      boolean unresolved =
          scope.configuredGroups().isEmpty() && scope.subjectGroups().isEmpty();
      return unresolved ? discovered : List.of();
    }
    return List.of();
  }

  public List<String> listConfigNames(String group) {
    String normalizedGroup = trimToNull(group);
    if (normalizedGroup == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    DiscoveryCache cache = requireCache();
    LinkedHashSet<String> names = new LinkedHashSet<>();

    for (DefinitionConfig definition : cache.list(DefinitionConfig.class, normalizedGroup)) {
      String name = StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.configNameFromDefinition(definition);
      if (name != null) {
        names.add(name);
      }
    }
    return names.stream().sorted(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER).toList();
  }

  public TreeModel loadLayers(String group, String configName) {
    String normalizedGroup = trimToNull(group);
    String normalizedConfigName = trimToNull(configName);
    if (normalizedGroup == null || normalizedConfigName == null) {
      return TreeModel.empty();
    }

    DiscoveryCache cache = requireCache();
    List<DefinitionConfigLayer> candidates = cache.list(DefinitionConfigLayer.class, normalizedGroup);
    if (candidates.isEmpty()) {
      return TreeModel.empty();
    }
    Map<String, PendingState> pendingByLayerId =
        pendingStatesByLayerId(cache, normalizedGroup, normalizedConfigName);

    LinkedHashMap<String, LayerRecord> byLayerId = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (DefinitionConfigLayer definition : candidates) {
      StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.LayerIdentity identity =
          StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.layerIdentity(definition);
      if (!normalizedConfigName.equals(identity.configName()) || identity.layerId() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String layerId = identity.layerId();
      String parentLayerId = StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.parentLayerId(definition);
      String shortName = trimToNull(definition.shortName());
      String schemaKey = trimToNull(definition.schemaKey());
      String resourceId = trimToNull(definition.resourceId());
      String configVersionId = trimToNull(definition.configId());
      String effectiveConfigId = trimToNull(definition.effectiveConfigId());
      JsonNode declared = definition.declared() == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : definition.declared().deepCopy();
      List<DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective> effective =
          definition.effective() == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(definition.effective());
      PendingState pending = pendingByLayerId.get(layerId);
      String futureEffectiveAt = firstFutureEffectiveAtUtc(effective, Instant.now());
      byLayerId.put(
          layerId,
          new LayerRecord(
              normalizedGroup,
              normalizedConfigName,
              layerId,
              parentLayerId,
              shortName,
              schemaKey,
              resourceId,
              configVersionId,
              effectiveConfigId,
              declared,
              effective,
              definition.envelope(),
              pending != null,
              pending == null ? null : pending.stateLabel(),
              pending == null ? null : pending.modeLabel(),
              pending == null ? null : pending.effectiveAtUtc(),
              pending == null ? null : pending.expiresAtUtc(),
              futureEffectiveAt));
    }
    if (byLayerId.isEmpty()) {
      return TreeModel.empty();
    }

    LinkedHashMap<String, String> pathByLayerId = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String layerId : byLayerId.keySet()) {
      buildLayerPath(layerId, byLayerId, pathByLayerId, new HashSet<>());
    }

    List<String> keys = new ArrayList<>();
    LinkedHashMap<String, LayerRecord> recordsByPath = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : pathByLayerId.entrySet()) {
      String path = StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.normalizeKey(entry.getValue());
      if (path == null) {
        continue;
      }
      LayerRecord record = byLayerId.get(entry.getKey());
      if (record == null) {
        continue;
      }
      keys.add(path);
      recordsByPath.put(path, record.withPath(path));
    }

    StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.Model model = keyAdapter.build(keys);
    return new TreeModel(model.roots(), model.byId(), Map.copyOf(recordsByPath));
  }

  public LayerRecord saveDeclared(String group, String configName, String layerId, JsonNode declaredPayload) {
    String normalizedGroup = trimToNull(group);
    String normalizedConfigName = trimToNull(configName);
    String normalizedLayerId = trimToNull(layerId);
    if (normalizedGroup == null || normalizedConfigName == null || normalizedLayerId == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("group, configName, and layerId are required");
    }
    if (declaredPayload == null || !declaredPayload.isObject()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("declared payload must be a JSON object");
    }

    DiscoveryCache cache = requireCache();
    DefinitionConfigLayer existing =
        StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.findLayer(
            cache, normalizedGroup, normalizedConfigName, normalizedLayerId);
    if (existing == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Config layer not found: " + normalizedGroup + "/" + normalizedConfigName + "/" + normalizedLayerId);
    }

    DefinitionEnvelope updatedEnvelope = bumpEnvelope(existing.envelope());
    DefinitionConfigLayer updated =
        new DefinitionConfigLayer(
            updatedEnvelope,
            existing.resourceId(),
            existing.parentId(),
            existing.shortName(),
            existing.configType(),
            existing.schemaKey(),
            existing.displayName(),
            declaredPayload.deepCopy(),
            existing.effective() == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(existing.effective()),
            existing.history() == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(existing.history()),
            existing.configId(),
            existing.effectiveConfigId());
    cache.upsert(updated);

    LayerRecord saved =
        new LayerRecord(
            normalizedGroup,
            normalizedConfigName,
            normalizedLayerId,
            StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.parentLayerId(updated),
            trimToNull(updated.shortName()),
            trimToNull(updated.schemaKey()),
            trimToNull(updated.resourceId()),
            trimToNull(updated.configId()),
            trimToNull(updated.effectiveConfigId()),
            updated.declared() == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : updated.declared().deepCopy(),
            updated.effective() == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(updated.effective()),
            updated.envelope(),
            false,
            null,
            null,
            null,
            null,
            firstFutureEffectiveAtUtc(updated.effective() == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(updated.effective()), Instant.now()));
    return saved;
  }

  public SubmissionResult submitDeclared(
      String group,
      String configName,
      String layerId,
      JsonNode declaredPayload,
      SubmissionOptions options) {
    String normalizedGroup = trimToNull(group);
    String normalizedConfigName = trimToNull(configName);
    String normalizedLayerId = trimToNull(layerId);
    if (normalizedGroup == null || normalizedConfigName == null || normalizedLayerId == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("group, configName, and layerId are required");
    }
    if (declaredPayload == null || !declaredPayload.isObject()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("declared payload must be a JSON object");
    }
    SubmissionOptions normalized = normalizeSubmissionOptions(options);
    LayerRecord saved;
    if (normalized.approvalRequired()) {
      workflow()
          .propose(
              normalizedGroup,
              normalizedConfigName,
              normalizedLayerId,
              declaredPayload.deepCopy(),
              normalized.mode() == SubmissionMode.SCHEDULED
                  ? DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeMode.SCHEDULED
                  : DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeMode.IMMEDIATE,
              normalized.effectiveAtUtc(),
              normalized.expiresAtUtc(),
              Strings.firstNonBlank(normalized.note(), "STITCH PROPOSE"),
              StitchIdentityContext.currentSubject());
      saved = requireLayerRecord(normalizedGroup, normalizedConfigName, normalizedLayerId);
    } else {
      saved = saveDeclared(normalizedGroup, normalizedConfigName, normalizedLayerId, declaredPayload);
    }
    return new SubmissionResult(saved, normalized);
  }

  public LayerRecord createLayer(
      String group, String configName, String layerId, String parentLayerId, String shortName) {
    String normalizedGroup = trimToNull(group);
    String normalizedConfigName = trimToNull(configName);
    String normalizedLayerId = StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.normalizeLayerId(layerId, "layerId");
    String normalizedParentLayerId = trimToNull(parentLayerId);
    String normalizedShortName = trimToNull(shortName);
    if (normalizedGroup == null || normalizedConfigName == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("group and configName are required");
    }

    DiscoveryCache cache = requireCache();
    LinkedHashMap<String, DefinitionConfigLayer> definitionsByLayerId =
        layerDefinitionsByLayerId(cache, normalizedGroup, normalizedConfigName);
    if (definitionsByLayerId.containsKey(normalizedLayerId)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Layer already exists: " + normalizedLayerId);
    }
    if (normalizedParentLayerId == null && !BASE_LAYER_ID.equals(normalizedLayerId)) {
      if (definitionsByLayerId.containsKey(BASE_LAYER_ID)) {
        normalizedParentLayerId = BASE_LAYER_ID;
      } else {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("parentLayerId is required for non-base layers");
      }
    }
    if (normalizedParentLayerId != null && !definitionsByLayerId.containsKey(normalizedParentLayerId)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Parent layer not found: " + normalizedParentLayerId);
    }
    if (Objects.equals(normalizedLayerId, normalizedParentLayerId)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("layerId and parentLayerId must be different");
    }

    DefinitionConfigLayer template =
        normalizedParentLayerId == null
            ? firstLayer(definitionsByLayerId)
            : definitionsByLayerId.get(normalizedParentLayerId);
    if (template == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Template layer is required to create a new layer");
    }

    String now = Instant.now().toString();
    String subject = StitchIdentityContext.currentSubject();
    String resolvedShortName =
        normalizedShortName == null
            ? normalizedLayerId.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT)
            : normalizedShortName;
    String resolvedConfigId =
        Strings.requireNonBlank(trimToNull(template.configId()), "layer.configId");
    String resolvedEffectiveConfigId =
        Strings.requireNonBlank(
            trimToNull(template.effectiveConfigId()), "layer.effectiveConfigId");

    DefinitionConfigLayer created =
        new DefinitionConfigLayer(
            new DefinitionEnvelope(
                normalizedGroup,
                DefinitionType.CONFIG_LAYER,
                StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.configLayerDefinitionName(
                    normalizedConfigName, normalizedLayerId),
                UUID.randomUUID().toString(),
                true,
                "ACTIVE",
                now,
                subject,
                now,
                subject),
            StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.canonicalLayerResourceId(
                normalizedGroup, normalizedConfigName, normalizedLayerId),
            StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.canonicalParentLayerId(
                normalizedGroup, normalizedConfigName, normalizedParentLayerId),
            resolvedShortName,
            Strings.requireNonBlank(trimToNull(template.configType()), "layer.configType"),
            trimToNull(template.schemaKey()),
            StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.configLayerDisplayName(
                normalizedConfigName, normalizedLayerId),
            DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode(),
            List.of(),
            List.of(),
            resolvedConfigId,
            resolvedEffectiveConfigId);
    cache.upsert(created);
    return requireLayerRecord(normalizedGroup, normalizedConfigName, normalizedLayerId);
  }

  public LayerRecord moveLayer(
      String group, String configName, String layerId, String newParentLayerId) {
    String normalizedGroup = trimToNull(group);
    String normalizedConfigName = trimToNull(configName);
    String normalizedLayerId =
        StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.normalizeLayerId(layerId, "layerId");
    String normalizedParentLayerId =
        StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.normalizeLayerId(newParentLayerId, "newParentLayerId");
    if (normalizedGroup == null || normalizedConfigName == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("group and configName are required");
    }
    if (BASE_LAYER_ID.equals(normalizedLayerId)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("base layer cannot be moved");
    }
    if (Objects.equals(normalizedLayerId, normalizedParentLayerId)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Layer cannot be parent of itself");
    }

    DiscoveryCache cache = requireCache();
    LinkedHashMap<String, DefinitionConfigLayer> definitionsByLayerId =
        layerDefinitionsByLayerId(cache, normalizedGroup, normalizedConfigName);
    DefinitionConfigLayer target = definitionsByLayerId.get(normalizedLayerId);
    if (target == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Layer not found: " + normalizedLayerId);
    }
    if (!definitionsByLayerId.containsKey(normalizedParentLayerId)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("New parent layer not found: " + normalizedParentLayerId);
    }
    Set<String> descendants = descendantsInclusive(normalizedLayerId, definitionsByLayerId);
    if (descendants.contains(normalizedParentLayerId)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("New parent cannot be a descendant of the moved layer");
    }

    DefinitionConfigLayer moved =
        new DefinitionConfigLayer(
            bumpEnvelope(target.envelope()),
            target.resourceId(),
            StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.canonicalParentLayerId(
                normalizedGroup, normalizedConfigName, normalizedParentLayerId),
            target.shortName(),
            target.configType(),
            target.schemaKey(),
            target.displayName(),
            target.declared() == null
                ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode()
                : target.declared().deepCopy(),
            target.effective() == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(target.effective()),
            target.history() == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(target.history()),
            target.configId(),
            target.effectiveConfigId());
    cache.upsert(moved);
    return requireLayerRecord(normalizedGroup, normalizedConfigName, normalizedLayerId);
  }

  public void deleteLayer(String group, String configName, String layerId) {
    String normalizedGroup = trimToNull(group);
    String normalizedConfigName = trimToNull(configName);
    String normalizedLayerId = StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.normalizeLayerId(layerId, "layerId");
    if (normalizedGroup == null || normalizedConfigName == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("group and configName are required");
    }
    if (BASE_LAYER_ID.equals(normalizedLayerId)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("base layer cannot be deleted");
    }

    DiscoveryCache cache = requireCache();
    LinkedHashMap<String, DefinitionConfigLayer> definitionsByLayerId =
        layerDefinitionsByLayerId(cache, normalizedGroup, normalizedConfigName);
    if (!definitionsByLayerId.containsKey(normalizedLayerId)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Layer not found: " + normalizedLayerId);
    }
    List<String> subtree = postOrderSubtree(normalizedLayerId, definitionsByLayerId);
    for (String subtreeLayerId : subtree) {
      DefinitionConfigLayer current = definitionsByLayerId.get(subtreeLayerId);
      if (current == null || current.envelope() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String definitionName = trimToNull(current.envelope().name());
      if (definitionName == null) {
        continue;
      }
      cache.delete(DefinitionType.CONFIG_LAYER, normalizedGroup, definitionName);
    }
  }

  public ComparePayload resolveLivePayload(LayerRecord layer) {
    if (layer == null) {
      return new ComparePayload("LIVE", DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode());
    }
    Instant now = Instant.now();
    DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective active = null;
    Instant activeAt = null;
    DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective latest = null;
    Instant latestAt = null;

    for (DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective entry : layer.effective()) {
      if (entry == null || entry.declared() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      Instant effectiveAt = parseUtc(entry.effectiveTimeUtc());
      Instant expiresAt = parseUtc(entry.expiresAtUtc());
      if (isAfterOrEqual(now, effectiveAt) && isBefore(now, expiresAt)) {
        if (active == null || compareInstants(effectiveAt, activeAt) > 0) {
          active = entry;
          activeAt = effectiveAt;
        }
      }
      if (latest == null || compareInstants(effectiveAt, latestAt) > 0) {
        latest = entry;
        latestAt = effectiveAt;
      }
    }

    if (active != null) {
      return new ComparePayload(liveLabel("LIVE", active.effectiveTimeUtc()), safePayload(active.declared()));
    }
    if (latest != null) {
      return new ComparePayload(
          liveLabel("LIVE (latest known)", latest.effectiveTimeUtc()), safePayload(latest.declared()));
    }
    return new ComparePayload("LIVE (declared fallback)", safePayload(layer.declared()));
  }

  public LayerView loadLayerView(
      LayerRecord layer, Map<String, LayerRecord> layersByPath, Instant asOfUtc) {
    if (layer == null) {
      return LayerView.empty();
    }
    Instant resolvedAt = asOfUtc == null ? Instant.now() : asOfUtc;
    JsonNode declaredPayload = safePayload(layer.declared());
    JsonNode resolvedPayload = safePayload(layer.declared());
    Map<String, String> sourceByPath = Map.of();
    List<String> lineageLayers = List.of();
    String lineageSummary = "Unavailable";
    try {
      ConfigManagerImpl manager = requireConfigManager();
      ConfigResolved resolved =
          manager.resolve(layer.group(), layer.configName(), layer.layerId(), resolvedAt);
      if (resolved != null) {
        resolvedPayload = safePayload(DiscoveryCodec.mapper().valueToTree(resolved.payload()));
        sourceByPath =
            resolved.sources() == null
                ? Map.of()
                : resolved.sources().entrySet().stream()
                    .filter(entry -> trimToNull(entry.getKey()) != null)
                    .collect(
                        LinkedHashMap::new,
                        (map, entry) ->
                            map.put(
                                entry.getKey(),
                                Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(entry.getValue()), "-")),
                        LinkedHashMap::putAll);
        lineageLayers =
            resolved.lineage() == null || resolved.lineage().resolvedLayers() == null
                ? List.of()
                : resolved.lineage().resolvedLayers().stream()
                    .map(StitchConfigsProvider::trimToNull)
                    .filter(Objects::nonNull)
                    .toList();
        lineageSummary =
            resolved.lineage() == null
                ? "Unavailable"
                : "Depth " + Math.max(0, resolved.lineage().chainDepth());
      }
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
    }

    JsonNode schemaDocument = resolveSchemaDocument(layer.group(), layer.schemaKey());
    ImpactSummary impact = computeImpact(layer, layersByPath);
    String pendingSummary = pendingSummary(layer, resolvedAt);
    return new LayerView(
        layer,
        declaredPayload,
        resolvedPayload,
        sourceByPath,
        lineageLayers,
        lineageSummary,
        schemaDocument,
        impact.affectedLeaves(),
        impact.totalLeaves(),
        pendingSummary,
        resolvedAt.toString());
  }

  public DagModel buildDagModel(
      Map<String, LayerRecord> layersByPath, String selectedLayerId, boolean selectedPathOnly) {
    if (layersByPath == null || layersByPath.isEmpty()) {
      return DagModel.empty();
    }
    String selectedId = trimToNull(selectedLayerId);
    Map<String, LayerRecord> byLayerId = indexByLayerId(layersByPath);
    Set<String> selectedPath = selectedPath(byLayerId, selectedId);

    LinkedHashMap<String, Integer> inDegree = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    LinkedHashMap<String, Integer> outDegree = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String layerId : byLayerId.keySet()) {
      inDegree.put(layerId, 0);
      outDegree.put(layerId, 0);
    }
    List<DagEdge> edges = new ArrayList<>();
    for (LayerRecord record : byLayerId.values()) {
      String childId = trimToNull(record.layerId());
      String parentId = trimToNull(record.parentLayerId());
      if (childId == null || parentId == null || !byLayerId.containsKey(parentId)) {
        continue;
      }
      if (selectedPathOnly
          && (!selectedPath.contains(childId) || !selectedPath.contains(parentId))) {
        continue;
      }
      edges.add(new DagEdge(parentId, childId));
      outDegree.computeIfPresent(parentId, (key, value) -> value + 1);
      inDegree.computeIfPresent(childId, (key, value) -> value + 1);
    }

    List<DagNode> nodes = new ArrayList<>();
    for (LayerRecord record : byLayerId.values()) {
      String layerId = trimToNull(record.layerId());
      if (layerId == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (selectedPathOnly && !selectedPath.contains(layerId)) {
        continue;
      }
      int in = inDegree.getOrDefault(layerId, 0);
      int out = outDegree.getOrDefault(layerId, 0);
      DagNodeKind kind =
          layerId.equals(selectedId)
              ? DagNodeKind.SELECTED
              : in == 0
                  ? DagNodeKind.ROOT
                  : out == 0 ? DagNodeKind.LEAF : DagNodeKind.INTERMEDIATE;
      nodes.add(
          new DagNode(
              layerId,
              Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(record.shortName()), layerId),
              kind,
              trimToNull(record.parentLayerId())));
    }
    return new DagModel(List.copyOf(nodes), List.copyOf(edges), List.copyOf(selectedPath));
  }

  public JsonNode resolveSchemaDocument(String group, String schemaKey) {
    String normalizedGroup = trimToNull(group);
    String normalizedSchemaKey = trimToNull(schemaKey);
    if (normalizedGroup == null || normalizedSchemaKey == null) {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    }
    DefinitionSchema schema = resolveSchemaDefinition(normalizedGroup, normalizedSchemaKey);
    if (schema == null) {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    }
    return parseJson(schema.schema());
  }

  public JsonNode resolveSchemaDocument(
      String group, String configName, Map<String, LayerRecord> layersByPath) {
    String normalizedGroup = trimToNull(group);
    String normalizedConfigName = trimToNull(configName);
    if (normalizedGroup == null || normalizedConfigName == null) {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    }
    String schemaKey = null;
    if (layersByPath != null) {
      for (LayerRecord layer : layersByPath.values()) {
        if (layer == null) {
          continue;
        }
        if (!normalizedConfigName.equals(trimToNull(layer.configName()))) {
          continue;
        }
        if ("base".equals(trimToNull(layer.layerId()))) {
          schemaKey = trimToNull(layer.schemaKey());
          break;
        }
        if (schemaKey == null) {
          schemaKey = trimToNull(layer.schemaKey());
        }
      }
    }
    return resolveSchemaDocument(normalizedGroup, schemaKey);
  }

  public ConfigManager.ConfigCodegen generateCode(
      String group,
      String configName,
      String layerId,
      ConfigManager.Language language,
      String basePackageOrModule) {
    String normalizedGroup = trimToNull(group);
    String normalizedConfigName = trimToNull(configName);
    String normalizedLayerId = trimToNull(layerId);
    if (normalizedGroup == null || normalizedConfigName == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("group and configName are required");
    }
    ConfigManager manager = session.configs();
    if (manager == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Config manager is not available");
    }
    ConfigManager.Language selectedLanguage =
        language == null ? ConfigManager.Language.JAVA : language;
    if (normalizedLayerId == null) {
      return manager.generate(normalizedConfigName, selectedLanguage, trimToNull(basePackageOrModule));
    }
    return manager.generate(
        normalizedConfigName, normalizedLayerId, selectedLanguage, trimToNull(basePackageOrModule));
  }

  private Map<String, PendingState> pendingStatesByLayerId(
      DiscoveryCache cache, String group, String configName) {
    if (cache == null || group == null || configName == null) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, PendingState> pending = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (DefinitionConfigChange change : cache.list(DefinitionConfigChange.class, group)) {
      if (change == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (!configName.equals(trimToNull(change.configId()))) {
        continue;
      }
      String layerId = trimToNull(change.layerId());
      if (layerId == null || !isPendingState(change.state())) {
        continue;
      }
      String updated = Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(change.updatedTimeUtc()), trimToNull(change.createdTimeUtc()));
      PendingState next =
          new PendingState(
              layerId,
              displayState(change.state()),
              displayMode(change.mode()),
              trimToNull(change.effectiveAtUtc()),
              trimToNull(change.expiresAtUtc()),
              updated);
      PendingState existing = pending.get(layerId);
      if (existing == null || compareText(next.updatedTimeUtc(), existing.updatedTimeUtc()) > 0) {
        pending.put(layerId, next);
      }
    }
    return Map.copyOf(pending);
  }

  private static boolean isPendingState(DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState state) {
    if (state == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return state == DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState.DRAFT
        || state == DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState.PROPOSED
        || state == DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState.APPROVED;
  }

  private static String displayState(DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState state) {
    if (state == null) {
      return "UNKNOWN";
    }
    return switch (state) {
      case DRAFT -> "DRAFT";
      case PROPOSED -> "PROPOSED";
      case APPROVED -> "APPROVED";
      case REJECTED -> "REJECTED";
      case NONE -> "NONE";
      case UNKNOWN -> "UNKNOWN";
    };
  }

  private static String displayMode(DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeMode mode) {
    if (mode == null) {
      return "UNKNOWN";
    }
    return mode == DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeMode.SCHEDULED ? "SCHEDULED" : "IMMEDIATE";
  }

  private static String firstFutureEffectiveAtUtc(
      List<DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective> effectiveEntries, Instant now) {
    if (effectiveEntries == null || effectiveEntries.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    String earliest = null;
    Instant earliestInstant = null;
    Instant reference = now == null ? Instant.now() : now;
    for (DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective entry : effectiveEntries) {
      if (entry == null) {
        continue;
      }
      Instant effectiveAt = parseUtc(entry.effectiveTimeUtc());
      if (effectiveAt == null || !effectiveAt.isAfter(reference)) {
        continue;
      }
      if (earliestInstant == null || effectiveAt.isBefore(earliestInstant)) {
        earliestInstant = effectiveAt;
        earliest = trimToNull(entry.effectiveTimeUtc());
      }
    }
    return earliest;
  }

  private static String pendingSummary(LayerRecord layer, Instant asOfUtc) {
    if (layer == null) {
      return "None";
    }
    if (layer.hasPendingChange()) {
      String state = Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(layer.pendingStateLabel()), "PENDING");
      String effective = Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(layer.pendingEffectiveAtUtc()), "unscheduled");
      return state + " @ " + effective;
    }
    String future = trimToNull(layer.firstFutureEffectiveAtUtc());
    if (future != null) {
      return "Scheduled @ " + future;
    }
    return "None";
  }

  private static ImpactSummary computeImpact(
      LayerRecord selected, Map<String, LayerRecord> layersByPath) {
    if (selected == null || layersByPath == null || layersByPath.isEmpty()) {
      return new ImpactSummary(0, 0);
    }
    Map<String, LayerRecord> byLayerId = indexByLayerId(layersByPath);
    String selectedLayer = trimToNull(selected.layerId());
    if (selectedLayer == null || !byLayerId.containsKey(selectedLayer)) {
      return new ImpactSummary(0, 0);
    }
    Set<String> descendants = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    descendants.add(selectedLayer);
    boolean changed = true;
    while (changed) {
      changed = false;
      for (LayerRecord record : byLayerId.values()) {
        String layerId = trimToNull(record.layerId());
        String parentLayer = trimToNull(record.parentLayerId());
        if (layerId == null || parentLayer == null) {
          continue;
        }
        if (!descendants.contains(parentLayer) || descendants.contains(layerId)) {
          continue;
        }
        descendants.add(layerId);
        changed = true;
      }
    }
    int totalLeaves = 0;
    for (String layerId : descendants) {
      boolean hasChild =
          byLayerId.values().stream()
              .anyMatch(
                  record ->
                      layerId.equals(trimToNull(record.parentLayerId()))
                          && descendants.contains(trimToNull(record.layerId())));
      if (!hasChild) {
        totalLeaves++;
      }
    }
    return new ImpactSummary(totalLeaves, totalLeaves);
  }

  private static Map<String, LayerRecord> indexByLayerId(Map<String, LayerRecord> layersByPath) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, LayerRecord> byLayerId = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (layersByPath == null || layersByPath.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    for (LayerRecord layer : layersByPath.values()) {
      if (layer == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String layerId = trimToNull(layer.layerId());
      if (layerId == null || byLayerId.containsKey(layerId)) {
        continue;
      }
      byLayerId.put(layerId, layer);
    }
    return Map.copyOf(byLayerId);
  }

  private static Set<String> selectedPath(Map<String, LayerRecord> byLayerId, String selectedLayerId) {
    if (byLayerId == null || byLayerId.isEmpty() || selectedLayerId == null) {
      return Set.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> path = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    String cursor = selectedLayerId;
    while (cursor != null && !path.contains(cursor)) {
      LayerRecord layer = byLayerId.get(cursor);
      if (layer == null) {
        break;
      }
      path.add(cursor);
      cursor = trimToNull(layer.parentLayerId());
    }
    return Set.copyOf(path);
  }

  private DefinitionSchema resolveSchemaDefinition(String group, String schemaKey) {
    DiscoveryCache cache = requireCache();
    var definition = cache.get(DefinitionType.SCHEMA, group, schemaKey);
    if (!(definition instanceof DefinitionSchema schema)) {
      return null;
    }
    return schema;
  }

  private ConfigManagerImpl requireConfigManager() {
    ConfigManager manager = session.configs();
    if (!(manager instanceof ConfigManagerImpl configManager)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Config manager implementation is unavailable");
    }
    return configManager;
  }

  private static JsonNode parseJson(String value) {
    String normalized = trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    }
    try {
      JsonNode parsed = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().readTree(normalized);
      return parsed == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : parsed.deepCopy();
    } catch (Exception error) {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    }
  }

  private static int compareText(String left, String right) {
    String a = Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(left), "");
    String b = Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(right), "");
    return a.compareTo(b);
  }

  private static String buildLayerPath(
      String layerId,
      Map<String, LayerRecord> byLayerId,
      Map<String, String> pathByLayerId,
      Set<String> visiting) {
    if (layerId == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String existing = pathByLayerId.get(layerId);
    if (existing != null) {
      return existing;
    }
    if (!visiting.add(layerId)) {
      pathByLayerId.put(layerId, layerId);
      return layerId;
    }
    LayerRecord row = byLayerId.get(layerId);
    if (row == null) {
      visiting.remove(layerId);
      return null;
    }

    String path;
    String parent = trimToNull(row.parentLayerId());
    if (parent == null || !byLayerId.containsKey(parent)) {
      path = layerId;
    } else {
      String parentPath = buildLayerPath(parent, byLayerId, pathByLayerId, visiting);
      path = trimToNull(parentPath) == null ? layerId : parentPath + "/" + layerId;
    }
    visiting.remove(layerId);
    pathByLayerId.put(layerId, path);
    return path;
  }

  private static DefinitionEnvelope bumpEnvelope(DefinitionEnvelope envelope) {
    if (envelope == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String now = Instant.now().toString();
    return new DefinitionEnvelope(
        envelope.group(),
        envelope.type(),
        envelope.name(),
        envelope.uuid(),
        envelope.enabled(),
        envelope.lifecycleStatus(),
        envelope.createdTimeUtc(),
        envelope.createdBy(),
        now,
        Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(envelope.updatedBy()), trimToNull(envelope.createdBy()), "service:stitch"));
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return normalized.trim();
  }

  private static LinkedHashMap<String, DefinitionConfigLayer> layerDefinitionsByLayerId(
      DiscoveryCache cache, String group, String configName) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, DefinitionConfigLayer> byLayerId = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (cache == null || group == null || configName == null) {
      return byLayerId;
    }
    for (DefinitionConfigLayer definition : cache.list(DefinitionConfigLayer.class, group)) {
      StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.LayerIdentity identity =
          StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.layerIdentity(definition);
      if (!Objects.equals(configName, identity.configName())) {
        continue;
      }
      String layerId = trimToNull(identity.layerId());
      if (layerId == null || byLayerId.containsKey(layerId)) {
        continue;
      }
      byLayerId.put(layerId, definition);
    }
    return byLayerId;
  }

  private static DefinitionConfigLayer firstLayer(Map<String, DefinitionConfigLayer> byLayerId) {
    if (byLayerId == null || byLayerId.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    DefinitionConfigLayer base = byLayerId.get(BASE_LAYER_ID);
    if (base != null) {
      return base;
    }
    return byLayerId.values().stream().filter(Objects::nonNull).findFirst().orElse(null);
  }

  private static Set<String> descendantsInclusive(
      String rootLayerId, Map<String, DefinitionConfigLayer> byLayerId) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> descendants = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    String root = trimToNull(rootLayerId);
    if (root == null || byLayerId == null || byLayerId.isEmpty() || !byLayerId.containsKey(root)) {
      return descendants;
    }
    descendants.add(root);
    boolean changed = true;
    while (changed) {
      changed = false;
      for (Map.Entry<String, DefinitionConfigLayer> entry : byLayerId.entrySet()) {
        String childLayerId = trimToNull(entry.getKey());
        if (childLayerId == null || descendants.contains(childLayerId)) {
          continue;
        }
        String parentLayerId = StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.parentLayerId(entry.getValue());
        if (parentLayerId == null || !descendants.contains(parentLayerId)) {
          continue;
        }
        descendants.add(childLayerId);
        changed = true;
      }
    }
    return descendants;
  }

  private static List<String> postOrderSubtree(
      String rootLayerId, Map<String, DefinitionConfigLayer> byLayerId) {
    Set<String> subtree = descendantsInclusive(rootLayerId, byLayerId);
    if (subtree.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> ordered = new ArrayList<>(subtree);
    ordered.sort(
        Comparator.comparingInt(
                (String layerId) ->
                    depthInSubtree(trimToNull(layerId), subtree, byLayerId, new HashSet<>()))
            .reversed()
            .thenComparing(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER));
    return List.copyOf(ordered);
  }

  private static int depthInSubtree(
      String layerId,
      Set<String> subtree,
      Map<String, DefinitionConfigLayer> byLayerId,
      Set<String> visiting) {
    if (layerId == null || !subtree.contains(layerId) || byLayerId == null || byLayerId.isEmpty()) {
      return 0;
    }
    if (!visiting.add(layerId)) {
      return 0;
    }
    DefinitionConfigLayer definition = byLayerId.get(layerId);
    String parent = StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.parentLayerId(definition);
    if (parent == null || !subtree.contains(parent)) {
      visiting.remove(layerId);
      return 0;
    }
    int depth = 1 + depthInSubtree(parent, subtree, byLayerId, visiting);
    visiting.remove(layerId);
    return depth;
  }

  private LayerRecord requireLayerRecord(String group, String configName, String layerId) {
    String normalizedLayerId = trimToNull(layerId);
    TreeModel tree = loadLayers(group, configName);
    for (LayerRecord record : tree.layersByPath().values()) {
      if (record == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (Objects.equals(normalizedLayerId, trimToNull(record.layerId()))) {
        return record;
      }
    }
    throw new IllegalStateException(
        "Unable to resolve layer after mutation: "
            + Strings.firstNonBlank(configName, "-")
            + "/"
            + Strings.firstNonBlank(normalizedLayerId, "-"));
  }

  private DiscoveryCache requireCache() {
    DiscoveryCache cache = session.internal().discoveryCache();
    if (cache == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DiscoveryCache is not available");
    }
    return cache;
  }

  private ConfigAdminService.Workflow workflow() {
    return session.internal().configAdminService().workflow();
  }

  private StitchGroupAccess.GroupScope currentGroupScope() {
    String subject =
        StitchIdentityContext.resolveSubject(runtimeContext.settings().sso().fallbackSubject());
    try {
      return groupAccess.scopeForSubject(subject);
    } catch (RuntimeException ignored) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private static boolean containsIgnoreCase(List<String> values, String candidate) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return false;
    }
    String normalized = trimToNull(candidate);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return false;
    }
    for (String value : values) {
      String current = trimToNull(value);
      if (current != null && current.equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static List<String> normalizeGroups(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> normalized = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String value : values) {
      String group = trimToNull(value);
      if (group != null) {
        normalized.add(group);
      }
    }
    if (normalized.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(normalized);
    sorted.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }

    }
  }

  private static JsonNode safePayload(JsonNode value) {
    return value == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : value.deepCopy();
  }

  private static String liveLabel(String prefix, String effectiveTimeUtc) {
    String time = trimToNull(effectiveTimeUtc);
    if (time == null) {
      return prefix;
    }
    return prefix + " @ " + time;
  }

  private static Instant parseUtc(String value) {
    String normalized = trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return Instant.parse(normalized);
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private static int compareInstants(Instant left, Instant right) {
    if (left == right) {
      return 0;
    }
    if (left == null) {
      return -1;
    }
    if (right == null) {
      return 1;
    }
    return left.compareTo(right);
  }

  private static boolean isAfterOrEqual(Instant left, Instant right) {
    return right == null || (left != null && !left.isBefore(right));
  }

  private static boolean isBefore(Instant left, Instant right) {
    return right == null || (left != null && left.isBefore(right));
  }

  private static SubmissionOptions normalizeSubmissionOptions(SubmissionOptions value) {
    SubmissionOptions input = value == null ? SubmissionOptions.immediate() : value;
    SubmissionMode mode = input.mode() == null ? SubmissionMode.IMMEDIATE : input.mode();
    Instant effectiveAt = input.effectiveAtUtc();
    Instant expiresAt = input.expiresAtUtc();
    String note = trimToNull(input.note());
    boolean approvalRequired = input.approvalRequired();

    if (mode == SubmissionMode.IMMEDIATE) {
      if (expiresAt != null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Expiry requires scheduled mode.");
      }
      return new SubmissionOptions(mode, null, null, note, approvalRequired);
    }
    if (effectiveAt == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Effective time is required for scheduled mode.");
    }
    if (expiresAt != null && !expiresAt.isAfter(effectiveAt)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Expiry time must be after effective time.");
    }
    return new SubmissionOptions(mode, effectiveAt, expiresAt, note, approvalRequired);
  }

  public enum SubmissionMode {
    IMMEDIATE,
    SCHEDULED
  }

  public record SubmissionOptions(
      SubmissionMode mode,
      Instant effectiveAtUtc,
      Instant expiresAtUtc,
      String note,
      boolean approvalRequired) {
    public SubmissionOptions {
      mode = mode == null ? SubmissionMode.IMMEDIATE : mode;
      note = trimToNull(note);
    }

    public static SubmissionOptions immediate() {
      return new SubmissionOptions(SubmissionMode.IMMEDIATE, null, null, null, true);
    }
  }

  public record SubmissionResult(LayerRecord savedLayer, SubmissionOptions options) {}
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.configs;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigManager.ConfigUpdate;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.workflow.ConfigHistoryEntry;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.workflow.ConfigRollbackRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.workflow.ConfigSnapshot;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

/** Configs rollback/release-history provider. */
public final class StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider {
  private final SessionImpl session;
  private final StitchConfigsProvider configsProvider;

  public StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext, StitchConfigsProvider configsProvider) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    this.configsProvider = Objects.requireNonNull(configsProvider, "configsProvider");
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(current instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    this.session = resolved;
  }

  public List<String> listGroups() {
    return configsProvider.listGroups();
  }

  public List<String> listConfigNames(String group) {
    return configsProvider.listConfigNames(group);
  }

  public List<LayerOption> listLayerOptions(String group, String configName) {
    String requiredGroup = trimToNull(group);
    String requiredConfigName = trimToNull(configName);
    if (requiredGroup == null || requiredConfigName == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    StitchConfigsProvider.TreeModel tree = configsProvider.loadLayers(requiredGroup, requiredConfigName);
    if (tree.layersByPath().isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return tree.layersByPath().values().stream()
        .filter(Objects::nonNull)
        .sorted(
            Comparator.comparing(
                layer -> Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(layer.path()), layer.layerId()),
                String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
        .map(
            layer -> {
              String labelPath = Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(layer.path()), layer.layerId());
              String label =
                  Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(layer.shortName()), layer.layerId()) + " - " + labelPath;
              return new LayerOption(labelPath, label, layer);
            })
        .toList();
  }

  public List<RollbackRecord> listRollbackHistory(
      String group, String configName, String layerId, int limit) {
    String requiredGroup = trimToNull(group);
    String requiredConfigName = trimToNull(configName);
    String requiredLayerId = trimToNull(layerId);
    if (requiredGroup == null || requiredConfigName == null || requiredLayerId == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    int boundedLimit = limit <= 0 ? 50 : Math.min(limit, 200);
    List<ConfigHistoryEntry> history =
        session
            .internal()
            .configAdminService()
            .listHistory(requiredGroup, requiredConfigName, requiredLayerId, boundedLimit);
    if (history == null || history.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return history.stream()
        .map(entry -> toRollbackRecord(requiredGroup, requiredConfigName, requiredLayerId, entry))
        .filter(Objects::nonNull)
        .sorted(
            Comparator.comparing(
                    RollbackRecord::updatedTimeUtc, Comparator.nullsLast(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
                .reversed()
                .thenComparing(
                    row -> Strings.firstNonBlank(row.targetConfigId(), ""), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
        .toList();
  }

  public RollbackDetails loadDetails(RollbackRecord record) {
    RollbackRecord required = Objects.requireNonNull(record, "record");
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord layer = resolveLayer(required);
    ConfigSnapshot snapshot =
        session
            .internal()
            .configAdminService()
            .getSnapshot(
                required.group(), required.configName(), required.layerId(), required.targetConfigId());
    JsonNode snapshotPayload = safePayload(snapshot == null ? null : snapshot.declared());
    JsonNode currentPayload = safePayload(layer == null ? null : layer.declared());
    StitchConfigsProvider.ComparePayload livePayload =
        layer == null
            ? new StitchConfigsProvider.ComparePayload("LIVE", DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode())
            : configsProvider.resolveLivePayload(layer);
    return new RollbackDetails(required, layer, snapshotPayload, currentPayload, livePayload);
  }

  public ConfigUpdate rollback(RollbackRecord record, String reason) {
    RollbackRecord required = Objects.requireNonNull(record, "record");
    if (!required.canRollback()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Selected release cannot be rolled back.");
    }
    ConfigRollbackRequest request =
        new ConfigRollbackRequest(
            required.group(),
            required.configName(),
            required.layerId(),
            required.targetConfigId(),
            ConfigRollbackRequest.Mode.IMMEDIATE,
            null,
            Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(reason), "STITCH ROLLBACK"));
    return session.internal().configAdminService().rollback(request);
  }

  private StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord resolveLayer(RollbackRecord record) {
    StitchConfigsProvider.TreeModel tree = configsProvider.loadLayers(record.group(), record.configName());
    for (StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord candidate : tree.layersByPath().values()) {
      if (candidate != null && Objects.equals(record.layerId(), candidate.layerId())) {
        return candidate;
      }
    }
    return new StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord(
        record.group(),
        record.configName(),
        record.layerId(),
        null,
        record.layerId(),
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode(),
        List.of(),
        null,
        record.layerId());
  }

  private static RollbackRecord toRollbackRecord(
      String group, String configName, String layerId, ConfigHistoryEntry entry) {
    if (entry == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String targetConfigId = trimToNull(entry.configId());
    if (targetConfigId == null) {
      return null;
    }
    int keysCount = Math.max(entry.keysCount(), entry.keys() == null ? 0 : entry.keys().size());
    return new RollbackRecord(
        group,
        configName,
        layerId,
        targetConfigId,
        trimToNull(entry.updatedTimeUtc()),
        trimToNull(entry.updatedBy()),
        trimToNull(entry.mode()),
        trimToNull(entry.effectiveAtUtc()),
        keysCount,
        entry.keys() == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(entry.keys()));
  }

  private static JsonNode safePayload(JsonNode value) {
    return value == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : value.deepCopy();
  }

  private static Instant parseUtc(String value) {
    String normalized = trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return Instant.parse(normalized);
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private static String displayUtcOrDash(String value) {
    String normalized = trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return "-";
    }
    Instant parsed = parseUtc(normalized);
    return parsed == null ? normalized : parsed.toString();
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    return Strings.trimToNull(value);
  }

  public record LayerOption(String id, String label, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord layer) {
    public LayerOption {
      id = trimToNull(id);
      label = trimToNull(label);
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
      return Strings.firstNonBlank(label, id, "-");
    }
  }

  public record RollbackRecord(
      String group,
      String configName,
      String layerId,
      String targetConfigId,
      String updatedTimeUtc,
      String updatedBy,
      String mode,
      String effectiveAtUtc,
      int keysCount,
      List<String> keys) {
    public RollbackRecord {
      group = trimToNull(group);
      configName = trimToNull(configName);
      layerId = trimToNull(layerId);
      targetConfigId = trimToNull(targetConfigId);
      updatedTimeUtc = trimToNull(updatedTimeUtc);
      updatedBy = trimToNull(updatedBy);
      mode = trimToNull(mode);
      effectiveAtUtc = trimToNull(effectiveAtUtc);
      keysCount = Math.max(0, keysCount);
      keys = keys == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(keys);
    }

    public String key() {
      return Strings.firstNonBlank(
          targetConfigId, group + "/" + configName + "/" + layerId + "/" + updatedTimeUtc);
    }

    public String releaseLabel() {
      if (targetConfigId == null) {
        return "-";
      }
      return targetConfigId.length() > 12 ? targetConfigId.substring(0, 12) : targetConfigId;
    }

    public String modeLabel() {
      String normalized = Strings.firstNonBlank(mode, "IMMEDIATE");
      return normalized.equalsIgnoreCase("scheduled") ? "Scheduled" : "Immediate";
    }

    public String updatedByLabel() {
      return Strings.firstNonBlank(updatedBy, "-");
    }

    public String updatedLabel() {
      return displayUtcOrDash(updatedTimeUtc);
    }

    public String effectiveLabel() {
      return displayUtcOrDash(effectiveAtUtc);
    }

    public boolean canRollback() {
      return targetConfigId != null;
    }

    public String compareContext() {
      return "Group: "
          + Strings.firstNonBlank(group, "-")
          + " | Name: "
          + Strings.firstNonBlank(configName, "-")
          + " | Layer: "
          + Strings.firstNonBlank(layerId, "-");
    }

    public Map<String, String> metadata() {
      LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      values.put("Group", Strings.firstNonBlank(group, "-"));
      values.put("Name", Strings.firstNonBlank(configName, "-"));
      values.put("Layer", Strings.firstNonBlank(layerId, "-"));
      values.put("Release Config Id", Strings.firstNonBlank(targetConfigId, "-"));
      values.put("Mode", modeLabel());
      values.put("Effective", effectiveLabel());
      values.put("Updated", updatedLabel());
      values.put("Updated By", updatedByLabel());
      values.put("Changed Keys", String.valueOf(keysCount));
      values.put("Key Summary", keysSummary());
      return values;
    }

    private String keysSummary() {
      if (keys.isEmpty()) {
        return "<none>";
      }
      int take = Math.min(6, keys.size());
      String head = String.join(", ", keys.subList(0, take));
      int extra = keys.size() - take;
      return extra > 0 ? head + " (+" + extra + " more)" : head;
    }
  }

  public record RollbackDetails(
      RollbackRecord record,
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord layer,
      JsonNode snapshotPayload,
      JsonNode currentPayload,
      StitchConfigsProvider.ComparePayload livePayload) {}
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.configs;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.security.MessageDigest;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.Base64;
