import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.CanonicalIds;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfigLayer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionSchema;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

/** Config schema provider for Configs -> Schemas browse/edit flows. */
public final class StitchConfigsSchemasProvider {
  private static final Pattern CONFIG_ID_PATTERN = Pattern.compile("[a-zA-Z0-9_-]+");
  private static final String CONFIG_SCHEMA_FORMAT = "FABRIC_SCHEMA_CONFIG";
  private static final String STITCH_ACTOR = "service:stitch";

  private final SessionImpl session;
  private final StitchConfigsProvider configsProvider;

  public StitchConfigsSchemasProvider(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext, StitchConfigsProvider configsProvider) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    this.configsProvider = Objects.requireNonNull(configsProvider, "configsProvider");
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(current instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    this.session = resolved;
  }

  public List<String> listGroups() {
    return configsProvider.listGroups();
  }

  public List<String> listConfigNames(String group) {
    return configsProvider.listConfigNames(group);
  }

  public SchemaContext loadSchemaForConfig(String group, String configName) {
    String requiredGroup = requireValue(group, "group");
    String requiredConfigName = requireValue(configName, "configName");
    DiscoveryCache cache = requireCache();

    String chosenSchemaKey = null;
    String chosenLayerId = null;

    for (DefinitionConfigLayer layer : cache.list(DefinitionConfigLayer.class, requiredGroup)) {
      LayerIdentity identity = layerIdentity(layer, requiredGroup);
      String schemaKey = trimToNull(layer == null ? null : layer.schemaKey());
      if (!isPlainSchemaKey(schemaKey)) {
        continue;
      }
      if (!requiredConfigName.equals(identity.configName()) || identity.layerId() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (chosenSchemaKey == null || "base".equalsIgnoreCase(identity.layerId())) {
        chosenSchemaKey = schemaKey;
        chosenLayerId = identity.layerId();
      }
    }
    if (chosenSchemaKey == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "No schema key found for " + requiredGroup + "/" + requiredConfigName);
    }

    Definition definition = cache.get(DefinitionType.SCHEMA, requiredGroup, chosenSchemaKey);
    if (!(definition instanceof DefinitionSchema schema) || !isConfigSchema(schema)) {
      return new SchemaContext(
          requiredGroup,
          requiredConfigName,
          chosenLayerId,
          chosenSchemaKey,
          false,
          DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode());
    }
    return new SchemaContext(
        requiredGroup,
        requiredConfigName,
        chosenLayerId,
        chosenSchemaKey,
        true,
        parseJson(schema.schema()));
  }

  public List<String> listSchemaKeys(String group) {
    String requiredGroup = requireValue(group, "group");
    DiscoveryCache cache = requireCache();
    LinkedHashSet<String> keys = new LinkedHashSet<>();

    for (DefinitionSchema schema : cache.list(DefinitionSchema.class, requiredGroup)) {
      if (!isConfigSchema(schema)) {
        continue;
      }
      addPlainKey(keys, schema == null || schema.envelope() == null ? null : schema.envelope().name());
    }
    for (DefinitionConfigLayer layer : cache.list(DefinitionConfigLayer.class, requiredGroup)) {
      addPlainKey(keys, layer == null ? null : layer.schemaKey());
    }
    return keys.stream().sorted(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER).toList();
  }

  public void saveSchema(String group, String schemaKey, JsonNode schemaDocument) {
    String requiredGroup = requireValue(group, "group");
    String requiredSchemaKey = requirePlainSchemaKey(requireValue(schemaKey, "schemaKey"), "schemaKey");
    JsonNode requiredDocument = requireObject(schemaDocument, "schemaDocument");
    DiscoveryCache cache = requireCache();

    Definition definition = cache.get(DefinitionType.SCHEMA, requiredGroup, requiredSchemaKey);
    if (!(definition instanceof DefinitionSchema existing) || !isConfigSchema(existing)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Schema not found: " + requiredGroup + "/" + requiredSchemaKey);
    }

    String nowUtc = Instant.now().toString();
    String schemaText = stringify(requiredDocument);
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = existing.envelope();
    DefinitionEnvelope rewrittenEnvelope =
        new DefinitionEnvelope(
            requiredGroup,
            DefinitionType.SCHEMA,
            requiredSchemaKey,
            envelope == null ? null : envelope.uuid(),
            envelope == null ? Boolean.TRUE : envelope.enabled(),
            envelope == null ? "ACTIVE" : envelope.lifecycleStatus(),
            envelope == null ? null : envelope.createdTimeUtc(),
            envelope == null ? null : envelope.createdBy(),
            nowUtc,
            Strings.firstNonBlank(
                trimToNull(envelope == null ? null : envelope.updatedBy()),
                trimToNull(envelope == null ? null : envelope.createdBy()),
                STITCH_ACTOR));

    DefinitionSchema rewritten =
        new DefinitionSchema(
            rewrittenEnvelope,
            existing.versionSemantic(),
            existing.versionNum(),
            existing.artifactType(),
            existing.format(),
            schemaText,
            existing.status(),
            existing.compatibility(),
            existing.refs(),
            existing.tags(),
            sha256Base64(schemaText),
            existing.createdTimeUtc(),
            existing.schemaUsage(),
            existing.schemaType(),
            existing.doc(),
            existing.usageGroup(),
            existing.semantic());
    cache.upsert(rewritten);
  }

  public ConfigCreateResult createConfig(
      String group, String configName, SchemaAssignmentMode mode, String sourceSchemaKey) {
    String requiredGroup = requireValue(group, "group");
    String requiredConfigName = requireConfigId(requireValue(configName, "configName"), "configName");
    SchemaAssignmentMode selectedMode = mode == null ? SchemaAssignmentMode.NEW_BLANK : mode;
    String normalizedSource = trimToNull(sourceSchemaKey);

    if ((selectedMode == SchemaAssignmentMode.REUSE_EXISTING
            || selectedMode == SchemaAssignmentMode.CLONE_EXISTING)
        && normalizedSource == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("sourceSchemaKey is required for mode " + selectedMode);
    }
    if (normalizedSource != null) {
      requirePlainSchemaKey(normalizedSource, "sourceSchemaKey");
    }

    DiscoveryCache cache = requireCache();
    ensureConfigMissing(cache, requiredGroup, requiredConfigName);

    String nowUtc = Instant.now().toString();
    String schemaKey = switch (selectedMode) {
      case NEW_BLANK -> {
        String key = defaultSchemaKey(requiredConfigName);
        ensureSchemaMissing(cache, requiredGroup, key);
        cache.upsert(newSchemaDefinition(requiredGroup, key, nowUtc, null));
        yield key;
      }
      case REUSE_EXISTING -> {
        ensureSchemaPresent(cache, requiredGroup, normalizedSource);
        yield normalizedSource;
      }
      case CLONE_EXISTING -> {
        String key = defaultSchemaKey(requiredConfigName);
        ensureSchemaMissing(cache, requiredGroup, key);
        DefinitionSchema source = ensureSchemaPresent(cache, requiredGroup, normalizedSource);
        cache.upsert(newSchemaDefinition(requiredGroup, key, nowUtc, source));
        yield key;
      }
    };

    cache.upsert(buildBaseConfigLayer(requiredGroup, requiredConfigName, schemaKey, nowUtc));
    return new ConfigCreateResult(requiredConfigName, schemaKey);
  }

  private static DefinitionSchema newSchemaDefinition(
      String group, String schemaKey, String nowUtc, DefinitionSchema source) {
    JsonNode schemaDoc =
        source == null ? blankSchemaDoc() : parseJson(source.schema());
    String schemaText = stringify(schemaDoc);
    return new DefinitionSchema(
        new DefinitionEnvelope(
            group,
            DefinitionType.SCHEMA,
            schemaKey,
            null,
            true,
            "ACTIVE",
            nowUtc,
            STITCH_ACTOR,
            nowUtc,
            STITCH_ACTOR),
        source == null
            ? "1.0.0"
            : Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(source.versionSemantic()), "1.0.0"),
        source == null || source.versionNum() == null ? 1 : source.versionNum(),
        source == null
            ? "config"
            : Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(source.artifactType()), "config"),
        source == null
            ? CONFIG_SCHEMA_FORMAT
            : Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(source.format()), CONFIG_SCHEMA_FORMAT),
        schemaText,
        source == null
            ? "ACTIVE"
            : Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(source.status()), "ACTIVE"),
        source == null || source.compatibility() == null
            ? DefinitionSchema.Compatibility.NONE
            : source.compatibility(),
        source == null ? null : source.refs(),
        source == null ? null : source.tags(),
        sha256Base64(schemaText),
        nowUtc,
        source == null || source.schemaUsage() == null
            ? DefinitionSchema.SchemaUsage.SERVICE
            : source.schemaUsage(),
        source == null || source.schemaType() == null
            ? DefinitionSchema.SchemaType.CONFIG
            : source.schemaType(),
        source == null ? null : source.doc(),
        source == null ? null : source.usageGroup(),
        source == null ? null : source.semantic());
  }

  private static DefinitionConfigLayer buildBaseConfigLayer(
      String group, String configName, String schemaKey, String nowUtc) {
    String layerId = "base";
    String definitionName = "config__" + configName + "__" + layerId;
    return new DefinitionConfigLayer(
        new DefinitionEnvelope(
            group,
            DefinitionType.CONFIG_LAYER,
            definitionName,
            null,
            true,
            "ACTIVE",
            nowUtc,
            STITCH_ACTOR,
            nowUtc,
            STITCH_ACTOR),
        "config:" + group + "/" + configName + "/" + layerId,
        null,
        "BASE",
        "config",
        schemaKey,
        configName,
        DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode(),
        List.of(),
        List.of(),
        configName,
        configName);
  }

  private static void ensureConfigMissing(DiscoveryCache cache, String group, String configName) {
    for (DefinitionConfigLayer layer : cache.list(DefinitionConfigLayer.class, group)) {
      LayerIdentity identity = layerIdentity(layer, group);
      if (configName.equals(identity.configName())) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Config already exists: " + configName);
      }
    }
  }

  private static void ensureSchemaMissing(DiscoveryCache cache, String group, String schemaKey) {
    if (cache.get(DefinitionType.SCHEMA, group, schemaKey) != null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Schema already exists for group='" + group + "': " + schemaKey);
    }
  }

  private static DefinitionSchema ensureSchemaPresent(
      DiscoveryCache cache, String group, String schemaKey) {
    Definition definition = cache.get(DefinitionType.SCHEMA, group, schemaKey);
    if (!(definition instanceof DefinitionSchema schema)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Schema not found for group='" + group + "': " + schemaKey);
    }
    if (!isConfigSchema(schema)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Schema is not config-compatible: " + schemaKey);
    }
    return schema;
  }

  private static JsonNode blankSchemaDoc() {
    ObjectNode node = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    node.putArray("groups");
    node.putArray("structs");
    node.putArray("fields");
    return node;
  }

  private static JsonNode parseJson(String value) {
    String normalized = trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    }
    try {
      JsonNode parsed = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().readTree(normalized);
      return parsed == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : parsed.deepCopy();
    } catch (Exception error) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Invalid schema JSON: " + error.getMessage(), error);
    }
  }

  private static String stringify(JsonNode value) {
    try {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().writeValueAsString(value == null ? blankSchemaDoc() : value);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Unable to serialize schema JSON", error);
    }
  }

  private static JsonNode requireObject(JsonNode value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || !value.isObject()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(fieldName + " must be a JSON object");
    }
    return value.deepCopy();
  }

  private static void addPlainKey(LinkedHashSet<String> keys, String candidate) {
    String value = trimToNull(candidate);
    if (isPlainSchemaKey(value)) {
      keys.add(value);
    }
  }

  private static String requireValue(String value, String fieldName) {
    String normalized = trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static String requireConfigId(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (!CONFIG_ID_PATTERN.matcher(value).matches()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          fieldName + " must contain only letters, numbers, '_' or '-'");
    }
    return value;
  }

  private static String requirePlainSchemaKey(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (!isPlainSchemaKey(value)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(fieldName + " must be a plain schema name");
    }
    return value;
  }

  private static boolean isPlainSchemaKey(String value) {
    String normalized = trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return false;
    }
    for (int i = 0; i < normalized.length(); i++) {
      char ch = normalized.charAt(i);
      if (ch == ':' || ch == '/' || ch == '@' || Character.isWhitespace(ch)) {
        return false;
      }
    }
    return true;
  }

  private static boolean isConfigSchema(DefinitionSchema schema) {
    if (schema == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return schema.schemaType() == DefinitionSchema.SchemaType.CONFIG
        || CONFIG_SCHEMA_FORMAT.equals(trimToNull(schema.format()));
  }

  private static LayerIdentity layerIdentity(DefinitionConfigLayer layer, String fallbackGroup) {
    if (layer == null) {
      return new LayerIdentity(null, null, null);
    }
    String group = trimToNull(layer.envelope() == null ? null : layer.envelope().group());
    String configName = trimToNull(layer.configId());
    String layerId = trimToNull(layer.effectiveConfigId());
    String resourceId = trimToNull(layer.resourceId());
    if (resourceId != null && resourceId.startsWith("config:")) {
      try {
        CanonicalIds.ParsedId parsed = CanonicalIds.parse(resourceId);
        if ("config".equals(parsed.type())) {
          configName = Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(parsed.namespace()), configName);
          layerId = Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(parsed.name()), layerId);
          group = Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(parsed.group()), group);
        }
      } catch (Exception ignored) {
      }
    }
    return new LayerIdentity(Strings.firstNonBlank(group, trimToNull(fallbackGroup)), configName, layerId);
  }

  private static String defaultSchemaKey(String configName) {
    return "config_" + configName;
  }

  private static String sha256Base64(String payload) {
    try {
      MessageDigest digest = MessageDigest.getInstance("SHA-256");
      byte[] bytes = digest.digest((payload == null ? "" : payload).getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
      return Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(bytes);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Unable to compute schema hash", error);
    }
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    return Strings.trimToNull(value);
  }

  private DiscoveryCache requireCache() {
    DiscoveryCache cache = session.internal().discoveryCache();
    if (cache == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DiscoveryCache is not available");
    }
    return cache;
  }

  public record SchemaContext(
      String group,
      String configName,
      String layerId,
      String schemaKey,
      boolean present,
      JsonNode schemaDocument) {
    public SchemaContext {
      group = trimToNull(group);
      configName = trimToNull(configName);
      layerId = trimToNull(layerId);
      schemaKey = trimToNull(schemaKey);
      schemaDocument =
          schemaDocument == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : schemaDocument.deepCopy();
    }
  }

  public enum SchemaAssignmentMode {
    NEW_BLANK,
    REUSE_EXISTING,
    CLONE_EXISTING
  }

  public record ConfigCreateResult(String configId, String schemaKey) {}

  private record LayerIdentity(String group, String configName, String layerId) {}
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/configs/StitchConfigsScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.configs;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.checkbox.Checkbox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.ComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.Icon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification.Position;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextField;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchActionStyles;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchEmptyState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchFiltersBar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchResultsToolbar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchTabbedDetailsPanel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialogs;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchHierarchicalBrowserScreen;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchTreeNav;

public class StitchConfigsScreen extends StitchHierarchicalBrowserScreen {
  private final StitchEmptyState noConfigSelected =
      new StitchEmptyState(
          "No config selected", "Choose Group and Name to load config layers.");
  private final StitchEmptyState noLayerSelected =
      new StitchEmptyState("No layer selected", "Select a config layer from the tree.");
  private final StitchEmptyState noLayerDetails =
      new StitchEmptyState("No layer details available", "Layer details could not be loaded.");
  private final StitchEmptyState noLayersFound =
      new StitchEmptyState("No layers found", "No config layers were found for the selected config name.");

  private final StitchConfigsProvider provider;
  private final boolean editable;
  private final StitchConfigSelectionBar selectionBar;
  private final StitchConfigLayerInspector layerInspector;
  private final Checkbox inheritedValuesHeaderToggle = new Checkbox();
  private final Button compareModeToggle;
  private final StitchFiltersBar filtersBar = new StitchFiltersBar();
  private final HorizontalLayout utilityActionsRow = new HorizontalLayout();
  private Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> layersByPath = Map.of();
  private StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView currentLayerView = StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView.empty();
  private boolean compareModeEnabled;
  private boolean showInheritedValues;
  private boolean lineageVisible;
  private final Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions> submissionOptionsByLayerPath =
      new LinkedHashMap<>();

  protected StitchConfigsScreen(
      StitchConfigsScreenConfig config, StitchConfigsProvider provider, boolean editable) {
    super(
        Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config").pageTitle(),
        config.pageSubtitle() == null ? "" : config.pageSubtitle(),
        "Refresh configs",
        "Refresh configs",
        "Declared JSON",
        editable ? "Editable config layer JSON" : "Config layer JSON");
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.editable = editable;
    this.selectionBar =
        new StitchConfigSelectionBar(provider::listGroups, provider::listConfigNames)
            .setSelectionRequestHandler(this::handleSelectionRequest)
            .setSelectionChangeListener(this::onSelectionChanged)
            .setFlatTopBarMode(true);
    this.selectionBar.addClassName("stitch-config-selection-bar--inline");
    this.selectionBar.setWidth(null);
    this.layerInspector =
        new StitchConfigLayerInspector(
            inspectorPanel(), editable, editorMode()::isEditMode, editorMode()::markDirty);
    inheritedValuesHeaderToggle.addClassName("stitch-configs-inherited-toggle");
    inheritedValuesHeaderToggle.addClassName("stitch-boolean-toggle");
    inheritedValuesHeaderToggle.setValue(showInheritedValues);
    inheritedValuesHeaderToggle.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Show inherited config values");
    inheritedValuesHeaderToggle.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Show inherited values");
    inheritedValuesHeaderToggle.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!event.isFromClient()) {
            return;
          }
          onInheritedVisibilityChanged(Boolean.TRUE.equals(event.getValue()));
        });
    this.compareModeToggle =
        utilityIconButton(
            "TABLE",
            "Compare Mode",
            VaadinIcon.TABLE,
            this::toggleCompareMode);

    utilityActionsRow.setPadding(false);
    utilityActionsRow.setSpacing(true);
    utilityActionsRow.setWidth(null);
    utilityActionsRow.setClassName("stitch-configs-utility-row");
    utilityActionsRow.add(compareModeToggle);

    actions().removeAll();
    Button refreshAction = new Button("REFRESH", event -> refreshRequested());
    refreshAction.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchResultsToolbar.stylePrimaryAction(refreshAction);
    refreshAction.addClassName("stitch-refresh-action");
    refreshAction.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Refresh configs");
    refreshAction.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Refresh configs");
    filtersBar.withGroupSelector(selectionBar).withRightAction(refreshAction);
    addToBody(filtersBar);

    initBrowser(
        new BrowserConfig(
            "Config Layers",
            "CONFIG VALUES",
            noConfigSelected,
            noConfigSelected,
            "Search layers",
            "Search config layers",
            this::nodeIcon,
            this::nodeDecorator,
            utilityActionsRow),
        new EditConfig(
            editable ? editorMode()::hasUnsavedChanges : () -> false,
            this::saveSelectedLayer,
            this::discardSelectedLayer,
            node -> false,
            this::editModeActions),
        this::detailSectionTitle,
        this::buildDetailContent,
        this::readOnlyActions,
        nodeId -> updateToolbarState());
    browserShell().layout().addClassName("stitch-tree-layout--configs");
    browserShell().treeNav().addClassName("stitch-tree-nav--configs-compact");
    browserShell()
        .treeNav()
        .withCustomActionsTrailing(true)
        .withNodeIconClickBehavior(StitchTreeNav.NodeIconClickBehavior.TOGGLE_EXPAND_COLLAPSE)
        .setNodeLabelClassNameProvider(this::nodeLabelClassName);
    browserShell().layout().split().setSplitterPosition(22);
    browserShell().setHeight(null);
    body().setFlexGrow(1, browserShell());
    browserShell().onAutoThresholdReached(this::onCompareThresholdReached);
    browserShell().onCheckedItemsChanged(ignored -> updateCompareToggleStateText());
    applyCompareMode(false);
    updateToolbarState();
    selectionBar.reload(false);
  }

  @Override
  protected void refreshRequested() {
    String selectedGroup = Strings.trimToNull(selectionBar.selectedGroup());
    String selectedName = Strings.trimToNull(selectionBar.selectedName());
    if (selectedGroup != null && selectedName != null) {
      loadSelectedConfig(selectedGroup, selectedName, true, true);
      updateToolbarState();
      return;
    }
    selectionBar.reload(true);
  }

  private void handleSelectionRequest(
      StitchConfigSelectionBar.Selection current,
      StitchConfigSelectionBar.Selection requested,
      Runnable apply,
      Runnable revert) {
    if (!(editable && editorMode().hasUnsavedChanges())) {
      apply.run();
      return;
    }
    dirtyStateSupport()
        .guard(
            () -> {
              if (saveSelectedLayer()) {
                apply.run();
                return true;
              }
              return false;
            },
            () -> {
              discardSelectedLayer();
              apply.run();
            },
            revert);
  }

  private void onSelectionChanged(StitchConfigSelectionBar.SelectionChange selection) {
    if (selection.group() == null || selection.name() == null) {
      StitchConfigSelectionContext.remember(selection.group(), selection.name());
      clearTreeForMissingName();
      updateToolbarState();
      return;
    }
    StitchConfigSelectionContext.remember(selection.group(), selection.name());
    loadSelectedConfig(selection.group(), selection.name(), selection.preserveTreeSelection(), false);
    updateToolbarState();
  }

  private void loadSelectedConfig(
      String group, String name, boolean preserveSelection, boolean silentNotification) {
    String desiredSelection = preserveSelection ? browserShell().selectedNodeId() : null;
    try {
      StitchConfigsProvider.TreeModel treeModel = provider.loadLayers(group, name);
      layersByPath = Map.copyOf(treeModel.layersByPath());
      submissionOptionsByLayerPath.clear();
      layerInspector.clearValidationErrors();
      editorMode().clear();
      applyTree(
          treeModel.roots(),
          treeModel.byId(),
          treeModel.roots().isEmpty() ? noLayersFound : noLayerSelected,
          noLayerDetails,
          desiredSelection,
          this::isLayerNode);
      currentLayerView = StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView.empty();
      browserShell().clearCheckedItems();
      applyCompareMode(compareModeEnabled);
      updateToolbarState();
      if (!silentNotification) {
        Notification.show(
            "Loaded " + layersByPath.size() + " layer(s) for " + name,
            1400,
            Position.BOTTOM_START);
      }
    } catch (Exception error) {
      layersByPath = Map.of();
      currentLayerView = StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView.empty();
      layerInspector.clearValidationErrors();
      editorMode().clear();
      clearTree(noConfigSelected, noConfigSelected);
      browserShell().clearCheckedItems();
      applyCompareMode(false);
      updateToolbarState();
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to load config layers", rootMessage(error));
    }
  }

  private void clearTreeForMissingName() {
    layersByPath = Map.of();
    currentLayerView = StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView.empty();
    layerInspector.clearValidationErrors();
    submissionOptionsByLayerPath.clear();
    editorMode().clear();
    clearTree(noConfigSelected, noConfigSelected);
    browserShell().clearCheckedItems();
    applyCompareMode(false);
    updateToolbarState();
  }

  private String detailSectionTitle(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    if (node == null) {
      return "Layer path";
    }
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record = layerFor(node);
    String path =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            record == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(record.path()),
            Strings.trimToNull(node.fullKey()));
    return formatPathForDisplay(path);
  }

  private Component buildDetailContent(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node, boolean editMode) {
    updateToolbarState();
    if (node == null) {
      currentLayerView = StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView.empty();
      return noLayerSelected;
    }
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record = layerFor(node);
    if (record == null) {
      currentLayerView = StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView.empty();
      return noLayerDetails;
    }
    currentLayerView = provider.loadLayerView(record, layersByPath, Instant.now());
    Component values =
        layerInspector.render(
        currentLayerView,
        editMode,
        false,
        showInheritedValues,
        resolvePreview(node, record),
        layersByPath);
    if (!lineageVisible) {
      return values;
    }
    Component lineage = layerInspector.renderLineage(currentLayerView, layersByPath, this::selectLayerFromLineage);
    VerticalLayout content = new VerticalLayout(lineage, values);
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(true);
    content.setWidthFull();
    content.addClassName("stitch-config-values-with-lineage");
    return content;
  }

  private List<Component> readOnlyActions(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    return List.of();
  }

  private boolean saveSelectedLayer() {
    if (!editable) {
      return true;
    }
    StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node = selectedNode();
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record = layerFor(node);
    if (record == null) {
      return false;
    }
    try {
      JsonNode declared = layerInspector.parseAndValidateEditorDeclaredJson(currentLayerView);
      StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions submissionOptions = submissionOptionsFor(record);
      StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionResult result =
          provider.submitDeclared(
              record.group(), record.configName(), record.layerId(), declared, submissionOptions);
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord saved = result.savedLayer();
      String key = node.fullKey();
      LinkedHashMap<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> updated = new LinkedHashMap<>(layersByPath);
      updated.put(key, saved.withPath(key));
      layersByPath = Map.copyOf(updated);
      setSubmissionOptions(saved, StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions.immediate());
      layerInspector.setPreviewValue(layerInspector.prettyJson(saved.declared()));
      loadSelectedConfig(record.group(), record.configName(), true, true);
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord refreshed = layerFor(selectedNode());
      if (refreshed != null) {
        setSubmissionOptions(refreshed, StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions.immediate());
      }
      String actionLabel =
          result.options() != null && result.options().approvalRequired()
              ? "Submitted "
              : "Updated ";
      Notification.show(
          actionLabel
              + Strings.firstNonBlank(record.layerId(), "layer")
              + " ("
              + submissionSummary(result.options())
              + ")",
          1600,
          Position.BOTTOM_START);
      return true;
    } catch (Exception error) {
      rerenderDetails();
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to save config layer", rootMessage(error));
      return false;
    }
  }

  private void discardSelectedLayer() {
    if (!editable) {
      return;
    }
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record = layerFor(selectedNode());
    if (record == null) {
      return;
    }
    layerInspector.clearValidationErrors();
    layerInspector.setPreviewValue(layerInspector.prettyJson(record.declared()));
    Notification.show("Discarded unsaved changes", 1400, Position.BOTTOM_START);
  }

  private String resolvePreview(
      StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record) {
    if (editable
        && editorMode().isEditMode()
        && editorMode().hasUnsavedChanges()
        && isCurrentSelection(node)) {
      return layerInspector.previewValue();
    }
    return layerInspector.prettyJson(record.declared());
  }

  private boolean isCurrentSelection(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    return node != null && Objects.equals(node.id(), browserShell().selectedNodeId());
  }

  private StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord layerFor(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    if (node == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String key = Strings.trimToNull(node.fullKey());
    if (key == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return layersByPath.get(key);
  }

  private boolean isLayerNode(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    return layerFor(node) != null;
  }

  private Component nodeIcon(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    VaadinIcon iconType =
        node == null || (node.children() != null && !node.children().isEmpty())
            ? VaadinIcon.FOLDER_OPEN_O
            : VaadinIcon.FILE_CODE;
    Icon icon = iconType.create();
    icon.getElement().setAttribute("aria-hidden", "true");
    return icon;
  }

  private Component nodeDecorator(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record = layerFor(node);
    if (record == null) {
      return null;
    }
    HorizontalLayout indicators = new HorizontalLayout();
    indicators.setPadding(false);
    indicators.setSpacing(true);
    indicators.addClassName("stitch-config-tree-indicators");

    if (record.hasPendingChange()) {
      indicators.add(indicator("Pending change", "stitch-config-tree-indicator--pending"));
    } else if (Strings.trimToNull(record.firstFutureEffectiveAtUtc()) != null) {
      indicators.add(indicator("Scheduled change", "stitch-config-tree-indicator--scheduled"));
    }

    if (indicators.getComponentCount() == 0) {
      return null;
    }
    return indicators;
  }

  private void onInheritedVisibilityChanged(boolean showInherited) {
    if (showInheritedValues == showInherited) {
      return;
    }
    showInheritedValues = showInherited;
    rerenderDetails();
  }

  private void toggleLineageInline() {
    lineageVisible = !lineageVisible;
    rerenderDetails();
    updateToolbarState();
  }

  private void selectLayerFromLineage(String nodeId) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(nodeId);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return;
    }
    browserShell().applySelectionById(normalized);
    updateToolbarState();
  }

  private List<Component> editModeActions(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    if (!editable || !editorMode().isEditMode()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record = layerFor(node);
    if (record == null) {
      return List.of();
    }

    Button manageLayers = new Button("MANAGE LAYERS", event -> openManageLayersRequested(record));
    manageLayers.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchActionStyles.applySecondary(manageLayers);
    manageLayers.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Manage config layers");

    Button submit = new Button("SUBMIT", event -> openSubmissionDialog(record));
    submit.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchActionStyles.applyPrimary(submit);
    submit.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Submit selected config layer changes");

    Button cancel = new Button("CANCEL", event -> cancelEditModeRequested());
    cancel.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchActionStyles.applyNeutral(cancel);
    cancel.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Cancel editing");
    return List.of(manageLayers, submit, cancel);
  }

  private void openManageLayersRequested(StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord selectedLayer) {
    if (selectedLayer == null) {
      return;
    }
    if (!editorMode().hasUnsavedChanges()) {
      openManageLayersDialog(selectedLayer);
      return;
    }
    dirtyStateSupport()
        .guard(
            () -> {
              if (saveSelectedLayer()) {
                openManageLayersDialog(selectedLayer);
                return true;
              }
              return false;
            },
            () -> {
              discardSelectedLayer();
              openManageLayersDialog(selectedLayer);
            },
            () -> {});
  }

  private void openManageLayersDialog(StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord selectedLayer) {
    String group = Strings.trimToNull(selectedLayer.group());
    String configName = Strings.trimToNull(selectedLayer.configName());
    if (group == null || configName == null) {
      Notification.show("Select Group and Name first.", 1400, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      return;
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> byLayerId = indexLayersById(layersByPath);
    if (byLayerId.isEmpty()) {
      Notification.show("No layers available to manage.", 1400, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      return;
    }

    String defaultLayerId = Strings.firstNonBlank(selectedLayer.layerId(), firstLayerId(byLayerId));
    ManageLayersDialog dialog =
        new ManageLayersDialog("MANAGE LAYERS - " + group + " / " + configName);
    dialog.setWidth("860px");
    dialog.setMaxWidth("96vw");
    dialog.setTop("8vh");

    StitchTabbedDetailsPanel tabs = new StitchTabbedDetailsPanel();
    tabs.addTab(
            "create",
            "CREATE",
            buildCreateLayerTab(dialog, group, configName, byLayerId, defaultLayerId))
        .addTab("move", "MOVE", buildMoveLayerTab(dialog, group, configName, byLayerId, defaultLayerId))
        .addTab(
            "delete",
            "DELETE",
            buildDeleteLayerTab(dialog, group, configName, byLayerId, defaultLayerId))
        .selectTab("create");

    dialog.addToBody(tabs);
    dialog.addSecondaryAction("Close", dialog::close);
    dialog.open();
  }

  private Component buildCreateLayerTab(
      StitchDialog dialog,
      String group,
      String configName,
      Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> byLayerId,
      String defaultLayerId) {
    List<String> layerIds = sortedLayerIds(byLayerId);
    ComboBox<String> parentLayer = layerCombo("Add Under Layer", byLayerId, layerIds);
    parentLayer.setValue(
        layerIds.contains(defaultLayerId)
            ? defaultLayerId
            : (layerIds.isEmpty() ? null : layerIds.get(0)));

    TextField newLayerId = new TextField("New Layer ID");
    newLayerId.setWidthFull();
    newLayerId.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "New layer id");

    TextField shortName = new TextField("Short Name (optional)");
    shortName.setWidthFull();
    shortName.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Optional short name");

    Div hint = new Div();
    hint.setText("New layer will be created as a child of this layer.");
    hint.addClassName("stitch-config-manage-layers-hint");

    Button create = new Button("CREATE LAYER");
    create.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchActionStyles.applyPrimary(create);
    create.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Create layer");
    create.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          String layerId = Strings.trimToNull(newLayerId.getValue());
          if (layerId == null) {
            Notification.show("New Layer ID is required.", 1600, Position.BOTTOM_START);
            return;
          }
          try {
            StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord created =
                provider.createLayer(
                    group,
                    configName,
                    layerId,
                    Strings.trimToNull(parentLayer.getValue()),
                    Strings.trimToNull(shortName.getValue()));
            dialog.close();
            refreshAfterLayerMutation(group, configName, created.layerId(), true);
            Notification.show(
                "Created layer " + Strings.firstNonBlank(created.layerId(), layerId),
                1600,
                Position.BOTTOM_START);
          } catch (Exception error) {
            StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to create layer", rootMessage(error));
          }
        });

    HorizontalLayout actions = new HorizontalLayout(create);
    actions.setPadding(false);
    actions.setSpacing(true);
    actions.setWidthFull();
    actions.setJustifyContentMode(
        com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.JustifyContentMode.END);
    actions.addClassName("stitch-config-manage-layers-actions");

    VerticalLayout content =
        manageLayersTabLayout(newLayerId, parentLayer, shortName, hint, actions);
    content.addClassName("stitch-config-manage-layers-tab");
    return content;
  }

  private Component buildMoveLayerTab(
      StitchDialog dialog,
      String group,
      String configName,
      Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> byLayerId,
      String defaultLayerId) {
    List<String> layerIds = sortedLayerIds(byLayerId);
    ComboBox<String> layerToMove = layerCombo("Layer To Move", byLayerId, layerIds);
    layerToMove.setValue(
        layerIds.contains(defaultLayerId)
            ? defaultLayerId
            : (layerIds.isEmpty() ? null : layerIds.get(0)));

    ComboBox<String> newParentLayer = layerCombo("New Parent Layer", byLayerId, List.of());

    Div hint = new Div();
    hint.setText("Moving a layer changes its position in the hierarchy.");
    hint.addClassName("stitch-config-manage-layers-hint");

    Button move = new Button("MOVE LAYER");
    move.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchActionStyles.applyPrimary(move);
    move.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Move layer");
    move.setEnabled(false);

    Runnable refreshParentCandidates =
        () -> {
          String movingLayerId = Strings.trimToNull(layerToMove.getValue());
          List<String> candidates = moveParentCandidates(byLayerId, movingLayerId);
          newParentLayer.setItems(candidates);
          String currentParent =
              movingLayerId == null
                  ? null
                  : Strings.trimToNull(
                      byLayerId.containsKey(movingLayerId)
                          ? byLayerId.get(movingLayerId).parentLayerId()
                          : null);
          if (currentParent != null && candidates.contains(currentParent)) {
            newParentLayer.setValue(currentParent);
          } else if (!candidates.isEmpty()) {
            newParentLayer.setValue(candidates.get(0));
          } else {
            newParentLayer.clear();
          }
          boolean movable = movingLayerId != null && !"base".equalsIgnoreCase(movingLayerId);
          move.setEnabled(movable && Strings.trimToNull(newParentLayer.getValue()) != null);
        };

    layerToMove.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!event.isFromClient()) {
            return;
          }
          refreshParentCandidates.run();
        });
    newParentLayer.addValueChangeListener(
        event ->
            move.setEnabled(
                Strings.trimToNull(layerToMove.getValue()) != null
                    && !"base".equalsIgnoreCase(layerToMove.getValue())
                    && Strings.trimToNull(newParentLayer.getValue()) != null));
    refreshParentCandidates.run();

    move.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          String movingLayerId = Strings.trimToNull(layerToMove.getValue());
          String newParentLayerId = Strings.trimToNull(newParentLayer.getValue());
          if (movingLayerId == null || newParentLayerId == null) {
            Notification.show("Select both layer and new parent.", 1600, Position.BOTTOM_START);
            return;
          }
          try {
            StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord moved =
                provider.moveLayer(group, configName, movingLayerId, newParentLayerId);
            dialog.close();
            refreshAfterLayerMutation(group, configName, moved.layerId(), true);
            Notification.show(
                "Moved layer " + Strings.firstNonBlank(moved.layerId(), movingLayerId),
                1600,
                Position.BOTTOM_START);
          } catch (Exception error) {
            StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to move layer", rootMessage(error));
          }
        });

    HorizontalLayout actions = new HorizontalLayout(move);
    actions.setPadding(false);
    actions.setSpacing(true);
    actions.setWidthFull();
    actions.setJustifyContentMode(
        com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.JustifyContentMode.END);
    actions.addClassName("stitch-config-manage-layers-actions");

    return manageLayersTabLayout(layerToMove, newParentLayer, hint, actions);
  }

  private Component buildDeleteLayerTab(
      StitchDialog dialog,
      String group,
      String configName,
      Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> byLayerId,
      String defaultLayerId) {
    List<String> layerIds = sortedLayerIds(byLayerId);
    ComboBox<String> layerToDelete = layerCombo("Layer To Delete", byLayerId, layerIds);
    layerToDelete.setValue(
        layerIds.contains(defaultLayerId)
            ? defaultLayerId
            : (layerIds.isEmpty() ? null : layerIds.get(0)));

    Div summary = new Div();
    summary.addClassName("stitch-config-manage-layers-summary");

    Checkbox confirm = new Checkbox("I understand this removes the selected layer.");
    confirm.addClassName("stitch-config-manage-layers-confirm");
    confirm.setValue(false);

    Button delete = new Button("DELETE LAYER");
    delete.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchActionStyles.applyDanger(delete);
    delete.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Delete layer");
    delete.setEnabled(false);

    Runnable refreshDeleteState =
        () -> {
          String layerId = Strings.trimToNull(layerToDelete.getValue());
          StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord layer = layerId == null ? null : byLayerId.get(layerId);
          boolean deletable = layerId != null && !"base".equalsIgnoreCase(layerId);
          int childCount = directChildrenCount(byLayerId, layerId);
          String path =
              Strings.firstNonBlank(
                  layer == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(layer.path()),
                  layerId,
                  "-");
          StringBuilder text = new StringBuilder();
          text.append("Layer: ").append(formatPathForDisplay(path));
          text.append(" | Children: ").append(Math.max(0, childCount));
          if (!deletable) {
            text.append(" | Delete not allowed for base layer.");
          }
          summary.setText(text.toString());
          delete.setEnabled(deletable && Boolean.TRUE.equals(confirm.getValue()));
        };

    layerToDelete.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!event.isFromClient()) {
            return;
          }
          confirm.setValue(false);
          refreshDeleteState.run();
        });
    confirm.addValueChangeListener(event -> refreshDeleteState.run());
    refreshDeleteState.run();

    delete.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          String layerId = Strings.trimToNull(layerToDelete.getValue());
          if (layerId == null) {
            Notification.show("Select a layer to delete.", 1600, Position.BOTTOM_START);
            return;
          }
          StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord deleting = byLayerId.get(layerId);
          String fallbackLayerId =
              Strings.trimToNull(deleting == null ? null : deleting.parentLayerId());
          if (fallbackLayerId == null || Objects.equals(fallbackLayerId, layerId)) {
            fallbackLayerId = firstLayerId(byLayerId);
            if (Objects.equals(fallbackLayerId, layerId)) {
              fallbackLayerId = null;
            }
          }
          try {
            provider.deleteLayer(group, configName, layerId);
            dialog.close();
            refreshAfterLayerMutation(group, configName, fallbackLayerId, true);
            Notification.show(
                "Deleted layer " + layerId,
                1600,
                Position.BOTTOM_START);
          } catch (Exception error) {
            StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to delete layer", rootMessage(error));
          }
        });

    HorizontalLayout actions = new HorizontalLayout(delete);
    actions.setPadding(false);
    actions.setSpacing(true);
    actions.setWidthFull();
    actions.setJustifyContentMode(
        com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.JustifyContentMode.END);
    actions.addClassName("stitch-config-manage-layers-actions");

    return manageLayersTabLayout(layerToDelete, summary, confirm, actions);
  }

  private void refreshAfterLayerMutation(
      String group, String configName, String preferredLayerId, boolean keepEditMode) {
    loadSelectedConfig(group, configName, false, true);
    String targetPath = pathForLayerId(preferredLayerId);
    if (targetPath != null) {
      browserShell().applySelectionById(targetPath);
    }
    if (keepEditMode && editable) {
      StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode selected = selectedNode();
      if (selected != null && layerFor(selected) != null) {
        editorMode().enterEditMode();
      }
    }
    rerenderDetails();
    updateToolbarState();
  }

  private String pathForLayerId(String layerId) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(layerId);
    if (normalized == null || layersByPath.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    for (StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record : layersByPath.values()) {
      if (record == null || !Objects.equals(normalized, Strings.trimToNull(record.layerId()))) {
        continue;
      }
      return Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(record.path()), Strings.trimToNull(record.layerId()));
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static VerticalLayout manageLayersTabLayout(Component... content) {
    VerticalLayout layout = new VerticalLayout();
    layout.setPadding(false);
    layout.setSpacing(true);
    layout.setWidthFull();
    layout.addClassName("stitch-config-manage-layers");
    if (content != null) {
      layout.add(content);
    }
    return layout;
  }

  private static ComboBox<String> layerCombo(
      String label, Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> byLayerId, List<String> layerIds) {
    ComboBox<String> combo = new ComboBox<>(label);
    combo.setItems(layerIds == null ? List.of() : layerIds);
    combo.setItemLabelGenerator(
        layerId -> {
          StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record = byLayerId == null ? null : byLayerId.get(layerId);
          String path =
              Strings.firstNonBlank(
                  record == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(record.path()),
                  Strings.trimToNull(layerId),
                  "-");
          return formatPathForDisplay(path);
        });
    combo.setWidthFull();
    combo.setClearButtonVisible(false);
    combo.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", Strings.firstNonBlank(label, "Layer"));
    return combo;
  }

  private static LinkedHashMap<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> indexLayersById(
      Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> layersByPath) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> byLayerId = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (layersByPath == null || layersByPath.isEmpty()) {
      return byLayerId;
    }
    for (StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record : layersByPath.values()) {
      if (record == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String layerId = Strings.trimToNull(record.layerId());
      if (layerId == null || byLayerId.containsKey(layerId)) {
        continue;
      }
      byLayerId.put(layerId, record);
    }
    return byLayerId;
  }

  private static List<String> sortedLayerIds(Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> byLayerId) {
    if (byLayerId == null || byLayerId.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> ids = new ArrayList<>(byLayerId.keySet());
    ids.sort(
        (left, right) -> {
          String leftPath = layerSortPath(byLayerId, left);
          String rightPath = layerSortPath(byLayerId, right);
          int compared = String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER.compare(leftPath, rightPath);
          if (compared != 0) {
            return compared;
          }
          return String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER.compare(
              Strings.firstNonBlank(left, ""),
              Strings.firstNonBlank(right, ""));
        });
    return List.copyOf(ids);
  }

  private static String layerSortPath(
      Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> byLayerId, String layerId) {
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record = byLayerId == null ? null : byLayerId.get(layerId);
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(
        record == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(record.path()),
        Strings.trimToNull(layerId),
        "");
  }

  private static String firstLayerId(Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> byLayerId) {
    if (byLayerId == null || byLayerId.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    return sortedLayerIds(byLayerId).stream().findFirst().orElse(null);
  }

  private static List<String> moveParentCandidates(
      Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> byLayerId, String movingLayerId) {
    if (byLayerId == null || byLayerId.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    String moving = Strings.trimToNull(movingLayerId);
    if (moving == null) {
      return sortedLayerIds(byLayerId);
    }
    Set<String> blocked = descendantsInclusive(byLayerId, moving);
    List<String> parentIds = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String candidate : sortedLayerIds(byLayerId)) {
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(candidate);
      if (normalized == null || blocked.contains(normalized)) {
        continue;
      }
      parentIds.add(normalized);
    }
    return List.copyOf(parentIds);
  }

  private static Set<String> descendantsInclusive(
      Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> byLayerId, String rootLayerId) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> descendants = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    String root = Strings.trimToNull(rootLayerId);
    if (root == null || byLayerId == null || byLayerId.isEmpty() || !byLayerId.containsKey(root)) {
      return descendants;
    }
    descendants.add(root);
    boolean changed = true;
    while (changed) {
      changed = false;
      for (Map.Entry<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> entry : byLayerId.entrySet()) {
        String candidate = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
        String parent =
            Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue() == null ? null : entry.getValue().parentLayerId());
        if (candidate == null || parent == null || descendants.contains(candidate)) {
          continue;
        }
        if (descendants.contains(parent)) {
          descendants.add(candidate);
          changed = true;
        }
      }
    }
    return descendants;
  }

  private static int directChildrenCount(
      Map<String, StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> byLayerId, String parentLayerId) {
    String parent = Strings.trimToNull(parentLayerId);
    if (parent == null || byLayerId == null || byLayerId.isEmpty()) {
      return 0;
    }
    int count = 0;
    for (StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record : byLayerId.values()) {
      if (record == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (Objects.equals(parent, Strings.trimToNull(record.parentLayerId()))) {
        count++;
      }
    }
    return count;
  }

  private void cancelEditModeRequested() {
    if (!editorMode().hasUnsavedChanges()) {
      editorMode().clear();
      rerenderDetails();
      updateToolbarState();
      return;
    }
    dirtyStateSupport()
        .guard(
            () -> {
              if (saveSelectedLayer()) {
                editorMode().clear();
                rerenderDetails();
                updateToolbarState();
                return true;
              }
              return false;
            },
            () -> {
              discardSelectedLayer();
              editorMode().clear();
              rerenderDetails();
              updateToolbarState();
            },
            () -> {});
  }

  private static Button actionButton(String label, String ariaLabel, Runnable onClick) {
    Button button = new Button(label == null ? "" : label.trim());
    button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    button.addClassName("stitch-configs-header-action");
    if ("EDIT".equalsIgnoreCase(button.getText())) {
      StitchActionStyles.applyPrimary(button);
    } else {
      StitchActionStyles.applyByLabel(button, button.getText());
    }
    button.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", Strings.firstNonBlank(ariaLabel, button.getText()));
    if (onClick != null) {
      button.addClickListener(event -> onClick.run());
    }
    return button;
  }

  private Button utilityIconButton(
      String actionLabel, String tooltip, VaadinIcon fallback, Runnable onClick) {
    Button button = new Button();
    button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL, ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY);
    button.setIcon((fallback == null ? VaadinIcon.CIRCLE_THIN : fallback).create());
    button.addClassName("stitch-configs-utility-button");
    button.addClassName("stitch-tree-nav-button");
    button.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", Strings.firstNonBlank(tooltip, actionLabel));
    button.getElement().setAttribute("title", Strings.firstNonBlank(tooltip, actionLabel));
    if (onClick != null) {
      button.addClickListener(event -> onClick.run());
    }
    return button;
  }

  private void toggleCompareMode() {
    compareModeEnabled = !compareModeEnabled;
    applyCompareMode(compareModeEnabled);
    updateCompareToggleStateText();
    if (!compareModeEnabled) {
      browserShell().clearCheckedItems();
    }
  }

  private void applyCompareMode(boolean enabled) {
    browserShell().withCheckboxSelectionEnabled(enabled);
    if (!enabled) {
      browserShell().clearCheckedItems();
      return;
    }
    browserShell()
        .withCheckboxSelectionMode(StitchTreeNav.CheckboxSelectionMode.NODE_AND_LEAF)
        .withCheckboxAutoTriggerCount(2)
        .withCheckboxMaxCheckedCount(2);
  }

  private void onCompareThresholdReached(
      List<StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> checkedNodes) {
    if (checkedNodes == null || checkedNodes.size() != 2) {
      return;
    }
    List<StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord> selected = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node : checkedNodes) {
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record = layerFor(node);
      if (record != null) {
        selected.add(record);
      }
    }
    if (selected.size() != 2) {
      return;
    }
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord left = selected.get(0);
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord right = selected.get(1);
    new org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchJsonDiffDialog(
            "Compare Layers - " + compareContext(left),
            layerLabel(left),
            left.declared(),
            layerLabel(right),
            right.declared())
        .open();
    browserShell().clearCheckedItems();
  }

  private void openDagDialog(StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord selected) {
    if (layersByPath.isEmpty()) {
      Notification.show("Select Group and Name first.", 1400, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      return;
    }
    if (selected == null) {
      Notification.show("Select a layer first.", 1400, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      return;
    }
    String selectedLayerId = Strings.trimToNull(selected.layerId());
    new StitchConfigDagDialog(
            "Config DAG - " + Strings.firstNonBlank(selectedConfigName(), "Selection"),
            provider,
            layersByPath,
            selectedLayerId)
        .open();
  }

  private void openJsonModesDialog(StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord selected) {
    String group = selectedGroup();
    String name = selectedConfigName();
    if (group == null || name == null) {
      Notification.show("Select Group and Name first.", 1400, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      return;
    }
    if (selected == null) {
      Notification.show("Select a layer first.", 1400, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      return;
    }
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView layerView =
        provider.loadLayerView(selected, layersByPath, Instant.now());
    new StitchConfigJsonModesDialog(provider, group, name, selected, layerView, layersByPath).open();
  }

  private String selectedGroup() {
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord selected = layerFor(selectedNode());
    if (selected != null) {
      return selected.group();
    }
    if (!layersByPath.isEmpty()) {
      return layersByPath.values().stream()
          .map(StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord::group)
          .map(Strings::trimToNull)
          .filter(Objects::nonNull)
          .findFirst()
          .orElse(null);
    }
    return null;
  }

  private String selectedConfigName() {
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord selected = layerFor(selectedNode());
    if (selected != null) {
      return selected.configName();
    }
    if (!layersByPath.isEmpty()) {
      return layersByPath.values().stream()
          .map(StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord::configName)
          .map(Strings::trimToNull)
          .filter(Objects::nonNull)
          .findFirst()
          .orElse(null);
    }
    return null;
  }

  private void updateCompareToggleStateText() {
    if (compareModeEnabled) {
      compareModeToggle.addClassName("stitch-active");
    } else {
      compareModeToggle.removeClassName("stitch-active");
    }
  }

  private void updateToolbarState() {
    boolean hasConfig = !layersByPath.isEmpty();
    boolean hasLayerSelected = layerFor(selectedNode()) != null;
    boolean editing = editable && editorMode().isEditMode();
    if (editing && compareModeEnabled) {
      compareModeEnabled = false;
      applyCompareMode(false);
    }
    compareModeToggle.setEnabled(hasConfig && !editing);
    browserShell().treeNav().setExpandCollapseEnabled(hasConfig);
    inheritedValuesHeaderToggle.setEnabled(hasLayerSelected && !editing);
    inheritedValuesHeaderToggle.setValue(showInheritedValues);
    updateDetailHeaderActions();
    updateCompareToggleStateText();
  }

  private void updateDetailHeaderActions() {
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord selected = layerFor(selectedNode());
    boolean editing = editable && editorMode().isEditMode();
    List<Component> actions = new ArrayList<>();
    if (selected != null && !editing) {
      if (editable) {
        actions.add(actionButton("EDIT", "Edit selected config layer", this::enterEditModeFromHeader));
      }
      actions.add(actionButton("OUTPUT", "Open JSON output modes", () -> openJsonModesDialog(selected)));
      Button lineageToggle =
          actionButton(
              "LINEAGE",
              lineageVisible ? "Hide inline lineage" : "Show inline lineage",
              this::toggleLineageInline);
      StitchActionStyles.applyNeutral(lineageToggle);
      if (lineageVisible) {
        StitchActionStyles.applySecondary(lineageToggle);
        lineageToggle.addClassName("stitch-active");
      }
      actions.add(lineageToggle);
      actions.add(actionButton("DAG", "Open config layer DAG", () -> openDagDialog(selected)));
    }
    actions.add(inheritedValuesHeaderToggle);
    browserShell().setDetailHeaderActions(actions.toArray(Component[]::new));
  }

  private void enterEditModeFromHeader() {
    StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node = selectedNode();
    if (!editable || editorMode().isEditMode() || node == null || !isLayerNode(node)) {
      return;
    }
    editorMode().enterEditMode();
    layerInspector.clearValidationErrors();
    rerenderDetails();
    updateToolbarState();
  }

  private String nodeLabelClassName(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record = layerFor(node);
    if (record == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (!isLeafNode(node)) {
      return "stitch-config-tree-label--branch";
    }
    return hasDeclaredOverrides(record)
        ? "stitch-config-tree-label--override"
        : "stitch-config-tree-label--leaf";
  }

  private static Component indicator(String tooltip, String variantClassName) {
    Div indicator = new Div();
    indicator.addClassName("stitch-config-tree-indicator");
    indicator.addClassName(variantClassName);
    String text = Strings.firstNonBlank(tooltip, "Indicator");
    indicator.getElement().setAttribute("title", text);
    indicator.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", text);
    return indicator;
  }

  private static boolean isLeafNode(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    return node != null && (node.children() == null || node.children().isEmpty());
  }

  private static boolean hasDeclaredOverrides(StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record) {
    if (record == null) {
      return false;
    }
    JsonNode declared = record.declared();
    if (!(declared instanceof ObjectNode objectNode)) {
      return declared != null && !declared.isNull() && !declared.isEmpty();
    }
    return objectNode.fieldNames().hasNext();
  }

  private static String compareContext(StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record) {
    return "Group: "
        + Strings.firstNonBlank(record.group(), "-")
        + " | Name: "
        + Strings.firstNonBlank(record.configName(), "-");
  }

  private static String layerLabel(StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record) {
    String layer = Strings.firstNonBlank(record.layerId(), "-");
    String path = Strings.trimToNull(record.path());
    if (path == null || path.equals(layer)) {
      return layer;
    }
    return layer + " (" + path + ")";
  }

  private static String formatPathForDisplay(String path) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(path);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return "Layer path";
    }
    return normalized.replace("/", " / ");
  }

  private void openSubmissionDialog(StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record) {
    if (record == null) {
      return;
    }
    JsonNode proposedDeclared;
    try {
      proposedDeclared = layerInspector.parseEditorDeclaredJson();
    } catch (Exception error) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to open submission dialog", rootMessage(error));
      return;
    }
    StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions defaultOptions =
        StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions.immediate();
    StitchConfigSubmissionDialog.open(
        compareContext(record) + " | Layer: " + layerLabel(record),
        defaultOptions,
        record.declared(),
        proposedDeclared,
        options -> {
          setSubmissionOptions(record, options);
          return saveSelectedLayer();
        });
  }

  private StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions submissionOptionsFor(
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record) {
    String key = submissionKey(record);
    if (key == null) {
      return StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions.immediate();
    }
    return submissionOptionsByLayerPath.getOrDefault(
        key, StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions.immediate());
  }

  private void setSubmissionOptions(
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record, StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions options) {
    String key = submissionKey(record);
    if (key == null) {
      return;
    }
    submissionOptionsByLayerPath.put(
        key, options == null ? StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions.immediate() : options);
  }

  private static String submissionKey(StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record) {
    if (record == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(record.path()), Strings.trimToNull(record.layerId()));
  }

  private static String submissionSummary(StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions options) {
    StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions value =
        options == null ? StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions.immediate() : options;
    String approval = value.approvalRequired() ? "Approval required" : "Approval optional";
    if (value.mode() == StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionMode.SCHEDULED) {
      String effective = Strings.firstNonBlank(value.effectiveAtUtc() == null ? null : value.effectiveAtUtc().toString(), "-");
      String expires =
          value.expiresAtUtc() == null ? "none" : value.expiresAtUtc().toString();
      return "Scheduled (" + effective + " -> " + expires + ", " + approval + ")";
    }
    return "Immediate (" + approval + ")";
  }

  private static final class ManageLayersDialog extends StitchDialog {
    private ManageLayersDialog(String title) {
      super(title, false);
    }
  }
}
