package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.configs;

public final class StitchConfigsScreenConfig {
  private final String id;
  private final String label;
  private final String routePath;
  private final String pageTitle;
  private final String pageSubtitle;
  private final int order;
  private final boolean enabled;

  private StitchConfigsScreenConfig(Builder builder) {
    this.id = require(builder.id, "id");
    this.label = require(builder.label, "label");
    this.routePath = require(builder.routePath, "routePath");
    this.pageTitle = require(builder.pageTitle, "pageTitle");
    this.pageSubtitle = optional(builder.pageSubtitle);
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.enabled = builder.enabled;
  }

  public static Builder builder(String id) {
    return new Builder(id);
  }

  public String id() {
    return id;
  }

  public String label() {
    return label;
  }

  public String routePath() {
    return routePath;
  }

  public String pageTitle() {
    return pageTitle;
  }

  public String pageSubtitle() {
    return pageSubtitle;
  }

  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public boolean enabled() {
    return enabled;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final String id;
    private String label;
    private String routePath;
    private String pageTitle;
    private String pageSubtitle;
    private int order;
    private boolean enabled = true;

    private Builder(String id) {
      this.id = require(id, "id");
      if ("edit".equalsIgnoreCase(id)) {
        this.label = "Edit";
        this.routePath = "configs/view";
        this.pageTitle = "Configs - Edit";
        this.pageSubtitle = "Edit config layer payloads by group, name, and layer.";
        this.order = 20;
        return;
      }
      if ("approvals".equalsIgnoreCase(id)) {
        this.label = "Approvals";
        this.routePath = "configs/control";
        this.pageTitle = "Configs - Approvals";
        this.pageSubtitle = "Pending publication review controls.";
        this.order = 40;
        this.enabled = false;
        return;
      }
      if ("rollbacks".equalsIgnoreCase(id)) {
        this.label = "Rollbacks";
        this.routePath = "configs/control";
        this.pageTitle = "Configs - Rollbacks";
        this.pageSubtitle = "Simplified rollback controls.";
        this.order = 50;
        this.enabled = false;
        return;
      }
      if ("control".equalsIgnoreCase(id)) {
        this.label = "Control";
        this.routePath = "configs/control";
        this.pageTitle = "Configs - Control";
        this.pageSubtitle = "Central publication, history, rollback, and emergency operations.";
        this.order = 30;
        return;
      }
      if ("schemas".equalsIgnoreCase(id)) {
        this.label = "Schemas";
        this.routePath = "assets/schemas";
        this.pageTitle = "Configs - Schemas";
        this.pageSubtitle = "Browse and edit config schema structure by group and config.";
        this.order = 60;
        this.enabled = false;
        return;
      }
      if ("watcher".equalsIgnoreCase(id)) {
        this.label = "Watcher";
        this.routePath = "configs/watcher";
        this.pageTitle = "Configs - Watcher";
        this.pageSubtitle = "Watch live config payload updates for a selected layer.";
        this.order = 70;
        return;
      }
      this.label = "View";
      this.routePath = "configs/view";
      this.pageTitle = "Configs - View";
      this.pageSubtitle = "Browse config layer payloads by group, name, and layer.";
      this.order = 10;
    }

    public Builder withLabel(String value) {
      this.label = require(value, "label");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRoutePath(String value) {
      this.routePath = require(value, "routePath");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageTitle(String value) {
      this.pageTitle = require(value, "pageTitle");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageSubtitle(String value) {
      this.pageSubtitle = optional(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.enabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public StitchConfigsScreenConfig build() {
      return new StitchConfigsScreenConfig(this);
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/configs/StitchConfigSubmissionDialog.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.configs;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.Grid;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.GridVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification.Position;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextArea;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialog;

/** Submission dialog with scheduling + approval options and staged-change summary. */
public final class StitchConfigSubmissionDialog extends StitchDialog {
  private final StitchConfigScheduleControls scheduleControls = new StitchConfigScheduleControls();
  private final TextArea noteField = new TextArea("Reason / Note");
  private final SubmissionHandler submissionHandler;

  private StitchConfigSubmissionDialog(
      String context,
      StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions initialOptions,
      JsonNode currentDeclared,
      JsonNode proposedDeclared,
      SubmissionHandler submissionHandler) {
    super("Config Submission", false);
    this.submissionHandler = submissionHandler == null ? options -> true : submissionHandler;

    addClassName("stitch-config-submit-dialog");
    setWidth("1120px");
    setMaxWidth("98vw");
    setTop("6vh");
    body().setWidthFull();
    body().addClassName("stitch-config-submit-dialog-body");

    List<ProposedChange> changes = buildProposedChanges(currentDeclared, proposedDeclared);

    Span contextLine = new Span(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(context), "Config submission"));
    contextLine.addClassName("stitch-config-submit-context");
    contextLine.getElement().setAttribute("aria-live", "polite");

    noteField.setWidthFull();
    noteField.setMaxLength(512);
    noteField.setClearButtonVisible(true);
    noteField.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Submission reason or note");

    scheduleControls.setSubmissionOptions(initialOptions);
    if (initialOptions != null && Strings.trimToNull(initialOptions.note()) != null) {
      noteField.setValue(initialOptions.note());
    }

    VerticalLayout optionsSection = section("Submission Options", scheduleControls, noteField);

    Span changesCount = new Span(changes.size() + " changed row" + (changes.size() == 1 ? "" : "s"));
    changesCount.addClassName("stitch-config-submit-count");

    Grid<ProposedChange> changesGrid = buildChangesGrid(changes);
    Div noChanges = new Div("No staged changes detected.");
    noChanges.addClassName("stitch-config-submit-empty");
    noChanges.setVisible(changes.isEmpty());
    changesGrid.setVisible(!changes.isEmpty());

    VerticalLayout changesSection = section("Proposed Changes", changesCount, noChanges, changesGrid);

    addToBody(contextLine, optionsSection, changesSection);
    addPrimaryAction("SUBMIT", this::applyRequested);
    addSecondaryAction("Cancel", this::close);
  }

  public static StitchConfigSubmissionDialog open(
      String context,
      StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions initialOptions,
      JsonNode currentDeclared,
      JsonNode proposedDeclared,
      SubmissionHandler submissionHandler) {
    StitchConfigSubmissionDialog dialog =
        new StitchConfigSubmissionDialog(
            context,
            initialOptions,
            currentDeclared,
            proposedDeclared,
            submissionHandler);
    dialog.open();
    return dialog;
  }

  private void applyRequested() {
    List<String> errors = scheduleControls.validationErrors();
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
      Notification.show(errors.get(0), 2500, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      return;
    }
    StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions options =
        scheduleControls.submissionOptions(Strings.trimToNull(noteField.getValue()));
    if (submissionHandler.onSubmit(options)) {
      close();
    }
  }

  private static VerticalLayout section(String title, Component... content) {
    VerticalLayout section = new VerticalLayout();
    section.setPadding(false);
    section.setSpacing(true);
    section.setWidthFull();
    section.addClassName("stitch-config-submit-section");

    Span heading = new Span(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(title), "Section"));
    heading.addClassName("stitch-config-submit-section-title");

    section.add(heading);
    if (content != null) {
      section.add(content);
    }
    return section;
  }

  private static Grid<ProposedChange> buildChangesGrid(List<ProposedChange> changes) {
    Grid<ProposedChange> grid = new Grid<>(ProposedChange.class, false);
    grid.addThemeVariants(GridVariant.LUMO_COMPACT);
    grid.addClassName("stitch-config-submit-changes-grid");
    grid.addClassName("stitch-results-grid");
    grid.setWidthFull();
    grid.setHeight("23rem");

    grid.addColumn(ProposedChange::path).setHeader("Path").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(1);
    grid.addComponentColumn(StitchConfigSubmissionDialog::changePill)
        .setHeader("Change")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setFlexGrow(0);
    grid.addComponentColumn(change -> valueCell(change.currentValue()))
        .setHeader("Current")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setFlexGrow(1);
    grid.addComponentColumn(change -> valueCell(change.newValue()))
        .setHeader("New")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setFlexGrow(1);
    grid.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Proposed config change summary");
    grid.setItems(changes == null ? List.of() : changes);
    return grid;
  }

  private static Component valueCell(String value) {
    String text = Strings.firstNonBlank(value, "-");
    Span span = new Span(text);
    span.addClassName("stitch-config-submit-cell");
    span.getElement().setProperty("title", text);
    return span;
  }

  private static Component changePill(ProposedChange change) {
    Span pill = new Span(Strings.firstNonBlank(change == null ? null : change.changeType(), "MODIFIED"));
    pill.addClassName("stitch-config-submit-change-pill");
    if (change != null) {
      pill.addClassName(
          "stitch-config-submit-change-pill--"
              + Strings.firstNonBlank(change.changeType(), "MODIFIED").toLowerCase());
    }
    return pill;
  }

  private static List<ProposedChange> buildProposedChanges(JsonNode currentDeclared, JsonNode proposedDeclared) {
    ObjectNode current = objectNode(currentDeclared);
    ObjectNode proposed = objectNode(proposedDeclared);

    Map<String, JsonNode> currentFlat = flattenLeaves(current);
    Map<String, JsonNode> proposedFlat = flattenLeaves(proposed);

    Set<String> allPaths = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    allPaths.addAll(currentFlat.keySet());
    allPaths.addAll(proposedFlat.keySet());

    List<String> orderedPaths = new ArrayList<>(allPaths);
    orderedPaths.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);

    List<ProposedChange> changes = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String path : orderedPaths) {
      boolean hadCurrent = currentFlat.containsKey(path);
      boolean hasProposed = proposedFlat.containsKey(path);
      JsonNode before = currentFlat.get(path);
      JsonNode after = proposedFlat.get(path);
      if (hadCurrent && hasProposed && jsonEquivalent(before, after)) {
        continue;
      }
      if (!hadCurrent && !hasProposed) {
        continue;
      }
      String type = changeType(hadCurrent, before, hasProposed, after);
      String currentValue = hadCurrent ? displayValue(before) : "-";
      String newValue = hasProposed ? displayValue(after) : "-";
      changes.add(new ProposedChange(path, type, currentValue, newValue));
    }
    changes.sort(Comparator.comparing(ProposedChange::path, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER));
    return List.copyOf(changes);
  }

  private static String changeType(
      boolean hadCurrent, JsonNode before, boolean hasProposed, JsonNode after) {
    if (!hadCurrent && hasProposed) {
      return "ADDED";
    }
    if (hadCurrent && !hasProposed) {
      return "CLEARED";
    }
    if (hadCurrent && hasProposed && after != null && after.isNull()) {
      return "REMOVED";
    }
    if (!jsonEquivalent(before, after)) {
      return "MODIFIED";
    }
    return "MODIFIED";
  }

  private static boolean jsonEquivalent(JsonNode left, JsonNode right) {
    if (left == right) {
      return true;
    }
    if (left == null || right == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return left.equals(right);
  }

  private static ObjectNode objectNode(JsonNode value) {
    if (value instanceof ObjectNode objectNode) {
      return objectNode.deepCopy();
    }
    return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
  }

  private static Map<String, JsonNode> flattenLeaves(JsonNode payload) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, JsonNode> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    flatten("", payload, values);
    return Map.copyOf(values);
  }

  private static void flatten(String prefix, JsonNode value, Map<String, JsonNode> output) {
    if (value == null || value.isNull()) {
      if (!prefix.isBlank()) {
        output.put(prefix, value);
      }
      return;
    }
    if (value.isObject()) {
      value.fieldNames().forEachRemaining(field -> flatten(join(prefix, field), value.get(field), output));
      return;
    }
    if (value.isArray()) {
      for (int index = 0; index < value.size(); index++) {
        flatten(join(prefix, "[" + index + "]"), value.get(index), output);
      }
      return;
    }
    if (!prefix.isBlank()) {
      output.put(prefix, value);
    }
  }

  private static String join(String left, String right) {
    if (Strings.trimToNull(left) == null) {
      return right;
    }
    if (right.startsWith("[")) {
      return left + right;
    }
    return left + "." + right;
  }

  private static String displayValue(JsonNode value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return "-";
    }
    if (value.isNull()) {
      return "null";
    }
    if (value.isTextual()) {
      return value.asText();
    }
    if (value.isNumber() || value.isBoolean()) {
      return value.asText();
    }
    return compactJson(value);
  }

  private static String compactJson(JsonNode value) {
    JsonNode safe = value == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : value;
    try {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().writeValueAsString(safe);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      return safe.toString();
    }
  }

  @FunctionalInterface
  public interface SubmissionHandler {
    boolean onSubmit(StitchConfigsProvider.SubmissionOptions options);
  }

  private record ProposedChange(String path, String changeType, String currentValue, String newValue) {
    private ProposedChange {
      path = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(path), "-");
      changeType = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(changeType), "MODIFIED");
      currentValue = Strings.firstNonBlank(currentValue, "-");
      newValue = Strings.firstNonBlank(newValue, "-");
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.configs;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicBoolean;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicReference;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.workflow.ConfigJsonDiff;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfigLayer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeConflationMode;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeSource;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeUpdate;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchSubscriptionScope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

/** Configs-domain realtime source adapter for Configs -> Watcher. */
public final class StitchConfigsWatcherProvider {
  private final SessionImpl session;
  private final StitchConfigsProvider configsProvider;

  public StitchConfigsWatcherProvider(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext, StitchConfigsProvider configsProvider) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    this.configsProvider = Objects.requireNonNull(configsProvider, "configsProvider");
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(current instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    this.session = resolved;
  }

  public List<String> listGroups() {
    return configsProvider.listGroups();
  }

  public List<String> listConfigNames(String group) {
    return configsProvider.listConfigNames(group);
  }

  public List<LayerOption> listLayerOptions(String group, String configName) {
    String normalizedGroup = trimToNull(group);
    String normalizedConfigName = trimToNull(configName);
    if (normalizedGroup == null || normalizedConfigName == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    StitchConfigsProvider.TreeModel tree = configsProvider.loadLayers(normalizedGroup, normalizedConfigName);
    if (tree.layersByPath().isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return tree.layersByPath().entrySet().stream()
        .sorted(Map.Entry.comparingByKey(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
        .map(
            entry -> {
              StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord record = entry.getValue();
              String path = Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(entry.getKey()), trimToNull(record.path()));
              String label = path == null ? Strings.firstNonBlank(record.layerId(), "-") : path;
              String shortName = trimToNull(record.shortName());
              if (shortName != null && !Objects.equals(shortName, trimToNull(record.layerId()))) {
                label = label + " (" + shortName + ")";
              }
              return new LayerOption(
                  Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(record.layerId()), label),
                  label,
                  path == null ? Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(record.layerId()), "-") : path);
            })
        .toList();
  }

  public JsonNode resolveSchemaDocument(String group, String configName, String layerId) {
    String normalizedGroup = trimToNull(group);
    String normalizedConfigName = trimToNull(configName);
    String normalizedLayerId = trimToNull(layerId);
    if (normalizedGroup == null || normalizedConfigName == null) {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    }
    StitchConfigsProvider.TreeModel tree = configsProvider.loadLayers(normalizedGroup, normalizedConfigName);
    if (tree.layersByPath().isEmpty()) {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    }

    if (normalizedLayerId != null) {
      StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord selected =
          tree.layersByPath().values().stream()
              .filter(Objects::nonNull)
              .filter(layer -> Objects.equals(trimToNull(layer.layerId()), normalizedLayerId))
              .findFirst()
              .orElse(null);
      if (selected != null) {
        JsonNode schema = configsProvider.resolveSchemaDocument(normalizedGroup, selected.schemaKey());
        if (schema != null && schema.isObject() && !schema.isEmpty()) {
          return schema;
        }
      }
    }
    return configsProvider.resolveSchemaDocument(
        normalizedGroup, normalizedConfigName, tree.layersByPath());
  }

  public StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy defaultUpdatePolicy() {
    return StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy.builder()
        .withConflationMode(StitchRealtimeConflationMode.LATEST_ONLY)
        .withDispatchIntervalMillis(200)
        .withMaxBatchSize(16)
        .withMaxQueueSize(256)
        .withStaleTimeoutMillis(30_000)
        .build();
  }

  public StitchSubscriptionScope defaultScope() {
    return StitchSubscriptionScope.PRIVATE;
  }

  public StitchRealtimeSource<WatchPayload> sourceFor(WatchTarget target) {
    WatchTarget required = Objects.requireNonNull(target, "target").normalized();
    if (!required.isComplete()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Watch target must include group, configName, and layerId.");
    }
    return listener -> {
      StitchRealtimeSource.Listener<WatchPayload> sink = Objects.requireNonNull(listener, "listener");
      AtomicBoolean closed = new AtomicBoolean(false);
      AtomicReference<WatchPayload> previous = new AtomicReference<>();

      sink.onSubscribed();
      WatchPayload initial = snapshot(required);
      previous.set(initial);
      sink.onUpdate(StitchRealtimeUpdate.snapshot(initial));

      AutoCloseable cacheHandle =
          requireCache()
              .registerListener(
                  DefinitionType.CONFIG_LAYER,
                  (key, definition) -> {
                    if (closed.get() || !matchesTarget(required, key, definition)) {
                      return;
                    }
                    try {
                      WatchPayload current = snapshot(required);
                      WatchPayload prior = previous.getAndSet(current);
                      List<String> changedPaths = diffPaths(prior == null ? null : prior.payload(), current.payload());
                      WatchPayload update = current.withChangedPaths(changedPaths);
                      if (changedPaths.isEmpty()) {
                        sink.onUpdate(StitchRealtimeUpdate.heartbeat(update));
                      } else {
                        sink.onUpdate(StitchRealtimeUpdate.delta(update));
                      }
                    } catch (Exception error) {
                      sink.onError(error, false);
                    }
                  });
      return () -> {
        if (!closed.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
          return;
        }
        try {
          if (cacheHandle != null) {
            cacheHandle.close();
          }
        } finally {
          sink.onUnsubscribed();
        }
      };
    };
  }

  private WatchPayload snapshot(WatchTarget target) {
    StitchConfigsProvider.TreeModel tree = configsProvider.loadLayers(target.group(), target.configName());
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord layer = findLayer(tree, target.layerId());
    Instant observedAt = Instant.now();
    if (layer == null) {
      return new WatchPayload(
          target,
          "LIVE",
          null,
          DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode(),
          List.of(),
          true,
          observedAt);
    }
    StitchConfigsProvider.LayerView view = configsProvider.loadLayerView(layer, tree.layersByPath(), observedAt);
    JsonNode resolved = view == null ? null : view.resolvedPayload();
    String source = "LIVE (resolved)";
    return new WatchPayload(
        target,
        source,
        Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(view == null ? null : view.layer().path()), trimToNull(layer.path())),
        safePayload(resolved),
        List.of(),
        false,
        observedAt);
  }

  private StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord findLayer(
      StitchConfigsProvider.TreeModel tree, String layerId) {
    if (tree == null || tree.layersByPath().isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    for (StitchConfigsProvider.LayerRecord candidate : tree.layersByPath().values()) {
      if (candidate != null && Objects.equals(trimToNull(candidate.layerId()), trimToNull(layerId))) {
        return candidate;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private DiscoveryCache requireCache() {
    DiscoveryCache cache = session.internal().discoveryCache();
    if (cache == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DiscoveryCache is not available");
    }
    return cache;
  }

  private static boolean matchesTarget(
      WatchTarget target, DiscoveryCache.ConfigKey key, Definition definition) {
    if (!(definition instanceof DefinitionConfigLayer layer)) {
      return false;
    }
    StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.LayerIdentity identity =
        StitchConfigLayerIdentitySupport.layerIdentity(layer);
    if (!Objects.equals(identity.group(), target.group())) {
      return false;
    }
    return Objects.equals(identity.configName(), target.configName());
  }

  private static List<String> diffPaths(JsonNode previous, JsonNode current) {
    if (previous == null || current == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<ConfigJsonDiff.DiffRow> rows = ConfigJsonDiff.diff(previous, current);
    if (rows == null || rows.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> changed = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (ConfigJsonDiff.DiffRow row : rows) {
      if (row == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String path = trimToNull(row.path());
      if (path != null) {
        changed.add(path);
      }
    }
    return changed.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(changed);
  }

  private static JsonNode safePayload(JsonNode value) {
    return value == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : value.deepCopy();
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    return Strings.trimToNull(value);
  }

  public record LayerOption(String id, String label, String path) {}

  public record WatchTarget(String group, String configName, String layerId) {
    public WatchTarget normalized() {
      return new WatchTarget(trimToNull(group), trimToNull(configName), trimToNull(layerId));
    }

    public boolean isComplete() {
      return trimToNull(group) != null
          && trimToNull(configName) != null
          && trimToNull(layerId) != null;
    }
  }

  public record WatchPayload(
      WatchTarget target,
      String sourceLabel,
      String layerPath,
      JsonNode payload,
      List<String> changedPaths,
      boolean missing,
      Instant observedAt) {
    public WatchPayload {
      target = target == null ? new WatchTarget(null, null, null) : target.normalized();
      sourceLabel = Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(sourceLabel), "LIVE");
      layerPath = trimToNull(layerPath);
      payload = safePayload(payload);
      changedPaths =
          changedPaths == null
              ? List.of()
              : changedPaths.stream().map(StitchConfigsWatcherProvider::trimToNull).filter(Objects::nonNull).toList();
      observedAt = observedAt == null ? Instant.now() : observedAt;
    }

    public WatchPayload withChangedPaths(List<String> value) {
      return new WatchPayload(target, sourceLabel, layerPath, payload, value, missing, Instant.now());
    }
  }
}

  protected StitchConfigsWatcherScreen(
      StitchConfigsScreenConfig config,

      StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry realtimeRegistry) {

  private void onSelectionChanged(StitchConfigSelectionBar.SelectionChange value) {
    selection = new StitchConfigSelectionBar.Selection(value.group(), value.name());
    StitchConfigSelectionContext.remember(selection.group(), selection.name());
    reloadLayerOptions(value.preserveTreeSelection());
    updateWatcherTarget(true);

  private void reloadLayerOptions(boolean preserveSelection) {
    String group = Strings.trimToNull(selection.group());
    String name = Strings.trimToNull(selection.name());
    if (group == null || name == null) {
      selectedLayer = null;
      suppressLayerEvents = true;
      layerSelector.clear();
      layerSelector.setItems(List.of());
      layerSelector.setEnabled(false);
      suppressLayerEvents = false;
      return;
    }

    List<StitchConfigsWatcherProvider.LayerOption> options = provider.listLayerOptions(group, name);
    StitchConfigsWatcherProvider.LayerOption current = selectedLayer;
    StitchConfigsWatcherProvider.LayerOption next =
        preserveSelection
            ? options.stream()
                .filter(
                    option ->
                        current != null
                            && Objects.equals(
                                Strings.trimToNull(option.id()), Strings.trimToNull(current.id())))
                .findFirst()
                .orElse(null)
            : null;
    selectedLayer = next;

    suppressLayerEvents = true;
    layerSelector.setItems(options);
    if (next == null) {
      layerSelector.clear();
    } else {
      layerSelector.setValue(next);
    }
    layerSelector.setEnabled(!options.isEmpty());
    suppressLayerEvents = false;
  }

  private void refreshRequested() {
    selectionBar.reload(true);
    if (activeTarget != null && activeTarget.isComplete()) {
      if (controller == null) {
        updateWatcherTarget(true);
      } else {
        controller.restart();
      }
    }
  }

  private void startWatching() {
    if (activeTarget == null || !activeTarget.isComplete()) {
      updateWatcherTarget(true);
      return;
    }
    if (controller == null) {
      bindTarget(activeTarget, true);
      return;
    }
    controller.start();
    refreshActionState();
  }

  private void stopWatching() {
    if (controller == null) {
      return;
    }
    controller.stop();
    refreshActionState();
  }

  private void updateWatcherTarget(boolean autoStart) {
    StitchConfigsWatcherProvider.WatchTarget next =
        new StitchConfigsWatcherProvider.WatchTarget(
                Strings.trimToNull(selection.group()),
                Strings.trimToNull(selection.name()),
                selectedLayer == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(selectedLayer.id()))
            .normalized();
    if (!next.isComplete()) {
      closeController();
      clearView("Select Group, Config, and Layer to start watching.");
      refreshActionState();
      return;
    }

    if (Objects.equals(next, activeTarget) && controller != null) {
      controller.setUi(currentUi());
      updateSelectionContext(next, selectedLayer == null ? null : selectedLayer.path());
      if (autoStart) {
        controller.start();
      }
      refreshActionState();
      return;
    }

    bindTarget(next, autoStart);
  }

  private void bindTarget(StitchConfigsWatcherProvider.WatchTarget target, boolean autoStart) {
    closeController();
    activeTarget = target;
    lastPayload = null;
    highlightedKeys.clear();

    schemaDoc = resolveSchemaDoc(target);
    buildSchemaPanels(schemaDoc);
    applyColumnLayout(columnsSelect.getValue() == null ? DEFAULT_COLUMNS : columnsSelect.getValue());

    if (groupPanels.isEmpty()) {
      emptyStateText.setText("Waiting for first live payload...");
      emptyState.setVisible(true);
      columnsHost.setVisible(false);
    }

    updateSelectionContext(target, selectedLayer == null ? null : selectedLayer.path());

    controller =
        new StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<>(
            provider.sourceFor(target),
            provider.defaultUpdatePolicy(),
            provider.defaultScope(),
            currentUi());

    registryBinding =
        realtimeRegistry.register(
            "Configs Watcher", selectionContextLabel(target, selectedLayer), controller, currentUi());
    statusBinding = controller == null ? () -> {} : statusBar.bind(controller);
    observerBinding =
        controller.addObserver(
            new StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController.Observer() {
              @Override
              public void onStateChanged(
                  StitchRealtimeConnectionState state,
                  org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchSubscriptionScope scope) {
                refreshActionState();
              }

              @Override
              public void onMetrics(
                  org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchUiUpdateDispatcher.Metrics metrics,
                  Instant lastUpdateAt) {
                refreshActionState();
              }

              @Override
              public void onError(Throwable error, boolean terminal) {
                refreshActionState();
              }
            });

    updateBinding =
        controller.addListener(
            new StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController.Listener<>() {
              @Override
              public void onUpdates(List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchConfigsWatcherProvider.WatchPayload>> updates) {
                if (updates == null || updates.isEmpty()) {
                  return;
                }
                StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchConfigsWatcherProvider.WatchPayload> last =
                    updates.get(updates.size() - 1);
                if (last == null || last.payload() == null) {
                  return;
                }
                lastPayload = last.payload();
                ensurePanelsForPayload(lastPayload.payload());
                int changed = applyPayload(lastPayload.payload(), true);
                if (changed == 0 && !lastPayload.changedPaths().isEmpty()) {
                  highlightPaths(lastPayload.changedPaths());
                }
                updateSelectionContext(lastPayload.target(), lastPayload.layerPath());
                refreshActionState();
              }
            });

    if (autoStart) {
      controller.start();
    }
    refreshActionState();
  }

  private void ensurePanelsForPayload(JsonNode payload) {
    if (!groupPanels.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    if (schemaDoc != null) {
      buildSchemaPanels(schemaDoc);
    }
    if (groupPanels.isEmpty()) {
      buildFallbackPanels(payload);
    }
    applyColumnLayout(columnsSelect.getValue() == null ? DEFAULT_COLUMNS : columnsSelect.getValue());
  }

  private ConfigSchemaDoc resolveSchemaDoc(StitchConfigsWatcherProvider.WatchTarget target) {
    if (target == null || !target.isComplete()) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      JsonNode schema = provider.resolveSchemaDocument(target.group(), target.configName(), target.layerId());
      if (schema == null || !schema.isObject() || schema.isEmpty()) {
        return null;
      }
      return ConfigSchemaCodec.parse(schema);
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private void buildSchemaPanels(ConfigSchemaDoc doc) {
    fieldsByKey.clear();
    groupPanels.clear();
    highlightedKeys.clear();
    columnsHost.removeAll();

    if (doc == null || doc.fields() == null || doc.fields().isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }

    Map<String, GroupMeta> groupMetaById = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    List<Group> orderedGroups =
        doc.groups() == null
            ? List.of()
            : doc.groups().stream()
                .filter(Objects::nonNull)
                .filter(group -> Strings.trimToNull(group.id()) != null)
                .sorted(
                    Comparator.comparingInt(
                            (Group group) -> group.order() == null ? Integer.MAX_VALUE : group.order())
                        .thenComparing(group -> Strings.trimToEmpty(group.id())))
                .toList();

    for (Group group : orderedGroups) {
      String id = Strings.trimToNull(group.id());
      if (id == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String label = Strings.trimToNull(group.label());
      groupMetaById.put(id, new GroupMeta(id, label == null ? id : label, group.order()));
    }
    groupMetaById.putIfAbsent(
        GROUP_UNGROUPED, new GroupMeta(GROUP_UNGROUPED, "Ungrouped", Integer.MAX_VALUE));

    Map<String, List<Field>> fieldsByGroup = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String groupId : groupMetaById.keySet()) {
      fieldsByGroup.put(groupId, new ArrayList<>());
    }

    List<Field> orderedFields =
        doc.fields().stream()
            .filter(Objects::nonNull)
            .filter(field -> Strings.trimToNull(field.key()) != null)
            .sorted(
                Comparator.comparingInt(
                        (Field field) -> field.order() == null ? Integer.MAX_VALUE : field.order())
                    .thenComparing(field -> Strings.trimToEmpty(field.key())))
            .toList();

    for (Field field : orderedFields) {
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(field.key());
      if (key == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String groupId = Strings.trimToNull(field.groupId());
      String normalizedGroupId = groupId == null ? GROUP_UNGROUPED : groupId;
      groupMetaById.putIfAbsent(
          normalizedGroupId,
          new GroupMeta(normalizedGroupId, normalizedGroupId, Integer.MAX_VALUE));
      fieldsByGroup.computeIfAbsent(normalizedGroupId, ignored -> new ArrayList<>()).add(field);
    }

    List<GroupMeta> orderedMeta = new ArrayList<>(groupMetaById.values());
    orderedMeta.sort(
        Comparator.comparingInt(
                (GroupMeta meta) -> meta.order() == null ? Integer.MAX_VALUE : meta.order())
            .thenComparing(meta -> Strings.trimToEmpty(meta.id())));

    for (GroupMeta groupMeta : orderedMeta) {
      List<Field> fields = fieldsByGroup.get(groupMeta.id());
      if (fields == null || fields.isEmpty()) {
        continue;
      }
      VerticalLayout card = new VerticalLayout();
      card.setPadding(false);
      card.setSpacing(false);
      card.setWidthFull();
      card.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-group-card");

      Span legend = new Span(groupMeta.label());
      legend.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-group-title");

      VerticalLayout rows = new VerticalLayout();
      rows.setPadding(false);
      rows.setSpacing(false);
      rows.setWidthFull();
      rows.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-group-rows");

      for (Field field : fields) {
        String key = Strings.trimToNull(field.key());
        if (key == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String label = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(field.label()), key);
        FieldRow row = newFieldRow(label, key);
        fieldsByKey.put(key, row);
        rows.add(row.row());
      }

      card.add(legend, rows);
      groupPanels.add(new GroupPanel(groupMeta.id(), card));
    }
  }

  private void buildFallbackPanels(JsonNode payload) {
    fieldsByKey.clear();
    groupPanels.clear();
    columnsHost.removeAll();

    JsonNode payloadObject = payload != null && payload.isObject() ? payload : null;
    if (payloadObject == null || payloadObject.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }

    List<String> keys = new ArrayList<>();
    payloadObject.fieldNames().forEachRemaining(keys::add);
    keys.removeIf(value -> Strings.trimToNull(value) == null);
    keys.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    if (keys.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }

    VerticalLayout card = new VerticalLayout();
    card.setPadding(false);
    card.setSpacing(false);
    card.setWidthFull();
    card.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-group-card");

    Span legend = new Span("Values");
    legend.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-group-title");

    VerticalLayout rows = new VerticalLayout();
    rows.setPadding(false);
    rows.setSpacing(false);
    rows.setWidthFull();
    rows.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-group-rows");

    for (String key : keys) {
      FieldRow row = newFieldRow(key, key);
      fieldsByKey.put(key, row);
      rows.add(row.row());
    }

    card.add(legend, rows);
    groupPanels.add(new GroupPanel(GROUP_UNGROUPED, card));
  }

  private FieldRow newFieldRow(String label, String fieldKey) {
    Span name = new Span(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(label), Strings.firstNonBlank(fieldKey, "-")));
    name.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-field-name");

    VerticalLayout valueHost = new VerticalLayout();
    valueHost.setPadding(false);
    valueHost.setSpacing(false);
    valueHost.setWidthFull();
    valueHost.setAlignItems(Alignment.STRETCH);
    valueHost.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-field-value-host");

    HorizontalLayout row = new HorizontalLayout();
    row.setPadding(false);
    row.setSpacing(true);
    row.setWidthFull();
    row.setAlignItems(Alignment.START);
    row.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-field-row");
    row.add(name, valueHost);
    row.expand(valueHost);

    FieldRow fieldRow = new FieldRow(row, valueHost, null);
    updateValueCell(fieldRow, null);
    return fieldRow;
  }

  private int applyPayload(JsonNode payload, boolean highlightChanges) {
    int changed = 0;
    for (Map.Entry<String, FieldRow> entry : fieldsByKey.entrySet()) {
      String key = entry.getKey();
      FieldRow row = entry.getValue();
      JsonNode value = resolveValueForField(payload, key);
      String nextToken = valueToken(value);
      if (!Objects.equals(row.valueToken(), nextToken)) {
        row.valueToken(nextToken);
        updateValueCell(row, value);
        changed++;
        if (highlightChanges) {
          row.row().addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-field-changed");
          highlightedKeys.add(key);
        }
      }
    }
    refreshActionState();
    return changed;
  }

  private void highlightPaths(List<String> changedPaths) {
    if (changedPaths == null || changedPaths.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    for (String changedPath : changedPaths) {
      String key = topLevelKey(changedPath);
      if (key == null) {
        continue;
      }
      FieldRow row = fieldsByKey.get(key);
      if (row == null) {
        continue;
      }
      row.row().addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-field-changed");
      highlightedKeys.add(key);
    }
    refreshActionState();
  }

  private void updateValueCell(FieldRow fieldRow, JsonNode value) {
    if (fieldRow == null || fieldRow.valueHost() == null || fieldRow.row() == null) {
      return;
    }
    VerticalLayout valueHost = fieldRow.valueHost();
    valueHost.removeAll();
    valueHost.add(valueComponent(value, 0));

    boolean nested = containsNestedTableValue(value, 0);
    if (nested) {
      fieldRow.row().addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-field-row-nested");
    } else {
      fieldRow.row().removeClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-field-row-nested");
    }
  }

  private static boolean containsNestedTableValue(JsonNode value, int depth) {
    if (value == null || value.isNull() || depth >= MAX_NESTED_DEPTH) {
      return false;
    }
    if (value.isObject()) {
      return true;
    }
    if (!value.isArray()) {
      return false;
    }
    for (JsonNode item : value) {
      if (item == null || item.isNull()) {
        continue;
      }
      if (item.isObject()) {
        return true;
      }
      if (item.isArray() && containsNestedTableValue(item, depth + 1)) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static String valueToken(JsonNode value) {
    if (value == null || value.isNull()) {
      return "<null>";
    }
    return value.toString();
  }

  private Component valueComponent(JsonNode value, int depth) {
    if (depth >= MAX_NESTED_DEPTH) {
      return scalarValueComponent(prettyInlineJson(value));
    }
    if (value == null || value.isNull()) {
      return scalarValueComponent(MISSING_VALUE_TEXT);
    }
    if (value.isObject()) {
      return structPanel(value, depth);
    }
    if (value.isArray()) {
      return listPanel(value, depth);
    }
    if (value.isTextual() || value.isBoolean() || value.isNumber()) {
      return scalarValueComponent(value.asText());
    }
    return scalarValueComponent(prettyInlineJson(value));
  }

  private Component scalarValueComponent(String text) {
    String value = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(text), MISSING_VALUE_TEXT);
    Span span = new Span(value);
    span.addClassNames("stitch-configs-watcher-field-value", "stitch-configs-watcher-field-value-text");
    span.getElement().setProperty("title", value);
    return span;
  }

  private Component structPanel(JsonNode objectValue, int depth) {
    VerticalLayout card = new VerticalLayout();
    card.setPadding(false);
    card.setSpacing(false);
    card.setWidthFull();
    card.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-struct-table");
    card.getStyle().set("margin-left", (Math.max(0, depth) * 8) + "px");
    if (depth > 0) {
      card.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-struct-table-nested");
    }

    if (objectValue == null || !objectValue.isObject() || objectValue.isEmpty()) {
      HorizontalLayout emptyRow = new HorizontalLayout();
      emptyRow.setPadding(false);
      emptyRow.setSpacing(false);
      emptyRow.setWidthFull();
      emptyRow.setAlignItems(Alignment.CENTER);
      emptyRow.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-struct-row");

      Span emptyName = new Span("Value");
      emptyName.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-struct-name");
      Span emptyValue = new Span("EMPTY");
      emptyValue.addClassNames(
          "stitch-configs-watcher-struct-value", "stitch-configs-watcher-field-value-text");
      emptyRow.add(emptyName, emptyValue);
      emptyRow.expand(emptyName);
      card.add(emptyRow);
      return card;
    }

    for (var fields = objectValue.fields(); fields.hasNext(); ) {
      var entry = fields.next();
      if (entry == null || entry.getKey() == null) {
        continue;
      }

      HorizontalLayout row = new HorizontalLayout();
      row.setPadding(false);
      row.setSpacing(false);
      row.setWidthFull();
      row.setAlignItems(Alignment.START);
      row.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-struct-row");

      Span name = new Span(entry.getKey());
      name.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-struct-name");

      VerticalLayout slot = new VerticalLayout();
      slot.setPadding(false);
      slot.setSpacing(false);
      slot.setWidthFull();
      slot.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-struct-value-slot");
      boolean scalarValue = isScalarLike(entry.getValue());
      slot.addClassName(
          scalarValue
              ? "stitch-configs-watcher-struct-value-slot--scalar"
              : "stitch-configs-watcher-struct-value-slot--nested");
      slot.setAlignItems(scalarValue ? Alignment.END : Alignment.STRETCH);
      slot.add(valueComponent(entry.getValue(), depth + 1));

      row.add(name, slot);
      row.expand(name, slot);
      card.add(row);
    }

    return card;
  }

  private Component listPanel(JsonNode arrayValue, int depth) {
    if (arrayValue == null || !arrayValue.isArray()) {
      return scalarValueComponent(MISSING_VALUE_TEXT);
    }
    if (arrayValue.isEmpty()) {
      return scalarValueComponent("[]");
    }

    VerticalLayout list = new VerticalLayout();
    list.setPadding(false);
    list.setSpacing(true);
    list.setWidthFull();
    list.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-array-list");
    list.getStyle().set("margin-left", (Math.max(0, depth) * 8) + "px");

    for (JsonNode item : arrayValue) {
      Component rendered = valueComponent(item, depth + 1);
      if (rendered instanceof VerticalLayout layout) {
        layout.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-array-item");
        list.add(layout);
      } else {
        VerticalLayout itemPanel = new VerticalLayout();
        itemPanel.setPadding(false);
        itemPanel.setSpacing(false);
        itemPanel.setWidthFull();
        itemPanel.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-array-item");
        itemPanel.add(rendered);
        list.add(itemPanel);
      }
    }
    return list;
  }

  private static boolean isScalarLike(JsonNode value) {
    return value == null || value.isNull() || value.isValueNode();
  }

  private void clearHighlights() {
    for (String key : new ArrayList<>(highlightedKeys)) {
      FieldRow row = fieldsByKey.get(key);
      if (row != null) {
        row.row().removeClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-field-changed");
      }
    }
    highlightedKeys.clear();
    refreshActionState();
    Notification.show("Cleared changed highlights", 1200, Position.BOTTOM_START);
  }

  private void applyColumnLayout(int requestedColumns) {
    int columns = Math.max(1, Math.min(4, requestedColumns));
    if (!Objects.equals(columnsSelect.getValue(), columns)) {
      suppressColumnsEvents = true;
      columnsSelect.setValue(columns);
      suppressColumnsEvents = false;
    }

    columnsHost.removeAll();
    if (groupPanels.isEmpty()) {
      emptyState.setVisible(true);
      columnsHost.setVisible(false);
      return;
    }

    int actualColumns = Math.max(1, Math.min(columns, groupPanels.size()));
    List<VerticalLayout> columnLayouts = new ArrayList<>(actualColumns);
    for (int i = 0; i < actualColumns; i++) {
      VerticalLayout column = new VerticalLayout();
      column.setPadding(false);
      column.setSpacing(true);
      column.setWidthFull();
      column.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-column");
      columnLayouts.add(column);
      columnsHost.add(column);
      columnsHost.setFlexGrow(1, column);
    }

    for (int i = 0; i < groupPanels.size(); i++) {
      GroupPanel panel = groupPanels.get(i);
      if (panel == null || panel.panel() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      columnLayouts.get(i % actualColumns).add(panel.panel());
    }

    emptyState.setVisible(false);
    columnsHost.setVisible(true);
  }

  private void updateSelectionContext(
      StitchConfigsWatcherProvider.WatchTarget target, String layerPath) {
    String context =
        target == null || !target.isComplete()
            ? "Selection: -"
            : "Selection: "
                + target.group()
                + " / "
                + target.configName()
                + " / "
                + Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(layerPath), target.layerId());
    selectionContext.setText(context);
  }

  private void refreshActionState() {
    boolean targetReady = activeTarget != null && activeTarget.isComplete();
    StitchRealtimeConnectionState state =
        controller == null ? StitchRealtimeConnectionState.DISCONNECTED : controller.state();
    boolean active =
        state == StitchRealtimeConnectionState.CONNECTED
            || state == StitchRealtimeConnectionState.CONNECTING
            || state == StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STALE;

    liveButton.setEnabled(targetReady && !active);
    stopButton.setEnabled(targetReady && active);
    clearButton.setEnabled(!highlightedKeys.isEmpty());
    refreshButton.setEnabled(true);
  }

  private void clearView(String message) {
    activeTarget = null;
    schemaDoc = null;
    lastPayload = null;
    fieldsByKey.clear();
    groupPanels.clear();
    highlightedKeys.clear();
    columnsHost.removeAll();

    emptyStateText.setText(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(message), "Select a watcher target."));
    emptyState.setVisible(true);
    columnsHost.setVisible(false);

    updateSelectionContext(null, null);
    statusBar.setMessage(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(message), ""));
  }

  private void closeController() {
    StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(registryBinding);
    registryBinding = () -> {};
    statusBinding.remove();
    statusBinding = () -> {};
    StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(observerBinding);
    observerBinding = () -> {};
    StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(updateBinding);
    updateBinding = () -> {};
    if (controller != null) {
      controller.close();
      controller = null;
    }
  }

  private static StitchConfigsScreenConfig requireConfig(Stitch stitch) {
    return stitch
        .features()
        .configs()
        .map(StitchConfigsFeature::watcher)
        .filter(StitchConfigsScreenConfig::enabled)
        .orElseThrow(NotFoundException::new);
  }

  private static String selectionContextLabel(
      StitchConfigsWatcherProvider.WatchTarget target,
      StitchConfigsWatcherProvider.LayerOption layerOption) {
    if (target == null || !target.isComplete()) {
      return null;
    }
    String layer =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            Strings.trimToNull(layerOption == null ? null : layerOption.path()),
            target.layerId());
    return target.group() + " / " + target.configName() + " / " + layer;
  }

  private static String topLevelKey(String path) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(path);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String value = normalized;
    if (value.startsWith("/")) {
      value = value.substring(1);
    }
    int slash = value.indexOf('/');
    if (slash >= 0) {
      value = value.substring(0, slash);
    }
    int dot = value.indexOf('.');
    if (dot >= 0) {
      value = value.substring(0, dot);
    }
    int bracket = value.indexOf('[');
    if (bracket >= 0) {
      value = value.substring(0, bracket);
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(value);
  }

  private static JsonNode resolveValueForField(JsonNode payload, String fieldKey) {
    if (payload == null || Strings.trimToNull(fieldKey) == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String key = Strings.trimToNull(fieldKey);
    for (JsonNode root : candidateRoots(payload)) {
      JsonNode direct = resolveFromNode(root, key);
      if (direct != null) {
        return direct;
      }
      if (!key.contains(".") && !key.contains("/") && !key.contains("[")) {
        JsonNode nested = findByLeafKey(root, key, 0);
        if (nested != null) {
          return nested;
        }
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static List<JsonNode> candidateRoots(JsonNode payload) {
    if (payload == null || payload.isNull()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<JsonNode> roots = new ArrayList<>();
    roots.add(payload);
    if (payload.isObject()) {
      addRootCandidate(roots, payload.get("resolved"));
      addRootCandidate(roots, payload.get("effective"));
      addRootCandidate(roots, payload.get("payload"));
      addRootCandidate(roots, payload.get("data"));
      addRootCandidate(roots, payload.get("config"));
    }
    return roots;
  }

  private static void addRootCandidate(List<JsonNode> roots, JsonNode candidate) {
    if (candidate == null || candidate.isNull()) {
      return;
    }
    for (JsonNode existing : roots) {
      if (existing == candidate) {
        return;
      }
    }
    roots.add(candidate);
  }

  private static JsonNode resolveFromNode(JsonNode root, String key) {
    if (root == null || root.isNull() || Strings.trimToNull(key) == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (root.isObject() && root.has(key)) {
      return root.get(key);
    }
    JsonNode byPath = valueAtPath(root, key);
    if (byPath != null) {
      return byPath;
    }
    if (!key.startsWith("/")) {
      JsonNode pointerNode = root.at("/" + key.replace(".", "/"));
      if (pointerNode != null && !pointerNode.isMissingNode()) {
        return pointerNode;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static JsonNode findByLeafKey(JsonNode root, String leafKey, int depth) {
    if (root == null || root.isNull() || Strings.trimToNull(leafKey) == null || depth > 8) {
      return null;
    }
    if (root.isObject()) {
      JsonNode direct = root.get(leafKey);
      if (direct != null) {
        return direct;
      }
      for (var fields = root.fields(); fields.hasNext(); ) {
        var entry = fields.next();
        JsonNode nested = findByLeafKey(entry == null ? null : entry.getValue(), leafKey, depth + 1);
        if (nested != null) {
          return nested;
        }
      }
      return null;
    }
    if (!root.isArray()) {
      return null;
    }
    for (JsonNode item : root) {
      JsonNode nested = findByLeafKey(item, leafKey, depth + 1);
      if (nested != null) {
        return nested;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static JsonNode valueAtPath(JsonNode root, String path) {
    if (root == null || Strings.trimToNull(path) == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(path);
    if (normalized.startsWith("/")) {
      JsonNode pointer = root.at(normalized);
      return pointer == null || pointer.isMissingNode() ? null : pointer;
    }

    List<String> segments = splitPathSegments(normalized);
    if (segments.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }

    JsonNode cursor = root;
    for (String segment : segments) {
      if (cursor == null || cursor.isNull()) {
        return null;
      }
      if (isInteger(segment)) {
        if (!cursor.isArray()) {
          return null;
        }
        int index = Integer.parseInt(segment);
        if (index < 0 || index >= cursor.size()) {
          return null;
        }
        cursor = cursor.get(index);
      } else {
        if (!cursor.isObject()) {
          return null;
        }
        cursor = cursor.get(segment);
      }
    }
    return cursor;
  }

  private static List<String> splitPathSegments(String path) {
    if (Strings.trimToNull(path) == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    String normalized = path.trim();
    List<String> segments = new ArrayList<>();
    StringBuilder token = new StringBuilder();
    int index = 0;
    while (index < normalized.length()) {
      char ch = normalized.charAt(index);
      if (ch == '.' || ch == '/') {
        if (token.length() > 0) {
          segments.add(token.toString());
          token.setLength(0);
        }
        index++;
        continue;
      }
      if (ch == '[') {
        if (token.length() > 0) {
          segments.add(token.toString());
          token.setLength(0);
        }
        int close = normalized.indexOf(']', index + 1);
        if (close < 0) {
          token.append(normalized.substring(index));
          break;
        }
        String inside = Strings.trimToNull(normalized.substring(index + 1, close));
        if (inside != null) {
          segments.add(inside);
        }
        index = close + 1;
        continue;
      }
      token.append(ch);
      index++;
    }
    if (token.length() > 0) {
      segments.add(token.toString());
    }
    return segments;
  }

  private static boolean isInteger(String value) {
    if (Strings.trimToNull(value) == null) {
      return false;
    }
    for (int i = 0; i < value.length(); i++) {
      if (!Character.isDigit(value.charAt(i))) {
        return false;
      }
    }
    return true;
  }

  private static String prettyJson(JsonNode value) {
    JsonNode payload = value == null ? MAPPER.createObjectNode() : value;
    try {
      return MAPPER.writerWithDefaultPrettyPrinter().writeValueAsString(payload);
    } catch (JsonProcessingException ex) {
      return payload.toString();
    }
  }

  private static String prettyInlineJson(JsonNode value) {
    if (value == null || value.isNull()) {
      return MISSING_VALUE_TEXT;
    }
    String rendered = prettyJson(value).replace('\n', ' ').replace("  ", " ").trim();
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(rendered), MISSING_VALUE_TEXT);
  }

  private static String formatInstant(Instant value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return "-";
    }
    return TS_FORMAT.format(value) + " UTC";
  }

  private static void styleActionButton(Button button, String ariaLabel) {
    button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    button.addClassName("stitch-configs-watcher-action");
    button
        .getElement()
        .setAttribute("aria-label", Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(ariaLabel), button.getText()));
  }

  private UI currentUi() {
    return getUI().orElse(null);
  }

  private record GroupMeta(String id, String label, Integer order) {}

  private record GroupPanel(String id, VerticalLayout panel) {}

  private static final class FieldRow {
    private final HorizontalLayout row;
    private final VerticalLayout valueHost;
    private String valueToken;

    private FieldRow(HorizontalLayout row, VerticalLayout valueHost, String valueToken) {
      this.row = row;
      this.valueHost = valueHost;
      this.valueToken = valueToken;
    }

    private HorizontalLayout row() {
      return row;
    }

    private VerticalLayout valueHost() {
      return valueHost;
    }

    private String valueToken() {
      return valueToken;
    }

    private void valueToken(String valueToken) {
      this.valueToken = valueToken;
    }
  }
}
